bharataṃ kekayīputram abravīd raghunandanaḥ ।। tvāṃ netum āgato vīra yudhājin mātulas tava ।। gamanāyābhicakrāma śatrughnasahitas tadā ।। mātṝṃś cāpi naraśreṣṭhaḥ śatrughnasahito yayau ।।
svapuraṃ prāviśad vīraḥ pitā tasya tutoṣa ha ।। mātulenāśvapatinā putrasnehena lālitaḥ ।। bhrātarau smaratāṃ vīrau vṛddhaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam ।। ubhau bharataśatrughnau mahendravaruṇopamau ।।
svaśarīrād vinirvṛttāś catvāra iva bāhavaḥ ।। svayambhūr iva bhūtānāṃ babhūva guṇavattaraḥ ।। pitaraṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ pūjayāmāsatus tadā ।। cakāra rāmo dharmātmā priyāṇi ca hitāni ca ।।
gurūṇāṃ gurukāryāṇi kāle kāle anvavaikṣata ।। rāmasya śīlavṛttena sarve viṣayavāsinaḥ ।। ucyamāno api paruṣaṃ nottaraṃ pratipadyate ।। na smaraty apakārāṇāṃ śatam apy ātmavattayā ।।
kathayann āsta vai nityam astrayogyāntareṣv api ।। vṛddhair abhivinītaś ca dvijair dharmārthadarśibhiḥ ।। laukike samayācare kṛtakalpo viśāradaḥ ।। yaḥ pragrahānugrahayor yathānyāyaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
śraiṣṭhyaṃ śāstrasamūheṣu prāpto vyāmiśrakeṣv api ।। vaihārikāṇāṃ śilpānāṃ vijñātārthavibhāgavit ।। dhanurvedavidāṃ śreṣṭho loke atirathasaṃmataḥ ।। apradhṛṣyaś ca saṃgrāme kruddhair api surāsuraiḥ ।।
na cāvamantā bhūtānāṃ na ca kālavaśānugaḥ ।। buddhyā bṛhaspates tulyo vīryeṇāpi śacīpateḥ ।। guṇair viruruce rāmo dīptaḥ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ ।। lokapālopamaṃ nātham akāmayata medinī ।।
dṛṣṭvā daśaratho rājā cakre cintāṃ paraṃtapaḥ ।। kadā nāma sutaṃ drakṣyāmy abhiṣiktam ahaṃ priyam ।। mattaḥ priyataro loke parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān ।। mahīdharasamo dhṛtyāṃ mattaś ca guṇavattaraḥ ।।
anena vayasā dṛṣṭvā yathā svargam avāpnuyām ।। niścitya sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ yuvarājam amanyata ।। samānināya medinyāḥ pradhānān pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। rājānam evābhimukhā niṣedur niyatā nṛpāḥ ।।
upopaviṣṭair nṛpatir vṛto babhau sahasracakṣur bhagavān ivāmaraiḥ ।। hitam uddharṣaṇaṃ cedam uvācāpratimaṃ vacaḥ ।। svareṇa mahatā rājā jīmūta iva nādayan ।। śreyasā yoktukāmo asmi sukhārham akhilaṃ jagat ।।
prajā nityam atandreṇa yathāśakty abhirakṣatā ।। pāṇḍur asyātapatrasya chāyāyāṃ jaritaṃ mayā ।। jīrṇasyāsya śarīrasya viśrāntim abhirocaye ।। pariśrānto asmi lokasya gurvīṃ dharmadhuraṃ vahan ।।
saṃnikṛṣṭān imān sarvān anumānya dvijarṣabhān ।। puraṃdarasamo vīrye rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ ।। yauvarājyena yoktāsmi prītaḥ puruṣapuṃgavam ।। trailokyam api nāthena yena syān nāthavattaram ।।
gatakleśo bhaviṣyāmi sute tasmin niveśya vai ।। vṛṣṭimantaṃ mahāmeghaṃ nardantam iva barhiṇaḥ ।। ūcuś ca manasā jñātvā vṛddhaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam ।। sa rāmaṃ yuvarājānam abhiṣiñcasva pārthivam ।।
ajānann iva jijñāsur idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। bhavanto draṣṭum icchanti yuvarājaṃ mamātmajam ।। bahavo nṛpa kalyāṇā guṇāḥ putrasya santi te ।। ikṣvākubhyo hi sarvebhyo apy atirakto viśāmpate ।।
dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca śīlavān anasūyakaḥ ।। mṛduś ca sthiracittaś ca sadā bhavyo anasūyakaḥ ।। bahuśrutānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ brāhmaṇānām upāsitā ।। devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ sarvāstreṣu viśāradaḥ ।।
gatvā saumitrisahito nāvijitya nivartate ।। paurān svajanavan nityaṃ kuśalaṃ paripṛcchati ।। nikhilenānupūrvyā ca pitā putrān ivaurasān ।। iti naḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ sadā rāmo abhibhāṣate ।।
utsaveṣu ca sarveṣu piteva parituṣyati ।। diṣṭyā putraguṇair yukto mārīca iva kaśyapaḥ ।। āśaṃsate janaḥ sarvo rāṣṭre puravare tathā ।। striyo vṛddhās taruṇyaś ca sāyamprātaḥ samāhitāḥ ।।
teṣām āyācitaṃ deva tvatprasādāt samṛdhyatām ।। paśyāmo yauvarājyasthaṃ tava rājottamātmajam ।। hitāya naḥ kṣipram udārajuṣṭaṃ mudābhiṣektuṃ varada tvam arhasi ।। pratigṛhyābravīd rājā tebhyaḥ priyahitaṃ vacaḥ ।।
yan me jyeṣṭhaṃ priyaṃ putraṃ yauvarājyastham icchatha ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca teṣām evopaśṛṇvatām ।। yauvarājyāya rāmasya sarvam evopakalpyatām ।। yathoktavacanaṃ prītau harṣayuktau dvijarṣabhau ।।
rāmaḥ kṛtātmā bhavatā śīghram ānīyatām iti ।। rāmaṃ tatrānayāṃcakre rathena rathināṃ varam ।। prācyodīcyāḥ pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca bhūmipāḥ ।। upāsāṃcakrire sarve taṃ devā iva vāsavam ।।
prāsādastho rathagataṃ dadarśāyāntam ātmajam ।। dīrghabāhuṃ mahāsattvaṃ mattamātaṃgagāminam ।। rūpaudāryaguṇaiḥ puṃsāṃ dṛṣṭicittāpahāriṇam ।। na tatarpa samāyāntaṃ paśyamāno narādhipaḥ ।।
pituḥ samīpaṃ gacchantaṃ prāñjaliḥ pṛṣṭhato anvagāt ।। āruroha nṛpaṃ draṣṭuṃ saha sūtena rāghavaḥ ।। nāma svaṃ śrāvayan rāmo vavande caraṇau pituḥ ।। gṛhyāñjalau samākṛṣya sasvaje priyam ātmajam ।।
dideśa rājā ruciraṃ rāmāya paramāsanam ।। svayeva prabhayā merum udaye vimalo raviḥ ।। vimalagrahanakṣatrā śāradī dyaur ivendunā ।। alaṃkṛtam ivātmānam ādarśatalasaṃsthitam ।।
uvācedaṃ vaco rājā devendram iva kaśyapaḥ ।। utpannas tvaṃ guṇaśreṣṭho mama rāmātmajaḥ priyaḥ ।। tasmāt tvaṃ puṣyayogena yauvarājyam avāpnuhi ।। guṇavaty api tu snehāt putra vakṣyāmi te hitam ।।
kāmakrodhasamutthāni tyajethā vyasanāni ca ।। amātyaprabhṛtīḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtīś cānurañjaya ।। tasmāt putra tvam ātmānaṃ niyamyaiva samācara ।। tvaritāḥ śīghram abhyetya kausalyāyai nyavedayan ।।
vyādideśa priyākhyebhyaḥ kausalyā pramadottamā ।। yayau svaṃ dyutimad veśma janaughaiḥ pratipūjitaḥ ।। narendram āmantrya gṛhāṇi gatvā devān samānarcur atīva hṛṣṭāḥ ।। mantrayitvā tataś cakre niścayajñaḥ sa niścayam ।।
rāmo rājīvatāmrākṣo yauvarājya iti prabhuḥ ।। sūtam ājñāpayāmāsa rāmaṃ punar ihānaya ।। rāmasya bhavanaṃ śīghraṃ rāmam ānayituṃ punaḥ ।। śrutvaiva cāpi rāmas taṃ prāptaṃ śaṅkānvito abhavat ।।
yad āgamanakṛtyaṃ te bhūyas tad brūhy aśeṣataḥ ।। śrutvā pramāṇam atra tvaṃ gamanāyetarāya vā ।। prayayau rājabhavanaṃ punar draṣṭuṃ nareśvaram ।। praveśayāmāsa gṛhaṃ vivikṣuḥ priyam uttamam ।।
dadarśa pitaraṃ dūrāt praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। pradiśya cāsmai ruciram āsanaṃ punar abravīt ।। annavadbhiḥ kratuśatais tatheṣṭaṃ bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ।। dattam iṣṭam adhītaṃ ca mayā puruṣasattama ।।
devarṣipitṛviprāṇām anṛṇo asmi tathātmanaḥ ।। ato yat tvām ahaṃ brūyāṃ tan me tvaṃ kartum arhasi ।। atas tvāṃ yuvarājānam abhiṣekṣyāmi putraka ।। sanirghātā maholkāś ca patantīha mahāsvanāḥ ।।
āvedayanti daivajñāḥ sūryāṅgārakarāhubhiḥ ।। rājā vā mṛtyum āpnoti ghorāṃ vāpadam ṛcchati ।। tāvad evābhiṣiñcasva calā hi prāṇināṃ matiḥ ।। śvaḥ puṣyayogaṃ niyataṃ vakṣyante daivacintakāḥ ।।
śvas tvāham abhiṣekṣyāmi yauvarājye paraṃtapa ।। saha vadhvopavastavyā darbhaprastaraśāyinā ।। bhavanti bahuvighnāni kāryāṇy evaṃvidhāni hi ।। tāvad evābhiṣekas te prāptakālo mato mama ।।
jyeṣṭhānuvartī dharmātmā sānukrośo jitendriyaḥ ।। satāṃ ca dharmanityānāṃ kṛtaśobhi ca rāghava ।। vrajeti rāmaḥ pitaram abhivādyābhyayād gṛham ।। tasmin kṣaṇe vinirgatya mātur antaḥpuraṃ yayau ।।
vāgyatāṃ devatāgāre dadarśa yācatīṃ śriyam ।। sītā cānāyitā śrutvā priyaṃ rāmābhiṣecanam ।। sumitrayānvāsyamānā sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca ।। prāṇāyāmena puruṣaṃ dhyāyamānā janārdanam ।।
uvāca vacanaṃ rāmo harṣayaṃs tām idaṃ tadā ।। bhavitā śvo abhiṣeko me yathā me śāsanaṃ pituḥ ।। evam ṛtvigupādhyāyaiḥ saha mām uktavān pitā ।। tāni me maṅgalāny adya vaidehyāś caiva kāraya ।।
harṣabāṣpakalaṃ vākyam idaṃ rāmam abhāṣata ।। jñātīn me tvaṃ śriyā yuktaḥ sumitrāyāś ca nandaya ।। yena tvayā daśaratho guṇair ārādhitaḥ pitā ।। yeyam ikṣvākurājyaśrīḥ putra tvāṃ saṃśrayiṣyati ।।
prāñjaliṃ prahvam āsīnam abhivīkṣya smayann iva ।। dvitīyaṃ me antarātmānaṃ tvām iyaṃ śrīr upasthitā ।। jīvitaṃ ca hi rājyaṃ ca tvadartham abhikāmaye ।। abhyanujñāpya sītāṃ ca jagāma svaṃ niveśanam ।।
purohitaṃ samāhūya vasiṣṭham idam abravīt ।। śrīyaśorājyalābhāya vadhvā saha yatavratam ।। svayaṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavān yayau rāmaniveśanam ।। tisraḥ kakṣyā rathenaiva viveśa munisattamaḥ ।।
mānayiṣyan sa mānārhaṃ niścakrāma niveśanāt ।। tato avatārayāmāsa parigṛhya rathāt svayam ।। priyārhaṃ harṣayan rāmam ity uvāca purohitaḥ ।। upavāsaṃ bhavān adya karotu saha sītayā ।।
pitā daśarathaḥ prītyā yayātiṃ nahuṣo yathā ।। mantravat kārayāmāsa vaidehyā sahitaṃ muniḥ ।। abhyanujñāpya kākutsthaṃ yayau rāmaniveśanāt ।। sabhājito viveśātha tān anujñāpya sarvaśaḥ ।।
yathā mattadvijagaṇaṃ praphullanalinaṃ saraḥ ।। nirgatya dadṛśe mārgaṃ vasiṣṭho janasaṃvṛtam ।। babhūvur abhisaṃbādhāḥ kutūhalajanair vṛtāḥ ।। babhūva rājamārgasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ ।।
āsīd ayodhyā nagarī samucchritagṛhadhvajā ।। rāmābhiṣekam ākāṅkṣann ākāṅkṣann udayaṃ raveḥ ।। utsuko abhūj jano draṣṭuṃ tam ayodhyāmahotsavam ।। vyūhann iva janaughaṃ taṃ śanai rājakulaṃ yayau ।।
samiyāya narendreṇa śakreṇeva bṛhaspatiḥ ।। papraccha sa ca tasmai tat kṛtam ity abhyavedayat ।। viveśāntaḥpuraṃ rājā siṃho giriguhām iva ।। vidīpayaṃś cāru viveśa pārthivaḥ śaśīva tārāgaṇasaṃkulaṃ nabhaḥ ।।
saha patnyā viśālākṣyā nārāyaṇam upāgamat ।। mahate daivatāyājyaṃ juhāva jvalite anale ।। dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ svāstīrṇe kuśasaṃstare ।। śrīmaty āyatane viṣṇoḥ śiśye naravarātmajaḥ ।।
alaṃkāravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ kārayāmāsa veśmanaḥ ।। pūrvāṃ saṃdhyām upāsīno jajāpa yatamānasaḥ ।। vimalakṣaumasaṃvīto vācayāmāsa ca dvijān ।। ayodhyāṃ pūrayāmāsa tūryaghoṣānunāditaḥ ।।
ayodhyānilayaḥ śrutvā sarvaḥ pramudito janaḥ ।। prabhātāṃ rajanīṃ dṛṣṭvā cakre śobhāṃ parāṃ punaḥ ।। catuṣpatheṣu rathyāsu caityeṣv aṭṭālakeṣu ca ।। kuṭumbināṃ samṛddheṣu śrīmatsu bhavaneṣu ca ।।
dhvajāḥ samucchritāś citrāḥ patākāś cābhavaṃs tadā ।। manaḥkarṇasukhā vācaḥ śuśruvuś ca tatas tataḥ ।। rāmābhiṣeke samprāpte catvareṣu gṛheṣu ca ।। rāmābhiṣekasaṃyuktāś cakrur eva mithaḥ kathāḥ ।।
rājamārgaḥ kṛtaḥ śrīmān paurai rāmābhiṣecane ।। dīpavṛkṣāṃs tathā cakrur anu rathyāsu sarvaśaḥ ।। ākāṅkṣamāṇā rāmasya yauvarājyābhiṣecanam ।। kathayanto mithas tatra praśaśaṃsur janādhipam ।।
jñātvā yo vṛddham ātmānaṃ rāmaṃ rājye ahbiṣekṣyati ।। cirāya bhavitā goptā dṛṣṭalokaparāvaraḥ ।। yathā ca bhrātṛṣu snigdhas tathāsmāsv api rāghavaḥ ।। yatprasādenābhiṣiktaṃ rāmaṃ drakṣyāmahe vayam ।।
digbhyo api śrutavṛttāntāḥ prāptā jānapadā janāḥ ।। rāmasya pūrayāmāsuḥ purīṃ jānapadā janāḥ ।। parvasūdīrṇavegasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ ।। samantataḥ sasvanam ākulaṃ babhau samudrayādobhir ivārṇavodakam ।।
prāsādaṃ candrasaṃkāśam āruroha yadṛcchayā ।। ayodhyāṃ mantharā tasmāt prāsādād anvavaikṣata ।। siktāṃ candanatoyaiś ca śiraḥsnātajanair vṛtām ।। uttamenābhisaṃyuktā harṣeṇārthaparā satī ।।
kārayiṣyati kiṃ vāpi samprahṛṣṭo mahīpatiḥ ।। ācacakṣe atha kubjāyai bhūyasīṃ rāghave śriyam ।। rājā daśaratho rāmam abhiṣecayitānagham ।। kailāsaśikharākārāt prāsādād avarohata ।।
śayānām etya kaikeyīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। upaplutamahaughena kim ātmānaṃ na budhyase ।। calaṃ hi tava saubhāgyaṃ nadyāḥ srota ivoṣṇage ।। kubjayā pāpadarśinyā viṣādam agamat param ।।
viṣaṇṇavadanāṃ hi tvāṃ lakṣaye bhṛśaduḥkhitām ।। uvāca krodhasaṃyuktā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradā ।। viṣādayantī provāca bhedayantī ca rāghavam ।। rāmaṃ daśaratho rājā yauvarājye abhiṣekṣyati ।।
dahyamānānaleneva tvaddhitārtham ihāgatā ।। tvadvṛddhau mama vṛddhiś ca bhaved atra na saṃśayaḥ ।। ugratvaṃ rājadharmāṇāṃ kathaṃ devi na budhyase ।। śuddhabhāve na jānīṣe tenaivam atisaṃdhitā ।।
arthenaivādya te bhartā kausalyāṃ yojayiṣyati ।। kālyaṃ sthāpayitā rāmaṃ rājye nihatakaṇṭake ।। āśīviṣa ivāṅkena bāle paridhṛtas tvayā ।। rājñā daśarathenādya saputrā tvaṃ tathā kṛtā ।।
rāmaṃ sthāpayatā rājye sānubandhā hatā hy asi ।। trāyasva putram ātmānaṃ māṃ ca vismayadarśane ।। evam ābharaṇaṃ tasyai kubjāyai pradadau śubham ।। kaikeyī mantharāṃ hṛṣṭā punar evābravīd idam ।।
etan me priyam ākhyātuḥ kiṃ vā bhūyaḥ karomi te ।। tasmāt tuṣṭāsmi yad rājā rāmaṃ rājye abhiṣekṣyati ।। tathā hy avocas tvam ataḥ priyottaraṃ varaṃ paraṃ te pradadāmi taṃ vṛṇu ।। uvācedaṃ tato vākyaṃ kopaduḥkhasamanvitā ।।
śokasāgaramadhyastham ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyase ।। yauvarājyena mahatā śvaḥ puṣyeṇa dvijottamaiḥ ।। upasthāsyasi kausalyāṃ dāsīva tvaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। aprahṛṣṭā bhaviṣyanti snuṣās te bharatakṣaye ।।
rāmasyaiva guṇān devī kaikeyī praśaśaṃsa ha ।। rāmo rājñaḥ suto jyeṣṭho yauvarājyam ato arhati ।। saṃtapyase kathaṃ kubje śrutvā rāmābhiṣecanam ।। pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyam avāpsyati nararṣabhaḥ ।।
kausalyāto atiriktaṃ ca sa tu śuśrūṣate hi mām ।। dīrgham uṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।। śokavyasanavistīrṇe majjantī duḥkhasāgare ।। rājavaṃśāt tu bharataḥ kaikeyi parihāsyate ।।
sthāpyamāneṣu sarveṣu sumahān anayo bhavet ।। sthāpayanty anavadyāṅgi guṇavatsv itareṣv api ।। anāthavat sukhebhyaś ca rājavaṃśāc ca vatsale ।। sapatnivṛddhau yā me tvaṃ pradeyaṃ dātum icchasi ।।
deśāntaraṃ nāyayitvā lokāntaram athāpi vā ।। saṃnikarṣāc ca sauhārdaṃ jāyate sthāvareṣv api ।। aśvinor iva saubhrātraṃ tayor lokeṣu viśrutam ।। rāmas tu bharate pāpaṃ kuryād iti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
etaddhi rocate mahyaṃ bhṛśaṃ cāpi hitaṃ tava ।। yadi ced bharato dharmāt pitryaṃ rājyam avāpsyati ।। samṛddhārthasya naṣṭārtho jīviṣyati kathaṃ vaśe ।। pracchādyamānaṃ rāmeṇa bharataṃ trātum arhasi ।।
rāmamātā sapatnī te kathaṃ vairaṃ na yātayet ।। ato hi saṃcintaya rājyam ātmaje parasya cādyaiva vivāsakāraṇam ।। dīrgham uṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya mantharām idam abravīt ।। yauvarājyena bharataṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecaye ।।
bharataḥ prāpnuyād rājyaṃ na tu rāmaḥ kathaṃcana ।। rāmārtham upahiṃsantī kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।। yathā te bharato rājyaṃ putraḥ prāpsyati kevalam ।। kiṃcid utthāya śayanāt svāstīrṇād idam abravīt ।।
bharataḥ prāpnuyād rājyaṃ na tu rāmaḥ kathaṃcana ।। rāmārtham upahiṃsantī kubjā vacanam abravīt ।। agacchat tvām upādāya devarājasya sāhyakṛt ।। vaijayantam iti khyātaṃ puraṃ yatra timidhvajaḥ ।।
dadau śakrasya saṃgrāmaṃ devasaṃghair anirjitaḥ ।। apavāhya tvayā devi saṃgrāmān naṣṭacetanaḥ ।। tuṣṭena tena dattau te dvau varau śubhadarśane ।। anabhijñā hy ahaṃ devi tvayaiva kathitaṃ purā ।।
pravrājanaṃ ca rāmasya tvaṃ varṣāṇi caturdaśa ।। mā smainaṃ pratyudīkṣethā mā cainam abhibhāṣathāḥ ।। tvatkṛte ca mahārājo viśed api hutāśanam ।। tava priyārthaṃ rājā hi prāṇān api parityajet ।।
mandasvabhāve budhyasva saubhāgyabalam ātmanaḥ ।। dadyād daśaratho rājā mā sma teṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। tau smāraya mahābhāge so artho mā tvām atikramet ।। vyavasthāpya mahārājaṃ tvam imaṃ vṛṇuyā varam ।।
bharataḥ kriyatāṃ rājā pṛthivyāṃ pārthivarṣabhaḥ ।। bharataś ca hatāmitras tava rājā bhaviṣyati ।। saṃgṛhītamanuṣyaś ca suhṛdbhiḥ sārdham ātmavān ।। rāmābhiṣekasaṃkalpān nigṛhya vinivartaya ।।
hṛṣṭā pratītā kaikeyī mantharām idam abravīt ।। pṛthivyām asi kubjānām uttamā buddhiniścaye ।। nāhaṃ samavabudhyeyaṃ kubje rājñaś cikīrṣitam ।। tvaṃ padmam iva vātena saṃnatā priyadarśanā ।।
adhastāc codaraṃ śāntaṃ sunābham iva lajjitam ।। jaṅghe bhṛśam upanyaste pādau cāpy āyatāv ubhau ।। agrato mama gacchantī rājahaṃsīva rājase ।। matayaḥ kṣatravidyāś ca māyāś cātra vasanti te ।।
abhiṣikte ca bharate rāghave ca vanaṃ gate ।। labdhārthā ca pratītā ca lepayiṣyāmi te sthagu ।। kārayiṣyāmi te kubje śubhāny ābharaṇāni ca ।। gamiṣyasi gatiṃ mukhyāṃ garvayantī dviṣajjanam ।।
pādau paricariṣyanti yathaiva tvaṃ sadā mama ।। śayānāṃ śayane śubhre vedyām agniśikhām iva ।। uttiṣṭha kuru kalyāṇaṃ rājānam anudarśaya ।। krodhāgāraṃ viśālākṣī saubhāgyamadagarvitā ।।
avamucya varārhāṇi śubhāny ābharaṇāni ca ।। saṃviśya bhūmau kaikeyī mantharām idam abravīt ।। vanaṃ tu rāghave prāpte bharataḥ prāpsyati kṣitim ।। asaṃvṛtām āstaraṇena medinīṃ tadādhiśiśye patiteva kiṃnarī ।।
narendrapatnī vimanā babhūva sā tamovṛtā dyaur iva magnatārakā ।। priyārhāṃ priyam ākhyātuṃ viveśāntaḥpuraṃ vaśī ।। pratapta iva duḥkhena so apaśyaj jagatīpatiḥ ।। apāpaḥ pāpasaṃkalpāṃ dadarśa dharaṇītale ।।
mahāgaja ivāraṇye snehāt parimamarśa tām ।। kāmī kamalapattrākṣīm uvāca vanitām idam ।। devi kenābhiyuktāsi kena vāsi vimānitā ।। bhūtopahatacitteva mama cittapramāthinī ।।
sukhitāṃ tvāṃ kariṣyanti vyādhim ācakṣva bhāmini ।। kaḥ priyaṃ labhatām adya ko vā sumahad apriyam ।। daridraḥ ko bhavatv āḍhyo dravyavān vāpy akiñcanaḥ ।। na te kaṃcid abhiprāyaṃ vyāhantum aham utsahe ।।
yāvad āvartate cakraṃ tāvatī me vasuṃdharā ।। paripīḍayituṃ bhūyo bhartāram upacakrame ।। abhiprāyas tu me kaścit tam icchāmi tvayā kṛtam ।। atha tad vyāhariṣyāmi yad abhiprārthitaṃ mayā ।।
tām uvāca mahātejāḥ kaikeyīm īṣadutsmitaḥ ।। manujo manujavyāghrād rāmād anyo na vidyate ।। etat samīkṣya kaikeyi brūhi yat sādhu manyase ।। kariṣyāmi tava prītiṃ sukṛtenāpi te śape ।।
vyājahāra mahāghoram abhyāgatam ivāntakam ।। tac chṛṇvantu trayastriṃśad devāḥ sendrapurogamāḥ ।। jagac ca pṛthivī caiva sagandharvā sarākṣasā ।। yāni cānyāni bhūtāni jānīyur bhāṣitaṃ tava ।।
varaṃ mama dadāty eṣa tan me śṛṇvantu devatāḥ ।। tataḥ param uvācedaṃ varadaṃ kāmamohitam ।। tau tāvad aham adyaiva vakṣyāmi śṛṇu me vacaḥ ।। anenaivābhiṣekeṇa bharato me abhiṣicyatām ।।
cīrājinajaṭādhārī rāmo bhavatu tāpasaḥ ।। adya caiva hi paśyeyaṃ prayāntaṃ rāghavaṃ vane ।। vyathito vilavaś caiva vyāghrīṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā mṛgaḥ ।। moham āpedivān bhūyaḥ śokopahatacetanaḥ ।।
kaikeyīm abravīt kruddhaḥ pradahann iva cakṣuṣā ।। kiṃ kṛtaṃ tava rāmeṇa pāpe pāpaṃ mayāpi vā ।। tasyaiva tvam anarthāya kiṃnimittam ihodyatā ।। avijñānān nṛpasutā vyālī tīkṣṇaviṣā yathā ।।
aparādhaṃ kam uddiśya tyakṣyāmīṣṭam ahaṃ sutam ।। jīvitaṃ vātmano rāmaṃ na tv eva pitṛvatsalam ।। apaśyatas tu me rāmaṃ naṣṭā bhavati cetanā ।। na tu rāmaṃ vinā dehe tiṣṭhet tu mama jīvitam ।।
api te caraṇau mūrdhnā spṛśāmy eṣa prasīda me ।। papāta devyāś caraṇau prasāritāv ubhāv asaṃspṛśya yathāturas tathā ।। yayātim iva puṇyānte devalokāt paricyutam ।। punar ākārayāmāsa tam eva varam aṅganā ।।
mama cemaṃ varaṃ kasmād vidhārayitum icchasi ।। pratyuvāca tataḥ kruddho muhūrtaṃ vihvalann iva ।। hantānārye mamāmitre rāmaḥ pravrājito vanam ।। akīrtir atulā loke dhruvaṃ paribhavaś ca me ।।
astam abhyagamat sūryo rajanī cābhyavartata ।। rājño vilapamānasya na vyabhāsata śarvarī ।। vilalāpārtavad duḥkhaṃ gaganāsaktalocanaḥ ।। nṛśaṃsāṃ kaikeyīṃ draṣṭuṃ yat kṛte vyasanaṃ mahat ।।
prasādayāmāsa punaḥ kaikeyīṃ cedam abravīt ।। prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ devi bhadre rājño viśeṣataḥ ।। kuru sādhu prasādaṃ me bāle sahṛdayā hy asi ।। śrutvā vicitraṃ karuṇaṃ vilāpaṃ bhartur nṛśaṃsā na cakāra vākyam ।।
samīkṣya putrasya vivāsanaṃ prati kṣitau visaṃjño nipapāta duḥkhitaḥ ।। viveṣṭamānam udīkṣya saikṣvākam idam abravīt ।। śeṣe kṣititale sannaḥ sthityāṃ sthātuṃ tvam arhasi ।। satyam āśritya hi mayā tvaṃ ca dharmaṃ pracoditaḥ ।।
pradāya pakṣiṇo rājañ jagāma gatim uttamām ।। yācamāne svake netre uddhṛtyāvimanā dadau ।। satyānurodhāt samaye velāṃ svāṃ nātivartate ।। agratas te parityaktā parityakṣyāmi jīvitam ।।
nāśakat pāśam unmoktuṃ balir indrakṛtaṃ yathā ।। sa dhuryo vai parispandan yugacakrāntaraṃ yathā ।। kṛcchrād dhairyeṇa saṃstabhya kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।। taṃ tyajāmi svajaṃ caiva tava putraṃ saha tvayā ।।
uvāca paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ vākyajñā roṣamūrchitā ।। ānāyayitum akliṣṭaṃ putraṃ rāmam ihārhasi ।। niḥsapatnāṃ ca māṃ kṛtvā kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi ।। rājā pracodito abhīkṣṇaṃ kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।।
jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ priyaṃ rāmaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi dhārmikam ।। svayam evābravīt sūtaṃ gaccha tvaṃ rāmam ānaya ।। śokāraktekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān udvīkṣyovāca dhārmikaḥ ।। pragṛhītāñjaliḥ kiṃcit tasmād deśād apākraman ।।
tadā sumantraṃ mantrajñā kaikeyī pratyuvāca ha ।। sa manyamānaḥ kalyāṇaṃ hṛdayena nananda ca ।। vyaktaṃ rāmo abhiṣekārtham ihāyāsyati dharmavit ।। nirjagāma mahātejā rāghavasya didṛkṣayā ।।
dadarśa paurān vividhān mahādhanān upasthitān dvāram upetya viṣṭhitān ।। upatasthur upasthānaṃ saharājapurohitāḥ ।। rāghavasyābhiṣekārthe prīyamāṇās tu saṃgatāḥ ।। abhiṣekāya rāmasya dvijendrair upakalpitam ।।
rāmaś ca samyagāstīrṇo bhāsvatā vyāghracarmaṇā ।। yāś cānyāḥ saritaḥ puṇyā hradāḥ kūpāḥ sarāṃsi ca ।। tābhyaś caivāhṛtaṃ toyaṃ samudrebhyaś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। padmotpalayutā bhānti pūrṇāḥ paramavāriṇā ।।
sajjaṃ tiṣṭhati rāmasya vālavyajanam uttamam ।। sajjaṃ dyutikaraṃ śrīmad abhiṣekapuraskṛtam ।। prasrutaś ca gajaḥ śrīmān aupavāhyaḥ pratīkṣate ।। vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi bandinaś ca tathāpare ।।
tathā jātīyam ādāya rājaputrābhiṣecanam ।। apaśyanto abruvan ko nu rājño naḥ prativedayet ।। yauvarājyābhiṣekaś ca sajjo rāmasya dhīmataḥ ।। abravīt tān idaṃ sarvān sumantro rājasatkṛtaḥ ।।
rājñaḥ saṃpratibuddhasya yac cāgamanakāraṇam ।। āśirbhir guṇayuktābhir abhituṣṭāva rāghavam ।। budhyasva nṛpaśārdūla kuru kāryam anantaram ।। darśanaṃ pratikāṅkṣante pratibudhyasva rāghava ।।
pratibudhya tato rājā idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। iti rājā daśarathaḥ sūtaṃ tatrānvaśāt punaḥ ।। nirjagāma nṛpāvāsān manyamānaḥ priyaṃ mahat ।। sa sūtas tatra śuśrāva rāmādhikaraṇāḥ kathāḥ ।।
rāmaveśma sumantras tu śakraveśmasamaprabham ।। kāñcanapratimaikāgraṃ maṇividrumatoraṇam ।। dāmabhir varamālyānāṃ sumahadbhir alaṃkṛtam ।। tataḥ samāsādya mahādhanaṃ mahat prahṛṣṭaromā sa babhūva sārathiḥ ।।
avāryamāṇaḥ praviveśa sārathiḥ prabhūtaratnaṃ makaro yathārṇavam ।। praviviktāṃ tataḥ kakṣyām āsasāda purāṇavit ।। apramādibhir ekāgraiḥ svanuraktair adhiṣṭhitām ।। dadarśa viṣṭhitān dvāri stryadhyakṣān susamāhitān ।।
sahabhāryāya rāmāya kṣipram evācacakṣire ।। tatraivānāyayāmāsa rāghavaḥ priyakāmyayā ।। dadarśa sūtaḥ paryaṅke sauvarṇe sottaracchade ।। anuliptaṃ parārdhyena candanena paraṃtapam ।।
upetaṃ sītayā bhūyaś citrayā śaśinaṃ yathā ।। vavande varadaṃ bandī niyamajño vinītavat ।। rājaputram uvācedaṃ sumantro rājasatkṛtaḥ ।। mahiṣyā saha kaikeyyā gamyatāṃ tatra māciram ।।
tataḥ saṃmānayāmāsa sītām idam uvāca ha ।। mantrayete dhruvaṃ kiṃcid abhiṣecanasaṃhitam ।। saṃcodayati rājānaṃ madarthaṃ madirekṣaṇā ।। dhruvam adyaiva māṃ rājā yauvarājye abhiṣekṣyati ।।
saha tvaṃ parivāreṇa sukham āsva ramasva ca ।। ādvāram anuvavrāja maṅgalāny abhidadhyuṣī ।। tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśam āruroha rathottamam ।। kareṇuśiśukalpaiś ca yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ ।।
prayayau tūrṇam āsthāya rāghavo jvalitaḥ śriyā ।। niketān niryayau śrīmān mahābhrād iva candramāḥ ।। jugopa bhrātaraṃ bhrātā ratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। tasya niṣkramamāṇasya janaughasya samantataḥ ।।
ātmādhikārā vividhāś ca vācaḥ prahṛṣṭarūpasya pure janasya ।। lābho janasyāsya yad eṣa sarvaṃ prapatsyate rāṣṭram idaṃ cirāya ।। mahīyamānaḥ pravaraiś ca vādakair abhiṣṭuto vaiśravaṇo yathā yayau ।। prabhūtaratnaṃ bahupaṇyasaṃcayaṃ dadarśa rāmo ruciraṃ mahāpatham ।।
apaśyan nagaraṃ śrīmān nānājanasamākulam ।। rājamārgaṃ yayau rāmo madhyenāgarudhūpitam ।। saṃvṛtaṃ vividhaiḥ paṇyair bhakṣyair uccāvacair api ।। yathārhaṃ cāpi sampūjya sarvān eva narān yayau ।।
adyopādāya taṃ mārgam abhiṣikto anupālaya ।। tataḥ sukhataraṃ sarve rāme vatsyāma rājani ।। yathā paśyāma niryāntaṃ rāmaṃ rājye pratiṣṭhitam ।। yathābhiṣeko rāmasya rājyenāmitatejasaḥ ।।
ātmasaṃpūjanīḥ śṛṇvan yayau rāmo mahāpatham ।। naraḥ śaknoty apākraṣṭum atikrānte api rāghave ।। caturṇāṃ hi vayaḥsthānāṃ tena te tam anuvratāḥ ।। rājaputraḥ pitur veśma praviveśa śriyā jvalan ।।
saṃnivartya janaṃ sarvaṃ śuddhāntaḥpuram abhyagāt ।। pratīkṣate tasya punaḥ sma nirgamaṃ yathodayaṃ candramasaḥ saritpatiḥ ।। kaikeyīsahitaṃ dīnaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā ।। tato vavande caraṇau kaikeyyāḥ susamāhitaḥ ।।
śaśāka nṛpatir dīno nekṣituṃ nābhibhāṣitum ।। rāmo api bhayam āpannaḥ padā spṛṣṭveva pannagam ।। niḥśvasantaṃ mahārājaṃ vyathitākulacetasam ।। upaplutam ivādityam uktānṛtam ṛṣiṃ yathā ।।
babhūva saṃrabdhataraḥ samudra iva parvaṇi ।। kiṃsvid adyaiva nṛpatir na māṃ pratyabhinandati ।। tasya mām adya samprekṣya kimāyāsaḥ pravartate ।। kaikeyīm abhivādyaiva rāmo vacanam abravīt ।।
kupitas tan mamācakṣva tvaṃ caivainaṃ prasādaya ।। saṃtāpo vābhitāpo vā durlabhaṃ hi sadā sukham ।। śatrughne vā mahāsattve mātṝṇāṃ vā mamāśubham ।। muhūrtam api neccheyaṃ jīvituṃ kupite nṛpe ।।
kathaṃ tasmin na varteta pratyakṣe sati daivate ।। ukto bhavatyā kopena yatrāsya lulitaṃ manaḥ ।। kiṃnimittam apūrvo ayaṃ vikāro manujādhipe ।। niyukto guruṇā pitrā nṛpeṇa ca hitena ca ।।
kariṣye pratijāne ca rāmo dvir nābhibhāṣate ।। uvāca rāmaṃ kaikeyī vacanaṃ bhṛśadāruṇam ।। rakṣitena varau dattau saśalyena mahāraṇe ।। gamanaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye tava cādyaiva rāghava ।।
ātmānaṃ ca naraśreṣṭha mama vākyam idaṃ śṛṇu ।। tvayāraṇyaṃ praveṣṭavyaṃ nava varṣāṇi pañca ca ।। abhiṣekam imaṃ tyaktvā jaṭācīradharo vasa ।। nānāratnasamākīrṇāṃ savājirathakuñjarām ।।
śrutvā na vivyathe rāmaḥ kaikeyīṃ cedam abravīt ।। jaṭācīradharo rājñaḥ pratijñām anupālayan ।। nābhinandati durdharṣo yathāpuram ariṃdamaḥ ।। yāsyāmi bhava suprītā vanaṃ cīrajaṭādharaḥ ।।
niyujyamāno viśrabdhaṃ kiṃ na kuryād ahaṃ priyam ।। svayaṃ yan nāha māṃ rājā bharatasyābhiṣecanam ।। hṛṣṭo bhrātre svayaṃ dadyāṃ bharatāyāpracoditaḥ ।। tava ca priyakāmārthaṃ pratijñām anupālayan ।।
vasudhāsaktanayano mandam aśrūṇi muñcati ।। bharataṃ mātulakulād adyaiva nṛpaśāsanāt ।। avicārya pitur vākyaṃ samāvastuṃ caturdaśa ।। prasthānaṃ śraddadhānā hi tvarayāmāsa rāghavam ।।
bharataṃ mātulakulād upāvartayituṃ narāḥ ।। rāma tasmād itaḥ śīghraṃ vanaṃ tvaṃ gantum arhasi ।। naitat kiṃcin naraśreṣṭha manyur eṣo apanīyatām ।। pitā tāvan na te rāma snāsyate bhokṣyate api vā ।।
mūrchito nyapatat tasmin paryaṅke hemabhūṣite ।। kaśayevāhato vājī vanaṃ gantuṃ kṛtatvaraḥ ।। śrutvā gatavyatho rāmaḥ kaikeyīṃ vākyam abravīt ।। viddhi mām ṛṣibhis tulyaṃ kevalaṃ dharmam āsthitam ।।
prāṇān api parityajya sarvathā kṛtam eva tat ।। yathā pitari śuśrūṣā tasya vā vacanakriyā ।। vane vatsyāmi vijane varṣāṇīha caturdaśa ।। yad rājānam avocas tvaṃ mameśvaratarā satī ।।
tato adyaiva gamiṣyāmi daṇḍakānāṃ mahad vanam ।। tathā bhavatyā kartavyaṃ sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। śokād aśaknuvan bāṣpaṃ praruroda mahāsvanam ।। kaikeyyāś cāpy anāryāyā niṣpapāta mahādyutiḥ ।।
niṣkramyāntaḥpurāt tasmāt svaṃ dadarśa suhṛjjanam ।। lakṣmaṇaḥ paramakruddhaḥ sumitrānandavardhanaḥ ।। śanair jagāma sāpekṣo dṛṣṭiṃ tatrāvicālayan ।। lokakāntasya kāntatvaṃ śītaraśmer iva kṣapā ।।
sarvalokātigasyeva lakṣyate cittavikriyā ।। praviveśātmavān veśma mātur apriyaśaṃsivān ।। na caiva rāmo atra jagāma vikriyāṃ suhṛjjanasyātmavipattiśaṅkayā ।। jagāma sahito bhrātrā mātur antaḥpuraṃ vaśī ।।
upaviṣṭaṃ gṛhadvāri tiṣṭhataś cāparān bahūn ।। brāhmaṇān vedasampannān vṛddhān rājñābhisatkṛtān ।। striyo vṛddhāś ca bālāś ca dvārarakṣaṇatatparāḥ ।। nyavedayanta tvaritā rāmamātuḥ priyaṃ tadā ।।
prabhāte tv akarot pūjāṃ viṣṇoḥ putrahitaiṣiṇī ।। agniṃ juhoti sma tadā mantravat kṛtamaṅgalā ।। dadarśa mātaraṃ tatra hāvayantīṃ hutāśanam ।। abhicakrāma saṃhṛṣṭā kiśoraṃ vaḍabā yathā ।।
kausalyā putravātsalyād idaṃ priyahitaṃ vacaḥ ।। prāpnuhy āyuś ca kīrtiṃ ca dharmaṃ copahitaṃ kule ।। adyaiva hi tvāṃ dharmātmā yauvarājye abhiṣekṣyati ।। sa svabhāvavinītaś ca gauravāc ca tadānataḥ ।।
idaṃ tava ca duḥkhāya vaidehyā lakṣmaṇasya ca ।। madhumūlaphalair jīvan hitvā munivad āmiṣam ।। māṃ punar daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ vivāsayati tāpasam ।। rāmas tūtthāpayāmāsa mātaraṃ gatacetasam ।।
pāṃśuguṇṭhitasarvāṅgīṃ vimamarśa ca pāṇinā ।। uvāca puruṣavyāghram upaśṛṇvati lakṣmaṇe ।। na sma duḥkham ato bhūyaḥ paśyeyam aham aprajā ।। aprajāsmīti saṃtāpo na hy anyaḥ putra vidyate ।।
api putre vipaśyeyam iti rāmāsthitaṃ mayā ।। ato duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu pramadānāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। kiṃ punaḥ proṣite tāta dhruvaṃ maraṇam eva me ।। kaikeyyāḥ putram anvīkṣya sa jano nābhibhāṣate ।।
atītāni prakāṅkṣantyā mayā duḥkhaparikṣayam ।। duḥkhaṃ saṃvardhito moghaṃ tvaṃ hi durgatayā mayā ।। prāvṛṣīva mahānadyāḥ spṛṣṭaṃ kūlaṃ navāmbhasā ।। yad antako adyaiva na māṃ jihīrṣati prasahya siṃho rudatīṃ mṛgīm iva ।।
anena duḥkhena ca deham arpitaṃ dhruvaṃ hy akāle maraṇaṃ na vidyate ।। tapaś ca taptaṃ yad apatyakāraṇāt suniṣphalaṃ bījam ivoptam ūṣare ।। gatāham adyaiva paretasaṃsadaṃ vinā tvayā dhenur ivātmajena vai ।। vyasanam upaniśāmya sā mahat sutam iva baddham avekṣya kiṃnarī ।।
uvāca lakṣmaṇo dīnas tat kālasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ ।। tyaktvā rājyaśriyaṃ gacchet striyā vākyavaśaṃ gataḥ ।। nṛpaḥ kim iva na brūyāc codyamānaḥ samanmathaḥ ।। yena nirvāsyate rāṣṭrād vanavāsāya rāghavaḥ ।।
amitro api nirasto api yo asya doṣam udāharet ।। avekṣamāṇaḥ ko dharmaṃ tyajet putram akāraṇāt ।। putraḥ ko hṛdaye kuryād rājavṛttam anusmaran ।। tāvad eva mayā sārdham ātmasthaṃ kuru śāsanam ।।
kaḥ samartho adhikaṃ kartuṃ kṛtāntasyeva tiṣṭhataḥ ।। kariṣyāmi śarais tīkṣṇair yadi sthāsyati vipriye ।। sarvān etān vadhiṣyāmi mṛdur hi paribhūyate ।। kasya śaktiḥ śriyaṃ dātuṃ bharatāyāriśāsana ।।
satyena dhanuṣā caiva datteneṣṭena te śape ।। praviṣṭaṃ tatra māṃ devi tvaṃ pūrvam avadhāraya ।। devī paśyatu me vīryaṃ rāghavaś caiva paśyatu ।। uvāca rāmaṃ kausalyā rudantī śokalālasā ।।
yad atrānantaraṃ tat tvaṃ kuruṣva yadi rocate ।। vihāya śokasaṃtaptāṃ gantum arhasi mām itaḥ ।। śuśrūṣa mām ihasthas tvaṃ cara dharmam anuttamam ।। pareṇa tapasā yuktaḥ kāśyapas tridivaṃ gataḥ ।।
tvāṃ nāham anujānāmi na gantavyam ito vanam ।। tvayā saha mama śreyas tṛṇānām api bhakṣaṇam ।। ahaṃ prāyam ihāsiṣye na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitum ।। brahmahatyām ivādharmāt samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ ।।
uvāca rāmo dharmātmā vacanaṃ dharmasaṃhitam ।। prasādaye tvāṃ śirasā gantum icchāmy ahaṃ vanam ।। gaur hatā jānatā dharmaṃ kaṇḍunāpi vipaścitā ।। khanadbhiḥ sāgarair bhūtim avāptaḥ sumahān vadhaḥ ।।
kṛttā paraśunāraṇye pitur vacanakāriṇā ।। pūrvair ayam abhipreto gato mārgo anugamyate ।। pitur hi vacanaṃ kurvan na kaścin nāma hīyate ।। abhiprāyam avijñāya satyasya ca śamasya ca ।।
dharmasaṃśritam etac ca pitur vacanam uttamam ।। na kartavyaṃ vṛthā vīra dharmam āśritya tiṣṭhatā ।। pitur hi vacanād vīra kaikeyyāhaṃ pracoditaḥ ।। dharmam āśraya mā taikṣṇyaṃ madbuddhir anugamyatām ।।
uvāca bhūyaḥ kausalyāṃ prāñjaliḥ śirasānataḥ ।। tīrṇapratijñaś ca vanāt punar eṣyāmy ahaṃ purīm ।। adīrghakāle na tu devi jīvite vṛṇe avarām adya mahīm adharmataḥ ।। athānujaṃ bhṛśam anuśāsya darśanaṃ cakāra tāṃ hṛdi jananīṃ pradakṣiṇam ।।
śvasantam iva nāgendraṃ roṣavisphāritekṣaṇam ।। uvācedaṃ sa dhairyeṇa dhārayan sattvam ātmavān ।। abhiṣekanivṛttyarthe so astu sambhārasambhramaḥ ।। mātā naḥ sā yathā na syāt saviśaṅkā tathā kuru ।।
manasi pratisaṃjātaṃ saumitre aham upekṣitum ।। mātṝṇāṃ vā pitur vāhaṃ kṛtam alpaṃ ca vipriyam ।। paralokabhayād bhīto nirbhayo astu pitā mama ।। satyaṃ neti manastāpas tasya tāpas tapec ca mām ।।
anvag evāham icchāmi vanaṃ gantum itaḥ punaḥ ।। sutaṃ bharatam avyagram abhiṣecayitā tataḥ ।। gate araṇyaṃ ca kaikeyyā bhaviṣyati manaḥsukham ।। tat tu nārhāmi saṃkleṣṭuṃ pravrajiṣyāmi māciram ।।
rājyasya ca vitīrṇasya punar eva nivartane ।। yadi bhāvo na daivo ayaṃ kṛtāntavihito bhavet ।। bhūtapūrvaṃ viśeṣo vā tasyā mayi sute api vā ।। ugrair vākyair ahaṃ tasyā nānyad daivāt samarthaye ।।
brūyāt sā prākṛteva strī matpīḍāṃ bhartṛsaṃnidhau ।। vyaktaṃ mayi ca tasyāṃ ca patito hi viparyayaḥ ।। yasya na grahaṇaṃ kiṃcit karmaṇo anyatra dṛśyate ।। yasya kiṃcit tathā bhūtaṃ nanu daivasya karma tat ।।
pratisaṃhāraya kṣipram ābhiṣecanikīṃ kriyām ।। daivābhipannā hi vadanty aniṣṭaṃ jānāsi daivaṃ ca tathā prabhāvam ।। śrutvā madhyaṃ jagāmeva manasā duḥkhaharṣayoḥ ।। niśaśvāsa mahāsarpo bilastha iva roṣitaḥ ।।
babhau kruddhasya siṃhasya mukhasya sadṛśaṃ mukham ।। tiryag ūrdhvaṃ śarīre ca pātayitvā śirodharām ।। asthāne sambhramo yasya jāto vai sumahān ayam ।। kathaṃ hy etad asambhrāntas tvadvidho vaktum arhati ।।
kiṃ nāma kṛpaṇaṃ daivam aśaktam abhiśaṃsasi ।। santi dharmopadhāḥ ślakṣṇā dharmātman kiṃ na budhyase ।। sa hi dharmo mama dveṣyaḥ prasaṅgād yasya muhyasi ।। tathāpy upekṣaṇīyaṃ te na me tad api rocate ।।
vīrāḥ saṃbhāvitātmāno na daivaṃ paryupāsate ।। na daivena vipannārthaḥ puruṣaḥ so avasīdati ।। daivamānuṣayor adya vyaktā vyaktir bhaviṣyati ।। yad daivād āhataṃ te adya dṛṣṭaṃ rājyābhiṣecanam ।।
pradhāvitam ahaṃ daivaṃ pauruṣeṇa nivartaye ।। na ca kṛtsnās trayo lokā vihanyuḥ kiṃ punaḥ pitā ।। araṇye te vivatsyanti caturdaśa samās tathā ।। abhiṣekavighātena putrarājyāya vartate ।।
prabhaviṣyati duḥkhāya yathograṃ pauruṣaṃ mama ।। āryaputrāḥ kariṣyanti vanavāsaṃ gate tvayi ।। prajā nikṣipya putreṣu putravat paripālane ।। naivam icchasi dharmātman rājyaṃ rāma tvam ātmani ।।
rājyaṃ ca tava rakṣeyam ahaṃ veleva sāgaram ।। aham eko mahīpālān alaṃ vārayituṃ balāt ।। nāsirābandhanārthāya na śarāḥ stambhahetavaḥ ।। na cāhaṃ kāmaye atyarthaṃ yaḥ syāc chatrur mato mama ।।
pragṛhītena vai śatruṃ vajriṇaṃ vā na kalpaye ।। hastyaśvanarahastoruśirobhir bhavitā mahī ।। patiṣyanti dvipā bhūmau meghā iva savidyutaḥ ।। kathaṃ puruṣamānī syāt puruṣāṇāṃ mayi sthite ।।
viniyokṣyāmy ahaṃ bāṇān nṛvājigajamarmasu ।। rājñaś cāprabhutāṃ kartuṃ prabhutvaṃ ca tava prabho ।। vasūnāṃ ca vimokṣasya suhṛdāṃ pālanasya ca ।। abhiṣecanavighnasya kartṝṇāṃ te nivāraṇe ।।
yathā taveyaṃ vasudhā vaśe bhavet tathaiva māṃ śādhi tavāsmi kiṃkaraḥ ।। uvāca pitrye vacane vyavasthitaṃ nibodha mām eṣa hi saumya satpathaḥ ।। kausalyā bāṣpasaṃruddhā vaco dharmiṣṭham abravīt ।। mayi jāto daśarathāt katham uñchena vartayet ।।
kathaṃ sa bhokṣyate nātho vane mūlaphalāny ayam ।। guṇavān dayito rājño rāghavo yad vivāsyate ।। pradhakṣyati yathā kakṣaṃ citrabhānur himātyaye ।। ahaṃ tvānugamiṣyāmi yatra putra gamiṣyasi ।।
śrutvā rāmo abravīd vākyaṃ mātaraṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitām ।। bhavatyā ca parityakto na nūnaṃ vartayiṣyati ।। sa bhavatyā na kartavyo manasāpi vigarhitaḥ ।। śuśrūṣā kriyatāṃ tāvat sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
tathety uvāca suprītā rāmam akliṣṭakāriṇam ।। bhūyas tām abravīd vākyaṃ mātaraṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitām ।। rājā bhartā guruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarveṣām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। varṣāṇi paramaprītaḥ sthāsyāmi vacane tava ।।
uvāca paramārtā tu kausalyā putravatsalā ।। yadi te gamane buddhiḥ kṛtā pitur apekṣayā ।। bhavatyā mama caivādya rājā prabhavati prabhuḥ ।। bhavatīm anuvarteta sa hi dharmarataḥ sadā ।।
śramaṃ nāvāpnuyāt kiṃcid apramattā tathā kuru ।। bhartāraṃ nānuvarteta sā ca pāpagatir bhavet ।। eṣa dharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭo loke vede śrutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ kālaṃ pratīkṣasva mamāgamanakāṅkṣiṇī ।।
yadi dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho dhārayiṣyati jīvitam ।। gaccha putra tvam ekāgro bhadraṃ te astu sadā vibho ।। uvāca rāmaṃ śubhalakṣaṇaṃ vaco babhūva ca svastyayanābhikāṅkṣiṇī ।। cakāra mātā rāmasya maṅgalāni manasvinī ।।
svasti dhātā vidhātā ca svasti pūṣā bhago aryamā ।। dināni ca muhūrtāś ca svasti kurvantu te sadā ।। skandaś ca bhagavān devaḥ somaś ca sabṛhaspatiḥ ।। mahāvanāni carato muniveṣasya dhīmataḥ ।।
sarīsṛpāś ca kīṭāś ca mā bhūvan gahane tava ।। mahiṣāḥ śṛṅgiṇo raudrā na te druhyantu putraka ।। mā ca tvāṃ hiṃsiṣuḥ putra mayā sampūjitās tv iha ।। sarvasampattayo rāma svastimān gaccha putraka ।।
sarvebhyaś caiva devebhyo ye ca te paripanthinaḥ ।। ye ca śeṣāḥ surās te tvāṃ rakṣantu vanavāsinam ।। stutibhiś cānurūpābhir ānarcāyatalocanā ।। vṛtranāśe samabhavat tat te bhavatu maṅgalam ।।
amṛtaṃ prārthayānasya tat te bhavatu maṅgalam ।। cakāra rakṣāṃ kausalyā mantrair abhijajāpa ca ।। avadat putra siddhārtho gaccha rāma yathāsukham ।। paśyāmi tvāṃ sukhaṃ vatsa susthitaṃ rājaveśmani ।।
abhiprayātasya vanaṃ cirāya te hitāni kāṅkṣantu diśaś ca rāghava ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ punaḥ punaś cāpi nipīḍya sasvaje ।। jagāma sītānilayaṃ mahāyaśāḥ sa rāghavaḥ prajvalitaḥ svayā śriyā ।। kṛtasvastyayano mātrā dharmiṣṭhe vartmani sthitaḥ ।।
hṛdayāny āmamantheva janasya guṇavattayā ।। tad eva hṛdi tasyāś ca yauvarājyābhiṣecanam ।। abhijñā rājadharmāṇāṃ rājaputraṃ pratīkṣate ।। prahṛṣṭajanasampūrṇaṃ hriyā kiṃcid avāṅmukhaḥ ।।
apaśyac chokasaṃtaptaṃ cintāvyākulitendriyam ।। āha duḥkhābhisaṃtaptā kim idānīm idaṃ prabho ।। procyate brāhmaṇaiḥ prājñaiḥ kena tvam asi durmanāḥ ।। āvṛtaṃ vadanaṃ valgu chattreṇābhivirājate ।।
candrahaṃsaprakāśābhyāṃ vījyate na tavānanam ।। stuvanto nādya dṛśyante maṅgalaiḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ ।। mūrdhni mūrdhāvasiktasya dadhati sma vidhānataḥ ।। anuvrajitum icchanti paurajānapadās tathā ।।
mukhyaḥ puṣyaratho yuktaḥ kiṃ na gacchati te agrataḥ ।। prayāṇe lakṣyate vīra kṛṣṇameghagiriprabhaḥ ।। bhadrāsanaṃ puraskṛtya yāntaṃ vīrapuraḥsaram ।। apūrvo mukhavarṇaś ca na praharṣaś ca lakṣyate ।।
sīte tatrabhavāṃs tātaḥ pravrājayati māṃ vanam ।। śṛṇu jānaki yenedaṃ krameṇābhyāgataṃ mama ।। kaikeyyai prītamanasā purā dattau mahāvarau ।। pracoditaḥ sa samayo dharmeṇa pratinirjitaḥ ।।
so ahaṃ tvām āgato draṣṭuṃ prasthito vijanaṃ vanam ।। tasmān na te guṇāḥ kathyā bharatasyāgrato mama ।। anukūlatayā śakyaṃ samīpe tasya vartitum ।। vanam adyaiva yāsyāmi sthirā bhava manasvini ।।
vratopavāsaratayā bhavitavyaṃ tvayānaghe ।। vanditavyo daśarathaḥ pitā mama nareśvaraḥ ।। dharmam evāgrataḥ kṛtvā tvattaḥ sammānam arhati ।। snehapraṇayasambhogaiḥ samā hi mama mātaraḥ ।।
tvayā lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau prāṇaiḥ priyatarau mama ।। sa hi rājā prabhuś caiva deśasya ca kulasya ca ।। rājānaḥ samprasīdanti prakupyanti viparyaye ।। samarthān sampragṛhṇanti janān api narādhipāḥ ।।
yathā vyalīkaṃ kuruṣe na kasyacit tathā tvayā kāryam idaṃ vaco mama ।। praṇayād eva saṃkruddhā bhartāram idam abravīt ।। svāni puṇyāni bhuñjānāḥ svaṃ svaṃ bhāgyam upāsate ।। ataś caivāham ādiṣṭā vane vastavyam ity api ।।
iha pretya ca nārīṇāṃ patir eko gatiḥ sadā ।। agratas te gamiṣyāmi mṛdnantī kuśakaṇṭakān ।। naya māṃ vīra viśrabdhaḥ pāpaṃ mayi na vidyate ।। sarvāvasthāgatā bhartuḥ pādacchāyā viśiṣyate ।।
nāsmi samprati vaktavyā vartitavyaṃ yathā mayā ।। acintayantī trīṃl lokāṃś cintayantī pativratam ।। saha raṃsye tvayā vīra vaneṣu madhugandhiṣu ।। anyasyāpi janasyeha kiṃ punar mama mānada ।।
na te duḥkhaṃ kariṣyāmi nivasantī saha tvayā ।। draṣṭuṃ sarvatra nirbhītā tvayā nāthena dhīmatā ।। iccheyaṃ sukhinī draṣṭuṃ tvayā vīreṇa saṃgatā ।। evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ vāhaṃ tvayā saha ।।
tvayā mama naravyāghra nāhaṃ tam api rocaye ।। vane nivatsyāmi yathā pitur gṛhe tavaiva pādāv upagṛhya saṃmatā ।। nayasva māṃ sādhu kuruṣva yācanāṃ na te mayāto gurutā bhaviṣyati ।। uvāca caināṃ bahu saṃnivartane vane nivāsasya ca duḥkhitāṃ prati ।।
nivartanārthe dharmātmā vākyam etad uvāca ha ।। ihācara svadharmaṃ tvaṃ mā yathā manasaḥ sukham ।। vane doṣā hi bahavo vadatas tān nibodha me ।। bahudoṣaṃ hi kāntāraṃ vanam ity abhidhīyate ।।
sadā sukhaṃ na jānāmi duḥkham eva sadā vanam ।। siṃhānāṃ ninadā duḥkhāḥ śrotuṃ duḥkham ato vanam ।। rātriṣu śramakhinnena tasmād duḥkhataraṃ vanam ।। jaṭābhāraś ca kartavyo valkalāmbaradhāriṇā ।।
bhayāni ca mahānty atra tato duḥkhataraṃ vanam ।। caranti pṛthivīṃ darpād ato duḥkhataraṃ vanam ।। tiṣṭhanty āvṛtya panthānam ato duḥkhataraṃ vanam ।। bādhante nityam abale sarvaṃ duḥkham ato vanam ।।
vane vyākulaśākhāgrās tena duḥkhataraṃ vanam ।। vimṛśann iha paśyāmi bahudoṣataraṃ vanam ।। na tasya sītā vacanaṃ cakāra tat tato abravīd rāmam idaṃ suduḥkhitā ।। prasaktāśrumukhī mandam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
guṇān ity eva tān viddhi tava snehapuraskṛtān ।। tvadviyogena me rāma tyaktavyam iha jīvitam ।। surāṇām īśvaraḥ śakraḥ pradharṣayitum ojasā ।। kāmam evaṃvidhaṃ rāma tvayā mama vidarśitam ।।
purā pitṛgṛhe satyaṃ vastavyaṃ kila me vane ।। vanavāsakṛtotsāhā nityam eva mahābala ।। sā tvayā saha tatrāhaṃ yāsyāmi priya nānyathā ।। kālaś cāyaṃ samutpannaḥ satyavāg bhavatu dvijaḥ ।।
prāpyante niyataṃ vīra puruṣair akṛtātmabhiḥ ।। bhikṣiṇyāḥ sādhuvṛttāyā mama mātur ihāgrataḥ ।। gamanaṃ vanavāsasya kāṅkṣitaṃ hi saha tvayā ।। vanavāsasya śūrasya caryā hi mama rocate ।।
bhartāram anugacchantī bhartā hi mama daivatam ।। śrutir hi śrūyate puṇyā brāhmaṇānāṃ yaśasvinām ।। adbhir dattā svadharmeṇa pretyabhāve api tasya sā ।। nābhirocayase netuṃ tvaṃ māṃ keneha hetunā ।।
netum arhasi kākutstha samānasukhaduḥkhinīm ।। viṣam agniṃ jalaṃ vāham āsthāsye mṛtyukāraṇāt ।। nānumene mahābāhus tāṃ netuṃ vijanaṃ vanam ।। snāpayantīva gām uṣṇair aśrubhir nayanacyutaiḥ ।।
krodhāviṣṭāṃ tu vaidehīṃ kākutstho bahv asāntvayat ।। vanavāsanimittāya bhartāram idam abravīt ।। praṇayāc cābhimānāc ca paricikṣepa rāghavam ।। rāma jāmātaraṃ prāpya striyaṃ puruṣavigraham ।।
tejo nāsti paraṃ rāme tapatīva divākare ।। yat parityaktukāmas tvaṃ mām ananyaparāyaṇām ।। sāvitrīm iva māṃ viddhi tvam ātmavaśavartinīm ।। tvayā rāghava gaccheyaṃ yathānyā kulapāṃsanī ।।
śailūṣa iva māṃ rāma parebhyo dātum icchasi ।। tapo vā yadi vāraṇyaṃ svargo vā syāt saha tvayā ।। pṛṣṭhatas tava gacchantyā vihāraśayaneṣv api ।। tūlājinasamasparśā mārge mama saha tvayā ।।
rajo ramaṇa tan manye parārdhyam iva candanam ।। kuthāstaraṇatalpeṣu kiṃ syāt sukhataraṃ tataḥ ।। dāsyasi svayam āhṛtya tan me amṛtarasopamam ।। ārtavāny upabhuñjānā puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ।।
matkṛte na ca te śoko na bhaviṣyāmi durbharā ।। iti jānan parāṃ prītiṃ gaccha rāma mayā saha ।। viṣam adyaiva pāsyāmi mā viśaṃ dviṣatāṃ vaśam ।। ujjhitāyās tvayā nātha tadaiva maraṇaṃ varam ।।
kiṃ punar daśavarṣāṇi trīṇi caikaṃ ca duḥkhitā ।। cukrośa patim āyastā bhṛśam āliṅgya sasvaram ।। cirasaṃniyataṃ bāṣpaṃ mumocāgnim ivāraṇiḥ ।। netrābhyāṃ parisusrāva paṅkajābhyām ivodakam ।।
uvāca vacanaṃ rāmaḥ pariviśvāsayaṃs tadā ।। na hi me asti bhayaṃ kiṃcit svayambhor iva sarvataḥ ।। vāsaṃ na rocaye araṇye śaktimān api rakṣaṇe ।। na vihātuṃ mayā śakyā kīrtir ātmavatā yathā ।।
taṃ cāham anuvarte adya yathā sūryaṃ suvarcalā ।। ataś cājñāṃ vyatikramya nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe ।। anugacchasva māṃ bhīru sahadharmacarī bhava ।। dehi cāśaṃsamānebhyaḥ saṃtvarasva ca māciram ।।
kṣipraṃ pramuditā devī dātum evopacakrame ।। dhanāni ratnāni ca dātum aṅganā pracakrame dharmabhṛtāṃ manasvinī ।। sthitaṃ prāggāminaṃ vīraṃ yācamānaṃ kṛtāñjalim ।। ko bhariṣyati kausalyāṃ sumitrāṃ vā yaśasvinīm ।।
sa kāmapāśaparyasto mahātejā mahīpatiḥ ।। duḥkhitānāṃ sapatnīnāṃ na kariṣyati śobhanam ।। pratyuvāca tadā rāmaṃ vākyajño vākyakovidam ।। kausalyāṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca prayato nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
yasyāḥ sahasraṃ grāmāṇāṃ samprāptam upajīvanam ।। agratas te gamiṣyāmi panthānam anudarśayan ।। vanyāni yāni cānyāni svāhārāṇi tapasvinām ।। ahaṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi jāgrataḥ svapataś ca te ।।
vrajāpṛcchasva saumitre sarvam eva suhṛjjanam ।। janakasya mahāyajñe dhanuṣī raudradarśane ।। ādityavimalau cobhau khaḍgau hemapariṣkṛtau ।। sa tvam āyudham ādāya kṣipram āvraja lakṣmaṇa ।।
ikṣvākugurum āmantrya jagrāhāyudham uttamam ।। rāmāya darśayāmāsa saumitriḥ sarvam āyudham ।। kāle tvam āgataḥ saumya kāṅkṣite mama lakṣmaṇa ।। brāhmaṇebhyas tapasvibhyas tvayā saha paraṃtapa ।।
teṣām api ca me bhūyaḥ sarveṣāṃ copajīvinām ।। abhiprayāsyāmi vanaṃ samastān abhyarcya śiṣṭān aparān dvijātīn ।। gatvā sa praviveśāśu suyajñasya niveśanam ।। sakhe abhyāgaccha paśya tvaṃ veśma duṣkarakāriṇaḥ ।।
juṣṭaṃ tat prāviśal lakṣmyā ramyaṃ rāmaniveśanam ।। suyajñam abhicakrāma rāghavo agnim ivārcitam ।। sahemasūtrair maṇibhiḥ keyūrair valayair api ।। suyajñaṃ sa tadovāca rāmaḥ sītāpracoditaḥ ।।
raśanāṃ cādhunā sītā dātum icchati te sakhe ।। tam apīcchati vaidehī pratiṣṭhāpayituṃ tvayi ।। taṃ te gajasahasreṇa dadāmi dvijapuṃgava ।। rāmalakṣmaṇasītānāṃ prayuyojāśiṣaḥ śivāḥ ।।
saumitriṃ tam uvācedaṃ brahmeva tridaśeśvaram ।। arcayāhūya saumitre ratnaiḥ sasyam ivāmbubhiḥ ।। ācāryas taittirīyāṇām abhirūpaś ca vedavit ।। kauśeyāni ca vastrāṇi yāvat tuṣyati sa dvijaḥ ।।
toṣayainaṃ mahārhaiś ca ratnair vastrair dhanais tathā ।। vyañjanārthaṃ ca saumitre gosahasram upākuru ।। yathoktaṃ brāhmaṇendrāṇām adadād dhanado yathā ।। sampradāya bahu dravyam ekaikasyopajīvinaḥ ।।
aśūnyaṃ kāryam ekaikaṃ yāvadāgamanaṃ mama ।। tato asya dhanam ājahruḥ sarvam evopajīvinaḥ ।। dvijebhyo bālavṛddhebhyaḥ kṛpaṇebhyo abhyadāpayat ।। ā pañcamāyāḥ kakṣyāyā nainaṃ kaścid avārayat ।।
uñchavṛttir vane nityaṃ pratyavekṣasva mām iti ।। parikṣipasi daṇḍena yāvat tāvad avāpsyasi ।। āvidhya daṇḍaṃ cikṣepa sarvaprāṇena vegitaḥ ।। manyur na khalu kartavyaḥ parihāso hy ayaṃ mama ।।
yaśobalaprītisukhopabṛṃhiṇīs tad āśiṣaḥ pratyavadan mahātmanaḥ ।। jagmatuḥ pitaraṃ draṣṭuṃ sītayā saha rāghavau ।। mālādāmabhir āsakte sītayā samalaṃkṛte ।। adhiruhya janaḥ śrīmān udāsīno vyalokayat ।।
āruhya tasmāt prāsādān dīnāḥ paśyanti rāghavam ।। ūcur bahuvidhā vācaḥ śokopahatacetasaḥ ।। tam ekaṃ sītayā sārdham anuyāti sma lakṣmaṇaḥ ।। necchaty evānṛtaṃ kartuṃ pitaraṃ dharmagauravāt ।।
tām adya sītāṃ paśyanti rājamārgagatā janāḥ ।। varṣam uṣṇaṃ ca śītaṃ ca neṣyaty āśu vivarṇatām ।। na hi rājā priyaṃ putraṃ vivāsayitum arhati ।। kiṃ punar yasya loko ayaṃ jito vṛttena kevalam ।।
rāghavaṃ śobhayanty ete ṣaḍguṇāḥ puruṣottamam ।। audakānīva sattvāni grīṣme salilasaṃkṣayāt ।। mūlasyevopaghātena vṛkṣaḥ puṣpaphalopagaḥ ।। gacchantam anugacchāmo yena gacchati rāghavaḥ ।।
ekaduḥkhasukhā rāmam anugacchāma dhārmikam ।। upāttadhanadhānyāni hṛtasārāṇi sarvaśaḥ ।। asmattyaktāni veśmāni kaikeyī pratipadyatām ।। asmābhiś ca parityaktaṃ puraṃ saṃpadyatāṃ vanam ।।
asmattyaktaṃ prapadyantāṃ sevyamānaṃ tyajantu ca ।। śuśrāva rāmaḥ śrutvā ca na vicakre asya mānasam ।। jagāma rāmaḥ pitaraṃ didṛkṣuḥ pitur nideśaṃ vidhivac cikīrṣuḥ ।। vyatiṣṭhata prekṣya tadā sumantraṃ pitur mahātmā pratihāraṇārtham ।।
sa rāghavaḥ prekṣya sumantram abravīn nivedayasvāgamanaṃ nṛpāya me ।। praviśya nṛpatiṃ sūto niḥśvasantaṃ dadarśa ha ।। rāmam evānuśocantaṃ sūtaḥ prāñjalir āsadat ।। brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dattvā sarvaṃ caivopajīvinām ।।
sarvān suhṛda āpṛcchya tvām idānīṃ didṛkṣate ।। vṛtaṃ rājaguṇaiḥ sarvair ādityam iva raśmibhiḥ ।। ākāśa iva niṣpaṅko narendraḥ pratyuvāca tam ।। dāraiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvair draṣṭum icchāmi rāghavam ।।
āryo hvayati vo rājā gamyatāṃ tatra māciram ।। pracakramus tad bhavanaṃ bhartur ājñāya śāsanam ।। kausalyāṃ parivāryātha śanair jagmur dhṛtavratāḥ ।। uvāca rājā taṃ sūtaṃ sumantrānaya me sutam ।।
jagāmābhimukhas tūrṇaṃ sakāśaṃ jagatīpateḥ ।। utpapātāsanāt tūrṇam ārtaḥ strījanasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। tam asaṃprāpya duḥkhārtaḥ papāta bhuvi mūrchitaḥ ।। visaṃjñam iva duḥkhena saśokaṃ nṛpatiṃ tadā ।।
hā hā rāmeti sahasā bhūṣaṇadhvanimūrchitaḥ ।। paryaṅke sītayā sārdhaṃ rudantaḥ samaveśayan ।। uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā śokārṇavapariplutam ।। prasthitaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ paśya tvaṃ kuśalena mām ।।
kāraṇair bahubhis tathyair vāryamāṇau na cecchataḥ ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ māṃ ca sītāṃ ca prajāpatir iva prajāḥ ।। uvāca rājā samprekṣya vanavāsāya rāghavam ।। ayodhyāyās tvam evādya bhava rājā nigṛhya mām ।।
pratyuvācāñjaliṃ kṛtvā pitaraṃ vākyakovidaḥ ।। ahaṃ tv araṇye vatsyāmi na me kāryaṃ tvayānṛtam ।। gacchasvāriṣṭam avyagraḥ panthānam akutobhayam ।। tarpitaḥ sarvakāmais tvaṃ śvaḥkāle sādhayiṣyasi ।।
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā dīno vacanam abravīt ।। apakramaṇam evātaḥ sarvakāmair ahaṃ vṛṇe ।। mayā visṛṣṭā vasudhā bharatāya pradīyatām ।। na hi kṣubhyati durdharṣaḥ samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ ।।
tvām ahaṃ satyam icchāmi nānṛtaṃ puruṣarṣabha ।। ahaṃ nideśaṃ bhavato anupālayan vanaṃ gamiṣyāmi cirāya sevitum ।। śivāṃ susīmām anuśāstu kevalaṃ tvayā yad uktaṃ nṛpate yathāstu tat ।। yathā nideśe tava śiṣṭasaṃmate vyapaitu duḥkhaṃ tava matkṛte anagha ।।
na jīvitaṃ tvām anṛtena yojayan vṛṇīya satyaṃ vratam astu te tathā ।। vanaṃ praviśyaiva vicitrapādapaṃ sukhī bhaviṣyāmi tavāstu nirvṛtiḥ ।। sabāṣpam atiniḥśvasya jagādedaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। rāghavasyānuyātrārthaṃ kṣipraṃ pratividhīyatām ।।
śobhayantu kumārasya vāhinīṃ suprasāritāḥ ।। teṣāṃ bahuvidhaṃ dattvā tān apy atra niyojaya ।। nadīś ca vividhāḥ paśyan na rājyaṃ saṃsmariṣyati ।। tau rāmam anugacchetāṃ vasantaṃ nirjane vane ।।
ṛṣibhiś ca samāgamya pravatsyati sukhaṃ vane ।। sarvakāmaiḥ punaḥ śrīmān rāmaḥ saṃsādhyatām iti ।। mukhaṃ cāpy agamacchoṣaṃ svaraś cāpi nyarudhyata ।। nirāsvādyatamaṃ śūnyaṃ bharato nābhipatsyate ।।
vahantaṃ kiṃ tudasi māṃ niyujya dhuri māhite ।। asamañja iti khyātaṃ tathāyaṃ gantum arhati ।। vrīḍitaś ca janaḥ sarvaḥ sā ca tan nāvabudhyata ।। śucir bahumato rājñaḥ kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।।
sarayvāḥ prakṣipann apsu ramate tena durmatiḥ ।। asamañjaṃ vṛṇīṣvaikam asmān vā rāṣṭravardhana ।। tāś cāpi rājñā saṃpṛṣṭā vākyaṃ prakṛtayo abruvan ।। sarayvāṃ prakṣipan maurkhyād atulāṃ prītim aśnute ।।
taṃ tatyājāhitaṃ putraṃ tāsāṃ priyacikīrṣayā ।। rāmaḥ kim akarot pāpaṃ yenaivam uparudhyate ।। śokopahatayā vācā kaikeyīm idam abravīt ।। sahaiva rājñā bharatena ca tvaṃ yathā sukhaṃ bhuṅkṣva cirāya rājyam ।।
anvabhāṣata vākyaṃ tu vinayajño vinītavat ।। kiṃ kāryam anuyātreṇa tyaktasaṅgasya sarvataḥ ।। rajjusnehena kiṃ tasya tyajataḥ kuñjarottamam ।। sarvāṇy evānujānāmi cīrāṇy evānayantu me ।।
caturdaśa vane vāsaṃ varṣāṇi vasato mama ।। uvāca paridhatsveti janaughe nirapatrapā ।। sūkṣmavastram avakṣipya munivastrāṇy avasta ha ।। tāpasāc chādane caiva jagrāha pitur agrataḥ ।।
samīkṣya cīraṃ saṃtrastā pṛṣatī vāgurām iva ।। kathaṃ nu cīraṃ badhnanti munayo vanavāsinaḥ ।। tasthau hy akuśalā tatra vrīḍitā janakātmajā ।। cīraṃ babandha sītāyāḥ kauśeyasyopari svayam ।।
pracukrośa janaḥ sarvo dhik tvāṃ daśarathaṃ tv iti ।। kaikeyi kuśacīreṇa na sītā gantum arhati ।। kim ebhiḥ kṛpaṇair bhūyaḥ pātakair api te kṛtaiḥ ।। avākśirasam āsīnam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
vṛddhā cākṣudraśīlā ca na ca tvāṃ devagarhite ।। adṛṣṭapūrvavyasanāṃ bhūyaḥ saṃmantum arhasi ।। yathā vanasthe mayi śokakarśitā na jīvitaṃ nyasya yamakṣayaṃ vrajet ।। samīkṣya saha bhāryābhī rājā vigatacetanaḥ ।।
na cainam abhisamprekṣya pratyabhāṣata durmanāḥ ।। vilalāpa mahābāhū rāmam evānucintayan ।। prāṇino hiṃsitā vāpi tasmād idam upasthitam ।। kaikeyyā kliśyamānasya mṛtyur mama na vidyate ।।
vihāya vasane sūkṣme tāpasācchādam ātmajam ।। svārthe prayatamānāyāḥ saṃśritya nikṛtiṃ tv imām ।। rāmeti sakṛd evoktvā vyāhartuṃ na śaśāka ha ।। netrābhyām aśrupūrṇābhyāṃ sumantram idam abravīt ।।
prāpayainaṃ mahābhāgam ito janapadāt param ।। pitrā mātrā ca yat sādhur vīro nirvāsyate vanam ।। yojayitvāyayau tatra ratham aśvair alaṃkṛtam ।। ācacakṣe añjaliṃ kṛtvā yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ ।।
uvāca deśakālajño niścitaṃ sarvataḥ śuci ।। varṣāṇy etāni saṃkhyāya vaidehyāḥ kṣipram ānaya ।। prāyacchat sarvam āhṛtya sītāyai kṣipram eva tat ।। bhūṣayāmāsa gātrāṇi tair vicitrair vibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
udyato aṃśumataḥ kāle khaṃ prabheva vivasvataḥ ।। anācarantīṃ kṛpaṇaṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya maithilīm ।। bhartāraṃ nānumanyante vinipātagataṃ striyaḥ ।। tava daivatam astv eṣa nirdhanaḥ sadhano api vā ।।
kṛtāñjalir uvācedaṃ śvaśrūm abhimukhe sthitā ।। abhijñāsmi yathā bhartur vartitavyaṃ śrutaṃ ca me ।। dharmād vicalituṃ nāham alaṃ candrād iva prabhā ।। nāpatiḥ sukham edhate yā syād api śatātmajā ।।
amitasya hi dātāraṃ bhartāraṃ kā na pūjayet ।। ārye kim avamanyeyaṃ strīṇāṃ bhartā hi daivatam ।। śuddhasattvā mumocāśru sahasā duḥkhaharṣajam ।। rāmaḥ paramadharmajño mātaraṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
kṣayo hi vanavāsasya kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati ।। sā samagram iha prāptaṃ māṃ drakṣyasi suhṛdvṛtam ।। trayaḥ śataśatārdhā hi dadarśāvekṣya mātaraḥ ।। dharmayuktam idaṃ vākyaṃ nijagāda kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
tan me samanujānīta sarvāś cāmantrayāmi vaḥ ।। mānavendrasya bhāryāṇām evaṃ vadati rāghave ।। vilapitaparidevanākulaṃ vyasanagataṃ tad abhūt suduḥkhitam ।। upasaṃgṛhya rājānaṃ cakrur dīnāḥ pradakṣiṇam ।।
rāghavaḥ śokasaṃmūḍho jananīm abhyavādayat ।। atha mātuḥ sumitrāyā jagrāha caraṇau punaḥ ।। hitakāmā mahābāhuṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya lakṣmaṇam ।। rāme pramādaṃ mā kārṣīḥ putra bhrātari gacchati ।।
eṣa loke satāṃ dharmo yaj jyeṣṭhavaśago bhavet ।। dānaṃ dīkṣā ca yajñeṣu tanutyāgo mṛdheṣu ca ।। ayodhyām aṭavīṃ viddhi gaccha tāta yathāsukham ।। vinīto vinayajñaś ca mātalir vāsavaṃ yathā ।।
kṣipraṃ tvāṃ prāpayiṣyāmi yatra māṃ rāma vakṣyasi ।। tāny upakramitavyāni yāni devyāsi coditaḥ ।। āruroha varārohā kṛtvālaṃkāram ātmanaḥ ।। rathopasthe pratinyasya sacarmakaṭhinaṃ ca tat ।।
sumantraḥ saṃmatān aśvān vāyuvegasamāñ jave ।। babhūva nagare mūrchā balamūrchā janasya ca ।। hayaśiñjitanirghoṣaṃ puram āsīn mahāsvanam ।। rāmam evābhidudrāva gharmārtaḥ salilaṃ yathā ।।
bāṣpapūrṇamukhāḥ sarve tam ūcur bhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ ।। mukhaṃ drakṣyāmi rāmasya durdarśaṃ no bhaviṣyati ।। yad devagarbhapratime vanaṃ yāti na bhidyate ।। na jahāti ratā dharme merum arkaprabhā yathā ।।
bhrātaraṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ yas tvaṃ paricariṣyasi ।। evaṃ vadantas te soḍhuṃ na śekur bāṣpam āgatam ।। nirjagāma priyaṃ putraṃ drakṣyāmīti bruvan gṛhāt ।। yathā nādaḥ kareṇūnāṃ baddhe mahati kuñjare ।।
paripūrṇaḥ śaśī kāle graheṇopapluto yathā ।। narāṇāṃ prekṣya rājānaṃ sīdantaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitam ।। antaḥpuraṃ samṛddhaṃ ca krośantaṃ paryadevayan ।। dharmapāśena saṃkṣiptaḥ prakāśaṃ nābhyudaikṣata ।।
dṛṣṭvā saṃcodayāmāsa śīghraṃ yāhīti sārathim ।। mātuś ca sahituṃ śaktas totrārdita iva dvipaḥ ।। asakṛt praikṣata tadā nṛtyantīm iva mātaram ।। sumantrasya babhūvātmā cakrayor iva cāntarā ।।
ciraṃ duḥkhasya pāpiṣṭham iti rāmas tam abravīt ।। vrajato api hayāñ śīghraṃ codayāmāsa sārathiḥ ।। manasāpy aśruvegaiś ca na nyavartata mānuṣam ।। ity amātyā mahārājam ūcur daśarathaṃ vacaḥ ।।
niśamya rājā kṛpaṇaḥ sabhāryo vyavasthitas taṃ sutam īkṣamāṇaḥ ।। ārtaśabdo hi saṃjajñe strīṇām antaḥpure mahān ।। yo gatiḥ śaraṇaṃ cāsīt sa nāthaḥ kva nu gacchati ।। kruddhān prasādayan sarvān samaduḥkhaḥ kva gacchati ।।
tathā yo vartate asmāsu mahātmā kva nu gacchati ।। paritrātā janasyāsya jagataḥ kva nu gacchati ।। dharmyaṃ satyavrataṃ rāmaṃ vanavāse pravatsyati ।। ruruduś caiva duḥkhārtāḥ sasvaraṃ ca vicukruśuḥ ।।
putraśokābhisaṃtaptaḥ śrutvā cāsīt suduḥkhitaḥ ।। vyasṛjan kavalān nāgā gāvo vatsān na pāyayan ।। dāruṇāḥ somam abhyetya grahāḥ sarve vyavasthitāḥ ।। viśākhāś ca sadhūmāś ca nabhasi pracakāśire ।।
āhāre vā vihāre vā na kaścid akaron manaḥ ।। na hṛṣṭo lakṣyate kaścit sarvaḥ śokaparāyaṇaḥ ।। na sūryas tapate lokaṃ sarvaṃ paryākulaṃ jagat ।। sarve sarvaṃ parityajya rāmam evānvacintayan ।।
śokabhāreṇa cākrāntāḥ śayanaṃ na jahus tadā ।। cacāla ghoraṃ bhayabhārapīḍitā sanāgayodhāśvagaṇā nanāda ca ।। naivekṣvākuvaras tāvat saṃjahārātmacakṣuṣī ।। tāvad vyavardhatevāsya dharaṇyāṃ putradarśane ।।
tadārtaś ca viṣaṇṇaś ca papāta dharaṇītale ।। vāmaṃ cāsyānvagāt pārśvaṃ kaikeyī bharatapriyā ।। uvāca rājā kaikeyīṃ samīkṣya vyathitendriyaḥ ।। na hi tvāṃ draṣṭum icchāmi na bhāryā na ca bāndhavī ।।
kevalārthaparāṃ hi tvāṃ tyaktadharmāṃ tyajāmy aham ।। anujānāmi tat sarvam asmiṃl loke paratra ca ।। yan me sa dadyāt pitrarthaṃ mā mā tad dattam āgamat ।। nyavartata tadā devī kausalyā śokakarśitā ।।
anvatapyata dharmātmā putraṃ saṃcintya tāpasam ।। rājño nātibabhau rūpaṃ grastasyāṃśumato yathā ।। nagarāntam anuprāptaṃ buddhvā putram athābravīt ।। padāni pathi dṛśyante sa mahātmā na dṛśyate ।।
kāṣṭhaṃ vā yadi vāśmānam upadhāya śayiṣyate ।। viniḥśvasan prasravaṇāt kareṇūnām ivarṣabhaḥ ।। rāmam utthāya gacchantaṃ lokanātham anāthavat ।। na hi taṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ vinā jīvitum utsahe ।।
apasnāta ivāriṣṭaṃ praviveśa purottamam ।। klāntadurbaladuḥkhārtāṃ nātyākīrṇamahāpathām ।। vilapan prāviśad rājā gṛhaṃ sūrya ivāmbudam ।। rāmeṇa rahitaṃ veśma vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca ।।
iti bruvantaṃ rājānam anayan dvāradarśinaḥ ।। adhiruhyāpi śayanaṃ babhūva lulitaṃ manaḥ ।। uccaiḥ svareṇa cukrośa hā rāghava jahāsi mām ।। pariṣvajanto ye rāmaṃ drakṣyanti punar āgatam ।।
rāmaṃ me anugatā dṛṣṭir adyāpi na nivartate ।। upopaviśyādhikam ārtarūpā viniḥśvasantī vilalāpa kṛcchram ।। kausalyā putraśokārtā tam uvāca mahīpatim ।। vicariṣyati kaikeyī nirmukteva hi pannagī ।।
trāsayiṣyati māṃ bhūyo duṣṭāhir iva veśmani ।। kāmakāro varaṃ dātum api dāsaṃ mamātmajam ।। pradiṣṭo rakṣasāṃ bhāgaḥ parvaṇīvāhitāgninā ।। vanam āviśate nūnaṃ sabhāryaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
tyaktānāṃ vanavāsāya kā nv avasthā bhaviṣyati ।। kathaṃ vatsyanti kṛpaṇāḥ phalamūlaiḥ kṛtāśanāḥ ।। sabhāryaṃ yat saha bhrātrā paśyeyam iha rāghavam ।। yaśasvinī hṛṣṭajanā sūcchritadhvajamālinī ।।
nandiṣyati purī hṛṣṭā samudra iva parvaṇi ।। puraskṛtya rathe sītāṃ vṛṣabho govadhūm iva ।। lājair avakariṣyanti praviśantāv ariṃdamau ।। pradiśantyaḥ purīṃ hṛṣṭāḥ kariṣyanti pradakṣiṇam ।।
abhyupaiṣyati dharmajñas trivarṣa iva māṃ lalan ।। pātu kāmeṣu vatseṣu mātṝṇāṃ śātitāḥ stanāḥ ।। kaikeyyā puruṣavyāghra bālavatseva gaur balāt ।। ekaputrā vinā putram ahaṃ jīvitum utsahe ।।
apaśyantyāḥ priyaṃ putraṃ mahābāhuṃ mahābalam ।। mahīm imāṃ raśmibhir uttamaprabho yathā nidāghe bhagavān divākaraḥ ।। idaṃ dharme sthitā dharmyaṃ sumitrā vākyam abravīt ।। kiṃ te vilapitenaivaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ ruditena vā ।।
sādhu kurvan mahātmānaṃ pitaraṃ satyavādinām ।। rāmo dharme sthitaḥ śreṣṭho na sa śocyaḥ kadācana ।। dayāvān sarvabhūteṣu lābhas tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। anugacchati vaidehī dharmātmānaṃ tavātmajam ।।
damasatyavrataparaḥ kiṃ na prāptas tavātmajaḥ ।। na gātram aṃśubhiḥ sūryaḥ saṃtāpayitum arhati ।। rāghavaṃ yuktaśītoṣṇaḥ seviṣyati sukho anilaḥ ।। raśmibhiḥ saṃspṛśañ śītaiś candramā hlādayiṣyati ।।
dānavendraṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā timidhvajasutaṃ raṇe ।। kṣipraṃ tisṛbhir etābhiḥ saha rāmo abhiṣekṣyate ।। samutsrakṣyasi netrābhyāṃ kṣipram ānandajaṃ payaḥ ।। mudāśru mokṣyase kṣipraṃ meghalekheva vārṣikī ।।
karābhyāṃ mṛdupīnābhyāṃ caraṇau pīḍayiṣyati ।। sadyaḥ śarīre vinanāśa śokaḥ śaradgato megha ivālpatoyaḥ ।। anujagmuḥ prayāntaṃ taṃ vanavāsāya mānavāḥ ।। naiva te saṃnyavartanta rāmasyānugatā ratham ।।
babhūva guṇasampannaḥ pūrṇacandra iva priyaḥ ।। kurvāṇaḥ pitaraṃ satyaṃ vanam evānvapadyata ।। uvāca rāmaḥ snehena tāḥ prajāḥ svāḥ prajā iva ।। matpriyārthaṃ viśeṣeṇa bharate sā niveśyatām ।।
kariṣyati yathāvad vaḥ priyāṇi ca hitāni ca ।। anurūpaḥ sa vo bhartā bhaviṣyati bhayāpahaḥ ।। api cāpi mayā śiṣṭaiḥ kāryaṃ vo bhartṛśāsanam ।। mahārājas tathā kāryo mama priyacikīrṣayā ।।
tathā tathā prakṛtayo rāmaṃ patim akāmayan ।। cakarṣeva guṇair baddhvā janaṃ punar ivāsanam ।। vayaḥprakampaśiraso dūrād ūcur idaṃ vacaḥ ।। upavāhyas tu vo bhartā nāpavāhyaḥ purād vanam ।।
avekṣya sahasā rāmo rathād avatatāra ha ।। saṃnikṛṣṭapadanyāso rāmo vanaparāyaṇaḥ ।। na śaśāka ghṛṇācakṣuḥ parimoktuṃ rathena saḥ ।। ūcuḥ paramasaṃtaptā rāmaṃ vākyam idaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
dvijaskandhādhirūḍhās tvām agnayo apy anuyānty amī ।। pṛṣṭhato anuprayātāni haṃsān iva jalātyaye ।। ebhiś chāyāṃ kariṣyāmaḥ svaiś chattrair vājapeyikaiḥ ।। tvatkṛte sā kṛtā vatsa vanavāsānusāriṇī ।।
vatsyanty api gṛheṣv eva dārāś cāritrarakṣitāḥ ।। tvayi dharmavyapekṣe tu kiṃ syād dharmam avekṣitum ।। śirobhir nibhṛtācāra mahīpatanapāṃsulaiḥ ।। teṣāṃ samāptir āyattā tava vatsa nivartane ।।
yācamāneṣu teṣu tvaṃ bhaktiṃ bhakteṣu darśaya ।। unnatā vāyuvegena vikrośantīva pādapāḥ ।। pakṣiṇo api prayācante sarvabhūtānukampinam ।। dadṛśe tamasā tatra vārayantīva rāghavam ।।
sītām udvīkṣya saumitrim idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। vanavāsasya bhadraṃ te sa notkaṇṭhitum arhasi ।। yathānilayam āyadbhir nilīnāni mṛgadvijaiḥ ।। sastrīpuṃsā gatān asmāñ śociṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
dharmārthakāmasahitair vākyair āśvāsayiṣyati ।। nānuśocāmi pitaraṃ mātaraṃ cāpi lakṣmaṇa ।। anveṣṭavyā hi vaidehyā rakṣaṇārthe sahāyatā ।। etaddhi rocate mahyaṃ vanye api vividhe sati ।।
apramattas tvam aśveṣu bhava saumyety uvāca ha ।। prabhūtayavasān kṛtvā babhūva pratyanantaraḥ ।। rāmasya śayanaṃ cakre sūtaḥ saumitriṇā saha ।। rāmaḥ saumitriṇā sārdhaṃ sabhāryaḥ saṃviveśa ha ।।
kathayāmāsa sūtāya rāmasya vividhān guṇān ।। sūtasya tamasātīre rāmasya bruvato guṇān ।। avasat tatra tāṃ rātriṃ rāmaḥ prakṛtibhiḥ saha ।। abravīd bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ puṇyalakṣaṇam ।।
vṛkṣamūleṣu saṃsuptān paśya lakṣmaṇa sāmpratam ।। api prāṇān asiṣyanti na tu tyakṣyanti niścayam ।। ratham āruhya gacchāmaḥ panthānam akutobhayam ।। svapeyur anuraktā māṃ vṛkṣamūlāni saṃśritāḥ ।।
na tu khalv ātmanā yojyā duḥkhena puravāsinaḥ ।। rocate me mahāprājña kṣipram āruhyatām iti ।। yojayitvātha rāmāya prāñjaliḥ pratyavedayat ।। udaṅmukhaḥ prayāhi tvaṃ ratham āsthāya sārathe ।।
yathā na vidyuḥ paurā māṃ tathā kuru samāhitaḥ ।। pratyāgamya ca rāmasya syandanaṃ pratyavedayat ।। śīghragām ākulāvartāṃ tamasām ataran nadīm ।। prāpadyata mahāmārgam abhayaṃ bhayadarśinām ।।
śokopahataniśceṣṭā babhūvur hatacetasaḥ ।। ālokam api rāmasya na paśyanti sma duḥkhitāḥ ।। mārganāśād viṣādena mahatā samabhiplutaḥ ।। kim idaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmo daivenopahatā iti ।।
ayodhyām agaman sarve purīṃ vyathitasajjanām ।। udgatānīva sattvāni babhūvur amanasvinām ।। aśrūṇi mumucuḥ sarve bāṣpeṇa pihitānanāḥ ।। na cāśobhanta paṇyāni nāpacan gṛhamedhinaḥ ।।
putraṃ prathamajaṃ labdhvā jananī nābhyanandata ।। vyagarhayanta duḥkhārtā vāgbhis totrair iva dvipān ।। putrair vā kiṃ sukhair vāpi ye na paśyanti rāghavam ।। yo anugacchati kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ paricaran vane ।।
yeṣu snāsyati kākutstho vigāhya salilaṃ śuci ।। āpagāś ca mahānūpāḥ sānumantaś ca parvatāḥ ।। priyātithim iva prāptaṃ nainaṃ śakṣyanty anarcitum ।। darśayiṣyanty anukrośād girayo rāmam āgatam ।।
pādapāḥ parvatāgreṣu ramayiṣyanti rāghavam ।। sa hi śūro mahābāhuḥ putro daśarathasya ca ।। sa hi nātho janasyāsya sa gatiḥ sa parāyaṇam ।। iti paurastriyo bhartṝn duḥkhārtās tat tad abruvan ।।
sītā nārījanasyāsya yogakṣemaṃ kariṣyati ।। saṃprīyetāmanojñena vāsena hṛtacetasā ।। na hi no jīvitenārthaḥ kutaḥ putraiḥ kuto dhanaiḥ ।। kaṃ sā parihared anyaṃ kaikeyī kulapāṃsanī ।।
jīvantyā jātu jīvantyaḥ putrair api śapāmahe ।। kas tāṃ prāpya sukhaṃ jīved adharmyāṃ duṣṭacāriṇīm ।। mṛte daśarathe vyaktaṃ vilopas tadanantaram ।। rāghavaṃ vānugacchadhvam aśrutiṃ vāpi gacchata ।।
bharate saṃnisṛṣṭāḥ smaḥ saunike paśavo yathā ।। cukruśur bhṛśasaṃtaptā mṛtyor iva bhayāgame ।। vilapya dīnā rurudur vicetasaḥ sutair hi tāsām adhiko hi so abhavat ।। jagāma puruṣavyāghraḥ pitur ājñām anusmaran ।।
upāsya sa śivāṃ saṃdhyāṃ viṣayāntaṃ vyagāhata ।। paśyann atiyayau śīghraṃ śarair iva hayottamaiḥ ।। rājānaṃ dhig daśarathaṃ kāmasya vaśam āgatam ।। tīkṣṇā saṃbhinnamaryādā tīkṣṇe karmaṇi vartate ।।
vanavāse mahāprājñaṃ sānukrośam atandritam ।। śṛṇvann atiyayau vīraḥ kosalān kosaleśvaraḥ ।। uttīryābhimukhaḥ prāyād agastyādhyuṣitāṃ diśam ।। gomatīṃ goyutānūpām atarat sāgaraṃgamām ।।
mayūrahaṃsābhirutāṃ tatāra syandikāṃ nadīm ।। sphītāṃ rāṣṭrāvṛtāṃ rāmo vaidehīm anvadarśayat ।। haṃsamattasvaraḥ śrīmān uvāca puruṣarṣabhaḥ ।। mṛgayāṃ paryaṭiṣyāmi mātrā pitrā ca saṃgataḥ ।।
ratir hy eṣātulā loke rājarṣigaṇasaṃmatā ।। taṃ tam artham abhipretya yayau vākyam udīrayan ।। āsasāda mahābāhuḥ śṛṅgaverapuraṃ prati ।। dadarśa rāghavo gaṅgāṃ puṇyām ṛṣiniṣevitām ।।
śiśumāraiś ca nakraiś ca bhujaṃgaiś ca niṣevitām ।। sumantram abravīt sūtam ihaivādya vasāmahe ।। sumahān iṅgudīvṛkṣo vasāmo atraiva sārathe ।। uktvā tam iṅgudīvṛkṣaṃ tadopayayatur hayaiḥ ।।
rathād avātarat tasmāt sabhāryaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ ।। vṛkṣamūlagataṃ rāmam upatasthe kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। niṣādajātyo balavān sthapatiś ceti viśrutaḥ ।। vṛddhaiḥ parivṛto amātyair jñātibhiś cāpy upāgataḥ ।।
saha saumitriṇā rāmaḥ samāgacchad guhena saḥ ।। yathāyodhyā tathedaṃ te rāma kiṃ karavāṇi te ।। arghyaṃ copānayat kṣipraṃ vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha ।। vayaṃ preṣyā bhavān bhartā sādhu rājyaṃ praśādhi naḥ ।।
śayanāni ca mukhyāni vājināṃ khādanaṃ ca te ।। arcitāś caiva hṛṣṭāś ca bhavatā sarvathā vayam ।। bhujābhyāṃ sādhuvṛttābhyāṃ pīḍayan vākyam abravīt ।। api te kuśalaṃ rāṣṭre mitreṣu ca dhaneṣu ca ।।
sarvaṃ tad anujānāmi na hi varte pratigrahe ।। viddhi praṇihitaṃ dharme tāpasaṃ vanagocaram ।। etāvatātrabhavatā bhaviṣyāmi supūjitaḥ ।। etaiḥ suvihitair aśvair bhaviṣyāmy aham arcitaḥ ।।
guhas tatraiva puruṣāṃs tvaritaṃ dīyatām iti ।। jalam evādade bhojyaṃ lakṣmaṇenāhṛtaṃ svayam ।। sabhāryasya tato abhyetya tasthau vṛkṣam upāśritaḥ ।। anvajāgrat tato rāmam apramatto dhanurdharaḥ ।।
adṛṣṭaduḥkhasya sukhocitasya sā tadā vyatīyāya cireṇa śarvarī ।। guhaḥ saṃtāpasaṃtapto rāghavaṃ vākyam abravīt ।। pratyāśvasihi sādhv asyāṃ rājaputra yathāsukham ।। guptyarthaṃ jāgariṣyāmaḥ kākutsthasya vayaṃ niśām ।।
bravīmy etad ahaṃ satyaṃ satyenaiva ca te śape ।। dharmāvāptiṃ ca vipulām arthāvāptiṃ ca kevalām ।। rakṣiṣyāmi dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sarvato jñātibhiḥ saha ।। caturaṅgaṃ hy api balaṃ sumahat prasahemahi ।।
nātra bhītā vayaṃ sarve dharmam evānupaśyatā ।। śakyā nidrā mayā labdhuṃ jīvitaṃ vā sukhāni vā ।। taṃ paśya sukhasaṃviṣṭaṃ tṛṇeṣu saha sītayā ।। eko daśarathasyaiṣa putraḥ sadṛśalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
vidhavā medinī nūnaṃ kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati ।। nirghoṣoparataṃ tāta manye rājaniveśanam ।। nāśaṃse yadi jīvanti sarve te śarvarīm imām ।। tad duḥkhaṃ yat tu kausalyā vīrasūr vinaśiṣyati ।।
rājavyasanasaṃsṛṣṭā sā purī vinaśiṣyati ।। rājye rāmam anikṣipya pitā me vinaśiṣyati ।। pretakāryeṣu sarveṣu saṃskariṣyanti bhūmipam ।। harmyaprāsādasampannāṃ gaṇikāvaraśobhitām ।।
sarvakalyāṇasampūrṇāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām ।। sukhitā vicariṣyanti rājadhānīṃ pitur mama ।। nivṛtte vanavāse asminn ayodhyāṃ praviśemahi ।। tiṣṭhato rājaputrasya śarvarī sātyavartata ।।
mumoca bāṣpaṃ vyasanābhipīḍito jvarāturo nāga iva vyathāturaḥ ।। uvāca rāmaḥ saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।। asau sukṛṣṇo vihagaḥ kokilas tāta kūjati ।। tarāma jāhnavīṃ saumya śīghragāṃ sāgaraṃgamām ।।
guham āmantrya sūtaṃ ca so atiṣṭhad bhrātur agrataḥ ।। jagmatur yena tau gaṅgāṃ sītayā saha rāghavau ।। kim ahaṃ karavāṇīti sūtaḥ prāñjalir abravīt ।। yānaṃ vihāya padbhyāṃ tu gamiṣyāmo mahāvanam ।।
sumantraḥ puruṣavyāghram aikṣvākam idam abravīt ।। tava sabhrātṛbhāryasya vāsaḥ prākṛtavad vane ।। mārdavārjavayor vāpi tvāṃ ced vyasanam āgatam ।। tvaṃ gatiṃ prāpsyase vīra trīṃl lokāṃs tu jayann iva ।।
kaikeyyā vaśam eṣyāmaḥ pāpāyā duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dūragataṃ rāmaṃ duḥkhārto rurude ciram ।। rāmas tu madhuraṃ vākyaṃ punaḥ punar uvāca tam ।। yathā daśaratho rājā māṃ na śocet tathā kuru ।।
kāmabhārāvasannaś ca tasmād etad bravīmi te ।। kaikeyyāḥ priyakāmārthaṃ kāryaṃ tad avikāṅkṣayā ।। yad eṣāṃ sarvakṛtyeṣu mano na pratihanyate ।। na ca tāmyati duḥkhena sumantra kuru tat tathā ।।
brūyās tvam abhivādyaiva mama hetor idaṃ vacaḥ ।। ayodhyāyāś cyutāś ceti vane vatsyāmaheti vā ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ māṃ ca sītāṃ ca drakṣyasi kṣipram āgatān ।। anyāś ca devīḥ sahitāḥ kaikeyīṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
sītāyā mama cāryasya vacanāl lakṣmaṇasya ca ।। āgataś cāpi bharataḥ sthāpyo nṛpamate pade ।। asmatsaṃtāpajaṃ duḥkhaṃ na tvām abhibhaviṣyati ।। tathā mātṛṣu vartethāḥ sarvāsv evāviśeṣataḥ ।।
tathaiva devī kausalyā mama mātā viśeṣataḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā snehāt kākutstham abravīt ।। bhaktimān iti tat tāvad vākyaṃ tvaṃ kṣantum arhasi ।। tava tāta viyogena putraśokākulām iva ।।
vinā rāmaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidīryetāpi sā purī ।। sūtāvaśeṣaṃ svaṃ sainyaṃ hatavīram ivāhave ।। cintayantyo adya nūnaṃ tvāṃ nirāhārāḥ kṛtāḥ prajāḥ ।। rathasthaṃ māṃ niśāmyaiva kuryuḥ śataguṇaṃ tataḥ ।।
nīto asau mātulakulaṃ saṃtāpaṃ mā kṛthā iti ।। katham apriyam evāhaṃ brūyāṃ satyam idaṃ vacaḥ ।। kathaṃ rathaṃ tvayā hīnaṃ pravakṣyanti hayottamāḥ ।। saratho agniṃ pravekṣyāmi tyaktamātra iha tvayā ।।
rathena pratibādhiṣye tāni sattvāni rāghava ।। āśaṃse tvatkṛtenāhaṃ vanavāsakṛtaṃ sukham ।। prītyābhihitam icchāmi bhava me patyanantaraḥ ।। ayodhyāṃ devalokaṃ vā sarvathā prajahāmy aham ।।
rājadhānī mahendrasya yathā duṣkṛtakarmaṇā ।। paricaryāṃ kariṣyanti prāpsyanti paramāṃ gatim ।। yad anena rathenaiva tvāṃ vaheyaṃ purīṃ punaḥ ।। kṣaṇabhūtāni yāsyanti śataśas tu tato anyathā ।।
bhaktaṃ bhṛtyaṃ sthitaṃ sthityāṃ tvaṃ na māṃ hātum arhasi ।। rāmo bhṛtyānukampī tu sumantram idam abravīt ।। śṛṇu cāpi yadarthaṃ tvāṃ preṣayāmi purīm itaḥ ।। kaikeyī pratyayaṃ gacched iti rāmo vanaṃ gataḥ ।।
rājānaṃ nātiśaṅketa mithyāvādīti dhārmikam ।। bharatārakṣitaṃ sphītaṃ putrarājyam avāpnuyāt ।। saṃdiṣṭaś cāsi yānarthāṃs tāṃs tān brūyās tathātathā ।। jaṭāḥ kṛtvā gamiṣyāmi nyagrodhakṣīram ānaya ।।
lakṣmaṇasyātmanaś caiva rāmas tenākaroj jaṭāḥ ।। aśobhetām ṛṣisamau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। vratam ādiṣṭavān rāmaḥ sahāyaṃ guham abravīt ।। bhavethā guha rājyaṃ hi durārakṣatamaṃ matam ।।
jagāma tūrṇam avyagraḥ sabhāryaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ ।। titīrṣuḥ śīghragāṃ gaṅgām idaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।। sītāṃ cāropayānvakṣaṃ parigṛhya manasvinīm ।। āropya maithilīṃ pūrvam ārurohātmavāṃs tataḥ ।।
tato niṣādādhipatir guho jñātīn acodayat ।। āsthāya nāvaṃ rāmas tu codayāmāsa nāvikān ।। śubhasphyavegābhihatā śīghraṃ salilam atyagāt ।। vaidehī prāñjalir bhūtvā tāṃ nadīm idam abravīt ।।
nideśaṃ pālayatv enaṃ gaṅge tvadabhirakṣitaḥ ।। bhrātrā saha mayā caiva punaḥ pratyāgamiṣyati ।। yakṣye pramuditā gaṅge sarvakāmasamṛddhaye ।। bhāryā codadhirājasya loke asmin sampradṛśyase ।।
prāptarājye naravyāghre śivena punar āgate ।। brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradāsyāmi tava priyacikīrṣayā ।। dakṣiṇā dakṣiṇaṃ tīraṃ kṣipram evābhyupāgamat ।। prātiṣṭhata saha bhrātrā vaidehyā ca paraṃtapaḥ ।।
agrato gaccha saumitre sītā tvām anugacchatu ।। adya duḥkhaṃ tu vaidehī vanavāsasya vetsyati ।। adhvaprakarṣād vinivṛttadṛṣṭir mumoca bāṣpaṃ vyathitas tapasvī ।। ādāya medhyaṃ tvaritaṃ bubhukṣitau vāsāya kāle yayatur vanaspatim ।।
rāmo ramayatāṃ śreṣṭha iti hovāca lakṣmaṇam ।। yā sumantreṇa rahitā tāṃ notkaṇṭhitum arhasi ।। yogakṣemo hi sītāyā vartate lakṣmaṇāvayoḥ ।। upāvartāmahe bhūmāv āstīrya svayam ārjitaiḥ ।।
imāḥ saumitraye rāmo vyājahāra kathāḥ śubhāḥ ।। kṛtakāmā tu kaikeyī tuṣṭā bhavitum arhati ।। api na cyāvayet prāṇān dṛṣṭvā bharatam āgatam ।। kiṃ kariṣyati kāmātmā kaikeyyā vaśam āgataḥ ।।
kāma evārdhadharmābhyāṃ garīyān iti me matiḥ ।। chandānuvartinaṃ putraṃ tāto mām iva lakṣmaṇa ।। muditān kosalān eko yo bhokṣyaty adhirājavat ।। tāte ca vayasātīte mayi cāraṇyam āśrite ।।
evam āpadyate kṣipraṃ rājā daśaratho yathā ।। kaikeyī saumya samprāptā rājyāya bharatasya ca ।। kausalyāṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca samprabādheta matkṛte ।। ayodhyām ita eva tvaṃ kāle praviśa lakṣmaṇa ।।
anāthāyā hi nāthas tvaṃ kausalyāyā bhaviṣyasi ।। paridadyā hi dharmajñe bharate mama mātaram ।। jananyā mama saumitre tad apy etad upasthitam ।। viprāyujyata kausalyā phalakāle dhig astu mām ।।
saumitre yo aham ambāyā dadmi śokam anantakam ।। yasyās tac chrūyate vākyaṃ śuka pādam arer daśa ।। putreṇa kim aputrāyā mayā kāryam ariṃdama ।। śete paramaduḥkhārtā patitā śokasāgare ।।
tareyam iṣubhiḥ kruddho nanu vīryam akāraṇam ।। tena lakṣmaṇa nādyāham ātmānam abhiṣecaye ।। aśrupūrṇamukho rāmo niśi tūṣṇīm upāviśat ।। samudram iva nirvegam āśvāsayata lakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
niṣprabhā tvayi niṣkrānte gatacandreva śarvarī ।। viṣādayasi sītāṃ ca māṃ caiva puruṣarṣabha ।। muhūrtam api jīvāvo jalān matsyāv ivoddhṛtau ।। draṣṭum iccheyam adyāhaṃ svargaṃ vāpi tvayā vinā ।।
samāḥ samastā vidadhe paraṃtapaḥ prapadya dharmaṃ sucirāya rāghavaḥ ।। vimale abhyudite sūrye tasmād deśāt pratasthire ।। jagmus taṃ deśam uddiśya vigāhya sumahad vanam ।। adṛṣṭapūrvān paśyantas tatra tatra yaśasvinaḥ ।।
nivṛttamātre divase rāmaḥ saumitrim abravīt ।। agner bhagavataḥ ketuṃ manye saṃnihito muniḥ ।। tathā hi śrūyate śabdo vāriṇo vārighaṭṭitaḥ ।। bharadvājāśrame caite dṛśyante vividhā drumāḥ ।।
gaṅgāyamunayoḥ saṃdhau prāpatur nilayaṃ muneḥ ।। gatvā muhūrtam adhvānaṃ bharadvājam upāgamat ।। sītayānugatau vīrau dūrād evāvatasthatuḥ ।। rāmaḥ saumitriṇā sārdhaṃ sītayā cābhyavādayat ।।
putrau daśarathasyāvāṃ bhagavan rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। māṃ cānuyātā vijanaṃ tapovanam aninditā ।। ayam anvagamad bhrātā vanam eva dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। dharmam evācariṣyāmas tatra mūlaphalāśanāḥ ।।
upānayata dharmātmā gām arghyam udakaṃ tataḥ ।। rāmam āgatam abhyarcya svāgatenāha taṃ muniḥ ।। bharadvājo abravīd vākyaṃ dharmayuktam idaṃ tadā ।। śrutaṃ tava mayā cedaṃ vivāsanam akāraṇam ।।
puṇyaś ca ramaṇīyaś ca vasatv iha bhavān sukham ।। pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ rāmaḥ sarvahite rataḥ ।। anena kāraṇenāham iha vāsaṃ na rocaye ।। ramate yatra vaidehī sukhārhā janakātmajā ।।
rāghavasya tato vākyam arthagrāhakam abravīt ।। maharṣisevitaḥ puṇyaḥ sarvataḥ sukhadarśanaḥ ।। citrakūṭa iti khyāto gandhamādanasaṃnibhaḥ ।। kalyāṇāni samādhatte na pāpe kurute manaḥ ।।
tapasā divam ārūḍhāḥ kapālaśirasā saha ।। iha vā vanavāsāya vasa rāma mayā saha ।। sabhāryaṃ saha ca bhrātrā pratijagrāha dharmavit ।। prapannā rajanī puṇyā citrāḥ kathayataḥ kathāḥ ।।
uvāca naraśārdūlo muniṃ jvalitatejasam ।। uṣitāḥ smeha vasatim anujānātu no bhavān ।। madhumūlaphalopetaṃ citrakūṭaṃ vrajeti ha ।। vicaranti vanānteṣu tāni drakṣyasi rāghava ।।
mṛgaiś ca mattair bahubhiś ca kuñjaraiḥ suramyam āsādya samāvasāśramam ।। maharṣim abhivādyātha jagmatus taṃ giriṃ prati ।। tataḥ pracakrame vaktuṃ vacanaṃ sa mahāmuniḥ ।। tatra yūyaṃ plavaṃ kṛtvā taratāṃśumatīṃ nadīm ।।
vivṛddhaṃ bahubhir vṛkṣaiḥ śyāmaṃ siddhopasevitam ।। palāśabadarīmiśraṃ rāma vaṃśaiś ca yāmunaiḥ ।। iti panthānam āvedya maharṣiḥ sa nyavartata ।। kṛtapuṇyāḥ sma saumitre munir yan no anukampate ।।
sītām evāgrataḥ kṛtvā kālindīṃ jagmatur nadīm ।। cakāra lakṣmaṇaś chittvā sītāyāḥ sukham āsanam ।। īṣat saṃlajjamānāṃ tām adhyāropayata plavam ।। tīrajair bahubhir vṛkṣaiḥ saṃterur yamunāṃ nadīm ।।
śyāmaṃ nyagrodham āseduḥ śītalaṃ haritacchadam ।। iti sītāñjaliṃ kṛtvā paryagacchad vanaspatim ।। bahūn medhyān mṛgān hatvā ceratur yamunāvane ।। samaṃ nadīvapram upetya saṃmataṃ nivāsam ājagmur adīnadarśanāḥ ।।
prabodhayāmāsa śanair lakṣmaṇaṃ raghunandanaḥ ।। sampratiṣṭhāmahe kālaḥ prasthānasya paraṃtapa ।। jahau nidrāṃ ca tandrīṃ ca prasaktaṃ ca pathi śramam ।। panthānam ṛṣiṇoddiṣṭaṃ citrakūṭasya taṃ yayuḥ ।।
sītāṃ kamalapattrākṣīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। svaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kiṃśukān paśya mālinaḥ śiśirātyaye ।। phalapattrair avanatān nūnaṃ śakṣyāmi jīvitum ।। madhūni madhukārībhiḥ saṃbhṛtāni nage nage ।।
ramaṇīye vanoddeśe puṣpasaṃstarasaṃkaṭe ।। citrakūṭam imaṃ paśya pravṛddhaśikharaṃ girim ।। ramyam āsedatuḥ śailaṃ citrakūṭaṃ manoramam ।। ayaṃ vāso bhavet tāvad atra saumya ramemahi ।।
kuruṣvāvasathaṃ saumya vāse me abhirataṃ manaḥ ।। ājahāra tataś cakre parṇaśālām ariṃdamaḥ ।। aiṇeyaṃ māṃsam āhṛtya śālāṃ yakṣyāmahe vayam ।। atha cikṣepa saumitriḥ samiddhe jātavedasi ।।
lakṣmaṇaḥ puruṣavyāghram atha rāghavam abravīt ।। devatā devasaṃkāśa yajasva kuśalo hy asi ।। pāpasaṃśamanaṃ rāmaś cakāra balim uttamam ।। vāsāya sarve viviśuḥ sametāḥ sabhāṃ yathā devagaṇāḥ sudharmām ।।
vanottame vyālamṛgānunādite tathā vijahruḥ susukhaṃ jitendriyāḥ ।। nananda hṛṣṭo mṛgapakṣijuṣṭāṃ jahau ca duḥkhaṃ puravipravāsāt ।। rāme dakṣiṇakūlasthe jagāma svagṛhaṃ guhaḥ ।। ayodhyām eva nagarīṃ prayayau gāḍhadurmanāḥ ।।
paśyann atiyayau śīghraṃ grāmāṇi nagarāṇi ca ।। ayodhyāṃ samanuprāpya nirānandāṃ dadarśa ha ।। sumantraś cintayāmāsa śokavegasamāhataḥ ।। iti cintāparaḥ sūtas tvaritaḥ praviveśa ha ।।
kva rāma iti pṛcchantaḥ sūtam abhyadravan narāḥ ।। anujñāto nivṛtto asmi dhārmikeṇa mahātmanā ।। aho dhig iti niḥśvasya hā rāmeti ca cukruśuḥ ।। hatāḥ sma khalu ye neha paśyāma iti rāghavam ।।
na drakṣyāmaḥ punar jātu dhārmikaṃ rāmam antarā ।। iti rāmeṇa nagaraṃ pitṛvat paripālitam ।। rāmaśokābhitaptānāṃ śuśrāva paridevanam ।। yatra rājā daśarathas tad evopayayau gṛham ।।
kakṣyāḥ saptābhicakrāma mahājanasamākulāḥ ।। rāmaśokābhitaptānāṃ mandaṃ śuśrāva jalpitam ।। sūtaḥ kiṃ nāma kausalyāṃ śocantīṃ prativakṣyati ।। ācchidya putre niryāte kausalyā yatra jīvati ।।
pradīptam iva śokena viveśa sahasā gṛham ।। putraśokaparidyūnam apaśyat pāṇḍure gṛhe ।। sumantro rāmavacanaṃ yathoktaṃ pratyavedayat ।। mūrchito nyapatad bhūmau rāmaśokābhipīḍitaḥ ।।
uddhṛtya bāhū cukrośa nṛpatau patite kṣitau ।। utthāpayāmāsa tadā vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। vanavāsād anuprāptaṃ kasmān na pratibhāṣase ।। uttiṣṭha sukṛtaṃ te astu śoke na syāt sahāyatā ।।
neha tiṣṭhati kaikeyī viśrabdhaṃ pratibhāṣyatām ।। dharaṇyāṃ nipapātāśu bāṣpaviplutabhāṣiṇī ।। patiṃ cāvekṣya tāḥ sarvāḥ sasvaraṃ ruruduḥ striyaḥ ।। striyaś ca sarvā ruruduḥ samantataḥ puraṃ tadāsīt punar eva saṃkulam ।।
athājuhāva taṃ sūtaṃ rāmavṛttāntakāraṇāt ।। viniḥśvasantaṃ dhyāyantam asvastham iva kuñjaram ।। aśrupūrṇamukhaṃ dīnam uvāca paramārtavat ।। bhūmipālātmajo bhūmau śete katham anāthavat ।।
sa vatsyati kathaṃ rāmo vijanaṃ vanam āśritaḥ ।। kathaṃ kumārau vaidehyā sārdhaṃ vanam upasthitau ।। rājaputrau kathaṃ pādair avaruhya rathād gatau ।। vanāntaṃ praviśantau tāv aśvināv iva mandaram ।।
āsitaṃ śayitaṃ bhuktaṃ sūta rāmasya kīrtaya ।। uvāca vācā rājānaṃ sabāṣpaparirabdhayā ।। añjaliṃ rāghavaḥ kṛtvā śirasābhipraṇamya ca ।। śirasā vandanīyasya vandyau pādau mahātmanaḥ ।।
ārogyam aviśeṣeṇa yathārhaṃ cābhivādanam ।। devi devasya pādau ca devavat paripālaya ।। sarvāsv eva yathānyāyaṃ vṛttiṃ vartasva mātṛṣu ।। pitaraṃ yauvarājyastho rājyastham anupālaya ।।
rāmo rājīvatāmrākṣo bhṛśam aśrūṇy avartayat ।। kenāyam aparādhena rājaputro vivāsitaḥ ।। rāmasya tu parityāge na hetum upalakṣaye ।। janayiṣyati saṃkrośaṃ rāghavasya vivāsanam ।।
bhrātā bhartā ca bandhuś ca pitā ca mama rāghavaḥ ।। sarvaloko anurajyeta kathaṃ tvānena karmaṇā ।। bhūtopahatacitteva viṣṭhitā vismṛtā sthitā ।। tena duḥkhena rudatī naiva māṃ kiṃcid abravīt ।।
mumoca sahasā bāṣpaṃ māṃ prayāntam udīkṣya sā ।। tathaiva sītā rudatī tapasvinī nirīkṣate rājarathaṃ tathaiva mām ।। uṣṇam aśru vimuñcanto rāme samprasthite vanam ।। prasthito ratham āsthāya tad duḥkham api dhārayan ।।
āśayā yadi māṃ rāmaḥ punaḥ śabdāpayed iti ।। api vṛkṣāḥ parimlānaḥ sapuṣpāṅkurakorakāḥ ।। rāmaśokābhibhūtaṃ tan niṣkūjam abhavad vanam ।। saṃtaptapadmāḥ padminyo līnamīnavihaṃgamāḥ ।।
nādya bhānty alpagandhīni phalāni ca yathā puram ।। narā rāmam apaśyanto niḥśvasanti muhur muhuḥ ।। hāhākārakṛtā nāryo rāmādarśanakarśitāḥ ।। anyonyam abhivīkṣante vyaktam ārtatarāḥ striyaḥ ।।
aham ārtatayā kaṃcid viśeṣaṃ nopalakṣaye ।। ārtasvaraparimlānā viniḥśvasitaniḥsvanā ।। kausalyā putrahīneva ayodhyā pratibhāti mā ।। bāṣpopahatayā rājā taṃ sūtam idam abravīt ।।
mayā na mantrakuśalair vṛddhaiḥ saha samarthitam ।। mayāyam arthaḥ sammohāt strīhetoḥ sahasā kṛtaḥ ।। kulasyāsya vināśāya prāptaṃ sūta yadṛcchayā ।। tvaṃ prāpayāśu māṃ rāmaṃ prāṇāḥ saṃtvarayanti mām ।।
na śakṣyāmi vinā rāmaṃ muhūrtam api jīvitum ।। mām eva ratham āropya śīghraṃ rāmāya darśaya ।। yadi jīvāmi sādhv enaṃ paśyeyaṃ saha sītayā ।। rāmaṃ yadi na paśyāmi gamiṣyāmi yamakṣayam ।।
imām avasthām āpanno neha paśyāmi rāghavam ।। dustaro jīvatā devi mayāyaṃ śokasāgaraḥ ।। itīva rājā vilapan mahāyaśāḥ papāta tūrṇaṃ śayane sa mūrchitaḥ ।। vacanam anuniśamya tasya devī bhayam agamat punar eva rāmamātā ।।
dharaṇyāṃ gatasattveva kausalyā sūtam abravīt ।। tān vinā kṣaṇam apy atra jīvituṃ notsahe hy aham ।। atha tān nānugacchāmi gamiṣyāmi yamakṣayam ।। idam āśvāsayan devīṃ sūtaḥ prāñjalir abravīt ।।
vyavadhūya ca saṃtāpaṃ vane vatsyati rāghavaḥ ।। ārādhayati dharmajñaḥ paralokaṃ jitendriyaḥ ।। visrambhaṃ labhate abhītā rāme saṃnyastamānasā ।। uciteva pravāsānāṃ vaidehī pratibhāti mā ।।
tathaiva ramate sītā nirjaneṣu vaneṣv api ।। rāmā rāme hy adhīnātmā vijane api vane satī ।। ayodhyāpi bhavet tasyā rāmahīnā tathā vanam ।। gatiṃ dṛṣṭvā nadīnāṃ ca pādapān vividhān api ।।
na hi gacchati vaidehyāś candrāṃśusadṛśī prabhā ।। vadanaṃ tadvadānyāyā vaidehyā na vikampate ।। adyāpi caraṇau tasyāḥ padmakośasamaprabhau ।। idānīm api vaidehī tadrāgā nyastabhūṣaṇā ।।
nāhārayati saṃtrāsaṃ bāhū rāmasya saṃśritā ।। idaṃ hi caritaṃ loke pratiṣṭhāsyati śāśvatam ।। vane ratā vanyaphalāśanāḥ pituḥ śubhāṃ pratijñāṃ paripālayanti te ।। na caiva devī virarāma kūjitāt priyeti putreti ca rāghaveti ca ।।
kausalyā rudatī svārtā bhartāram idam abravīt ।। sānukrośo vadānyaś ca priyavādī ca rāghavaḥ ।। duḥkhitau sukhasaṃvṛddhau vane duḥkhaṃ sahiṣyataḥ ।। katham uṣṇaṃ ca śītaṃ ca maithilī prasahiṣyate ।।
vanyaṃ naivāram āhāraṃ kathaṃ sītopabhokṣyate ।। kathaṃ kravyādasiṃhānāṃ śabdaṃ śroṣyaty aśobhanam ।। bhujaṃ parighasaṃkāśam upadhāya mahābalaḥ ।। kadā drakṣyāmi rāmasya vadanaṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam ।।
apaśyantyā na taṃ yad vai phalatīdaṃ sahasradhā ।। jahyād rājyaṃ ca kośaṃ ca bharatenopabhokṣyate ।। bhrātā jyeṣṭho variṣṭhaś ca kimarthaṃ nāvamaṃsyate ।। evam eva naravyāghraḥ paralīḍhaṃ na maṃsyate ।।
naitāni yātayāmāni kurvanti punar adhvare ।। nābhimantum alaṃ rāmo naṣṭasomam ivādhvaram ।। balavān iva śārdūlo vāladher abhimarśanam ।। svayam eva hataḥ pitrā jalajenātmajo yathā ।।
yadi te dharmanirate tvayā putre vivāsite ।। tṛtīyā jñātayo rājaṃś caturthī neha vidyate ।। na vanaṃ gantum icchāmi sarvathā hi hatā tvayā ।। hatā saputrāsmi hatāś ca paurāḥ sutaś ca bhāryā ca tava prahṛṣṭau ।।
tataḥ sa śokaṃ praviveśa pārthivaḥ svaduṣkṛtaṃ cāpi punas tadāsmarat ।। śrāvitaḥ paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ ।। yad anena kṛtaṃ pūrvam ajñānāc chabdavedhinā ।। dahyamānas tu śokābhyāṃ kausalyām āha bhūpatiḥ ।।
vatsalā cānṛśaṃsā ca tvaṃ hi nityaṃ pareṣv api ।। dharmaṃ vimṛśamānānāṃ pratyakṣaṃ devi daivatam ।। nārhase vipriyaṃ vaktuṃ duḥkhitāpi suduḥkhitam ।। kausalyā vyasṛjad bāṣpaṃ praṇālīva navodakam ।।
sambhramād abravīt trastā tvaramāṇākṣaraṃ vacaḥ ।। yācitāsmi hatā deva hantavyāhaṃ na hi tvayā ।। ubhayor lokayor vīra patyā yā saṃprasādyate ।। putraśokārtayā tat tu mayā kim api bhāṣitam ।।
śoko nāśayate sarvaṃ nāsti śokasamo ripuḥ ।। soḍhum āpatitaḥ śokaḥ susūkṣmo api na śakyate ।। yaḥ śokahataharṣāyāḥ pañcavarṣopamo mama ।। adīnām iva vegena samudrasalilaṃ mahat ।।
mandaraśmir abhūt suryo rajanī cābhyavartata ।। śokena ca samākrānto nidrāyā vaśam eyivān ।। atha rājā daśarathaḥ sa cintām abhyapadyata ।। āviveśopasargas taṃ tamaḥ sūryam ivāsuram ।।
kausalyāṃ putraśokārtām idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। tad eva labhate bhadre kartā karmajam ātmanaḥ ।। doṣaṃ vā yo na jānāti sa bāla iti hocyate ।। puṣpaṃ dṛṣṭvā phale gṛdhnuḥ sa śocati phalāgame ।।
rāmaṃ phalāgame tyaktvā paścāc chocāmi durmatiḥ ।। tad idaṃ me anusaṃprāptaṃ devi duḥkhaṃ svayaṃ kṛtam ।। evaṃ mamāpy avijñātaṃ śabdavedhyamayaṃ phalam ।। tataḥ prāvṛḍ anuprāptā madakāmavivardhinī ।।
paretācaritāṃ bhīmāṃ ravir āviśate diśam ।। tato jahṛṣire sarve bhekasāraṅgabarhiṇaḥ ।। ābabhau mattasāraṅgas toyarāśir ivācalaḥ ।। vyāyāmakṛtasaṃkalpaḥ sarayūm anvagāṃ nadīm ।।
anyaṃ vā śvāpadaṃ kaṃcij jighāṃsur ajitendriyaḥ ।। acakṣur viṣaye ghoṣaṃ vāraṇasyeva nardataḥ ।। amuñcaṃ niśitaṃ bāṇam aham āśīviṣopamam ।। katham asmadvidhe śastraṃ nipatet tu tapasvini ।।
iṣuṇābhihataḥ kena kasya vā kiṃ kṛtaṃ mayā ।। kathaṃ nu śastreṇa vadho madvidhasya vidhīyate ।। ko vadhena mamārthī syāt kiṃ vāsyāpakṛtaṃ mayā ।। na kaścit sādhu manyeta yathaiva gurutalpagam ।।
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cobhāv anuśocāmi madvidhe ।। mayi pañcatvam āpanne kāṃ vṛttiṃ vartayiṣyati ।। kena sma nihatāḥ sarve subālenākṛtātmanā ।। karābhyāṃ saśaraṃ cāpaṃ vyathitasyāpatad bhuvi ।।
apaśyam iṣuṇā tīre sarayvās tāpasaṃ hatam ।। ity uvāca vacaḥ krūraṃ didhakṣann iva tejasā ।। jihīrṣur ambho gurvarthaṃ yad ahaṃ tāḍitas tvayā ।। dvāv andhau nihatau vṛddhau mātā janayitā ca me ।।
