ciram āśākṛtāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ kaṣṭāṃ saṃdhārayiṣyataḥ ।। pitā yan māṃ na jānāti śayānaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi ।। bhidyamānam ivāśaktas trātum anyo nago nagam ।। na tvām anudahet kruddho vanaṃ vahnir ivaidhitaḥ ।।
taṃ prasādaya gatvā tvaṃ na tvāṃ sa kupitaḥ śapet ।। ruṇaddhi mṛdu sotsedhaṃ tīram amburayo yathā ।। śūdrāyām asmi vaiśyena jāto janapadādhipa ।। tasya tv ānamyamānasya taṃ bāṇam aham uddharam ।।
tataḥ sarayvāṃ tam ahaṃ śayānaṃ samīkṣya bhadre subhṛśaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ ।। ekas tv acintayaṃ buddhyā kathaṃ nu sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।। āśramaṃ tam ahaṃ prāpya yathākhyātapathaṃ gataḥ ।। apaśyaṃ tasya pitarau lūnapakṣāv iva dvijau ।।
tām āśāṃ matkṛte hīnāv udāsīnāv anāthavat ।। kiṃ cirāyasi me putra pānīyaṃ kṣipram ānaya ।। utkaṇṭhitā te māteyaṃ praviśa kṣipram āśramam ।। na tan manasi kartavyaṃ tvayā tāta tapasvinā ।।
samāsaktās tvayi prāṇāḥ kiṃcin nau nābhibhāṣase ।। hīnavyañjanayā prekṣya bhīto bhīta ivābruvam ।। ācacakṣe tv ahaṃ tasmai putravyasanajaṃ bhayam ।। sajjanāvamataṃ duḥkham idaṃ prāptaṃ svakarmajam ।।
jighāṃsuḥ śvāpadaṃ kiṃcin nipāne vāgataṃ gajam ।। dvipo ayam iti matvā hi bāṇenābhihato mayā ।। vinirbhinnaṃ gataprāṇaṃ śayānaṃ bhuvi tāpasam ।। visṛṣṭo ambhasi nārācas tena te nihataḥ sutaḥ ।।
bhagavantāv ubhau śocann andhāv iti vilapya ca ।। śeṣam evaṃgate yat syāt tat prasīdatu me muniḥ ।। mām uvāca mahātejāḥ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam ।। phalen mūrdhā sma te rājan sadyaḥ śatasahasradhā ।।
jñānapūrvaṃ kṛtaḥ sthānāc cyāvayed api vajriṇam ।। api hy adya kulaṃ na syād rāghavāṇāṃ kuto bhavān ।। adya taṃ draṣṭum icchāvaḥ putraṃ paścimadarśanam ।। śayānaṃ bhuvi niḥsaṃjñaṃ dharmarājavaśaṃ gatam ।।
asparśayam ahaṃ putraṃ taṃ muniṃ saha bhāryayā ।। nipetatuḥ śarīre asya pitā cāsyedam abravīt ।। kiṃ nu nāliṅgase putra sukumāra vaco vada ।। adhīyānasya madhuraṃ śāstraṃ vānyad viśeṣataḥ ।।
ślāghayiṣyaty upāsīnaḥ putraśokabhayārditam ।। bhojayiṣyaty akarmaṇyam apragraham anāyakam ।। kathaṃ putra bhariṣyāmi kṛpaṇāṃ putragardhinīm ।। śvo mayā saha gantāsi jananyā ca samedhitaḥ ।।
kṣipram eva gamiṣyāvas tvayā hīnau yamakṣayam ।। kṣamatāṃ dharmarājo me bibhṛyāt pitarāv ayam ।। tena satyena gacchāśu ye lokāḥ śastrayodhinām ।। hatās tv abhimukhāḥ putra gatiṃ tāṃ paramāṃ vraja ।।
nahuṣo dhundhumāraś ca prāptās tāṃ gaccha putraka ।। bhūmidasyāhitāgneś ca ekapatnīvratasya ca ।। na hi tv asmin kule jāto gacchaty akuśalāṃ gatim ।। tato asmai kartum udakaṃ pravṛttaḥ saha bhāryayā ।।
āśvāsya ca muhūrtaṃ tu pitarau vākyam abravīt ।। bhavantāv api ca kṣipraṃ mama mūlam upaiṣyataḥ ।। āruroha divaṃ kṣipraṃ muniputro jitendriyaḥ ।। mām uvāca mahātejāḥ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam ।।
yac chareṇaikaputraṃ māṃ tvam akārṣīr aputrakam ।। tena tvām abhiśapsyāmi suduḥkham atidāruṇam ।। evaṃ tvaṃ putraśokena rājan kālaṃ kariṣyasi ।। yad ahaṃ putraśokena saṃtyakṣyāmy adya jīvitam ।।
na tan me sadṛśaṃ devi yan mayā rāghave kṛtam ।। dūtā vaivasvatasyaite kausalye tvarayanti mām ।। na hi paśyāmi dharmajñaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam ।। mukhaṃ drakṣyanti rāmasya varṣe pañcadaśe punaḥ ।।
dhanyā drakṣyanti rāmasya tārādhipanibhaṃ mukham ।। sugandhi mama nāthasya dhanyā drakṣyanti tanmukham ।। drakṣyanti sukhino rāmaṃ śukraṃ mārgagataṃ yathā ।। saṃsādayati vegena yathā kūlaṃ nadīrayaḥ ।।
rājā daśarathaḥ śocañ jīvitāntam upāgamat ।। gate ardharātre bhṛśaduḥkhapīḍitas tadā jahau prāṇam udāradarśanaḥ ।। bandinaḥ paryupātiṣṭhaṃs tat pārthivaniveśanam ।। strīvarṣavarabhūyiṣṭhā upatasthur yathāpuram ।।
āninyuḥ snānaśikṣājñā yathākālaṃ yathāvidhi ।। upaninyus tathāpy anyāḥ kumārībahulāḥ striyaḥ ।। tāḥ striyas tu samāgamya bhartāraṃ pratyabodhayan ।। pratisrotas tṛṇāgrāṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ saṃcakampire ।।
yat tad āśaṅkitaṃ pāpaṃ tasya jajñe viniścayaḥ ।। kareṇava ivāraṇye sthānapracyutayūthapāḥ ।। kausalyā ca sumitrā ca tyaktanidre babhūvatuḥ ।। hā nātheti parikruśya petatur dharaṇītale ।।
na babhrāja rajodhvastā tāreva gaganacyutā ।। sarvatas tumulākrandaṃ paritāpārtabāndhavam ।। babhūva naradevasya sadma diṣṭāntam īyuṣaḥ ।। bhṛśaṃ rudantyaḥ karuṇaṃ suduḥkhitāḥ pragṛhya bāhū vyalapann anāthavat ।।
hataprabham ivādityaṃ svargasthaṃ prekṣya bhūmipam ।। upagṛhya śiro rājñaḥ kaikeyīṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। tyaktvā rājānam ekāgrā nṛśaṃse duṣṭacāriṇi ।। vipathe sārthahīneva nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe ।।
icchej jīvitum anyatra kaikeyyās tyaktadharmaṇaḥ ।। kubjānimittaṃ kaikeyyā rāghavāṇāṃ kulaṃ hatam ।। sabhāryaṃ janakaḥ śrutvā paritapsyaty ahaṃ yathā ।। duḥkhasyānucitā duḥkhaṃ vane paryudvijiṣyati ।।
niśamya nūnaṃ saṃtrastā rāghavaṃ saṃśrayiṣyati ।। so api śokasamāviṣṭo nanu tyakṣyati jīvitam ।। vyapaninyuḥ suduḥkhārtāṃ kausalyāṃ vyāvahārikāḥ ।। rājñaḥ sarvāṇy athādiṣṭāś cakruḥ karmāṇy anantaram ।।
sarvajñāḥ kartum īṣus te tato rakṣanti bhūmipam ।। hā mṛto ayam iti jñātvā striyas tāḥ paryadevayan ।। rudantyaḥ śokasaṃtaptāḥ kṛpaṇaṃ paryadevayan ।। purī nārājatāyodhyā hīnā rājñā mahātmanā ।।
śūnyacatvaraveśmāntā na babhrāja yathāpuram ।। purī babhāse rahitā mahātmanā na cāsrakaṇṭhākulamārgacatvarā ।। tadā nagaryāṃ naradevasaṃkṣaye babhūvur ārtā na ca śarma lebhire ।। sametya rājakartāraḥ sabhām īyur dvijātayaḥ ।।
kātyāyano gautamaś ca jābāliś ca mahāyaśāḥ ।। vasiṣṭham evābhimukhāḥ śreṣṭhaṃ rājapurohitam ।। asmin pañcatvam āpanne putraśokena pārthive ।। lakṣmaṇaś cāpi tejasvī rāmeṇaiva gataḥ saha ।।
pure rājagṛhe ramye mātāmahaniveśane ।। arājakaṃ hi no rāṣṭraṃ na vināśam avāpnuyāt ।। abhivarṣati parjanyo mahīṃ divyena vāriṇā ।। nārājake pituḥ putro bhāryā vā vartate vaśe ।।
idam atyāhitaṃ cānyat kutaḥ satyam arājake ।। udyānāni ca ramyāṇi hṛṣṭāḥ puṇyagṛhāṇi ca ।। sattrāṇy anvāsate dāntā brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।। utsavāś ca samājāś ca vardhante rāṣṭravardhanāḥ ।।
kathābhir anurajyante kathāśīlāḥ kathāpriyaiḥ ।। narā niryānty araṇyāni nārībhiḥ saha kāminaḥ ।। śerate vivṛtadvārāḥ kṛṣigorakṣajīvinaḥ ।। gacchanti kṣemam adhvānaṃ bahupuṇyasamācitāḥ ।।
bhāvayann ātmanātmānaṃ yatra sāyaṃgṛho muniḥ ।। na cāpy arājake senā śatrūn viṣahate yudhi ।। agopālā yathā gāvas tathā rāṣṭram arājakam ।। matsyā iva narā nityaṃ bhakṣayanti parasparam ।।
te api bhāvāya kalpante rājadaṇḍanipīḍitāḥ ।। rājā cen na bhavel loke vibhajan sādhvasādhunī ।। nātikramāmahe sarve velāṃ prāpyeva sāgaraḥ ।। kumāram ikṣvākusutaṃ vadānyaṃ tvam eva rājānam ihābhiṣiñca ।।
mitrāmātyagaṇān sarvān brāhmaṇāṃs tān idaṃ vacaḥ ।। bharato vasati bhrātrā śatrughnena samanvitaḥ ।। ānetuṃ bhrātarau vīrau kiṃ samīkṣāmahe vayam ।। teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt ।।
śrūyatām itikartavyaṃ sarvān eva bravīmi vaḥ ।। tyaktaśokair idaṃ vācyaḥ śāsanād bharato mama ।। tvaramāṇaś ca niryāhi kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ tvayā ।। bhavantaḥ śaṃsiṣur gatvā rāghavāṇām imaṃ kṣayam ।।
vasiṣṭhenābhyanujñātā dūtāḥ saṃtvaritā yayuḥ ।। pāñcāladeśam āsādya madhyena kurujāṅgalam ।। upātijagmur vegena śaradaṇḍāṃ janākulām ।। abhigamyābhivādyaṃ taṃ kuliṅgāṃ prāviśan purīm ।।
viṣṇoḥ padaṃ prekṣamāṇā vipāśāṃ cāpi śālmalīm ।। girivrajaṃ puravaraṃ śīghram āsedur añjasā ।। aheḍamānās tvarayā sma dūtā rātryāṃ tu te tat puram eva yātāḥ ।। bharatenāpi tāṃ rātriṃ svapno dṛṣṭo ayam apriyaḥ ।।
putro rājādhirājasya subhṛśaṃ paryatapyata ।। āyāsaṃ hi vineṣyantaḥ sabhāyāṃ cakrire kathāḥ ।। nāṭakāny apare prāhur hāsyāni vividhāni ca ।। goṣṭhīhāsyāni kurvadbhir na prāhṛṣyata rāghavaḥ ।।
suhṛdbhiḥ paryupāsīnaḥ kiṃ sakhe nānumodase ।। śṛṇu tvaṃ yannimittaṃ me dainyam etad upāgatam ।। patantam adriśikharāt kaluṣe gomayahrade ।। pibann añjalinā tailaṃ hasann iva muhur muhuḥ ।।
tailenābhyaktasarvāṅgas tailam evāvagāhata ।। sahasā cāpi saṃśāntaṃ jvalitaṃ jātavedasam ।। ahaṃ paśyāmi vidhvastān sadhūmāṃś caiva parvatān ।। prahasanti sma rājānaṃ pramadāḥ kṛṣṇapiṅgalāḥ ।।
rathena kharayuktena prayāto dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।। ahaṃ rāmo atha vā rājā lakṣmaṇo vā mariṣyati ।। etannimittaṃ dīno ahaṃ tan na vaḥ pratipūjaye ।। jugupsann iva cātmānaṃ na ca paśyāmi kāraṇam ।।
bhayaṃ mahat taddhṛdayān na yāti me vicintya rājānam acintyadarśanam ।। praviśyāsahyaparikhaṃ ramyaṃ rājagṛhaṃ puram ।। rājñaḥ pādau gṛhītvā tu tam ūcur bharataṃ vacaḥ ।। tvaramāṇaś ca niryāhi kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ tvayā ।।
daśakoṭyas tu sampūrṇās tathaiva ca nṛpātmaja ।। dūtān uvāca bharataḥ kāmaiḥ sampratipūjya tān ।। kaccic cārogatā rāme lakṣmaṇe vā mahātmani ।। arogā cāpi kausalyā mātā rāmasya dhīmataḥ ।।
śatrughnasya ca vīrasya sārogā cāpi madhyamā ।। arogā cāpi kaikeyī mātā me kim uvāca ha ।। kuśalās te naravyāghra yeṣāṃ kuśalam icchasi ।। āpṛcche ahaṃ mahārājaṃ dūtāḥ saṃtvarayanti mām ।।
dūtaiḥ saṃcodito vākyaṃ mātāmaham uvāca ha ।। punar apy aham eṣyāmi yadā me tvaṃ smariṣyasi ।। tam uvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ śirasy āghrāya rāghavam ।। mātaraṃ kuśalaṃ brūyāḥ pitaraṃ ca paraṃtapa ।।
tau ca tāta maheṣvāsau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। abhisatkṛtya kaikeyo bharatāya dhanaṃ dadau ।। satkṛtya kaikeyī putraṃ kekayo dhanam ādiśat ।। dadāv aśvapatiḥ śīghraṃ bharatāyānuyāyinaḥ ।।
kharāñ śīghrān susaṃyuktān mātulo asmai dhanaṃ dadau ।। daṃṣṭrāyudhān mahākāyāñ śunaś copāyanaṃ dadau ।। ratham āruhya bharataḥ śatrughnasahito yayau ।। uṣṭrago'śvakharair bhṛtyā bharataṃ yāntam anvayuḥ ।।
ādāya śatrughnam apetaśatrur gṛhād yayau siddha ivendralokāt ।। śatadrūm atarac chrīmān nadīm ikṣvākunandanaḥ ।। śilām ākurvatīṃ tīrtvā āgneyaṃ śalyakartanam ।। atyayāt sa mahāśailān vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ prati ।।
yamunāṃ prāpya saṃtīrṇo balam āśvāsayat tadā ।। tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca prāyād ādāya codakam ।। bhadro bhadreṇa yānena mārutaḥ kham ivātyayāt ।। varūthaṃ ca yayau ramyaṃ grāmaṃ daśarathātmajaḥ ।।
udyānam ujjihānāyāḥ priyakā yatra pādapāḥ ।। anujñāpyātha bharato vāhinīṃ tvarito yayau ।। anyā nadīś ca vividhāḥ pārvatīyais turaṃgamaiḥ ।। ekasāle sthāṇumatīṃ vinate gomatīṃ nadīm ।।
bharataḥ kṣipram āgacchat supariśrāntavāhanaḥ ।। ayodhyāṃ manunā rājñā nirmitāṃ sa dadarśa ha ।। ayodhyām agrato dṛṣṭvā rathe sārathim abravīt ।। ayodhyā dṛśyate dūrāt sārathe pāṇḍumṛttikā ।।
bhūyiṣṭham ṛddhair ākīrṇā rājarṣivarapālitā ।। samantān naranārīṇāṃ tam adya na śṛṇomy aham ।। samantād vipradhāvadbhiḥ prakāśante mamānyadā ।। araṇyabhūteva purī sārathe pratibhāti me ।।
niryānto vābhiyānto vā naramukhyā yathāpuram ।। nimittāny amanojñāni tena sīdati me manaḥ ।। dvāḥsthair utthāya vijayaṃ pṛṣṭas taiḥ sahito yayau ।। sūtam aśvapateḥ klāntam abravīt tatra rāghavaḥ ।।
ākārās tān ahaṃ sarvān iha paśyāmi sārathe ।। sastrīpuṃsaṃ ca paśyāmi janam utkaṇṭhitaṃ pure ।। tāṃ śūnyaśṛṅgāṭakaveśmarathyāṃ rajo'ruṇadvārakapāṭayantrām ।। avākśirā dīnamanā na hṛṣṭaḥ pitur mahātmā praviveśa veśma ।।
jagāma bharato draṣṭuṃ mātaraṃ mātur ālaye ।। utpapāta tadā hṛṣṭā tyaktvā sauvarṇamānasam ।। bharataḥ prekṣya jagrāha jananyāś caraṇau śubhau ।। aṅke bharatam āropya praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame ।।
api nādhvaśramaḥ śīghraṃ rathenāpatatas tava ।। pravāsāc ca sukhaṃ putra sarvaṃ me vaktum arhasi ।। ācaṣṭa bharataḥ sarvaṃ mātre rājīvalocanaḥ ।। ambāyāḥ kuśalī tāto yudhājin mātulaś ca me ।।
pariśrāntaṃ pathy abhavat tato ahaṃ pūrvam āgataḥ ।। yad ahaṃ praṣṭum icchāmi tad ambā vaktum arhati ।। na cāyam ikṣvākujanaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ pratibhāti me ।। tam ahaṃ nādya paśyāmi draṣṭum icchann ihāgataḥ ।।
āhosvid amba jyeṣṭhāyāḥ kausalyāyā niveśane ।। yā gatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ te pitā gataḥ ।। papāta sahasā bhūmau pitṛśokabalārditaḥ ।। vilalāpa mahātejā bhrāntākulitacetanaḥ ।।
tad idaṃ na vibhāty adya vihīnaṃ tena dhīmatā ।। utthāpayitvā śokārtaṃ vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। tvadvidhā na hi śocanti santaḥ sadasi saṃmatāḥ ।। jananīṃ pratyuvācedaṃ śokair bahubhir āvṛtaḥ ।।
ity ahaṃ kṛtasaṃkalpo hṛṣṭo yātrām ayāsiṣam ।। pitaraṃ yo na paśyāmi nityaṃ priyahite ratam ।। dhanyā rāmādayaḥ sarve yaiḥ pitā saṃskṛtaḥ svayam ।। upajighreddhi māṃ mūrdhni tātaḥ saṃnamya satvaram ।।
yena māṃ rajasā dhvastam abhīkṣṇaṃ parimārjati ।। tasya māṃ śīghram ākhyāhi rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ ।। tasya pādau grahīṣyāmi sa hīdānīṃ gatir mama ।। paścimaṃ sādhusaṃdeśam icchāmi śrotum ātmanaḥ ।।
sa mahātmā paraṃ lokaṃ gato gatimatāṃ varaḥ ।। kāladharmaparikṣiptaḥ pāśair iva mahāgajaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābāhuṃ drakṣyanti punar āgatam ।। viṣaṇṇavadano bhūtvā bhūyaḥ papraccha mātaram ।।
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā sītayā ca samaṃ gataḥ ।। mātāsya yugapad vākyaṃ vipriyaṃ priyaśaṅkayā ।। daṇḍakān saha vaidehyā lakṣmaṇānucaro gataḥ ।। svasya vaṃśasya māhātmyāt praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame ।।
kaccin nāḍhyo daridro vā tenāpāpo vihiṃsitaḥ ।। kasmāt sa daṇḍakāraṇye bhrūṇaheva vivāsitaḥ ।। tenaiva strīsvabhāvena vyāhartum upacakrame ।। na rāmaḥ paradārāṃś ca cakṣurbhyām api paśyati ।।
yācitas te pitā rājyaṃ rāmasya ca vivāsanam ।। rāmaś ca sahasaumitriḥ preṣitaḥ saha sītayā ।। putraśokaparidyūnaḥ pañcatvam upapedivān ।। tvatkṛte hi mayā sarvam idam evaṃvidhaṃ kṛtam ।।
saṃkālya rājānam adīnasattvam ātmānam urvyām abhiṣecayasva ।। bharato duḥkhasaṃtapta idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। vihīnasyātha pitrā ca bhrātrā pitṛsamena ca ।। rājānaṃ pretabhāvasthaṃ kṛtvā rāmaṃ ca tāpasam ।।
aṅgāram upagūhya sma pitā me nāvabuddhavān ।। duṣkaraṃ yadi jīvetāṃ prāpya tvāṃ jananīṃ mama ।। vartate guruvṛttijño yathā mātari vartate ।। tvayi dharmaṃ samāsthāya bhaginyām iva vartate ।।
prasthāpya vanavāsāya kathaṃ pāpe na śocasi ।। pravrājya cīravasanaṃ kiṃ nu paśyasi kāraṇam ।। tathā hy anartho rājyārthaṃ tvayā nīto mahān ayam ।। kena śaktiprabhāvena rājyaṃ rakṣitum utsahe ।।
apāśrito abhūd dharmātmā merur meruvanaṃ yathā ।। damyo dhuram ivāsādya saheyaṃ kena caujasā ।। nivartayiṣyāmi vanād bhrātaraṃ svajanapriyam ।। śokāturaś cāpi nanāda bhūyaḥ siṃho yathā parvatagahvarasthaḥ ।।
roṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ ।। parityaktā ca dharmeṇa mā mṛtaṃ rudatī bhava ।। yayor mṛtyur vivāsaś ca tvatkṛte tulyam āgatau ।। kaikeyi narakaṃ gaccha mā ca bhartuḥ salokatām ।।
sarvalokapriyaṃ hitvā mamāpy āpāditaṃ bhayam ।। ayaśo jīvaloke ca tvayāhaṃ pratipāditaḥ ।। na te aham abhibhāṣyo asmi durvṛtte patighātini ।। duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭās tvāṃ prāpya kuladūṣiṇīm ।।
rākṣasī tatra jātāsi kulapradhvaṃsinī pituḥ ।। vanaṃ prasthāpito duḥkhāt pitā ca tridivaṃ gataḥ ।। bhrātṛbhyāṃ ca parityakte sarvalokasya cāpriye ।। kṛtvā kaṃ prāpsyase tv adya lokaṃ nirayagāminī ।।
jyeṣṭhaṃ pitṛsamaṃ rāmaṃ kausalyāyātmasambhavam ।। tasmāt priyataro mātuḥ priyatvān na tu bāndhavaḥ ।। vahamānau dadarśorvyāṃ putrau vigatacetasau ।। ruroda putraśokena bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇā ।।
bindavaḥ patitā gātre sūkṣmāḥ surabhigandhinaḥ ।। indraḥ prāñjalir udvignaḥ surarājo abravīd vacaḥ ।। kutonimittaḥ śokas te brūhi sarvahitaiṣiṇi ।। pratyuvāca tato dhīrā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradā ।।
ahaṃ tu magnau śocāmi svaputrau viṣame sthitau ।। ardyamānau balīvardau karṣakeṇa surādhipa ।। yau dṛṣṭvā paritapye ahaṃ nāsti putrasamaḥ priyaḥ ।। kiṃ punar yā vinā rāmaṃ kausalyā vartayiṣyati ।।
tasmāt tvaṃ satataṃ duḥkhaṃ pretya ceha ca lapsyase ।। vardhanaṃ yaśasaś cāpi kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। svayam eva pravekṣyāmi vanaṃ muniniṣevitam ।। papāta bhuvi saṃkruddho niḥśvasann iva pannagaḥ ।।
babhūva bhūmau patito nṛpātmajaḥ śacīpateḥ ketur ivotsavakṣaye ।। kausalyā śabdam ājñāya sumitrām idam abravīt ।। tam ahaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi bharataṃ dīrghadarśinam ।। pratasthe bharato yatra vepamānā vicetanā ।।
pratasthe bharato yatra kausalyāyā niveśanam ।। paryaṣvajetāṃ duḥkhārtāṃ patitāṃ naṣṭacetanām ।। samprāptaṃ bata kaikeyyā śīghraṃ krūreṇa karmaṇā ।। kaikeyī kaṃ guṇaṃ tatra paśyati krūradarśinī ।।
hiraṇyanābho yatrāste suto me sumahāyaśāḥ ।। agnihotraṃ puraskṛtya prasthāsye yatra rāghavaḥ ।। yatrāsau puruṣavyāghras tapyate me tapaḥ sutaḥ ।। hastyaśvarathasampūrṇaṃ rājyaṃ niryātitaṃ tayā ।।
kausalyāṃ pratyuvācedaṃ śokair bahubhir āvṛtām ।। vipulāṃ ca mama prītiṃ sthirāṃ jānāsi rāghave ।। satyasaṃdhaḥ satāṃ śreṣṭho yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। hantu pādena gāṃ suptāṃ yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।।
adharmo yo asya so asyās tu yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। tatas tu druhyatāṃ pāpaṃ yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। adharmo yo asya so asyāstu yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। tāṃ vipralapatāṃ pāpaṃ yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।।
mā sma kārṣīt satāṃ dharmaṃ yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। sa nāśayatu duṣṭātmā yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। gurūṃś cāpy avajānātu yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। sa eko mṛṣṭam aśnātu yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।।
bhṛtyatyāge ca yat pāpaṃ tat pāpaṃ pratipadyatām ।। tac ca pāpaṃ bhavet tasya yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। mitradrohe ca yat pāpaṃ tat pāpaṃ pratipadyatām ।। mā sma kārṣīt sa śuśrūṣāṃ yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।।
bhraśyatu kṣipram adyaiva yasyāryo anumate gataḥ ।। evam āśvāsayann eva duḥkhārto nipapāta ha ।। bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt ।। śapathaiḥ śapamāno hi prāṇān uparuṇatsi me ।।
vatsa satyapratijño me satāṃ lokān avāpsyasi ।। mohāc ca śokasaṃrodhād babhūva lulitaṃ manaḥ ।। muhur muhur niḥśvasataś ca dīrghaṃ sā tasya śokena jagāma rātriḥ ।। uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho vasiṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhavāg ṛṣiḥ ।।
prāptakālaṃ narapateḥ kuru saṃyānam uttaram ।। pretakāryāṇi sarvāṇi kārayāmāsa dharmavit ।। āpītavarṇavadanaṃ prasuptam iva bhūmipam ।। tato daśarathaṃ putro vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ ।।
vivāsya rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam ।। hīnaṃ puruṣasiṃhena rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। tvayi prayāte svas tāta rāme ca vanam āśrite ।। hīnacandreva rajanī nagarī pratibhāti mām ।।
abravīd vacanaṃ bhūyo vasiṣṭhas tu mahān ṛṣiḥ ।। tāny avyagraṃ mahābāho kriyantām avicāritam ।। ṛtvikpurohitācāryāṃs tvarayāmāsa sarvaśaḥ ।। ṛtvigbhir yājakaiś caiva te hriyante yathāvidhi ।।
bāṣpakaṇṭhā vimanasas tam ūhuḥ paricārakāḥ ।। prakiranto janā mārgaṃ nṛpater agrato yayuḥ ।। devadārūṇi cāhṛtya citāṃ cakrus tathāpare ।। tataḥ saṃveśayāmāsuś citāmadhye tam ṛtvijaḥ ।।
jaguś ca te yathāśāstraṃ tatra sāmāni sāmagāḥ ।। nagarān niryayus tatra vṛddhaiḥ parivṛtās tadā ।। striyaś ca śokasaṃtaptāḥ kausalyāpramukhās tadā ।। ārtānāṃ karuṇaṃ kāle krośantīnāṃ sahasraśaḥ ।।
yānebhyaḥ sarayūtīram avaterur varāṅganāḥ ।। puraṃ praviśyāśruparītanetrā bhūmau daśāhaṃ vyanayanta duḥkham ।। dvādaśe ahani samprāpte śrāddhakarmāṇy akārayat ।। bāstikaṃ bahuśuklaṃ ca gāś cāpi śataśas tathā ।।
brāhmaṇebhyo dadau putro rājñas tasyaurdhvadaihikam ।। vilalāpa mahābāhur bharataḥ śokamūrchitaḥ ।। citāmūle pitur vākyam idam āha suduḥkhitaḥ ।। tasmin vanaṃ pravrajite śūnye tyakto asmy ahaṃ tvayā ।।
tām ambāṃ tāta kausalyāṃ tyaktvā tvaṃ kva gato nṛpa ।। pituḥ śarīranirvāṇaṃ niṣṭanan viṣasāda ha ।। utthāpyamānaḥ śakrasya yantradhvaja iva cyutaḥ ।। antakāle nipatitaṃ yayātim ṛṣayo yathā ।।
visaṃjño nyapatad bhūmau bhūmipālam anusmaran ।। smṛtvā pitur guṇāṅgāni tāni tāni tadā tadā ।। varadānamayo akṣobhyo amajjayac chokasāgaraḥ ।। kva tāta bharataṃ hitvā vilapantaṃ gato bhavān ।।
pravārayasi naḥ sarvāṃs tan naḥ ko adya kariṣyati ।। vihīnā yā tvayā rājñā dharmajñena mahātmanā ।। kiṃ me jīvitasāmarthyaṃ pravekṣyāmi hutāśanam ।। ayodhyāṃ na pravekṣyāmi pravekṣyāmi tapovanam ।।
bhṛśam ārtatarā bhūyaḥ sarva evānugāminaḥ ।। dharaṇyāṃ saṃvyaceṣṭetāṃ bhagnaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhau ।। vasiṣṭho bharataṃ vākyam utthāpya tam uvāca ha ।। teṣu cāparihāryeṣu naivaṃ bhavitum arhati ।।
śrāvayāmāsa tattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtabhavābhavau ।। varṣātapapariklinnau pṛthag indradhvajāv iva ।। amātyās tvarayanti sma tanayau cāparāḥ kriyāḥ ।। bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
sa rāmaḥ sattvasampannaḥ striyā pravrājito vanam ।। kiṃ na mocayate rāmaṃ kṛtvāpi pitṛnigraham ।। utpathaṃ yaḥ samārūḍho nāryā rājā vaśaṃ gataḥ ।। prāgdvāre abhūt tadā kubjā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ।।
mekhalādāmabhiś citrai rajjubaddheva vānarī ।। gṛhītvākaruṇāṃ kubjāṃ śatrughnāya nyavedayat ।। seyaṃ pāpā nṛśaṃsā ca tasyāḥ kuru yathāmati ।। antaḥpuracarān sarvān ity uvāca dhṛtavrataḥ ।।
yayā seyaṃ nṛśaṃsasya karmaṇaḥ phalam aśnutām ।। gṛhītā balavat kubjā sā tadgṛham anādayat ।। kruddham ājñāya śatrughnaṃ vyapalāyata sarvaśaḥ ।। yathāyaṃ samupakrānto niḥśeṣaṃ naḥ kariṣyati ।।
kausalyāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmaḥ sā hi no astu dhruvā gatiḥ ।। vicakarṣa tadā kubjāṃ krośantīṃ pṛthivītale ।। citraṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tad vyaśīryata ।। aśobhata tadā bhūyaḥ śāradaṃ gaganaṃ yathā ।।
kaikeyīm abhinirbhartsya babhāṣe paruṣaṃ vacaḥ ।। śatrughnabhayasaṃtrastā putraṃ śaraṇam āgatā ।। avadhyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pramadāḥ kṣamyatām iti ।। yadi māṃ dhārmiko rāmo nāsūyen mātṛghātakam ।।
tvāṃ ca māṃ caiva dharmātmā nābhibhāṣiṣyate dhruvam ।। nyavartata tato roṣāt tāṃ mumoca ca mantharām ।। niḥśvasantī suduḥkhārtā kṛpaṇaṃ vilalāpa ca ।। śanaiḥ samāśvāsayad ārtarūpāṃ krauñcīṃ vilagnām iva vīkṣamāṇām ।।
sametya rājakartāro bharataṃ vākyam abruvan ।। rāmaṃ pravrājya vai jyeṣṭhaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam ।। saṃgatyā nāparādhnoti rājyam etad anāyakam ।। pratīkṣate tvāṃ svajanaḥ śreṇayaś ca nṛpātmaja ।।
abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ pāhi cāsmān nararṣabha ।। bharatas taṃ janaṃ sarvaṃ pratyuvāca dhṛtavrataḥ ।। naivaṃ bhavanto māṃ vaktum arhanti kuśalā janāḥ ।। ahaṃ tv araṇye vatsyāmi varṣāṇi nava pañca ca ।।
ānayiṣyāmy ahaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaraṃ rāghavaṃ vanāt ।। puraskṛtya gamiṣyāmi rāmahetor vanaṃ prati ।। āneṣyāmi tu vai rāmaṃ havyavāham ivādhvarāt ।। vane vatsyāmy ahaṃ durge rāmo rājā bhaviṣyati ।।
rakṣiṇaś cānusaṃyāntu pathi durgavicārakāḥ ।। pratyuvāca janaḥ sarvaḥ śrīmadvākyam anuttamam ।। yas tvaṃ jyeṣṭhe nṛpasute pṛthivīṃ dātum icchasi ।। praharṣajās taṃ prati bāṣpabindavo nipetur āryānananetrasambhavāḥ ।।
panthānaṃ naravarabhaktimāñ janaś ca vyādiṣṭas tava vacanāc ca śilpivargaḥ ।। svakarmābhiratāḥ śūrāḥ khanakā yantrakās tathā ।। tathā vardhakayaś caiva mārgiṇo vṛkṣatakṣakāḥ ।। samarthā ye ca draṣṭāraḥ puratas te pratasthire ।।
aśobhata mahāvegaḥ sāgarasyeva parvaṇi ।। karaṇair vividhopetaiḥ purastāt sampratasthire ।। janās te cakrire mārgaṃ chindanto vividhān drumān ।। kecit kuṭhāraiṣ ṭaṅkaiś ca dātraiś chindan kvacit kvacit ।।
vidhamanti sma durgāṇi sthalāni ca tatas tataḥ ।। nimnabhāgāṃs tathā kecit samāṃś cakruḥ samantataḥ ।। bibhidur bhedanīyāṃś ca tāṃs tān deśān narās tadā ।। udapānān bahuvidhān vedikāparimaṇḍitān ।।
mattodghuṣṭadvijagaṇaḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। bahv aśobhata senāyāḥ panthāḥ svargapathopamaḥ ।। ramaṇīyeṣu deśeṣu bahusvāduphaleṣu ca ।। bhūyas taṃ śobhayāmāsur bhūṣābhir bhūṣaṇopamam ।।
niveśaṃ sthāpayāmāsur bharatasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tatrendrakīlapratimāḥ pratolīvaraśobhitāḥ ।। patākāśobhitāḥ sarve sunirmitamahāpathāḥ ।। samucchritair niveśās te babhuḥ śakrapuropamāḥ ।।
śītalāmalapānīyāṃ mahāmīnasamākulām ।। narendramārgaḥ sa tathā vyarājata krameṇa ramyaḥ śubhaśilpinirmitaḥ ।। tuṣṭuvur vāgviśeṣajñāḥ stavair maṅgalasaṃhitaiḥ ।। dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca śataśo vādyāṃś coccāvacasvarān ।।
bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ bhūyaḥ śokair arandhrayat ।। nāhaṃ rājeti cāpy uktvā śatrughnam idam abravīt ।। visṛjya mayi duḥkhāni rājā daśaratho gataḥ ।। paribhramati rājaśrīr naur ivākarṇikā jale ।।
kṛpaṇaṃ ruruduḥ sarvāḥ sasvaraṃ yoṣitas tadā ।। sabhām ikṣvākunāthasya praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ ।। sudharmām iva dharmātmā sagaṇaḥ pratyapadyata ।। adhyāsta sarvavedajño dūtān anuśaśāsa ca ।।
kṣipram ānayatāvyagrāḥ kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ hi naḥ ।। rathair aśvair gajaiś cāpi janānām upagacchatām ।। pratyanandan prakṛtayo yathā daśarathaṃ tathā ।। daśarathasutaśobhitā sabhā sadaśaratheva babhau yathā purā ।।
dadarśa buddhisampannaḥ pūrṇacandrāṃ niśām iva ।। adṛśyata ghanāpāye pūrṇacandreva śarvarī ।। idaṃ purohito vākyaṃ bharataṃ mṛdu cābravīt ।। dhanadhānyavatīṃ sphītāṃ pradāya pṛthivīṃ tava ।।
nājahāt pitur ādeśaṃ śaśī jyotsnām ivoditaḥ ।। tad bhuṅkṣva muditāmātyaḥ kṣipram evābhiṣecaya ।। koṭyāparāntāḥ sāmudrā ratnāny abhiharantu te ।। jagāma manasā rāmaṃ dharmajño dharmakāṅkṣayā ।।
vilalāpa sabhāmadhye jagarhe ca purohitam ।। dharme prayatamānasya ko rājyaṃ madvidho haret ।। rājyaṃ cāhaṃ ca rāmasya dharmaṃ vaktum ihārhasi ।। labdhum arhati kākutstho rājyaṃ daśaratho yathā ।।
ikṣvākūṇām ahaṃ loke bhaveyaṃ kulapāṃsanaḥ ।। ihastho vanadurgasthaṃ namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। trayāṇām api lokānāṃ rāghavo rājyam arhati ।। harṣān mumucur aśrūṇi rāme nihitacetasaḥ ।।
vane tatraiva vatsyāmi yathāryo lakṣmaṇas tathā ।। samakṣam āryamiśrāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ guṇavartinām ।। samīpastham uvācedaṃ sumantraṃ mantrakovidam ।। yātrām ājñāpaya kṣipraṃ balaṃ caiva samānaya ।।
prahṛṣṭaḥ so adiśat sarvaṃ yathā saṃdiṣṭam iṣṭavat ।। śrutvā yātrāṃ samājñaptāṃ rāghavasya nivartane ।। yātrāgamanam ājñāya tvarayanti sma harṣitāḥ ।। saha yodhair balādhyakṣā balaṃ sarvam acodayan ।।
rathaṃ me tvarayasveti sumantraṃ pārśvato abravīt ।। rathaṃ gṛhītvā prayayau yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ ।। guruṃ mahāraṇyagataṃ yaśasvinaṃ prasādayiṣyan bharato abravīt tadā ।। ānetum icchāmi hi taṃ vanasthaṃ prasādya rāmaṃ jagato hitāya ।।
śaśāsa sarvān prakṛtipradhānān balasya mukhyāṃś ca suhṛjjanaṃ ca ।। ayūyujann uṣṭrarathān kharāṃś ca nāgān hayāṃś caiva kulaprasūtān ।। prayayau bharataḥ śīghraṃ rāmadarśanakāṅkṣayā ।। adhiruhya hayair yuktān rathān sūryarathopamān ।।
anvayur bharataṃ yāntam ikṣvākukulanandanam ।। anvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam ।। anvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam ।। rāmānayanasaṃhṛṣṭā yayur yānena bhāsvatā ।।
tasyaiva ca kathāś citrāḥ kurvāṇā hṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। kadā drakṣyāmahe rāmaṃ jagataḥ śokanāśanam ।। tamaḥ sarvasya lokasya samudyann iva bhāskaraḥ ।। pariṣvajānāś cānyonyaṃ yayur nāgarikās tadā ।।
rāmaṃ prati yayur hṛṣṭāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayas tadā ।। sūtrakarmakṛtaś caiva ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ ।। dantakārāḥ sudhākārās tathā gandhopajīvinaḥ ।। snāpakācchādakā vaidyā dhūpakāḥ śauṇḍikās tathā ।।
śailūṣāś ca saha strībhir yānti kaivartakās tathā ।। gorathair bharataṃ yāntam anujagmuḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। sarve te vividhair yānaiḥ śanair bharatam anvayuḥ ।। vyavātiṣṭhata sā senā bharatasyānuyāyinī ।।
bharataḥ sacivān sarvān abravīd vākyakovidaḥ ।। viśrāntāḥ pratariṣyāmaḥ śva idānīṃ mahānadīm ।। aurdhvadehanimittārtham avatīryodakaṃ nadīm ।। nyaveśayaṃs tāṃś chandena svena svena pṛthakpṛthak ।।
uvāsa rāmasya tadā mahātmano vicintayāno bharato nivartanam ।। niṣādarājo dṛṣṭvaiva jñātīn saṃtvarito abravīt ।। nāsyāntam avagacchāmi manasāpi vicintayan ।। bandhayiṣyati vā dāśān atha vāsmān vadhiṣyati ।।
bharataḥ kaikeyīputro hantuṃ samadhigacchati ।। tasyārthakāmāḥ saṃnaddhā gaṅgānūpe atra tiṣṭhata ।। balayuktā nadīrakṣā māṃsamūlaphalāśanāḥ ।। saṃnaddhānāṃ tathā yūnāṃ tiṣṭhantv ity abhyacodayat ।।
seyaṃ svastimayī senā gaṅgām adya tariṣyati ।। abhicakrāma bharataṃ niṣādādhipatir guhaḥ ।। bharatāyācacakṣe atha vinayajño vinītavat ।। kuśalo daṇḍakāraṇye vṛddho bhrātuś ca te sakhā ।।
asaṃśayaṃ vijānīte yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। uvāca vacanaṃ śīghraṃ guhaḥ paśyatu mām iti ।। āgamya bharataṃ prahvo guho vacanam abravīt ।। nivedayāmas te sarve svake dāśakule vasa ।।
ārdraṃ ca māṃsaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca vanyaṃ coccāvacaṃ mahat ।। arcito vividhaiḥ kāmaiḥ śvaḥ sasainyo gamiṣyasi ।। pratyuvāca mahāprājño vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitam ।। yo me tvam īdṛśīṃ senām eko abhyarcitum icchasi ।।
abravīd bharataḥ śrīmān niṣādādhipatiṃ punaḥ ।। gahano ayaṃ bhṛśaṃ deśo gaṅgānūpo duratyayaḥ ।। abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ guho gahanagocaraḥ ।। ahaṃ cānugamiṣyāmi rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ ।।
iyaṃ te mahatī senā śaṅkāṃ janayatīva me ।। bharataḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā guhaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। rāghavaḥ sa hi me bhrātā jyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛsamo mama ।। buddhir anyā na te kāryā guha satyaṃ bravīmi te ।।
punar evābravīd vākyaṃ bharataṃ prati harṣitaḥ ।। ayatnād āgataṃ rājyaṃ yas tvaṃ tyaktum ihecchasi ।। yas tvaṃ kṛcchragataṃ rāmaṃ pratyānayitum icchasi ।। babhau naṣṭaprabhaḥ sūryo rajanī cābhyavartata ।।
śatrughnena saha śrīmāñ śayanaṃ punar āgamat ।। upasthito hy anarhasya dharmaprekṣasya tādṛśaḥ ।। vanadāhābhisaṃtaptaṃ gūḍho agnir iva pādapam ।। yathā sūryāṃśusaṃtapto himavān prasruto himam ।।
dainyapādapasaṃghena śokāyāsādhiśṛṅgiṇā ।। ākrānto duḥkhaśailena mahatā kaikayīsutaḥ ।। sudurmanās taṃ bharataṃ tadā punar guhaḥ samāśvāsayad agrajaṃ prati ।। bharatāyāprameyāya guho gahanagocaraḥ ।।
bhrātṛguptyartham atyantam ahaṃ lakṣmaṇam abruvam ।। pratyāśvasihi śeṣvāsyāṃ sukhaṃ rāghavanandana ।। dharmātmaṃs tasya guptyarthaṃ jāgariṣyāmahe vayam ।। motsuko bhūr bravīmy etad apy asatyaṃ tavāgrataḥ ।।
dharmāvāptiṃ ca vipulām arthāvāptiṃ ca kevalām ।। rakṣiṣyāmi dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sarvaiḥ svair jñātibhiḥ saha ।। caturaṅgaṃ hy api balaṃ prasahema vayaṃ yudhi ।। anunītā vayaṃ sarve dharmam evānupaśyatā ।।
śakyā nidrā mayā labdhuṃ jīvitaṃ vā sukhāni vā ।। taṃ paśya guha saṃviṣṭaṃ tṛṇeṣu saha sītayā ।। eko daśarathasyaiṣa putraḥ sadṛśalakṣaṇaḥ ।। vidhavā medinī nūnaṃ kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati ।।
nirghoṣoparataṃ nūnam adya rājaniveśanam ।। nāśaṃse yadi te sarve jīveyuḥ śarvarīm imām ।। duḥkhitā yā tu kausalyā vīrasūr vinaśiṣyati ।। rājye rāmam anikṣipya pitā me vinaśiṣyati ।।
pretakāryeṣu sarveṣu saṃskariṣyanti bhūmipam ।। harmyaprāsādasampannāṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitām ।। sarvakalyāṇasampūrṇāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām ।। sukhitā vicariṣyanti rājadhānīṃ pitur mama ।।
nivṛtte samaye hy asmin sukhitāḥ praviśemahi ।। tiṣṭhato rājaputrasya śarvarī sātyavartata ।। asmin bhāgīrathītīre sukhaṃ saṃtāritau mayā ।। vareṣucāpāsidharau paraṃtapau vyavekṣamāṇau saha sītayā gatau ।।
dhyānaṃ jagāma tatraiva yatra tac chrutam apriyam ।। puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣas taruṇaḥ priyadarśanaḥ ।। papāta sahasā totrair hṛdi viddha iva dvipaḥ ।। pariṣvajya rurodoccair visaṃjñaḥ śokakarśitaḥ ।।
upavāsakṛśā dīnā bhartṛvyasanakarśitāḥ ।। kausalyā tv anusṛtyainaṃ durmanāḥ pariṣasvaje ।। paripapraccha bharataṃ rudantī śokalālasā ।। adya rājakulasyāsya tvadadhīnaṃ hi jīvitam ।।
vṛtte daśarathe rājñi nātha ekas tvam adya naḥ ।। putra vā hy ekaputrāyāḥ sahabhārye vanaṃ gate ।। kausalyāṃ parisāntvyedaṃ guhaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। asvapac chayane kasmin kiṃ bhuktvā guha śaṃsa me ।।
yadvidhaṃ pratipede ca rāme priyahite atithau ।। rāmāyābhyavahārārthaṃ bahu copahṛtaṃ mayā ।। na hi tat pratyagṛhṇāt sa kṣatradharmam anusmaran ।। iti tena vayaṃ rājann anunītā mahātmanā ।।
aupavāsyaṃ tadākārṣīd rāghavaḥ saha sītayā ।। vāgyatās te trayaḥ saṃdhyām upāsata samāhitāḥ ।। svayam ānīya barhīṃṣi kṣipraṃ rāghavakāraṇāt ।। prakṣālya ca tayoḥ pādāv apacakrāma lakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
yasmin rāmaś ca sītā ca rātriṃ tāṃ śayitāv ubhau ।। mahad dhanuḥ sajyam upohya lakṣmaṇo niśām atiṣṭhat parito asya kevalam ।। atandribhir jñātibhir āttakārmukair mahendrakalpaṃ paripālayaṃs tadā ।। iṅgudīmūlam āgamya rāmaśayyām avekṣya tām ।।
śarvarī śayitā bhūmāv idam asya vimarditam ।। jāto daśarathenorvyāṃ na rāmaḥ svaptum arhati ।। śayitvā puruṣavyāghraḥ kathaṃ śete mahītale ।। haimarājatabhaumeṣu varāstaraṇaśāliṣu ।।
pāṇḍurābhraprakāśeṣu śukasaṃgharuteṣu ca ।। mṛdaṅgavaraśabdaiś ca satataṃ pratibodhitaḥ ।। gāthābhir anurūpābhiḥ stutibhiś ca paraṃtapaḥ ।। muhyate khalu me bhāvaḥ svapno ayam iti me matiḥ ।।
yatra dāśarathī rāmo bhūmāv evaṃ śayīta saḥ ।। dayitā śayitā bhūmau snuṣā daśarathasya ca ।। sthaṇḍile kaṭhine sarvaṃ gātrair vimṛditaṃ tṛṇam ।। tatra tatra hi dṛśyante saktāḥ kanakabindavaḥ ।।
tathā hy ete prakāśante saktāḥ kauśeyatantavaḥ ।। sukumārī satī duḥkhaṃ na vijānāti maithilī ।। sarvalokapriyas tyaktvā rājyaṃ priyam anuttamam ।। sukhabhāgī ca duḥkhārhaḥ śayito bhuvi rāghavaḥ ।।
vayaṃ saṃśayitāḥ sarve hīnās tena mahātmanā ।। gate daśarathe svarge rāme cāraṇyam āśrite ।। vane api vasatas tasya bāhuvīryābhirakṣitām ।। apāvṛtapuradvārāṃ rājadhānīm arakṣitām ।।
śatravo nābhimanyante bhakṣān viṣakṛtān iva ।। phalamūlāśano nityaṃ jaṭācīrāṇi dhārayan ।। taṃ pratiśravam āmucya nāsya mithyā bhaviṣyati ।। lakṣmaṇena saha tv āryo ayodhyāṃ pālayiṣyati ।।
api me devatāḥ kuryur imaṃ satyaṃ manoratham ।। tato anuvatsyāmi cirāya rāghavaṃ vane vasan nārhati mām upekṣitum ।। bharataḥ kālyam utthāya śatrughnam idam abravīt ।। śīghram ānaya bhadraṃ te tārayiṣyati vāhinīm ।।
ity evam abravīd bhrātrā śatrughno api pracoditaḥ ।। āgamya prāñjaliḥ kāle guho bharatam abravīt ।। kaccic ca saha sainyasya tava sarvam anāmayam ।। rāmasyānuvaśo vākyaṃ bharato apīdam abravīt ।।
gaṅgāṃ tu naubhir bahvībhir dāśāḥ saṃtārayantu naḥ ।। pratipraviśya nagaraṃ taṃ jñātijanam abravīt ।। nāvaḥ samanukarṣadhvaṃ tārayiṣyāma vāhinīm ।। pañca nāvāṃ śatāny eva samāninyuḥ samantataḥ ।।
śobhamānāḥ patākinyo yuktavātāḥ susaṃhatāḥ ।। sanandighoṣāṃ kalyāṇīṃ guho nāvam upāharat ।। kausalyā ca sumitrā ca yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ ।। anantaraṃ rājadārās tathaiva śakaṭāpaṇāḥ ।।
bhāṇḍāni cādadānānāṃ ghoṣas tridivam aspṛśat ।। vahantyo janam ārūḍhaṃ tadā saṃpetur āśugāḥ ।। kaścit tatra vahanti sma yānayugyaṃ mahādhanam ।। nivṛttāḥ kāṇḍacitrāṇi kriyante dāśabandhubhiḥ ।।
tarantaḥ sma prakāśante sadhvajā iva parvatāḥ ।। anye kumbhaghaṭais terur anye teruś ca bāhubhiḥ ।। maitre muhūrte prayayau prayāgavanam uttamam ।। draṣṭuṃ bharadvājam ṛṣipravaryam ṛtvigvṛtaḥ san bharataḥ pratasthe ।।
balaṃ sarvam avasthāpya jagāma saha mantribhiḥ ।। vasāno vāsasī kṣaume purodhāya purohitam ।। mantriṇas tān avasthāpya jagāmānu purohitam ।। saṃcacālāsanāt tūrṇaṃ śiṣyān arghyam iti bruvan ।।
abudhyata mahātejāḥ sutaṃ daśarathasya tam ।। ānupūrvyāc ca dharmajñaḥ papraccha kuśalaṃ kule ।। jānan daśarathaṃ vṛttaṃ na rājānam udāharat ।। śarīre agniṣu vṛkṣeṣu śiṣyeṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu ।।
bharataṃ pratyuvācedaṃ rāghavasnehabandhanāt ।। etad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ na hi me śudhyate manaḥ ।। bhrātrā saha sabhāryo yaś ciraṃ pravrājito vanam ।। vanavāsī bhavetīha samāḥ kila caturdaśa ।।
akaṇṭakaṃ bhoktumanā rājyaṃ tasyānujasya ca ।। paryaśrunayano duḥkhād vācā saṃsajjamānayā ।। matto na doṣam āśaṅker naivaṃ mām anuśādhi hi ।। nāham etena tuṣṭaś ca na tad vacanam ādade ।।
pratinetum ayodhyāṃ ca pādau tasyābhivanditum ।। śaṃsa me bhagavan rāmaḥ kva samprati mahīpatiḥ ।। guruvṛttir damaś caiva sādhūnāṃ cānuyāyitā ।। apṛcchaṃ tvāṃ tavātyarthaṃ kīrtiṃ samabhivardhayan ।।
etaṃ me kuru suprājña kāmaṃ kāmārthakovida ।। cakāra buddhiṃ ca tadā mahāśrame niśānivāsāya narādhipātmajaḥ ।। bharataṃ kaikayīputram ātithyena nyamantrayat ।। pādyam arghyaṃ tathātithyaṃ vane yad upapadyate ।।
jāne tvāṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ tuṣyes tvaṃ yena kenacit ।। mama prītir yathārūpā tvam arho manujarṣabha ।। kasmān nehopayāto asi sabalaḥ puruṣarṣabha ।। sasainyo nopayāto asmi bhagavan bhagavadbhayāt ।।
pracchādya mahatīṃ bhūmiṃ bhagavann anuyānti mām ।। na hiṃsyur iti tenāham eka evāgatas tataḥ ।। tathā tu cakre bharataḥ senāyāḥ samupāgamam ।। ātithyasya kriyāhetor viśvakarmāṇam āhvayat ।।
ātithyaṃ kartum icchāmi tatra me saṃvidhīyatām ।। pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca samāyāntv adya sarvaśaḥ ।। aparāś codakaṃ śītam ikṣukāṇḍarasopamam ।। tathaivāpsaraso devīr gandharvīś cāpi sarvaśaḥ ।।
sarvās tumburuṇā sārdham āhvaye saparicchadāḥ ।। divyanārīphalaṃ śaśvat tat kauberam ihaiva tu ।। bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca coṣyaṃ ca lehyaṃ ca vividhaṃ bahu ।। surādīni ca peyāni māṃsāni vividhāni ca ।।
śikṣāsvarasamāyuktaṃ tapasā cābravīn muniḥ ।। ājagmus tāni sarvāṇi daivatāni pṛthakpṛthak ।। upaspṛśya vavau yuktyā supriyātmā sukhaḥ śivaḥ ।। devadundubhighoṣaś ca dikṣu sarvāsu śuśruve ।।
prajagur devagandharvā vīṇāḥ pramumucuḥ svarān ।। viveśoccāritaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ samo layaguṇānvitaḥ ।। dadarśa bhārataṃ sainyaṃ vidhānaṃ viśvakarmaṇaḥ ।। śādvalair bahubhiś channā nīlavaiḍūryasaṃnibhaiḥ ।।
āmalakyo babhūvuś ca cūtāś ca phalabhūṣaṇāḥ ।। ājagāma nadī divyā tīrajair bahubhir vṛtā ।। harmyaprāsādasaṃghātās toraṇāni śubhāni ca ।। śuklamālyakṛtākāraṃ divyagandhasamukṣitam ।।
divyaiḥ sarvarasair yuktaṃ divyabhojanavastravat ।। kḷptasarvāsanaṃ śrīmat svāstīrṇaśayanottamam ।। veśma tad ratnasampūrṇaṃ bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ ।। babhūvuś ca mudā yuktās taṃ dṛṣṭvā veśmasaṃvidhim ।।
bharato mantribhiḥ sārdham abhyavartata rājavat ।। vālavyajanam ādāya nyaṣīdat sacivāsane ।। tataḥ senāpatiḥ paścāt praśāstā ca niṣedatuḥ ।। upātiṣṭhanta bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt ।।
ramyāś cāvasathā divyā brahmaṇas tu prasādajāḥ ।। āgur viṃśatisāhasrā brahmaṇā prahitāḥ striyaḥ ।। āgur viṃśatisāhasrāḥ kuberaprahitāḥ striyaḥ ।। āgur viṃśatisāhasrā nandanād apsarogaṇāḥ ।।
ete gandharvarājāno bharatasyāgrato jaguḥ ।। upānṛtyaṃs tu bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt ।। prayāge tāny adṛśyanta bharadvājasya śāsanāt ।। aśvatthā nartakāś cāsan bharadvājasya tejasā ।।
prahṛṣṭās tatra saṃpetuḥ kubjā bhūtvātha vāmanāḥ ।। pramadāvigrahaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājāśrame avasan ।। māṃsāni ca sumedhyāni bhakṣyantāṃ yāvad icchatha ।। apy ekam ekaṃ puruṣaṃ pramadāḥ sapta cāṣṭa ca ।।
parimṛjya tathā nyāyaṃ pāyayanti varāṅganāḥ ।। ikṣvākuvarayodhānāṃ codayanto mahābalāḥ ।। mattapramattamuditā camūḥ sā tatra saṃbabhau ।। apsarogaṇasaṃyuktāḥ sainyā vācam udairayan ।।
kuśalaṃ bharatasyāstu rāmasyāstu tathā sukham ।। anāthās taṃ vidhiṃ labdhvā vācam etām udairayan ।। bharatasyānuyātāraḥ svargo ayam iti cābruvan ।। divyān udvīkṣya bhakṣyāṃs tān abhavad bhakṣaṇe matiḥ ।।
babhūvus te bhṛśaṃ tṛptāḥ sarve cāhatavāsasaḥ ।। babhūvuḥ subhṛtās tatra nānyo hy anyam akalpayat ।। rajasā dhvastakeśo vā naraḥ kaścid adṛśyata ।। phalaniryūhasaṃsiddhaiḥ sūpair gandharasānvitaiḥ ।।
dadṛśur vismitās tatra narā lauhīḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। tāś ca kāmadughā gāvo drumāś cāsan madhuścyutaḥ ।। prataptapiṭharaiś cāpi mārgamāyūrakaukkuṭaiḥ ।। yauvanasthasya gaurasya kapitthasya sugandhinaḥ ।।
babhūvuḥ pāyasasyānte śarkarāyāś ca saṃcayāḥ ।। dadṛśur bhājanasthāni tīrtheṣu saritāṃ narāḥ ।। śuklāṃś candanakalkāṃś ca samudgeṣv avatiṣṭhataḥ ।। pādukopānahāṃ caiva yugmān yatra sahasraśaḥ ।।
marmatrāṇāni citrāṇi śayanāny āsanāni ca ।। avagāhya sutīrthāṃś ca hradān sotpalapuṣkarān ।। nirvāpārthaṃ paśūnāṃ te dadṛśus tatra sarvaśaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvātithyaṃ kṛtaṃ tādṛg bharatasya maharṣiṇā ।।
bharadvājāśrame ramye sā rātrir vyatyavartata ।। bharadvājam anujñāpya tāś ca sarvā varāṅganāḥ ।। tathaiva divyā vividhāḥ sraguttamāḥ pṛthakprakīrṇā manujaiḥ pramarditāḥ ।। kṛtātithyo bharadvājaṃ kāmād abhijagāma ha ।।
hutāgnihotro bharataṃ bharadvājo abhyabhāṣata ।। samagras te janaḥ kaccid ātithye śaṃsa me anagha ।। āśramād abhiniṣkrāntam ṛṣim uttamatejasam ।। tarpitaḥ sarvakāmaiś ca sāmātyo balavat tvayā ।।
api preṣyān upādāya sarve sma susukhoṣitāḥ ।। samīpaṃ prasthitaṃ bhrātur maitreṇekṣasva cakṣuṣā ।। ācakṣva katamo mārgaḥ kiyān iti ca śaṃsa me ।। pratyuvāca mahātejā bharadvājo mahātapāḥ ।।
citrakūṭo giris tatra ramyanirdarakānanaḥ ।। puṣpitadrumasaṃchannā ramyapuṣpitakānanā ।। tayoḥ parṇakuṭī tāta tatra tau vasato dhruvam ।। vāhayasva mahābhāga tato drakṣyasi rāghavam ।।
hitvā yānāni yānārhā brāhmaṇaṃ paryavārayan ।। kausalyā tatra jagrāha karābhyāṃ caraṇau muneḥ ।। kaikeyī tasya jagrāha caraṇau savyapatrapā ।। adūrād bharatasyaiva tasthau dīnamanās tadā ।।
viśeṣaṃ jñātum icchāmi mātṝṇāṃ tava rāghava ।। uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā vākyaṃ vacanakovidaḥ ।। pitur hi mahiṣīṃ devīṃ devatām iva paśyasi ।। kausalyā suṣuve rāmaṃ dhātāram aditir yathā ।।
karṇikārasya śākheva śīrṇapuṣpā vanāntare ।। ubhau lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau vīrau satyaparākramau ।। rājā putravihīnaś ca svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ ।। yatomūlaṃ hi paśyāmi vyasanaṃ mahad ātmanaḥ ।।
sa niśaśvāsa tāmrākṣo nāgaḥ kruddha ivāsakṛt ।। pratyuvāca mahābuddhir idaṃ vacanam arthavat ।। rāmapravrājanaṃ hy etat sukhodarkaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। āmantrya bharataḥ sainyaṃ yujyatām ity acodayat ।।
adhyārohat prayāṇārthī bahūn bahuvidho janaḥ ।। jīmūtā iva gharmānte saghoṣāḥ sampratasthire ।। prayayuḥ sumahārhāṇi pādair eva padātayaḥ ।। rāmadarśanakāṅkṣiṇyaḥ prayayur muditās tadā ।।
āsthāya prayayau śrīmān bharataḥ saparicchadaḥ ।। vanāni tu vyatikramya juṣṭāni mṛgapakṣibhiḥ ।। mahad vanaṃ tat pravigāhamānā rarāja senā bharatasya tatra ।। arditā yūthapā mattāḥ sayūthāḥ sampradudruvuḥ ।।
dṛśyante vanarājīṣu giriṣv api nadīṣu ca ।। vṛto mahatyā nādinyā senayā caturaṅgayā ।। mahīṃ saṃchādayāmāsa prāvṛṣi dyām ivāmbudaḥ ।। anālakṣyā ciraṃ kālaṃ tasmin kāle babhūva bhūḥ ।।
uvāca bharataḥ śrīmān vasiṣṭhaṃ mantriṇāṃ varam ।। vyaktaṃ prāptāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ bharadvājo yam abravīt ।। etat prakāśate dūrān nīlameghanibhaṃ vanam ।। vāraṇair avamṛdyante māmakaiḥ parvatopamaiḥ ।।
nīlā ivātapāpāye toyaṃ toyadharā ghanāḥ ।। hayaiḥ samantād ākīrṇaṃ makarair iva sāgaram ।। vāyupraviddhāḥ śaradi megharājir ivāmbare ।। meghaprakāśaiḥ phalakair dākṣiṇātyā yathā narāḥ ।।
ayodhyeva janākīrṇā samprati pratibhāti mā ।। taṃ vahaty anilaḥ śīghraṃ kurvann iva mama priyam ।। etān saṃpatataḥ śīghraṃ paśya śatrughna kānane ।। etam āviśataḥ śailam adhivāsaṃ patatriṇām ।।
tāpasānāṃ nivāso ayaṃ vyaktaṃ svargapatho yathā ।। manojñarūpā lakṣyante kusumair iva citritāḥ ।। yathā tau puruṣavyāghrau dṛśyete rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। viviśus tad vanaṃ śūrā dhūmaṃ ca dadṛśus tataḥ ।।
nāmanuṣye bhavaty agnir vyaktam atraiva rāghavau ।। anye rāmopamāḥ santi vyaktam atra tapasvinaḥ ।। sainyān uvāca sarvāṃs tān amitrabalamardanaḥ ।। aham eva gamiṣyāmi sumantro gurur eva ca ।।
bharato yatra dhūmāgraṃ tatra dṛṣṭiṃ samādadhāt ।। babhūva hṛṣṭā nacireṇa jānatī priyasya rāmasya samāgamaṃ tadā ।। vaidehyāḥ priyamākāṅkṣan svaṃ ca cittaṃ vilobhayan ।। bhāryām amarasaṃkāśaḥ śacīm iva puraṃdaraḥ ।।
mano me bādhate dṛṣṭvā ramaṇīyam imaṃ girim ।। śikharaiḥ kham ivodviddhair dhātumadbhir vibhūṣitam ।। pītamāñjiṣṭhavarṇāś ca kecin maṇivaraprabhāḥ ।। virājante acalendrasya deśā dhātuvibhūṣitāḥ ।।
aduṣṭair bhāty ayaṃ śailo bahupakṣisamākulaḥ ।। aṅkolair bhavyatiniśair bilvatindukaveṇubhiḥ ।। badaryāmalakair nīpair vetradhanvanabījakaiḥ ।। evamādibhir ākīrṇaḥ śriyaṃ puṣyaty ayaṃ giriḥ ।।
kiṃnarān dvaṃdvaśo bhadre ramamāṇān manasvinaḥ ।। paśya vidyādharastrīṇāṃ krīḍoddeśān manoramān ।। sravadbhir bhāty ayaṃ śailaḥ sravan mada iva dvipaḥ ।। ghrāṇatarpaṇam abhyetya kaṃ naraṃ na praharṣayet ।।
lakṣmaṇena ca vatsyāmi na māṃ śokaḥ pradhakṣyati ।। vicitraśikhare hy asmin ratavān asmi bhāmini ।। pituś cānṛṇatā dharme bharatasya priyaṃ tathā ।। paśyantī vividhān bhāvān manovākkāyasaṃyatān ।।
vanavāsaṃ bhavārthāya pretya me prapitāmahāḥ ।। bahulā bahulair varṇair nīlapītasitāruṇaiḥ ।। oṣadhyaḥ svaprabhā lakṣmyā bhrājamānāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। kecid ekaśilā bhānti parvatasyāsya bhāmini ।।
citrakūṭasya kūṭo asau dṛśyate sarvataḥ śivaḥ ।। kāmināṃ svāstarān paśya kuśeśayadalāyutān ।। kāmibhir vanite paśya phalāni vividhāni ca ।। parvataś citrakūṭo asau bahumūlaphalodakaḥ ।।
ratiṃ prapatsye kuladharmavardhinīṃ satāṃ pathi svair niyamaiḥ paraiḥ sthitaḥ ।। adarśayac chubhajalāṃ ramyāṃ mandākinīṃ nadīm ।। videharājasya sutāṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।। kusumair upasaṃpannāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm ।।
rājantīṃ rājarājasya nalinīm iva sarvataḥ ।। tīrthāni ramaṇīyāni ratiṃ saṃjanayanti me ।। ṛṣayas tv avagāhante nadīṃ mandākinīṃ priye ।। ete apare viśālākṣi munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।।
pādapaiḥ pattrapuṣpāṇi sṛjadbhir abhito nadīm ।। kaccit siddhajanākīrṇāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm ।। poplūyamānān aparān paśya tvaṃ jalamadhyagān ।। adhirohanti kalyāṇi niṣkūjantaḥ śubhā giraḥ ।।
adhikaṃ puravāsāc ca manye ca tava darśanāt ।। nityavikṣobhitajalāṃ vigāhasva mayā saha ।। kamalāny avamajjantī puṣkarāṇi ca bhāmini ।। manyasva vanite nityaṃ sarayūvad imāṃ nadīm ।।
tvaṃ cānukūlā vaidehi prītiṃ janayatho mama ।। nāyodhyāyai na rājyāya spṛhaye adya tvayā saha ।। supuṣpitaiḥ puṣpadharair alaṃkṛtāṃ na so asti yaḥ syān na gatakramaḥ sukhī ।। cacāra ramyaṃ nayanāñjanaprabhaṃ sa citrakūṭaṃ raghuvaṃśavardhanaḥ ।।
sainyareṇuś ca śabdaś ca prādurāstāṃ nabhaḥspṛśau ।। arditā yūthapā mattāḥ sayūthā dudruvur diśaḥ ।। tāṃś ca vipradrutān sarvān yūthapān anvavaikṣata ।। uvāca rāmaḥ saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam ।।
bhīmastanitagambhīras tumulaḥ śrūyate svanaḥ ।। sarvam etad yathātattvam acirāj jñātum arhasi ।। prekṣamāṇo diśaḥ sarvāḥ pūrvāṃ diśam avaikṣata ।। rathāśvagajasambādhāṃ yattair yuktāṃ padātibhiḥ ।।
śaśaṃsa senāṃ rāmāya vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। sajyaṃ kuruṣva cāpaṃ ca śarāṃś ca kavacaṃ tathā ।। aṅgāvekṣasva saumitre kasyaitāṃ manyase camūm ।। didhakṣann iva tāṃ senāṃ ruṣitaḥ pāvako yathā ।।
āvāṃ hantuṃ samabhyeti kaikeyyā bharataḥ sutaḥ ।। virājaty udgataskandhaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathe ।। ete bhrājanti saṃhṛṣṭā gajān āruhya sādinaḥ ।। api nau vaśam āgacchet kovidāradhvajo raṇe ।।
tvayā rāghava samprāptaṃ sītayā ca mayā tathā ।। samprāpto ayam arir vīra bharato vadhya eva me ।। etasmin nihate kṛtsnām anuśādhi vasuṃdharām ।। mayā paśyet suduḥkhārtā hastibhagnam iva drumam ।।
kaluṣeṇādya mahatā medinī parimucyatām ।। mokṣyāmi śatrusainyeṣu kakṣeṣv iva hutāśanam ।। bhindañ śatruśarīrāṇi kariṣye śoṇitokṣitam ।। śvāpadāḥ parikarṣantu narāṃś ca nihatān mayā ।।
sasainyaṃ bharataṃ hatvā bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। rāmas tu parisāntvyātha vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। maheṣvāse mahāprājñe bharate svayam āgate ।। asmāsu manasāpy eṣa nāhitaṃ kiṃcid ācaret ।।
īdṛśaṃ vā bhayaṃ te adya bharataṃ yo atra śaṅkase ।। ahaṃ hy apriyam uktaḥ syāṃ bharatasyāpriye kṛte ।। bhrātā vā bhrātaraṃ hanyāt saumitre prāṇam ātmanaḥ ।। vakṣyāmi bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyam asmai pradīyatām ।।
rājyam asmai prayaccheti bāḍham ity eva vakṣyati ।। lakṣmaṇaḥ praviveśeva svāni gātrāṇi lajjayā ।। eṣa manye mahābāhur ihāsmān draṣṭum āgataḥ ।। imāṃ vāpy eṣa vaidehīm atyantasukhasevinīm ।।
vāyuvegasamau vīra javanau turagottamau ।। nāgaḥ śatruṃjayo nāma vṛddhas tātasya dhīmataḥ ।। lakṣmaṇaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā tasthau rāmasya pārśvataḥ ।। samantāt tasya śailasya senāvāsam akalpayat ।।
pārśve nyaviśad āvṛtya gajavājirathākulā ।। prasādanārthaṃ raghunandanasya virocate nītimatā praṇītā ।। abhigantuṃ sa kākutstham iyeṣa guruvartakam ।। bharato bhrātaraṃ vākyaṃ śatrughnam idam abravīt ।।
lubdhaiś ca sahitair ebhis tvam anveṣitum arhasi ।। vaidehīṃ vā mahābhāgāṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati ।। bhrātuḥ padmapalāśākṣaṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati ।। śirasā dhārayiṣyāmi na me śāntir bhaviṣyati ।।
abhiṣekajalaklinno na me śāntir bhaviṣyati ।। bhartāraṃ sāgarāntāyāḥ pṛthivyā yānugacchati ।। yasmin vasati kākutsthaḥ kubera iva nandane ।। yad adhyāste mahātejā rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।।
padbhyām eva mahātejāḥ praviveśa mahad vanam ।। puṣpitāgrāṇi madhyena jagāma vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। rāmāśramagatasyāgner dadarśa dhvajam ucchritam ।। atra rāma iti jñātvā gataḥ pāram ivāmbhasaḥ ।।
guhena sārdhaṃ tvarito jagāma punar niveśyaiva camūṃ mahātmā ।। jagāma bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ śatrughnam anudarśayan ।। iti tvaritam agre sa jagāma guruvatsalaḥ ।। rāmadarśanajas tarṣo bharatasyeva tasya ca ।।
bhrātuḥ parṇakuṭīṃ śrīmān uṭajaṃ ca dadarśa ha ।। kāṣṭhāni cāvabhagnāni puṣpāṇy avacitāni ca ।। mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca karīṣaiḥ śītakāraṇāt ।। śatrughnaṃ cābravīd dhṛṣṭas tān amātyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
nātidūre hi manye ahaṃ nadīṃ mandākinīm itaḥ ।। abhijñānakṛtaḥ panthā vikāle gantum icchatā ।। śailapārśve parikrāntam anyonyam abhigarjatām ।। tasyāsau dṛśyate dhūmaḥ saṃkulaḥ kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ ।।
āryaṃ drakṣyāmi saṃhṛṣṭo maharṣim iva rāghavam ।। mandākinīm anuprāptas taṃ janaṃ cedam abravīt ।। janendro nirjanaṃ prāpya dhin me janma sajīvitam ।। sarvān kāmān parityajya vane vasati rāghavaḥ ।।
rāmasya nipatiṣyāmi sītāyāś ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। dadarśa mahatīṃ puṇyāṃ parṇaśālāṃ manoramām ।। viśālāṃ mṛdubhis tīrṇāṃ kuśair vedim ivādhvare ।। rukmapṛṣṭhair mahāsāraiḥ śobhitāṃ śatrubādhakaiḥ ।।
śobhitāṃ dīptavadanaiḥ sarpair bhogavatīm iva ।। rukmabinduvicitrābhyāṃ carmabhyāṃ cāpi śobhitām ।। arisaṃghair anādhṛṣyāṃ mṛgaiḥ siṃhaguhām iva ।। dadarśa bharatas tatra puṇyāṃ rāmaniveśane ।।
uṭaje rāmam āsīnaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇam ।। dadarśa rāmam āsīnam abhitaḥ pāvakopamam ।। pṛthivyāḥ sagarāntāyā bhartāraṃ dharmacāriṇam ।। sthaṇḍile darbhasaṃstīrṇe sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca ।।
abhyadhāvata dharmātmā bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ ।। aśaknuvan dhārayituṃ dhairyād vacanam abravīt ।। vanyair mṛgair upāsīnaḥ so ayam āste mamāgrajaḥ ।। mṛgājine so ayam iha pravaste dharmam ācaran ।।
so ayaṃ jaṭābhāram imaṃ sahate rāghavaḥ katham ।। śarīrakleśasambhūtaṃ sa dharmaṃ parimārgate ।। malena tasyāṅgam idaṃ katham āryasya sevyate ।। dhig jīvitaṃ nṛśaṃsasya mama lokavigarhitam ।।
pādāv aprāpya rāmasya papāta bharato rudan ।। uktvāryeti sakṛd dīnaṃ punar novāca kiṃcana ।। āryety evābhisaṃkruśya vyāhartuṃ nāśakat tataḥ ।। tāv ubhau sa samāliṅgya rāmo apy aśrūṇy avartayat ।।
divākaraś caiva niśākaraś ca yathāmbare śukrabṛhaspatibhyām ।। vanaukasas te api samīkṣya sarve apy aśrūṇy amuñcan pravihāya harṣam ।। aṅke bharatam āropya paryapṛcchat samāhitaḥ ।। na hi tvaṃ jīvatas tasya vanam āgantum arhasi ।।
duṣpratīkam araṇye asmin kiṃ tāta vanam āgataḥ ।। rājasūyāśvamedhānām āhartā dharmaniścayaḥ ।। ikṣvākūṇām upādhyāyo yathāvat tāta pūjyate ।। sukhinī kaccid āryā ca devī nandati kaikayī ।।
anasūyur anudraṣṭā satkṛtas te purohitaḥ ।। hutaṃ ca hoṣyamāṇaṃ ca kāle vedayate sadā ।। sudhanvānam upādhyāyaṃ kaccit tvaṃ tāta manyase ।। kulīnāś ceṅgitajñāś ca kṛtās te tāta mantriṇaḥ ।।
susaṃvṛto mantradharair amātyaiḥ śāstrakovidaiḥ ।। kaccic cāpararātriṣu cintayasy arthanaipuṇam ।। kaccit te mantrito mantro rāṣṭraṃ na paridhāvati ।। kṣipram ārabhase kartuṃ na dīrghayasi rāghava ।।
vidus te sarvakāryāṇi na kartavyāni pārthivāḥ ।। tvayā vā tava vāmātyair budhyate tāta mantritam ।। paṇḍito hy arthakṛcchreṣu kuryān niḥśreyasaṃ mahat ।। atha vāpy ayutāny eva nāsti teṣu sahāyatā ।।
rājānaṃ rājamātraṃ vā prāpayen mahatīṃ śriyam ।। jaghanyāś ca jaghanyeṣu bhṛtyāḥ karmasu yojitāḥ ।। śreṣṭhāñ śreṣṭheṣu kaccit tvaṃ niyojayasi karmasu ।। ugrapratigrahītāraṃ kāmayānam iva striyaḥ ।।
śūram aiśvaryakāmaṃ ca yo na hanti sa vadhyate ।। kulīnaś cānuraktaś ca dakṣaḥ senāpatiḥ kṛtaḥ ।। dṛṣṭāpadānā vikrāntās tvayā satkṛtya mānitāḥ ।। samprāptakālaṃ dātavyaṃ dadāsi na vilambase ।।
bhartuḥ kupyanti duṣyanti so anarthaḥ sumahān smṛtaḥ ।। kaccit prāṇāṃs tavārtheṣu saṃtyajanti samāhitāḥ ।। yathoktavādī dūtas te kṛto bharata paṇḍitaḥ ।। tribhis tribhir avijñātair vetsi tīrthāni cārakaiḥ ।।
durbalān anavajñāya vartase ripusūdana ।। anarthakuśalā hy ete bālāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ ।। buddhimān vīkṣikīṃ prāpya nirarthaṃ pravadanti te ।। satyanāmāṃ dṛḍhadvārāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṃkulām ।।
jitendriyair mahotsāhair vṛtām āryaiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। kaccit samuditāṃ sphītām ayodhyāṃ parirakṣasi ।। devasthānaiḥ prapābhiś ca taḍāgaiś copaśobhitaḥ ।। sukṛṣṭasīmā paśumān hiṃsābhir parivarjitaḥ ।।
kaccij janapadaḥ sphītaḥ sukhaṃ vasati rāghava ।। vārttāyāṃ saṃśritas tāta loko hi sukham edhate ।। rakṣyā hi rājñā dharmeṇa sarve viṣayavāsinaḥ ।। kaccin na śraddadhāsyāsāṃ kaccid guhyaṃ na bhāṣase ।।
utthāyotthāya pūrvāhṇe rājaputro mahāpathe ।। yantraiś ca paripūrṇāni tathā śilpidhanurdharaiḥ ।। apātreṣu na te kaccit kośo gacchati rāghava ।। yodheṣu mitravargeṣu kaccid gacchati te vyayaḥ ।।
apṛṣṭaḥ śāstrakuśalair na lobhād badhyate śuciḥ ।। kaccin na mucyate coro dhanalobhān nararṣabha ।। arthaṃ virāgāḥ paśyanti tavāmātyā bahuśrutāḥ ।। tāni putrapaśūn ghnanti prītyartham anuśāsataḥ ।।
dānena manasā vācā tribhir etair bubhūṣase ।। caityāṃś ca sarvān siddhārthān brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyasi ।। ubhau vā prītilobhena kāmena na vibādhase ।। vibhajya kāle kālajña sarvān bharata sevase ।।
āśaṃsante mahāprājña paurajānapadaiḥ saha ।। adarśanaṃ jñānavatām ālasyaṃ pañcavṛttitām ।। niścitānām anārambhaṃ mantrasyāparirakṣaṇam ।। kaccit tvaṃ varjayasy etān rājadoṣāṃś caturdaśa ।।
kaccid āśaṃsamānebhyo mitrebhyaḥ samprayacchasi ।। kiṃ me dharmād vihīnasya rājadharmaḥ kariṣyati ।। jyeṣṭhaputre sthite rājan na kanīyān bhaven nṛpaḥ ।। abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ kulasyāsya bhavāya naḥ ।।
yasya dharmārthasahitaṃ vṛttam āhur amānuṣam ।। divam ārya gato rājā yāyajūkaḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।। ahaṃ cāyaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ pūrvam eva kṛtodakau ।। akṣayyaṃ bhavatīty āhur bhavāṃś caiva pituḥ priyaḥ ।।
rāghavo bharatenoktāṃ babhūva gatacetanaḥ ।। vane paraśunā kṛttas tathā bhuvi papāta ha ।। kūlaghātapariśrāntaṃ prasuptam iva kuñjaram ।। rudantaḥ saha vaidehyā siṣicuḥ salilena vai ।।
upākrāmata kākutsthaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bahubhāṣitum ।। yo mṛto mama śokena na mayā cāpi saṃskṛtaḥ ।। śatrugheṇa ca sarveṣu pretakṛtyeṣu satkṛtaḥ ।। nivṛttavanavāso api nāyodhyāṃ gantum utsahe ।।
ko nu śāsiṣyati punas tāte lokāntaraṃ gate ।। vākyāni tāni śroṣyāmi kutaḥ karṇasukhāny aham ।। uvāca śokasaṃtaptaḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanām ।। bharato duḥkham ācaṣṭe svargataṃ pṛthivīpatim ।।
uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ tatra duḥkhito duḥkhitaṃ vacaḥ ।। jalakriyārthaṃ tātasya gamiṣyāmi mahātmanaḥ ।। ahaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmi gatir hy eṣā sudāruṇā ।। mṛdur dāntaś ca śāntaś ca rāme ca dṛḍhabhaktimān ।।
avātārayad ālambya nadīṃ mandākinīṃ śivām ।। nadīṃ mandākinīṃ ramyāṃ sadā puṣpitakānanām ।। siṣicus tūdakaṃ rājñe tata etad bhavatv iti ।। diśaṃ yāmyām abhimukho rudan vacanam abravīt ।।
pitṛlokagatasyādya maddattam upatiṣṭhatu ।। pituś cakāra tejasvī nivāpaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ।। nyasya rāmaḥ suduḥkhārto rudan vacanam abravīt ।। yadannaḥ puruṣo bhavati tadannās tasya devatāḥ ।।
āruroha naravyāghro ramyasānuṃ mahīdharam ।। parijagrāha pāṇibhyām ubhau bharatalakṣmaṇau ।। bhrātṝṇāṃ saha vaidehyā siṃhānāṃ nardatām iva ।। teṣām eva mahāñ śabdaḥ śocatāṃ pitaraṃ mṛtam ।।
apy ekamanaso jagmur yathāsthānaṃ pradhāvitāḥ ।। sukumārās tathaivānye padbhir eva narā yayuḥ ।। draṣṭukāmo janaḥ sarvo jagāma sahasāśramam ।। yayur bahuvidhair yānaiḥ khuranemisamākulaiḥ ।।
mumoca tumulaṃ śabdaṃ dyaur ivābhrasamāgame ।। āvāsayanto gandhena jagmur anyad vanaṃ tataḥ ।। vyāghragokarṇagavayā vitreṣuḥ pṛṣataiḥ saha ।। tathā puṃskokilāḥ krauñcā visaṃjñā bhejire diśaḥ ।।
manuṣyair āvṛtā bhūmir ubhayaṃ prababhau tadā ।। paryaṣvajata dharmajñaḥ pitṛvan mātṛvac ca saḥ ।। cakāra sarvān savayasyabāndhavān yathārham āsādya tadā nṛpātmajaḥ ।। guhā girīṇāṃ ca diśaś ca saṃtataṃ mṛdaṅgaghoṣapratimo viśuśruve ।।
abhicakrāma taṃ deśaṃ rāmadarśanatarṣitaḥ ।। dadṛśus tatra tat tīrthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇasevitam ।। sumitrām abravīd dīnā yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ ।। vane prāk kevalaṃ tīrthaṃ ye te nirviṣayīkṛtāḥ ।।
svayaṃ harati saumitrir mama putrasya kāraṇāt ।। pitur iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ nyastam āyatalocanā ।। uvāca devī kausalyā sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ ।। rāghaveṇa pitur dattaṃ paśyataitad yathāvidhi ।।
naitad aupayikaṃ manye bhuktabhogasya bhojanam ।। katham iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ sa bhuṅkte vasudhādhipaḥ ।। yatra rāmaḥ pitur dadyād iṅgudīkṣodam ṛddhimān ।। kathaṃ duḥkhena hṛdayaṃ na sphoṭati sahasradhā ।।
dadṛśuś cāśrame rāmaṃ svargāc cyutam ivāmaram ।। ārtā mumucur aśrūṇi sasvaraṃ śokakarśitāḥ ।। mātṝṇāṃ manujavyāghraḥ sarvāsāṃ satyasaṃgaraḥ ।। pramamārjū rajaḥ pṛṣṭhād rāmasyāyatalocanāḥ ।।
abhyavādayatāsaktaṃ śanai rāmād anantaram ।। vṛttiṃ daśarathāj jāte lakṣmaṇe śubhalakṣaṇe ।। śvaśrūṇām aśrupūrṇākṣī sā babhūvāgrataḥ sthitā ।। vanavāsakṛśāṃ dīnāṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt ।।
rāmapatnī kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ samprāptā nirjane vane ।। kāñcanaṃ rajasā dhvastaṃ kliṣṭaṃ candram ivāmbudaiḥ ।। bhṛśaṃ manasi vaidehi vyasanāraṇisambhavaḥ ।। pādāv āsādya jagrāha vasiṣṭhasya sa rāghavaḥ ।।
pragṛhya pādau susamṛddhatejasaḥ sahaiva tenopaviveśa rāghavaḥ ।। janena dharmajñatamena dharmavān upopaviṣṭo bharatas tadāgrajam ।। śriyā jvalantaṃ bharataḥ kṛtāñjalir yathā mahendraḥ prayataḥ prajāpatim ।। itīva tasyāryajanasya tattvato babhūva kautūhalam uttamaṃ tadā ।।
vṛtāḥ suhṛdbhiś ca virejur adhvare yathā sadasyaiḥ sahitās trayo agnayaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame ।। yasmāt tvam āgato deśam imaṃ cīrajaṭājinī ।। hitvā rājyaṃ praviṣṭas tvaṃ tat sarvaṃ vaktum arhasi ।।
pragṛhya balavad bhūyaḥ prāñjalir vākyam abravīt ।। gataḥ svargaṃ mahābāhuḥ putraśokābhipīḍitaḥ ।। cakāra sumahat pāpam idam ātmayaśoharam ।। patiṣyati mahāghore niraye jananī mama ।।
abhiṣiñcasva cādyaiva rājyena maghavān iva ।। tvatsakāśam anuprāptāḥ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi ।। rājyaṃ prāpnuhi dharmeṇa sakāmān suhṛdaḥ kuru ।। śaśinā vimaleneva śāradī rajanī yathā ।।
bhrātuḥ śiṣyasya dāsasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi ।। pūjitaṃ puruṣavyāghra nātikramitum utsahe ।। rāmasya śirasā pādau jagrāha bharataḥ punaḥ ।। bhrātaraṃ bharataṃ rāmaḥ pariṣvajyedam abravīt ।।
rājyahetoḥ kathaṃ pāpam ācaret tvadvidho janaḥ ।। na cāpi jananīṃ bālyāt tvaṃ vigarhitum arhasi ।। tāvad dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha jananyām api gauravam ।। mātāpitṛbhyām ukto ahaṃ katham anyat samācare ।।
vastavyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye mayā valkalavāsasā ।। vyādiśya ca mahātejā divaṃ daśaratho gataḥ ।। pitrā dattaṃ yathābhāgam upabhoktuṃ tvam arhasi ।। upabhokṣye tv ahaṃ dattaṃ bhāgaṃ pitrā mahātmanā ।।
tad eva manye paramātmano hitaṃ na sarvalokeśvarabhāvam avyayam ।। śocatām eva rajanī duḥkhena vyatyavartata ।। mandākinyāṃ hutaṃ japyaṃ kṛtvā rāmam upāgaman ।। bharatas tu suhṛnmadhye rāmaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
tad dadāmi tavaivāhaṃ bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam ।। durāvāraṃ tvadanyena rājyakhaṇḍam idaṃ mahat ।। anugantuṃ na śaktir me gatiṃ tava mahīpate ।। rāma tena tu durjīvaṃ yaḥ parān upajīvati ।।
hrasvakena durāroho rūḍhaskandho mahādrumaḥ ।। sa tāṃ nānubhavet prītiṃ yasya hetoḥ prabhāvitaḥ ।। yadi tvam asmān ṛṣabho bhartā bhṛtyān na śādhi hi ।। pratapantam ivādityaṃ rājye sthitam ariṃdamam ।।
antaḥpuragatā nāryo nandantu susamāhitāḥ ।। bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaṃ pratyanuyācataḥ ।। rāmaḥ kṛtātmā bharataṃ samāśvāsayad ātmavān ।। itaś cetarataś cainaṃ kṛtāntaḥ parikarṣati ।।
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam ।। evaṃ narasya jātasya nānyatra maraṇād bhayam ।। tathāvasīdanti narā jarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ gatāḥ ।। āyūṃṣi kṣapayanty āśu grīṣme jalam ivāṃśavaḥ ।।
āyus te hīyate yasya sthitasya ca gatasya ca ।। gatvā sudīrgham adhvānaṃ saha mṛtyur nivartate ।। jarayā puruṣo jīrṇaḥ kiṃ hi kṛtvā prabhāvayet ।। ātmano nāvabudhyante manuṣyā jīvitakṣayam ।।
ṛtūnāṃ parivartena prāṇināṃ prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। sametya ca vyapeyātāṃ kālam āsādya kaṃcana ।। sametya vyavadhāvanti dhruvo hy eṣāṃ vinābhavaḥ ।। tena tasmin na sāmarthyaṃ pretasyāsty anuśocataḥ ।।
aham apy āgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhato bhavatām iti ।। tam āpannaḥ kathaṃ śoced yasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ ।। ātmā sukhe niyoktavyaḥ sukhabhājaḥ prajāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dhūtapāpo gataḥ svargaṃ pitā naḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।।
arthādānāc ca dhārmeṇa pitā nas tridivaṃ gataḥ ।। uttamaṃ cāyur āsādya svar gataḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। daivīm ṛddhim anuprāpto brahmalokavihāriṇīm ।। tvadvidho yadvidhaś cāpi śrutavān buddhimattaraḥ ।।
varjanīyā hi dhīreṇa sarvāvasthāsu dhīmatā ।। tathā pitrā niyukto asi vaśinā vadatāṃ vara ।। tatraivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi pitur āryasya śāsanam ।। tat tvayāpi sadā mānyaṃ sa vai bandhuḥ sa naḥ pitā ।।
uvāca bharataś citraṃ dhārmiko dhārmikaṃ vacaḥ ।। na tvāṃ pravyathayed duḥkhaṃ prītir vā na praharṣayet ।। yathā mṛtas tathā jīvan yathāsati tathā sati ।। sa evaṃ vyasanaṃ prāpya na viṣīditum arhati ।।
sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca buddhimāṃś cāsi rāghava ।। aviṣahyatamaṃ duḥkham āsādayitum arhati ।। kṣudrayā tad aniṣṭaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān mama ।। hanmi tīvreṇa daṇḍena daṇḍārhāṃ pāpakāriṇīm ।।
jānan dharmam adharmiṣṭhaṃ kuryāṃ karma jugupsitam ।। tātaṃ na parigarheyaṃ daivataṃ ceti saṃsadi ।। striyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ san kuryād dharmajña dharmavit ।। rājñaivaṃ kurvatā loke pratyakṣā sā śrutiḥ kṛtā ।।
tātasya yad atikrāntaṃ pratyāharatu tad bhavān ।। tad apatyaṃ mataṃ loke viparītam ato anyathā ।। abhipattā kṛtaṃ karma loke dhīravigarhitam ।। paurajānapadān sarvāṃs trātu sarvam idaṃ bhavān ।।
īdṛśaṃ vyāhataṃ karma na bhavān kartum arhati ।। dharmeṇa caturo varṇān pālayan kleśam āpnuhi ।। āhur dharmajña dharmajñās taṃ kathaṃ tyaktum arhasi ।। sa kathaṃ pālayiṣyāmi bhūmiṃ bhavati tiṣṭhati ।।
bhavatā ca vinā bhūto na vartayitum utsahe ।। anuśādhi svadharmeṇa dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ ।। ṛtvijaḥ savasiṣṭhāś ca mantravan mantrakovidāḥ ।। vijitya tarasā lokān marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ ।।
suhṛdas tarpayan kāmais tvam evātrānuśādhi mām ।। adya bhītāḥ pālayantāṃ durhṛdas te diśo daśa ।। adya tatra bhavantaṃ ca pitaraṃ rakṣa kilbiṣāt ।। bāndhaveṣu ca sarveṣu bhūteṣv iva maheśvaraḥ ।।
gamiṣyati gamiṣyāmi bhavatā sārdham apy aham ।। na caiva cakre gamanāya sattvavān matiṃ pitus tadvacane pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। na yāty ayodhyām iti duḥkhito abhavat sthirapratijñatvam avekṣya harṣitaḥ ।। tathā bruvāṇaṃ bharataṃ pratuṣṭuvuḥ praṇamya rāmaṃ ca yayācire saha ।।
pratyuvāca tataḥ śrīmāñ jñātimadhye atisatkṛtaḥ ।। jātaḥ putro daśarathāt kaikeyyāṃ rājasattamāt ।। mātāmahe samāśrauṣīd rājyaśulkam anuttamam ।। samprahṛṣṭo dadau rājā varam ārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
ayācata naraśreṣṭhaṃ dvau varau varavarṇinī ।। tac ca rājā tathā tasyai niyuktaḥ pradadau varam ।। caturdaśa vane vāsaṃ varṣāṇi varadānikam ।। śītayā cāpratidvandvaḥ satyavāde sthitaḥ pituḥ ।।
kartum arhati rājendraṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecanāt ।। pitaraṃ trāhi dharmajña mātaraṃ cābhinandaya ।। gayena yajamānena gayeṣv eva pitṝn prati ।। tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ pitṝn yat pāti vā sutaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ vai samavetānām api kaścid gayāṃ vrajet ।। tasmāt trāhi naraśreṣṭha pitaraṃ narakāt prabho ।। śatrughnasahito vīra saha sarvair dvijātibhiḥ ।। ābhyāṃ tu sahito rājan vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca ।।
gaccha tvaṃ puravaram adya samprahṛṣṭaḥ saṃhṛṣṭas tv aham api daṇḍakān pravekṣye ।। eteṣām aham api kānanadrumāṇāṃ chāyāṃ tām atiśayinīṃ sukhaṃ śrayiṣye ।। catvāras tanayavarā vayaṃ narendraṃ satyasthaṃ bharata carāma mā viṣādam ।। uvāca rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmāpetam idaṃ vacaḥ ।।
prākṛtasya narasyeva āryabuddhes tapasvinaḥ ।। yad eko jāyate jantur eka eva vinaśyati ।। unmatta iva sa jñeyo nāsti kāciddhi kasyacit ।। utsṛjya ca tam āvāsaṃ pratiṣṭhetāpare ahani ।।
āvāsamātraṃ kākutstha sajjante nātra sajjanāḥ ।। āsthātuṃ kāpathaṃ duḥkhaṃ viṣamaṃ bahukaṇṭakam ।। ekaveṇīdharā hi tvāṃ nagarī sampratīkṣate ।। vihara tvam ayodhyāyāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭape ।।
anyo rājā tvam anyaś ca tasmāt kuru yad ucyate ।। pravṛttir eṣā martyānāṃ tvaṃ tu mithyā vihanyase ।। te hi duḥkham iha prāpya vināśaṃ pretya bhejire ।। annasyopadravaṃ paśya mṛto hi kim aśiṣyati ।।
dadyāt pravasataḥ śrāddhaṃ na tat pathy aśanaṃ bhavet ।। yajasva dehi dīkṣasva tapas tapyasva saṃtyaja ।। pratyakṣaṃ yat tad ātiṣṭha parokṣaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kuru ।। rājyaṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva bharatena prasāditaḥ ।।
uvāca parayā yuktyā svabuddhyā cāvipannayā ।। akāryaṃ kāryasaṃkāśam apathyaṃ pathyasaṃmitam ।। mānaṃ na labhate satsu bhinnacāritradarśanaḥ ।। cāritram eva vyākhyāti śuciṃ vā yadi vāśucim ।।
lakṣaṇyavad alakṣaṇyo duḥśīlaḥ śīlavān iva ।। abhipatsye śubhaṃ hitvā kriyāvidhivivarjitam ।। bahu maṃsyati māṃ loke durvṛttaṃ lokadūṣaṇam ।। anayā vartamāno ahaṃ vṛttyā hīnapratijñayā ।।
yadvṛttāḥ santi rājānas tadvṛttāḥ santi hi prajāḥ ।। tasmāt satyātmakaṃ rājyaṃ satye lokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। satyavādī hi loke asmin paramaṃ gacchati kṣayam ।। dharmaḥ satyaṃ paro loke mūlaṃ svargasya cocyate ।।
satyamūlāni sarvāṇi satyān nāsti paraṃ padam ।। vedāḥ satyapratiṣṭhānās tasmāt satyaparo bhavet ।। majjaty eko hi niraya ekaḥ svarge mahīyate ।। satyapratiśravaḥ satyaṃ satyena samayīkṛtaḥ ।।
setuṃ satyasya bhetsyāmi guroḥ satyapratiśravaḥ ।। naiva devā na pitaraḥ pratīcchantīti naḥ śrutam ।। bhāraḥ satpuruṣācīrṇas tadartham abhinandyate ।। kṣudrair nṛśaṃsair lubdhaiś ca sevitaṃ pāpakarmabhiḥ ।।
anṛtaṃ jihvayā cāha trividhaṃ karma pātakam ।। svargasthaṃ cānubadhnanti satyam eva bhajeta tat ।। āha yuktikarair vākyair idaṃ bhadraṃ kuruṣva ha ।। bharatasya kariṣyāmi vaco hitvā guror vacaḥ ।।
prahṛṣṭamānasā devī kaikeyī cābhavat tadā ।। mūlaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pitṝn devāṃś ca tarpayan ।। akuhaḥ śraddadhānaḥ san kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ ।। agnir vāyuś ca somaś ca karmaṇāṃ phalabhāginaḥ ।।
tapāṃsy ugrāṇi cāsthāya divaṃ yātā maharṣayaḥ ।। dvijātidevātithipūjanaṃ ca panthānam āhus tridivasya santaḥ ।। ahiṃsakā vītamalāś ca loke bhavanti pūjyā munayaḥ pradhānāḥ ।। nivartayitukāmas tu tvām etad vākyam abravīt ।।
tataḥ samabhavad brahmā svayambhūr daivataiḥ saha ।। asṛjac ca jagat sarvaṃ saha putraiḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ ।। tasmān marīciḥ saṃjajñe marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ sutaḥ ।। sa tu prajāpatiḥ pūrvam ikṣvākus tu manoḥ sutaḥ ।।
tam ikṣvākum ayodhyāyāṃ rājānaṃ viddhi pūrvakam ।। kukṣer athātmajo vīro vikukṣir udapadyata ।। bāṇasya tu mahābāhur anaraṇyo mahāyaśāḥ ।। anaraṇye mahārāje taskaro vāpi kaścana ।।
sa satyavacanād vīraḥ saśarīro divaṃ gataḥ ।। dhundhumārān mahātejā yuvanāśvo vyajāyata ।। māndhātus tu mahātejāḥ susaṃdhir udapadyata ।। yaśasvī dhruvasaṃdhes tu bharato ripusūdanaḥ ।।
haihayās tālajaṅghāś ca śūrāś ca śaśabindavaḥ ।। dve cāsya bhārye garbhiṇyau babhūvatur iti śrutiḥ ।। tam ṛṣiṃ samupāgamya kālindī tv abhyavādayat ।। tataḥ sā gṛham āgamya devī putraṃ vyajāyata ।।
gareṇa saha tenaiva jātaḥ sa sagaro abhavat ।। iṣṭvā parvaṇi vegena trāsayantam imāḥ prajāḥ ।। jīvann eva sa pitrā tu nirastaḥ pāpakarmakṛt ।। dilīpo aṃśumataḥ putro dilīpasya bhagīrathaḥ ।।
kakutsthasya tu putro abhūd raghur yena tu rāghavaḥ ।। kalmāṣapādaḥ saudāsa ity evaṃ prathito bhuvi ।। yas tu tad vīryam āsādya sahaseno vyanīnaśat ।। sudarśanasyāgnivarṇa agnivarṇasya śīghragaḥ ।।
praśuśrukasya putro abhūd ambarīṣo mahādyutiḥ ।। nahuṣasya ca nābhāgaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।। ajasya caiva dharmātmā rājā daśarathaḥ sutaḥ ।। tad gṛhāṇa svakaṃ rājyam avekṣasva jagan nṛpa ।।
pūrvajenāvaraḥ putro jyeṣṭho rājye abhiṣicyate ।। prabhūtaratnām anuśādhi medinīṃ prabhūtarāṣṭrāṃ pitṛvan mahāyaśāḥ ।। abravīd dharmasaṃyuktaṃ punar evāparaṃ vacaḥ ।। ācāryaś caiva kākutstha pitā mātā ca rāghava ।।
prajñāṃ dadāti cācāryas tasmāt sa gurur ucyate ।। mama tvaṃ vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim ।। eṣu tāta caran dharmaṃ nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim ।। asyās tu vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim ।।
ātmānaṃ nātivartes tvaṃ satyadharmaparākrama ।। pratyuvāca samāsīnaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ ।। na supratikaraṃ tat tu mātrā pitrā ca yat kṛtam ।। nityaṃ ca priyavādena tathā saṃvardhanena ca ।।
ājñātaṃ yan mayā tasya na tan mithyā bhaviṣyati ।। uvāca paramodāraḥ sūtaṃ paramadurmanāḥ ।। āryaṃ pratyupavekṣyāmi yāvan me na prasīdati ।। śeṣye purastāc chālāyā yāvan na pratiyāsyati ।।
kuśottaram upasthāpya bhūmāv evāstarat svayam ।। kiṃ māṃ bharata kurvāṇaṃ tāta pratyupavekṣyasi ।। na tu mūrdhāvasiktānāṃ vidhiḥ pratyupaveśane ।। puravaryām itaḥ kṣipram ayodhyāṃ yāhi rāghava ।।
uvāca sarvataḥ prekṣya kim āryaṃ nānuśāsatha ।। kākutstham abhijānīmaḥ samyag vadati rāghavaḥ ।। ata eva na śaktāḥ smo vyāvartayitum añjasā ।। evaṃ nibodha vacanaṃ suhṛdāṃ dharmacakṣuṣām ।।
uttiṣṭha tvaṃ mahābāho māṃ ca spṛśa tathodakam ।। śṛṇvantu me pariṣado mantriṇaḥ śreṇayas tathā ।। āryaṃ paramadharmajñam abhijānāmi rāghavam ।। aham eva nivatsyāmi caturdaśa vane samāḥ ।।
uvāca rāmaḥ samprekṣya paurajānapadaṃ janam ।। na tal lopayituṃ śakyaṃ mayā vā bharatena vā ।। yuktam uktaṃ ca kaikeyyā pitrā me sukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। sarvam evātra kalyāṇaṃ satyasaṃdhe mahātmani ।।
bhrātrā saha bhaviṣyāmi pṛthivyāḥ patir uttamaḥ ।। anṛtān mocayānena pitaraṃ taṃ mahīpatim ।। vismitāḥ saṃgamaṃ prekṣya samavetā maharṣayaḥ ।। tau bhrātarau mahātmānau kākutsthau praśaśaṃsire ।।
śrutvā vayaṃ hi sambhāṣām ubhayoḥ spṛhayāmahe ।। bharataṃ rājaśārdūlam ity ūcuḥ saṃgatā vacaḥ ।। grāhyaṃ rāmasya vākyaṃ te pitaraṃ yady avekṣase ।। anṛṇatvāc ca kaikeyyāḥ svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ ।।
rājarṣayaś caiva tathā sarve svāṃ svāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥ ।। rāmaḥ saṃhṛṣṭavadanas tān ṛṣīn abhyapūjayat ।। kṛtāñjalir idaṃ vākyaṃ rāghavaṃ punar abravīt ।। kartum arhasi kākutstha mama mātuś ca yācanām ।।
paurajānapadāṃś cāpi raktān rañjayituṃ tathā ।। tvām eva pratikāṅkṣante parjanyam iva karṣakāḥ ।। śaktimān asi kākutstha lokasya paripālane ।। bhṛśaṃ samprārthayāmāsa rāmam evaṃ priyaṃvadaḥ ।।
śyāmaṃ nalinapattrākṣaṃ mattahaṃsasvaraṃ svayam ।। bhṛśam utsahase tāta rakṣituṃ pṛthivīm api ।। sarvakāryāṇi saṃmantrya sumahānty api kāraya ।। atīyāt sāgaro velāṃ na pratijñām ahaṃ pituḥ ।।
na tan manasi kartavyaṃ vartitavyaṃ ca mātṛvat ।। tejasādityasaṃkāśaṃ pratipaccandradarśanam ।। ete hi sarvalokasya yogakṣemaṃ vidhāsyataḥ ।। prāyacchat sumahātejā bharatāya mahātmane ।।
pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ cakāra caivottamanāgamūrdhani ।। vyasarjayad rāghavavaṃśavardhanaḥ sthitaḥ svadharme himavān ivācalaḥ ।। sa tv eva mātṝn abhivādya sarvā rudan kuṭīṃ svāṃ praviveśa rāmaḥ ।। āruroha rathaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ ।।
agrataḥ prayayuḥ sarve mantriṇo mantrapūjitāḥ ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ ca kurvāṇāś citrakūṭaṃ mahāgirim ।। prayayau tasya pārśvena sasainyo bharatas tadā ।। āśramaṃ yatra sa munir bharadvājaḥ kṛtālayaḥ ।।
avatīrya rathāt pādau vavande kulanandanaḥ ।। api kṛtyaṃ kṛtaṃ tāta rāmeṇa ca samāgatam ।। pratyuvāca bharadvājaṃ bharato dharmavatsalaḥ ।। rāghavaḥ paramaprīto vasiṣṭhaṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
caturdaśa hi varṣāṇi yā pratijñā pitur mama ।। vākyajño vākyakuśalaṃ rāghavaṃ vacanaṃ mahat ।। ayodhyāyāṃ mahāprājña yogakṣemakare tava ।। pāduke hemavikṛte mama rājyāya te dadau ।।
ayodhyām eva gacchāmi gṛhītvā pāduke śubhe ।। bharadvājaḥ śubhataraṃ munir vākyam udāharat ।। yad āryaṃ tvayi tiṣṭhet tu nimne vṛṣṭim ivodakam ।। yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro dharmātmā dharmavatsalaḥ ।।
āmantrayitum ārebhe caraṇāv upagṛhya ca ।। bharatas tu yayau śrīmān ayodhyāṃ saha mantribhiḥ ।। punar nivṛttā vistīrṇā bharatasyānuyāyinī ।। dadṛśus tāṃ punaḥ sarve gaṅgāṃ śivajalāṃ nadīm ।।
śṛṅgaverapuraṃ ramyaṃ praviveśa sasainikaḥ ।। bharato duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ sārathiṃ cedam abravīt ।। nirākārā nirānandā dīnā pratihatasvanā ।। ayodhyāṃ bharataḥ kṣipraṃ praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ ।।
timirābhyāhatāṃ kālīm aprakāśāṃ niśām iva ।। graheṇābhyutthitenaikāṃ rohiṇīm iva pīḍitām ।। līnamīnajhaṣagrāhāṃ kṛśāṃ girinadīm iva ।। havirabhyukṣitāṃ paścāc chikhāṃ vipralayaṃ gatām ।।
hatapravīrām āpannāṃ camūm iva mahāhave ।। praśāntamārutoddhūtāṃ jalormim iva niḥsvanām ।। sutyākāle vinirvṛtte vediṃ gataravām iva ।। govṛṣeṇa parityaktāṃ gavāṃ patnīm ivotsukām ।।
viyuktāṃ maṇibhir jātyair navāṃ muktāvalīm iva ।। saṃhṛtadyutivistārāṃ tārām iva divaś cyutām ।। drutadāvāgnivipruṣṭāṃ klāntāṃ vanalatām iva ।। pracchannaśaśinakṣatrāṃ dyām ivāmbudharair vṛtām ।।
hataśauṇḍām ivākāśe pānabhūmim asaṃskṛtām ।। upayuktodakāṃ bhagnāṃ prapāṃ nipatitām iva ।। bhūmau bāṇair viniṣkṛttāṃ patitāṃ jyām ivāyudhāt ।। nikṣiptabhāṇḍām utsṛṣṭāṃ kiśorīm iva durbalām ।।
pracchannāṃ nīlajīmūtair bhāskarasya prabhām iva ।। vāhayantaṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ sārathiṃ vākyam abravīt ।। yathāpuram ayodhyāyāṃ gītavāditraniḥsvanaḥ ।। dhūpitāgarugandhaś ca na pravāti samantataḥ ।।
nedānīṃ śrūyate puryām asyāṃ rāme vivāsite ।। saṃpatadbhir ayodhyāyāṃ na vibhānti mahāpathāḥ ।। tena hīnāṃ narendreṇa siṃhahīnāṃ guhām iva ।। bharataḥ śokasaṃtapto gurūn idam athābravīt ।।
tatra duḥkham idaṃ sarvaṃ sahiṣye rāghavaṃ vinā ।। rāmaṃ pratīkṣe rājyāya sa hi rājā mahāyaśāḥ ।। abruvan mantriṇaḥ sarve vasiṣṭhaś ca purohitaḥ ।। vacanaṃ bhrātṛvātsalyād anurūpaṃ tavaiva tat ।।
āryamārgaṃ prapannasya nānumanyeta kaḥ pumān ।। abravīt sārathiṃ vākyaṃ ratho me yujyatām iti ।। āruroha rathaṃ śrīmāñ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ ।। yayatuḥ paramaprītau vṛtau mantripurohitaiḥ ।।
prayayuḥ prāṅmukhāḥ sarve nandigrāmo yato abhavat ।। prayayau bharate yāte sarve ca puravāsinaḥ ।। nandigrāmaṃ yayau tūrṇaṃ śirasy ādhāya pāduke ।। avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gurūn idam uvāca ha ।।
tam imaṃ pālayiṣyāmi rāghavāgamanaṃ prati ।। caraṇau tau tu rāmasya drakṣyāmi sahapādukau ।। nivedya gurave rājyaṃ bhajiṣye guruvṛttitām ।। rājyaṃ cedam ayodhyāṃ ca dhūtapāpo bhavāmi ca ।।
prītir mama yaśaś caiva bhaved rājyāc caturguṇam ।। nandigrāme akarod rājyaṃ duḥkhito mantribhiḥ saha ।। nandigrāme avasad vīraḥ sasainyo bharatas tadā ।। bhrātur vacanakārī ca pratijñāpāragas tadā ।।
bharataḥ śāsanaṃ sarvaṃ pādukābhyāṃ nyavedayat ।। lakṣayāmāsa sodvegam athautsukyaṃ tapasvinām ।। rāmam āśritya niratās tān alakṣayad utsukān ।। anyonyam upajalpantaḥ śanaiś cakrur mithaḥ kathāḥ ।।
kṛtāñjalir uvācedam ṛṣiṃ kulapatiṃ tataḥ ।। dṛśyate vikṛtaṃ yena vikriyante tapasvinaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇasyarṣibhir dṛṣṭaṃ nānurūpam ivātmanaḥ ।। pramadābhyucitāṃ vṛttiṃ sītā yuktaṃ na vartate ।।
vepamāna ivovāca rāmaṃ bhūtadayāparam ।। calanaṃ tāta vaidehyās tapasviṣu viśeṣataḥ ।। rakṣobhyas tena saṃvignāḥ kathayanti mithaḥ kathāḥ ।। utpāṭya tāpasān sarvāñ janasthānaniketanān ।।
avaliptaś ca pāpaś ca tvāṃ ca tāta na mṛṣyate ।। tadā prabhṛti rakṣāṃsi viprakurvanti tāpasān ।। nānā rūpair virūpaiś ca rūpair asukhadarśanaiḥ ।। pratighnanty aparān kṣipram anāryāḥ purataḥ sthitāḥ ।।
ramante tāpasāṃs tatra nāśayanto alpacetasaḥ ।। kalaśāṃś ca pramṛdnanti havane samupasthite ।। gamanāyānyadeśasya codayanty ṛṣayo adya mām ।। darśayanti hi duṣṭās te tyakṣyāma imam āśramam ।।
purāṇāśramam evāhaṃ śrayiṣye sagaṇaḥ punaḥ ।। sahāsmābhir ito gaccha yadi buddhiḥ pravartate ।। samarthasyāpi hi sato vāso duḥkham ihādya te ।। na śaśākottarair vākyair avaroddhuṃ samutsukam ।।
sa jagāmāśramaṃ tyaktvā kulaiḥ kulapatiḥ saha ।। samyakprītais tair anumata upadiṣṭārthaḥ puṇyaṃ vāsāya svanilayam upasaṃpede ।। rāghavaṃ hi satatam anugatās tāpasāś cārṣicaritadhṛtaguṇāḥ ।। na tatrārocayad vāsaṃ kāraṇair bahubhis tadā ।।
sā ca me smṛtir anveti tān nityam anuśocataḥ ।। hayahastikarīṣaiś ca upamardaḥ kṛto bhṛśam ।। prātiṣṭhata sa vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca saṃgataḥ ।। taṃ cāpi bhagavān atriḥ putravat pratyapadyata ।।
saumitriṃ ca mahābhāgāṃ sītāṃ ca samasāntvayat ।। sāntvayāmāsa dharmajñaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। pratigṛhṇīṣva vaidehīm abravīd ṛṣisattamaḥ ।। daśa varṣāṇy anāvṛṣṭyā dagdhe loke nirantaram ।।
ugreṇa tapasā yuktā niyamaiś cāpy alaṃkṛtā ।। anasūyāvratais tāta pratyūhāś ca nibarhitāḥ ।। daśarātraṃ kṛtvā rātriḥ seyaṃ māteva te anagha ।। abhigacchatu vaidehī vṛddhām akrodhanāṃ sadā ।।
sītām uvāca dharmajñām idaṃ vacanam uttamam ।। śreyo'rtham ātmanaḥ śīghram abhigaccha tapasvinīm ।। tāṃ śīghram abhigaccha tvam abhigamyāṃ tapasvinīm ।। tām atripatnīṃ dharmajñām abhicakrāma maithilī ।।
satataṃ vepamānāṅgīṃ pravāte kadalī yathā ।। abhyavādayad avyagrā svaṃ nāma samudāharat ।। baddhāñjalipuṭā hṛṣṭā paryapṛcchad anāmayam ।। sāntvayanty abravīd dhṛṣṭā diṣṭyā dharmam avekṣase ।।
avaruddhaṃ vane rāmaṃ diṣṭyā tvam anugacchasi ।। yāsāṃ strīṇāṃ priyo bhartā tāsāṃ lokā mahodayāḥ ।। strīṇām āryasvabhāvānāṃ paramaṃ daivataṃ patiḥ ।। sarvatra yogyaṃ vaidehi tapaḥ kṛtam ivāvyayam ।।
kāmavaktavyahṛdayā bhartṛnāthāś caranti yāḥ ।। akāryavaśam āpannāḥ striyo yāḥ khalu tadvidhāḥ ।। striyaḥ svarge cariṣyanti yathā puṇyakṛtas tathā ।। pratipūjya vaco mandaṃ pravaktum upacakrame ।।
viditaṃ tu mamāpy etad yathā nāryāḥ patir guruḥ ।। advaidham upacartavyas tathāpy eṣa mayā bhavet ।। sthirānurāgo dharmātmā mātṛvartī pitṛpriyaḥ ।। tām eva nṛpanārīṇām anyāsām api vartate ।।
mātṛvad vartate vīro mānam utsṛjya dharmavit ।। samāhitaṃ hi me śvaśrvā hṛdaye yat sthitaṃ mama ।। anuśiṣṭā jananyāsmi vākyaṃ tad api me dhṛtam ।। patiśuśrūṣaṇān nāryās tapo nānyad vidhīyate ।।
tathā vṛttiś ca yātā tvaṃ patiśuśrūṣayā divam ।। rohiṇī ca vinā candraṃ muhūrtam api dṛśyate ।। devaloke mahīyante puṇyena svena karmaṇā ।। śirasy āghrāya covāca maithilīṃ harṣayanty uta ।।
tat saṃśritya balaṃ sīte chandaye tvāṃ śucivrate ।। kṛtam ity abravīt sītā tapobalasamanvitām ।। saphalaṃ ca praharṣaṃ te hanta sīte karomy aham ।। aṅgarāgaṃ ca vaidehi mahārham anulepanam ।।
anurūpam asaṃkliṣṭaṃ nityam eva bhaviṣyati ।। śobhayiṣyāmi bhartāraṃ yathā śrīr viṣṇum avyayam ।। maithilī pratijagrāha prītidānam anuttamam ।। śliṣṭāñjalipuṭā dhīrā samupāsta tapodhanām ।।
vacanaṃ praṣṭum ārebhe kathāṃ kāṃcid anupriyām ।। rāghaveṇeti me sīte kathā śrutim upāgatā ।। yathānubhūtaṃ kārtsnyena tan me tvaṃ vaktum arhasi ।। śrūyatām iti coktvā vai kathayāmāsa tāṃ kathām ।।
kṣatradharmaṇy abhirato nyāyataḥ śāsti medinīm ।। ahaṃ kilotthitā bhittvā jagatīṃ nṛpateḥ sutā ।। pāṃśuguṇṭhitasarvāṅgīṃ vismito janako abhavat ।। mameyaṃ tanayety uktvā sneho mayi nipātitaḥ ।।
evam etan narapate dharmeṇa tanayā tava ।। avāpto vipulām ṛddhiṃ mām avāpya narādhipaḥ ।। tayā saṃbhāvitā cāsmi snigdhayā mātṛsauhṛdāt ।। cintām abhyagamad dīno vittanāśād ivādhanaḥ ।।
pradharṣaṇām avāpnoti śakreṇāpi samo bhuvi ।। cintārṇavagataḥ pāraṃ nāsasādāplavo yathā ।। sadṛśaṃ cānurūpaṃ ca mahīpālaḥ patiṃ mama ।। svayaṃ varaṃ tanūjāyāḥ kariṣyāmīti dhīmataḥ ।।
dattaṃ dhanurvaraṃ prītyā tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau ।। tan na śaktā namayituṃ svapneṣv api narādhipāḥ ।। samavāye narendrāṇāṃ pūrvam āmantrya pārthivān ।। tasya me duhitā bhāryā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
abhivādya nṛpā jagmur aśaktās tasya tolane ।। viśvāmitreṇa sahito yajñaṃ draṣṭuṃ samāgataḥ ।। viśvāmitras tu dharmātmā mama pitrā supūjitaḥ ।। ity uktas tena vipreṇa tad dhanuḥ samupānayat ।।
jyāṃ samāropya jhaṭiti pūrayāmāsa vīryavān ।। tasya śabdo abhavad bhīmaḥ patitasyāśaner iva ।। udyatā dātum udyamya jalabhājanam uttamam ।। avijñāya pituś chandam ayodhyādhipateḥ prabhoḥ ।।
mama pitrā ahaṃ dattā rāmāya viditātmane ।। bhāryārthe lakṣmaṇasyāpi dattā pitrā mama svayam ।। anuraktā ca dharmeṇa patiṃ vīryavatāṃ varam ।। paryaṣvajata bāhubhyāṃ śirasy āghrāya maithilīm ।।
yathā svayaṃvaraṃ vṛttaṃ tat sarvaṃ hi śrutaṃ mayā ।। ravir astaṃ gataḥ śrīmān upohya rajanīṃ śivām ।। saṃdhyākāle nilīnānāṃ nidrārthaṃ śrūyate dhvaniḥ ।। sahitā upavartante salilāplutavalkalāḥ ।।
kapotāṅgāruṇo dhūmo dṛśyate pavanoddhataḥ ।। viprakṛṣṭe api ye deśe na prakāśanti vai diśaḥ ।। tapovanamṛgā hy ete veditīrtheṣu śerate ।। jyotsnāprāvaraṇaś candro dṛśyate abhyudito ambare ।।
kathayantyā hi madhuraṃ tvayāhaṃ paritoṣitā ।। prītiṃ janaya me vatsa divyālaṃkāraśobhinī ।। praṇamya śirasā tasyai rāmaṃ tv abhimukhī yayau ।। rāghavaḥ prītidānena tapasvinyā jaharṣa ca ।।
prītidānaṃ tapasvinyā vasanābharaṇasrajām ।। maithilyāḥ satkriyāṃ dṛṣṭvā mānuṣeṣu sudurlabhām ।। arcitas tāpasaiḥ siddhair uvāsa raghunandanaḥ ।। āpṛcchetāṃ naravyāghrau tāpasān vanagocarān ।।
vanasya tasya saṃcāraṃ rākṣasaiḥ samabhiplutam ।। anena tu vanaṃ durgaṃ gantuṃ rāghava te kṣamam ।। vanaṃ sabhāryaḥ praviveśa rāghavaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ sūrya ivābhramaṇḍalam ।। dadarśa rāmo durdharṣas tāpasāśramamaṇḍalam ।।
yathā pradīptaṃ durdharṣaṃ gagane sūryamaṇḍalam ।। pūjitaṃ copanṛttaṃ ca nityam apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। samidbhis toyakalaśaiḥ phalamūlaiś ca śobhitam ।। balihomārcitaṃ puṇyaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam ।।
phalamūlāśanair dāntaiś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraiḥ ।। puṇyaiś ca niyatāhāraiḥ śobhitaṃ paramarṣibhiḥ ।। brahmavidbhir mahābhāgair brāhmaṇair upaśobhitam ।। abhyagacchan mahātejā vijyaṃ kṛtvā mahad dhanuḥ ।।
abhyagacchaṃs tadā prītā vaidehīṃ ca yaśasvinīm ।। maṅgalāni prayuñjānāḥ pratyagṛhṇan dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। dadṛśur vismitākārā rāmasya vanavāsinaḥ ।। āścaryabhūtān dadṛśuḥ sarve te vanacāriṇaḥ ।।
atithiṃ parṇaśālāyāṃ rāghavaṃ saṃnyaveśayan ।। ājahrus te mahābhāgāḥ salilaṃ dharmacāriṇaḥ ।। nivedayitvā dharmajñās tataḥ prāñjalayo abruvan ।। pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca rājā daṇḍadharo guruḥ ।।
rājā tasmād varān bhogān bhuṅkte lokanamaskṛtaḥ ।। nagarastho vanastho vā tvaṃ no rājā janeśvaraḥ ।। rakṣitavyās tvayā śaśvad garbhabhūtās tapodhanāḥ ।। anyaiś ca vividhāhāraiḥ salakṣmaṇam apūjayan ।।
nyāyavṛttā yathānyāyaṃ tarpayāmāsur īśvaram ।। āmantrya sa munīn sarvān vanam evānvagāhata ।। dhvastavṛkṣalatāgulmaṃ durdarśasalilāśayam ।। lakṣmaṇānugato rāmo vanamadhyaṃ dadarśa ha ।।
dadarśa giriśṛṅgābhaṃ puruṣādaṃ mahāsvanam ।। bībhatsaṃ viṣamaṃ dīrghaṃ vikṛtaṃ ghoradarśanam ।। trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakam ।। saviṣāṇaṃ vasādigdhaṃ gajasya ca śiro mahat ।।
sa rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva sītāṃ dṛṣṭvā ca maithilīm ।। sa kṛtvā bhairavaṃ nādaṃ cālayann iva medinīm ।। yuvāṃ jaṭācīradharau sabhāryau kṣīṇajīvitau ।। kathaṃ tāpasayor vāṃ ca vāsaḥ pramadayā saha ।।
ahaṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ virādho nāma rākṣasaḥ ।। yuvayoḥ pāpayoś cāhaṃ pāsyāmi rudhiraṃ mṛdhe ।। sītā prāvepatodvegāt pravāte kadalī yathā ।। abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā ।।
atyantasukhasaṃvṛddhāṃ rājaputrīṃ yaśasvinīm ।। kaikeyyās tu susaṃvṛttaṃ kṣipram adyaiva lakṣmaṇa ।। adyedānīṃ sakāmā sā yā mātā mama madhyamā ।। pitur vināśāt saumitre svarājyaharaṇāt tathā ।।
abravīl lakṣmaṇaḥ kruddho ruddho nāga iva śvasan ।। mayā preṣyeṇa kākutstha kimarthaṃ paritapyase ।। virādhasya gatāsor hi mahī pāsyati śoṇitam ।। taṃ virādhe vimokṣyāmi vajrī vajram ivācale ।।
vyapanayatu tanoś ca jīvitaṃ patatu tataś ca mahīṃ vighūrṇitaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ pṛcchate brūtaṃ kau yuvāṃ kva gamiṣyathaḥ ।। pṛcchantaṃ sumahātejā ikṣvākukulam ātmanaḥ ।। tvāṃ tu veditum icchāvaḥ kas tvaṃ carasi daṇḍakān ।।
hanta vakṣyāmi te rājan nibodha mama rāghava ।। virādha iti mām āhuḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvarākṣasāḥ ।। śastreṇāvadhyatā loke acchedyābhedyatvam eva ca ।। tvaramāṇau pālayethāṃ na vāṃ jīvitam ādade ।।
rākṣasaṃ vikṛtākāraṃ virādhaṃ pāpacetasam ।। raṇe samprāpsyase tiṣṭha na me jīvan gamiṣyasi ।। suśīghram abhisaṃdhāya rākṣasaṃ nijaghāna ha ।। rukmapuṅkhān mahāvegān suparṇānilatulyagān ।।
nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ pāvakopamāḥ ।। pragṛhyāśobhata tadā vyāttānana ivāntakaḥ ।। dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ cicheda rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।। rāmas tu dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ tarasā tasya rakṣasaḥ ।।
idaṃ provāca kākutsthaṃ virādhaḥ puruṣarṣabham ।। vaidehī ca mahābhāgā lakṣmaṇaś ca mahāyaśāḥ ।। tumburur nāma gandharvaḥ śapto vaiśravaṇena hi ।। yadā dāśarathī rāmas tvāṃ vadhiṣyati saṃyuge ।।
iti vaiśravaṇo rājā rambhāsaktam uvāca ha ।। bhavanaṃ svaṃ gamiṣyāmi svasti vo astu paraṃtapa ।। adhyardhayojane tāta maharṣiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaḥ ।। avaṭe cāpi māṃ rāma nikṣipya kuśalī vraja ।।
avaṭe ye nidhīyante teṣāṃ lokāḥ sanātanāḥ ।। babhūva svargasamprāpto nyastadeho mahābalaḥ ।। virādhaṃ prākṣipac chvabhre nadantaṃ bhairavasvanam ।। vijahratus tau muditau mahāvane divi sthitau candradivākarāv iva ।।
abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo bhrātaraṃ dīptatejasam ।। abhigacchāmahe śīghraṃ śarabhaṅgaṃ tapodhanam ।। āśramaṃ śarabhaṅgasya rāghavo abhijagāma ha ।। samīpe śarabhaṅgasya dadarśa mahad adbhutam ।।
asaṃspṛśantaṃ vasudhāṃ dadarśa vibudheśvaram ।। tadvidhair eva bahubhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ mahātmabhiḥ ।। dadarśādūratas tasya taruṇādityasaṃnibham ।। apaśyad vimalaṃ chattraṃ citramālyopaśobhitam ।।
gṛhīte vananārībhyāṃ dhūyamāne ca mūrdhani ।। antarikṣagataṃ devaṃ vāgbhir agryābhir īḍire ।। antarikṣagatā divyās ta ime harayo dhruvam ।। śataṃ śataṃ kuṇḍalino yuvānaḥ khaḍgapāṇayaḥ ।।
rūpaṃ bibhrati saumitre pañcaviṃśativārṣikam ।। yatheme puruṣavyāghrā dṛśyante priyadarśanāḥ ।। yāvaj janāmy ahaṃ vyaktaṃ ka eṣa dyutimān rathe ।। abhicakrāma kākutsthaḥ śarabhaṅgāśramaṃ prati ।।
