śarabhaṅgam anujñāpya vibudhān idam abravīt ।। niṣṭhāṃ nayata tāvat tu tato māṃ draṣṭum arhati ।। karma hy anena kartavyaṃ mahad anyaiḥ suduṣkaram ।। rathena hariyuktena yayau divam ariṃdamaḥ ।।
agnihotram upāsīnaṃ śarabhaṅgam upāgamat ।। niṣedus tadanujñātā labdhavāsā nimantritāḥ ।। śarabhaṅgaś ca tat sarvaṃ rāghavāya nyavedayat ।। jitam ugreṇa tapasā duṣprāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ ।।
brahmalokaṃ na gacchāmi tvām adṛṣṭvā priyātithim ।। brāhmyāś ca nākapṛṣṭhyāś ca pratigṛhṇīṣva māmakān ।। ṛṣiṇā śarabhaṅgena rāghavo vākyam abravīt ।। āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane ।।
śarabhaṅgo mahāprājñaḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ ।। ramaṇīye vanoddeśe sa te vāsaṃ vidhāsyati ।। yāvaj jahāmi gātrāṇi jīrṇāṃ tvacam ivoragaḥ ।। śarabhaṅgo mahātejāḥ praviveśa hutāśanam ।।
jīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ tathāsthīni yac ca māṃsaṃ ca śoṇitam ।। utthāyāgnicayāt tasmāc charabhaṅgo vyarocata ।। devānāṃ ca vyatikramya brahmalokaṃ vyarohata ।। pitāmahaś cāpi samīkṣya taṃ dvijaṃ nananda susvāgatam ity uvāca ha ।।
abhyagacchanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ jvalitatejasam ।। aśmakuṭṭāś ca bahavaḥ pattrāhārāś ca tāpasāḥ ।। munayaḥ salilāhārā vāyubhakṣās tathāpare ।। tathordhvavāsino dāntās tathārdrapaṭavāsasaḥ ।।
śarabhaṅgāśrame rāmam abhijagmuś ca tāpasāḥ ।। ūcuḥ paramadharmajñam ṛṣisaṃghāḥ samāhitāḥ ।। pradhānaś cāsi nāthaś ca devānāṃ maghavān iva ।। pitṛvratatvaṃ satyaṃ ca tvayi dharmaś ca puṣkalaḥ ।।
arthitvān nātha vakṣyāmas tac ca naḥ kṣantum arhasi ।। yo hared baliṣaḍbhāgaṃ na ca rakṣati putravat ।। nityayuktaḥ sadā rakṣan sarvān viṣayavāsinaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ sthānam āsādya tatra cāpi mahīyate ।।
tatra rājñaś caturbhāgaḥ prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ ।। tvan nātho anāthavad rāma rākṣasair vadhyate bhṛśam ।। hatānāṃ rākṣasair ghorair bahūnāṃ bahudhā vane ।। citrakūṭālayānāṃ ca kriyate kadanaṃ mahat ।।
kriyamāṇaṃ vane ghoraṃ rakṣobhir bhīmakarmabhiḥ ।। paripālaya no rāma vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥ ।। naivam arhatha māṃ vaktum ājñāpyo ahaṃ tapasvinām ।। tapasvināṃ raṇe śatrūn hantum icchāmi rākṣasān ।।
tapodhanaiś cāpi sabhājyavṛttaḥ sutīkṣṇam evābhijagāma vīraḥ ।। sutīkṣṇasyāśramapadaṃ jagāma saha tair dvijaiḥ ।। dadarśa vipulaṃ śailaṃ mahāmegham ivonnatam ।। kānanaṃ tau viviśatuḥ sītayā saha rāghavau ।।
dadarśāśramam ekānte cīramālāpariṣkṛtam ।। rāmaḥ sutīkṣṇaṃ vidhivat tapovṛddham abhāṣata ।। tan mābhivada dharmajña maharṣe satyavikrama ।। samāśliṣya ca bāhubhyām idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
āśramo ayaṃ tvayākrāntaḥ sanātha iva sāmpratam ।। devalokam ito vīra dehaṃ tyaktvā mahītale ।। sarvāṃl lokāñ jitān āha mama puṇyena karmaṇā ।। matprasādāt sabhāryas tvaṃ viharasva salakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
pratyuvācātmavān rāmo brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ ।। āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane ।। ākhyātaḥ śarabhaṅgena gautamena mahātmanā ।। abravīn madhuraṃ vākyaṃ harṣeṇa mahatāplutaḥ ।।
ṛṣisaṃghānucaritaḥ sadā mūlaphalair yutaḥ ।। aṭitvā pratigacchanti lobhayitvākutobhayāḥ ।। uvāca vacanaṃ dhīro vikṛṣya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ ।। hanyāṃ niśitadhāreṇa śareṇāśanivarcasā ।।
etasminn āśrame vāsaṃ ciraṃ tu na samarthaye ।। anvāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ tatra vāsam akalpayat ।। tābhyāṃ susatkṛtya dadau mahātmā saṃdhyānivṛttau rajanīṃ samīkṣya ।। pariṇāmya niśāṃ tatra prabhāte pratyabudhyata ।।
upāspṛśat suśītena jalenotpalagandhinā ।। kālyaṃ vidhivad abhyarcya tapasviśaraṇe vane ।। sutīkṣṇam abhigamyedaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abruvan ।। āpṛcchāmaḥ prayāsyāmo munayas tvarayanti naḥ ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ puṇyaśīlānāṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām ।। dharmanityais tapodāntair viśikhair iva pāvakaiḥ ।। amārgeṇāgatāṃ lakṣmīṃ prāpyevānvayavarjitaḥ ।। vavande sahasaumitriḥ sītayā saha rāghavaḥ ।।
gāḍham āliṅgya sasneham idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। sītayā cānayā sārdhaṃ chāyayevānuvṛttayā ।। eṣāṃ tapasvināṃ vīra tapasā bhāvitātmanām ।। praśāntamṛgayūthāni śāntapakṣigaṇāni ca ।।
kāraṇḍavavikīrṇāni taṭākāni sarāṃsi ca ।। ramaṇīyāny araṇyāni mayūrābhirutāni ca ।। āgantavyaṃ ca te dṛṣṭvā punar evāśramaṃ mama ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ muniṃ kṛtvā prasthātum upacakrame ।।
dadau sītā tayor bhrātroḥ khaḍgau ca vimalau tataḥ ।। niṣkrāntāv āśramād gantum ubhau tau rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। vaidehī snigdhayā vācā bhartāram idam abravīt ।। nivṛttena ca śakyo ayaṃ vyasanāt kāmajād iha ।।
paradārābhigamanaṃ vinā vairaṃ ca raudratā ।। kuto abhilaṣaṇaṃ strīṇāṃ pareṣāṃ dharmanāśanam ।। tava vaśyendriyatvaṃ ca jānāmi śubhadarśana ।। nirvairaṃ kriyate mohāt tac ca te samupasthitam ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya vadhaḥ saṃyati rakṣasām ।। prasthitas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā dhṛtabāṇaśarāsanaḥ ।। tvadvṛttaṃ cintayantyā vai bhaven niḥśreyasaṃ hitam ।। kāraṇaṃ tatra vakṣyāmi vadantyāḥ śrūyatāṃ mama ।।
dṛṣṭvā vanacarān sarvān kaccit kuryāḥ śaravyayam ।। samīpataḥ sthitaṃ tejobalam ucchrayate bhṛśam ।। kasmiṃścid abhavat puṇye vane ratamṛgadvije ।। khaḍgapāṇir athāgacchad āśramaṃ bhaṭarūpadhṛk ।।
sa nyāsavidhinā dattaḥ puṇye tapasi tiṣṭhataḥ ।। vane tu vicaraty eva rakṣan pratyayam ātmanaḥ ।। na vinā yāti taṃ khaḍgaṃ nyāsarakṣaṇatatparaḥ ।। cakāra raudrīṃ svāṃ buddhiṃ tyaktvā tapasi niścayam ।।
tasya śastrasya saṃvāsāj jagāma narakaṃ muniḥ ।। na kathaṃcana sā kāryā gṛhītadhanuṣā tvayā ।। aparādhaṃ vinā hantuṃ lokān vīra na kāmaye ।। dhanuṣā kāryam etāvad ārtānām abhirakṣaṇam ।।
vyāviddham idam asmābhir deśadharmas tu pūjyatām ।। punar gatvā tv ayodhyāyāṃ kṣatradharmaṃ cariṣyasi ।। yadi rājyaṃ hi saṃnyasya bhaves tvaṃ nirato muniḥ ।। dharmeṇa labhate sarvaṃ dharmasāram idaṃ jagat ।।
prāpyate nipuṇair dharmo na sukhāl labhyate sukham ।। sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ tubhyaṃ trailokyam api tattvataḥ ।। vicārya buddhyā tu sahānujena yad rocate tat kuru mācireṇa ।। śrutvā dharme sthito rāmaḥ pratyuvācātha maithilīm ।।
kulaṃ vyapadiśantyā ca dharmajñe janakātmaje ।। kṣatriyair dhāryate cāpo nārtaśabdo bhaved iti ।। māṃ sīte svayam āgamya śaraṇyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। na labhante sukhaṃ bhītā rākṣasaiḥ krūrakarmabhiḥ ।।
bhakṣyante rākṣasair bhīmair naramāṃsopajīvibhiḥ ।। asmān abhyavapadyeti mām ūcur dvijasattamāḥ ।। kṛtvā caraṇaśuśrūṣāṃ vākyam etad udāhṛtam ।। kiṃ karomīti ca mayā vyāhṛtaṃ dvijasaṃnidhau ।।
arditāḥ sma bhṛśaṃ rāma bhavān nas trātum arhati ।। dharṣayanti sma durdharṣā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।। gatiṃ mṛgayamāṇānāṃ bhavān naḥ paramā gatiḥ ।। cirārjitaṃ tu necchāmas tapaḥ khaṇḍayituṃ vayam ।।
tena śāpaṃ na muñcāmo bhakṣyamāṇāś ca rākṣasaiḥ ।। rakṣa nas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā tvannāthā hi vayaṃ vane ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ daṇḍakāraṇye saṃśrutaṃ janakātmaje ।। munīnām anyathā kartuṃ satyam iṣṭaṃ hi me sadā ।।
na tu pratijñāṃ saṃśrutya brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ ।। anuktenāpi vaidehi pratijñāya tu kiṃ punaḥ ।। sadṛśaṃ cānurūpaṃ ca kulasya tava śobhane ।। rāmo dhanuṣmān saha lakṣmaṇena jagāma ramyāṇi tapovanāni ।।
pṛṣṭhatas tu dhanuṣpāṇir lakṣmaṇo anujagāma ha ।। nadīś ca vividhā ramyā jagmatuḥ saha sītayā ।। sarāṃsi ca sapadmāni yutāni jalajaiḥ khagaiḥ ।। mahiṣāṃś ca varāhāṃś ca gajāṃś ca drumavairiṇaḥ ।।
dadṛśuḥ sahitā ramyaṃ taṭākaṃ yojanāyatam ।। sārasair haṃsakādambaiḥ saṃkulaṃ jalacāribhiḥ ।। gītavāditranirghoṣo na tu kaścana dṛśyate ।। muniṃ dharmabhṛtaṃ nāma praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame ।।
kautūhalaṃ mahaj jātaṃ kim idaṃ sādhu kathyatām ।। prabhāvaṃ sarasaḥ kṛtsnam ākhyātum upacakrame ।। nirmitaṃ tapasā rāma muninā māṇḍakarṇinā ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vāyubhakṣo jalāśrayaḥ ।।
asmākaṃ kasyacit sthānam eṣa prārthayate muniḥ ।। pradhānāpsarasaḥ pañcavidyuccalitavarcasaḥ ।। nīto madanavaśyatvaṃ surāṇāṃ kāryasiddhaye ।। taṭāke nirmitaṃ tāsām asminn antarhitaṃ gṛham ।।
ramayanti tapoyogān muniṃ yauvanam āsthitam ।। śrūyate bhūṣaṇonmiśro gītaśabdo manoharaḥ ।। rāghavaḥ pratijagrāha saha bhrātrā mahāyaśāḥ ।। kuśacīraparikṣiptaṃ nānāvṛkṣasamāvṛtam ।।
tadā tasmin sa kākutsthaḥ śrīmaty āśramamaṇḍale ।। jagāma cāśramāṃs teṣāṃ paryāyeṇa tapasvinām ।। kvacit paridaśān māsān ekaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kvacit ।। aparatrādhikān māsān adhyardham adhikaṃ kvacit ।।
ramataś cānukūlyena yayuḥ saṃvatsarā daśa ।। sutīkṣṇasyāśramaṃ śrīmān punar evājagāma ha ।। tatrāpi nyavasad rāmaḥ kaṃcit kālam ariṃdamaḥ ।। upāsīnaḥ sa kākutsthaḥ sutīkṣṇam idam abravīt ।।
vasatīti mayā nityaṃ kathāḥ kathayatāṃ śrutam ।। kutrāśramapadaṃ puṇyaṃ maharṣes tasya dhīmataḥ ।। agastyam abhigaccheyam abhivādayituṃ munim ।। yad ahaṃ taṃ munivaraṃ śuśrūṣeyam api svayam ।।
sutīkṣṇaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ prīto daśarathātmajam ।। agastyam abhigaccheti sītayā saha rāghava ।। aham ākhyāsi te vatsa yatrāgastyo mahāmuniḥ ।। dakṣiṇena mahāñ śrīmān agastyabhrātur āśramaḥ ।।
bahupuṣpaphale ramye nānāśakuninādite ।। haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇāś cakravākopaśobhitāḥ ।। dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āsthāya vanakhaṇḍasya pārśvataḥ ।। raṃsyate tatra vaidehī lakṣmaṇaś ca tvayā saha ।।
adyaiva gamane buddhiṃ rocayasva mahāyaśaḥ ।। pratasthe agastyam uddiśya sānujaḥ saha sītayā ।। sarāṃsi saritaś caiva pathi mārgavaśānugāḥ ।। idaṃ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।।
agastyasya muner bhrātur dṛśyate puṇyakarmaṇaḥ ।। saṃnatāḥ phalabhāreṇa puṣpabhāreṇa ca drumāḥ ।। gandho ayaṃ pavanotkṣiptaḥ sahasā kaṭukodayaḥ ।। lūnāś ca pathi dṛśyante darbhā vaiḍūryavarcasaḥ ।।
pāvakasyāśramasthasya dhūmāgraṃ sampradṛśyate ।। puṣpopahāraṃ kurvanti kusumaiḥ svayam ārjitaiḥ ।। agastyasyāśramo bhrātur nūnam eṣa bhaviṣyati ।। yasya bhrātrā kṛteyaṃ dik śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā ।।
bhrātarau sahitāv āstāṃ brāhmaṇaghnau mahāsurau ।। āmantrayati viprān sa śrāddham uddiśya nirghṛṇaḥ ।। tān dvijān bhojayāmāsa śrāddhadṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। vātāpe niṣkramasveti svareṇa mahatā vadan ।।
bhittvā bhittvā śarīrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ viniṣpatat ।। vināśitāni saṃhatya nityaśaḥ piśitāśanaiḥ ।। anubhūya kila śrāddhe bhakṣitaḥ sa mahāsuraḥ ।। bhrātaraṃ niṣkramasveti ilvalaḥ so abhyabhāṣata ।।
abravīt prahasan dhīmān agastyo munisattamaḥ ।। bhrātus te meṣarūpasya gatasya yamasādanam ।। pradharṣayitum ārebhe muniṃ krodhān niśācaraḥ ।। cakṣuṣānalakalpena nirdagdho nidhanaṃ gataḥ ।।
viprānukampayā yena karmedaṃ duṣkaraṃ kṛtam ।। rāmasyāstaṃ gataḥ sūryaḥ saṃdhyākālo abhyavartata ।। praviveśāśramapadaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ cābhyavādayan ।। nyavasat tāṃ niśām ekāṃ prāśya mūlaphalāni ca ।।
bhrātaraṃ tam agastyasya āmantrayata rāghavaḥ ।। āmantraye tvāṃ gacchāmi guruṃ te draṣṭum agrajam ।। yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa vanaṃ tac cāvalokayan ।। ciribilvān madhūkāṃś ca bilvān api ca tindukān ।।
dadarśa rāmaḥ śataśas tatra kāntārapādapān ।। mattaiḥ śakunisaṃghaiś ca śataśaḥ pratināditān ।। pṛṣṭhato anugataṃ vīraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam ।। āśramo nātidūrastho maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ ।।
āśramo dṛśyate tasya pariśrāntaśramāpahaḥ ।। praśāntamṛgayūthaś ca nānāśakunināditaḥ ।। dakṣiṇā dik kṛtā yena śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā ।। dig iyaṃ dakṣiṇā trāsād dṛśyate nopabhujyate ।।
tadā prabhṛti nirvairāḥ praśāntā rajanīcarāḥ ।। prathitā triṣu lokeṣu durdharṣā krūrakarmabhiḥ ।। saṃdeśaṃ pālayaṃs tasya vindhyaḥ śailo na vardhate ।। agastyasyāśramaḥ śrīmān vinītamṛgasevitaḥ ।।
asmān adhigatān eṣa śreyasā yojayiṣyati ।। śeṣaṃ ca vanavāsasya saumya vatsyāmy ahaṃ prabho ।। agastyaṃ niyatāhāraṃ satataṃ paryupāsate ।। nṛśaṃsaḥ kāmavṛtto vā munir eṣa tathāvidhaḥ ।।
vasanti niyatāhārā dharmam ārādhayiṣṇavaḥ ।। tyaktvā dehān navair dehaiḥ svaryātāḥ paramarṣayaḥ ।। atra devāḥ prayacchanti bhūtair ārādhitāḥ śubhaiḥ ।। nivedayeha māṃ prāptam ṛṣaye saha sītayā ।।
agastyaśiṣyam āsādya vākyam etad uvāca ha ।। rāmaḥ prāpto muniṃ draṣṭuṃ bhāryayā saha sītayā ।। anukūlaś ca bhaktaś ca yadi te śrotram āgataḥ ।। draṣṭum icchāmahe sarve bhagavantaṃ nivedyatām ।।
tathety uktvāgniśaraṇaṃ praviveśa niveditum ।। kṛtāñjalir uvācedaṃ rāmāgamanam añjasā ।। praviṣṭāv āśramapadaṃ sītayā saha bhāryayā ।। yad atrānantaraṃ tattvam ājñāpayitum arhasi ।।
vaidehīṃ ca mahābhāgām idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। manasā kāṅkṣitaṃ hy asya mayāpy āgamanaṃ prati ।। praveśyatāṃ samīpaṃ me kiṃ cāsau na praveśitaḥ ।। abhivādyābravīc chiṣyas tatheti niyatāñjaliḥ ।।
kvāsau rāmo muniṃ draṣṭum etu praviśatu svayam ।। darśayāmāsa kākutsthaṃ sītāṃ ca janakātmajām ।। prāveśayad yathānyāyaṃ satkārārthaṃ susatkṛtam ।। praśāntahariṇākīrṇam āśramaṃ hy avalokayan ।।
viṣṇoḥ sthānaṃ mahendrasya sthānaṃ caiva vivasvataḥ ।। dhātur vidhātuḥ sthānaṃ ca vāyoḥ sthānaṃ tathaiva ca ।। abravīd vacanaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam ।। audāryeṇāvagacchāmi nidhānaṃ tapasām imam ।।
jagrāha paramaprītas tasya pādau paraṃtapaḥ ।। sītayā saha vaidehyā tadā rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ ।। kuśalapraśnam uktvā ca āsyatām iti so abravīt ।। vānaprasthena dharmeṇa sa teṣāṃ bhojanaṃ dadau ।।
uvāca rāmam āsīnaṃ prāñjaliṃ dharmakovidam ।। duḥsākṣīva pare loke svāni māṃsāni bhakṣayet ।। pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca bhavān prāptaḥ priyātithiḥ ।। pūjayitvā yathākāmaṃ punar eva tato abravīt ।।
vaiṣṇavaṃ puruṣavyāghra nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। datto mama mahendreṇa tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau ।। mahārajatakośo ayam asir hemavibhūṣitaḥ ।। ājahāra śriyaṃ dīptāṃ purā viṣṇur divaukasām ।।
jayāya pratigṛhṇīṣva vajraṃ vajradharo yathā ।। dattvā rāmāya bhagavān agastyaḥ punar abravīt ।। abhivādayituṃ yan māṃ prāptau sthaḥ saha sītayā ।। vyaktam utkaṇṭhate cāpi maithilī janakātmajā ।।
prājyadoṣaṃ vanaṃ prāptā bhartṛsnehapracoditā ।। duṣkaraṃ kṛtavaty eṣā vane tvām anugacchatī ।। samastham anurajyante viṣamasthaṃ tyajanti ca ।। garuḍānilayoḥ śaighryam anugacchanti yoṣitaḥ ।।
ślāghyā ca vyapadeśyā ca yathā devī hy arundhatī ।। vaidehyā cānayā rāma vatsyasi tvam ariṃdama ।। uvāca praśritaṃ vākyam ṛṣiṃ dīptam ivānalam ।। guṇaiḥ sabhrātṛbhāryasya varadaḥ parituṣyati ।।
yatrāśramapadaṃ kṛtvā vaseyaṃ nirataḥ sukham ।। dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ dharmātmā dhīro dhīrataraṃ vacaḥ ।। deśo bahumṛgaḥ śrīmān pañcavaṭy abhiviśrutaḥ ।। ramasva tvaṃ pitur vākyaṃ yathoktam anupālayan ।।
tapasaś ca prabhāvena snehād daśarathasya ca ।। iha vāsaṃ pratijñāya mayā saha tapovane ।। sa hi ramyo vanoddeśo maithilī tatra raṃsyate ।। godāvaryāḥ samīpe ca maithilī tatra raṃsyate ।।
viviktaś ca mahābāho puṇyo ramyas tathaiva ca ।। api cātra vasan rāmas tāpasān pālayiṣyasi ।। uttareṇāsya gantavyaṃ nyagrodham abhigacchatā ।। khyātaḥ pañcavaṭīty eva nityapuṣpitakānanaḥ ।।
satkṛtyāmantrayāmāsa tam ṛṣiṃ satyavādinam ।। tadāśramāt pañcavaṭīṃ jagmatuḥ saha sītayā ।। yathopadiṣṭena pathā maharṣiṇā prajagmatuḥ pañcavaṭīṃ samāhitau ।। āsasāda mahākāyaṃ gṛdhraṃ bhīmaparākramam ।।
menāte rākṣasaṃ pakṣiṃ bruvāṇau ko bhavān iti ।। uvāca vatsa māṃ viddhi vayasyaṃ pitur ātmanaḥ ।। sa tasya kulam avyagram atha papraccha nāma ca ।। ācacakṣe dvijas tasmai sarvabhūtasamudbhavam ।।
tān me nigadataḥ sarvān āditaḥ śṛṇu rāghava ।। śeṣaś ca saṃśrayaś caiva bahuputraś ca vīryavān ।। pulastyaś cāṅgirāś caiva pracetāḥ pulahas tathā ।। kaśyapaś ca mahātejās teṣām āsīc ca paścimaḥ ।।
ṣaṣṭir duhitaro rāma yaśasvinyo mahāyaśaḥ ।। aditiṃ ca ditiṃ caiva danum api ca kālakām ।। tās tu kanyās tataḥ prītaḥ kaśyapaḥ punar abravīt ।। aditis tanmanā rāma ditiś ca danur eva ca ।।
adityāṃ jajñire devās trayastriṃśad ariṃdama ।। ditis tv ajanayat putrān daityāṃs tāta yaśasvinaḥ ।। danus tv ajanayat putram aśvagrīvam ariṃdama ।। krauñcīṃ bhāsīṃ tathā śyenīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrīṃ tathā śukīm ।।
ulūkāñ janayat krauñcī bhāsī bhāsān vyajāyata ।। dhṛtarāṣṭrī tu haṃsāṃś ca kalahaṃsāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। śukī natāṃ vijajñe tu natāyā vinatā sutā ।। mṛgīṃ ca mṛgamandāṃ ca harīṃ bhadramadām api ।।
sarvalakṣaṇasampannāṃ surasāṃ kadrukām api ।। ṛkṣāś ca mṛgamandāyāḥ sṛmarāś camarās tathā ।। tasyās tv airāvataḥ putro lokanātho mahāgajaḥ ।। golāṅgūlāṃś ca śārdūlī vyāghrāṃś cājanayat sutān ।।
diśāgajaṃ tu śvetākṣaṃ śvetā vyajanayat sutam ।। rohiṇīṃ nāma bhadraṃ te gandharvīṃ ca yaśasvinīm ।। surasājanayan nāgān rāma kadrūś ca pannagān ।। brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyāñ śūdrāṃś ca manujarṣabha ।।
ūrubhyāṃ jajñire vaiśyāḥ padbhyāṃ śūdrā iti śrutiḥ ।। vinatā ca śukī pautrī kadrūś ca surasā svasā ।। dvau putrau vinatāyās tu garuḍo aruṇa eva ca ।। jaṭāyur iti māṃ viddhi śyenīputram ariṃdama ।।
sītāṃ ca tāta rakṣiṣye tvayi yāte salakṣmaṇe ।। pitur hi śuśrāva sakhitvam ātmavāñ jaṭāyuṣā saṃkathitaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। jagāma tāṃ pañcavaṭīṃ salakṣmaṇo ripūn didhakṣañ śalabhān ivānalaḥ ।। uvāca bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam ।।
ayaṃ pañcavaṭīdeśaḥ saumya puṣpitakānanaḥ ।। āśramaḥ katarasmin no deśe bhavati saṃmataḥ ।। tādṛśo dṛśyatāṃ deśaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭajalāśayaḥ ।। saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ ca yatra syāt samitpuṣpakuśodakam ।।
sītāsamakṣaṃ kākutstham idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। svayaṃ tu rucire deśe kriyatām iti māṃ vada ।। vimṛśan rocayāmāsa deśaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam ।। hastau gṛhītvā hastena rāmaḥ saumitrim abravīt ।।
ihāśramapadaṃ saumya yathāvat kartum arhasi ।। adūre dṛśyate ramyā padminī padmaśobhitā ।। iyaṃ godāvarī ramyā puṣpitais tarubhir vṛtā ।। nātidūre na cāsanne mṛgayūthanipīḍitā ।।
dṛśyante girayaḥ saumya phullais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ ।। gavākṣitā ivābhānti gajāḥ paramabhaktibhiḥ ।। nīvārais timiśaiś caiva puṃnāgaiś copaśobhitāḥ ।। puṣpagulmalatopetais tais tais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ ।।
dhavāśvakarṇakhadiraiḥ śamīkiṃśukapāṭalaiḥ ।। iha vatsyāma saumitre sārdham etena pakṣiṇā ।। acireṇāśramaṃ bhrātuś cakāra sumahābalaḥ ।। sustambhāṃ maskarair dīrghaiḥ kṛtavaṃśāṃ suśobhanām ।।
snātvā padmāni cādāya saphalaḥ punar āgataḥ ।। darśayāmāsa rāmāya tad āśramapadaṃ kṛtam ।। rāghavaḥ parṇaśālāyāṃ harṣam āhārayat param ।। atisnigdhaṃ ca gāḍhaṃ ca vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।।
pradeyo yannimittaṃ te pariṣvaṅgo mayā kṛtaḥ ।। tvayā putreṇa dharmātmā na saṃvṛttaḥ pitā mama ।। tasmin deśe bahuphale nyavasat sa sukhaṃ vaśī ।। anvāsyamāno nyavasat svargaloke yathāmaraḥ ।।
śaradvyapāye hemanta ṛtur iṣṭaḥ pravartate ।। prayayāv abhiṣekārthaṃ ramyāṃ godāvarīṃ nadīm ।। pṛṣṭhato anuvrajan bhrātā saumitrir idam abravīt ।। alaṃkṛta ivābhāti yena saṃvatsaraḥ śubhaḥ ।।
jalāny anupabhogyāni subhago havyavāhanaḥ ।। kṛtāgrayaṇakāḥ kāle santo vigatakalmaṣāḥ ।। vicaranti mahīpālā yātrārthaṃ vijigīṣavaḥ ।। vihīnatilakeva strī nottarā dik prakāśate ।।
yathārthanāmā suvyaktaṃ himavān himavān giriḥ ।। divasāḥ subhagādityāś chāyāsaliladurbhagāḥ ।। śūnyāraṇyā himadhvastā divasā bhānti sāmpratam ।। śītā vṛddhatarāyāmās triyāmā yānti sāmpratam ।।
niḥśvāsāndha ivādarśaś candramā na prakāśate ।। sīteva cātapaśyāmā lakṣyate na tu śobhate ।। pravāti paścimo vāyuḥ kāle dviguṇaśītalaḥ ।। śobhante abhyudite sūrye nadadbhiḥ krauñcasārasaiḥ ।।
śobhante kiṃcidālambāḥ śālayaḥ kanakaprabhāḥ ।। dūram abhyuditaḥ sūryaḥ śaśāṅka iva lakṣyate ।। saṃraktaḥ kiṃcid āpāṇḍur ātapaḥ śobhate kṣitau ।। vanānāṃ śobhate bhūmir niviṣṭataruṇātapā ।।
prasuptā iva lakṣyante vipuṣpā vanarājayaḥ ।। himārdravālukais tīraiḥ sarito bhānti sāmpratam ।। śaityād agāgrastham api prāyeṇa rasavaj jalam ।। nālaśeṣā himadhvastā na bhānti kamalākarāḥ ।।
tapaś carati dharmātmā tvadbhaktyā bharataḥ pure ।। tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śete śīte mahītale ।। vṛtaḥ prakṛtibhir nityaṃ prayāti sarayūṃ nadīm ।। kathaṃ tv apararātreṣu sarayūm avagāhate ।।
dharmajñaḥ satyavādī ca hrīniṣedho jitendriyaḥ ।। saṃtyajya vividhān bhogān āryaṃ sarvātmanāśritaḥ ।। vanastham api tāpasye yas tvām anuvidhīyate ।। khyāto lokapravādo ayaṃ bharatenānyathākṛtaḥ ।।
kathaṃ nu sāmbā kaikeyī tādṛśī krūradarśinī ।। parivādaṃ jananyās tam asahan rāghavo abravīt ।। tām evekṣvākunāthasya bharatasya kathāṃ kuru ।। bharatasnehasaṃtaptā bāliśī kriyate punaḥ ।।
cakre abhiṣekaṃ kākutsthaḥ sānujaḥ saha sītayā ।। stuvanti smoditaṃ sūryaṃ devatāś ca samāhitāḥ ।। kṛtābhiṣekas tv agarājaputryā rudraḥ sanandī bhagavān iveśaḥ ।। tasmād godāvarītīrāt tato jagmuḥ svam āśramam ।।
kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ karma parṇaśālām upāgamat ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā cakāra vividhāḥ kathāḥ ।। taṃ deśaṃ rākṣasī kācid ājagāma yadṛcchayā ।। bhaginī rāmam āsādya dadarśa tridaśopamam ।।
sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ pārthivavyañjanānvitam ।। babhūvendropamaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasī kāmamohitā ।। viśālākṣaṃ virūpākṣī sukeśaṃ tāmramūrdhajā ।। taruṇaṃ dāruṇā vṛddhā dakṣiṇaṃ vāmabhāṣiṇī ।।
śarīrajasamāviṣṭā rākṣasī rāmam abravīt ।। āgatas tvam imaṃ deśaṃ kathaṃ rākṣasasevitam ।। ṛjubuddhitayā sarvam ākhyātum upacakrame ।। tasyāham agrajaḥ putro rāmo nāma janaiḥ śrutaḥ ।।
iyaṃ bhāryā ca vaidehī mama sīteti viśrutā ।। dharmārthaṃ dharmakāṅkṣī ca vanaṃ vastum ihāgataḥ ।। iha vā kiṃnimittaṃ tvam āgatā brūhi tattvataḥ ।। śrūyatāṃ rāma vakṣyāmi tattvārthaṃ vacanaṃ mama ।।
araṇyaṃ vicarāmīdam ekā sarvabhayaṃkarā ।। pravṛddhanidraś ca sadā kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ ।। prakhyātavīryau ca raṇe bhrātarau kharadūṣaṇau ।। cirāya bhava bhartā me sītayā kiṃ kariṣyasi ।।
aham evānurūpā te bhāryā rūpeṇa paśya mām ।। anena saha te bhrātrā bhakṣayiṣyāmi mānuṣīm ।। paśyan saha mayā kānta daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi ।। idaṃ vacanam ārebhe vaktuṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ ।।
svacchayā ślakṣṇayā vācā smitapūrvam athābravīt ।। tvadvidhānāṃ tu nārīṇāṃ suduḥkhā sasapatnatā ।। śrīmān akṛtadāraś ca lakṣmaṇo nāma vīryavān ।। anurūpaś ca te bhartā rūpasyāsya bhaviṣyati ।।
asapatnā varārohe merum arkaprabhā yathā ।। visṛjya rāmaṃ sahasā tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।। mayā saha sukhaṃ sarvān daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi ।। tataḥ śūrpaṇakhīṃ smitvā lakṣmaṇo yuktam abravīt ।।
so aham āryeṇa paravān bhrātrā kamalavarṇini ।। āryasya tvaṃ viśālākṣi bhāryā bhava yavīyasī ।। bhāryāṃ vṛddhāṃ parityajya tvām evaiṣa bhajiṣyati ।। mānuṣeṣu varārohe kuryād bhāvaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
manyate tad vacaḥ satyaṃ parihāsāvicakṣaṇā ।। sītayā saha durdharṣam abravīt kāmamohitā ।। vṛddhāṃ bhāryām avaṣṭabhya na māṃ tvaṃ bahu manyase ।। tvayā saha cariṣyāmi niḥsapatnā yathāsukham ।।
abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddhā maholkā rohiṇīm iva ।। nigṛhya rāmaḥ kupitas tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।। na kāryaḥ paśya vaidehīṃ kathaṃcit saumya jīvatīm ।। rākṣasīṃ puruṣavyāghra virūpayitum arhasi ।।
uddhṛtya khaḍgaṃ cicheda karṇanāsaṃ mahābalaḥ ।। yathāgataṃ pradudrāva ghorā śūrpaṇakhā vanam ।। nanāda vividhān nādān yathā prāvṛṣi toyadaḥ ।। pragṛhya bāhū garjantī praviveśa mahāvanam ।।
upetya taṃ bhrātaram ugratejasaṃ papāta bhūmau gaganād yathāśaniḥ ।। virūpaṇaṃ cātmani śoṇitokṣitā śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā ।। bhaginīṃ krodhasaṃtaptaḥ kharaḥ papraccha rākṣasaḥ ।। imām avasthāṃ nītā tvaṃ kenāntakasamā gatā ।।
ko ayam evaṃ mahāvīryas tvāṃ virūpāṃ cakāra ha ।। antarena sahasrākṣaṃ mahendraṃ pākaśāsanam ।। salile kṣīram āsaktaṃ niṣpibann iva sārasaḥ ।। saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ raktaṃ medinī kasya pāsyati ।।
prahṛṣṭā bhakṣayiṣyanti nihatasya mayā raṇe ।। mayāpakṛṣṭaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ śaktās trātuṃ mahāhave ।। yena tvaṃ durvinītena vane vikramya nirjitā ।। tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā vākyaṃ sabāṣpam idam abravīt ।।
puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣau cīrakṛṣṇājināmbarau ।। devau vā mānuṣau vā tau na tarkayitum utsahe ।। dṛṣṭā tatra mayā nārī tayor madhye sumadhyamā ।। imām avasthāṃ nītāhaṃ yathānāthāsatī tathā ।।
saphenaṃ pātum icchāmi rudhiraṃ raṇamūrdhani ।। tasyās tayoś ca rudhiraṃ pibeyam aham āhave ।। vyādideśa kharaḥ kruddho rākṣasān antakopamān ।। praviṣṭau daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ ghoraṃ pramadayā saha ।।
iyaṃ ca rudhiraṃ teṣāṃ bhaginī mama pāsyati ।। śīghraṃ saṃpadyatāṃ gatvā tau pramathya svatejasā ।। tatra jagmus tayā sārdhaṃ ghanā vāteritā yathā ।। rakṣasām ācacakṣe tau bhrātarau saha sītayā ।।
dadṛśuḥ sītayā sārdhaṃ vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca ।। abravīd bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam ।। imān asyā vadhiṣyāmi padavīm āgatān iha ।। tatheti lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ rāmasya pratyapūjayat ।।
cakāra sajyaṃ dharmātmā tāni rakṣāṃsi cābravīt ।। praviṣṭau sītayā sārdhaṃ duścaraṃ daṇḍakāvanam ।। vasantau daṇḍakāraṇye kimartham upahiṃsatha ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ tu niyogena prāpto ahaṃ saśarāsanaḥ ।।
yadi prāṇair ihārtho vo nivartadhvaṃ niśācarāḥ ।। ūcur vācaṃ susaṃkruddhā brahmaghnāḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ ।। paruṣāmadhurābhāṣaṃ hṛṣṭā dṛṣṭaparākramam ।। tvam eva hāsyase prāṇān adyāsmābhir hato yudhi ।।
asmākam agrataḥ sthātuṃ kiṃ punar yoddhum āhave ।। prāṇāṃs tyakṣyasi vīryaṃ ca dhanuś ca karapīḍitam ।। cikṣipus tāni śūlāni rāghavaṃ prati durjayam ।। tāvadbhir eva cicheda śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
jagrāha paramakruddhaś caturdaśa śilāśitān ।। mumoca rāghavo bāṇān vajrān iva śatakratuḥ ।। antarikṣe maholkānāṃ babhūvus tulyavarcasaḥ ।। viniṣpetus tadā bhūmau nyamajjantāśanisvanāḥ ।।
nipetuḥ śoṇitārdrāṅgā vikṛtā vigatāsavaḥ ।। paritrastā punas tatra vyasṛjad bhairavaṃ ravam ।। papāta punar evārtā saniryāseva vallarī ।। vadhaṃ ca teṣāṃ nikhilena rakṣasāṃ śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā ।।
uvāca vyaktayā vācā tām anarthārtham āgatām ।। tvatpriyārthaṃ vinirdiṣṭāḥ kimarthaṃ rudyate punaḥ ।। ghnanto api na nihantavyā na na kuryur vaco mama ।। hā nātheti vinardantī sarpavad veṣṭase kṣitau ।।
uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha mā bhaiṣīr vaiklavyaṃ tyajyatām iha ।। vimṛjya nayane sāsre kharaṃ bhrātaram abravīt ।। nihantuṃ rāghavaṃ ghorā matpriyārthaṃ salakṣmaṇam ।। samare nihatāḥ sarve sāyakair marmabhedibhiḥ ।।
rāmasya ca mahat karma mahāṃs trāso abhavan mama ।। śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ punaḥ prāptā sarvato bhayadarśinī ।। kiṃ māṃ na trāyase magnāṃ vipule śokasāgare ।। ye ca me padavīṃ prāptā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।।
daṇḍakāraṇyanilayaṃ jahi rākṣasakaṇṭakam ।। tava caivāgrataḥ prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi nirapatrapā ।। sthātuṃ pratimukhe śaktaḥ sacāpasya mahāraṇe ।। mānuṣau yan na śaknoṣi hantuṃ tau rāmalakṣmaṇau ।।
niḥsattvasyālpavīryasya vāsas te kīdṛśas tv iha ।। bhrātā cāsya mahāvīryo yena cāsmi virūpitā ।। uvāca rakṣasāṃ madhye kharaḥ kharataraṃ vacaḥ ।। na śakyate dhārayituṃ lavaṇāmbha ivotthitam ।।
ātmā duścaritaiḥ prāṇān hato yo adya vimokṣyati ।। ahaṃ rāmaṃ saha bhrātrā nayāmi yamasādanam ।। rāmasya rudhiraṃ raktam uṣṇaṃ pāsyasi rākṣasi ।। praśaśaṃsa punar maurkhyād bhrātaraṃ rakṣasāṃ varam ।।
abravīd dūṣaṇaṃ nāma kharaḥ senāpatiṃ tadā ।। rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānāṃ samareṣv anivartinām ।। lokahiṃsāvihārāṇāṃ balinām ugratejasām ।। sarvodyogam udīrṇānāṃ rakṣasāṃ saumya kāraya ।।
śarāṃś ca citrān khaḍgāṃś ca śaktīś ca vividhāḥ śitāḥ ।। vadhārthaṃ durvinītasya rāmasya raṇakovidaḥ ।। sadaśvaiḥ śabalair yuktam ācacakṣe atha dūṣaṇaḥ ।। hemacakram asaṃbādhaṃ vaidūryamayakūbaram ।।
māṅgalyaiḥ pakṣisaṃghaiś ca tārābhiś ca samāvṛtam ।। sadaśvayuktaṃ so amarṣād āruroha rathaṃ kharaḥ ।। tasthuḥ saṃparivāryainaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ ca mahābalam ।। niryātety abravīd dṛṣṭvā rathasthaḥ sarvarākṣasān ।।
nirjagāma janasthānān mahānādaṃ mahājavam ।। khaḍgaiś cakraiś ca hastasthair bhrājamānaiś ca tomaraiḥ ।। gadāsimusalair vajrair gṛhītair bhīmadarśanaiḥ ।। niryātāni janasthānāt kharacittānuvartinām ।।
kharasyāpi rathaḥ kiṃcij jagāma tadanantaram ।। kharasya matam ājñāya sārathiḥ samacodayat ।। śabdenāpūrayām āsa diśaḥ pratidiśas tathā ।। acūcudat sārathim unnadan punar mahābalo megha ivāśmavarṣavān ।।
abhyavarṣan mahāmeghas tumulo gardabhāruṇaḥ ।। same puṣpacite deśe rājamārge yadṛcchayā ।। alātacakrapratimaṃ pratigṛhya divākaram ।। samākramya mahākāyas tasthau gṛdhraḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।।
visvarān vividhāṃś cakrur māṃsādā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।। aśivaṃ yātudhānānāṃ śivā ghorā mahāsvanāḥ ।। ākāśaṃ tad anākāśaṃ cakrur bhīmā balāhakāḥ ।। diśo vā vidiśo vāpi suvyaktaṃ na cakāśire ।।
kharasyābhimukhaṃ nedus tadā ghorā mṛgāḥ khagāḥ ।। nedur balasyābhimukhaṃ jvālodgāribhir ānanaiḥ ।। jagrāha sūryaṃ svarbhānur aparvaṇi mahāgrahaḥ ।। utpetuś ca vinā rātriṃ tārāḥ khadyotasaprabhāḥ ।।
tasmin kṣaṇe babhūvuś ca vinā puṣpaphalair drumāḥ ।। vīcīkūcīti vāśyanto babhūvus tatra sārikāḥ ।। pracacāla mahī cāpi saśailavanakānanā ।। prākampata bhujaḥ savyaḥ kharaś cāsyāvasajjata ।।
lalāṭe ca rujā jātā na ca mohān nyavartata ।। abravīd rākṣasān sarvān prahasan sa kharas tadā ।। na cintayāmy ahaṃ vīryād balavān durbalān iva ।। mṛtyuṃ maraṇadharmeṇa saṃkruddho yojayāmy aham ।।
ahatvā sāyakais tīkṣṇair nopāvartitum utsahe ।। yannimittaṃ tu rāmasya lakṣmaṇasya viparyayaḥ ।। yuṣmākam etat pratyakṣaṃ nānṛtaṃ kathayāmy aham ।। vajrahastaṃ raṇe hanyāṃ kiṃ punas tau ca mānuṣau ।।
praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mṛtyupāśāvapāśitā ।। ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ ।। svasti gobrāhmaṇebhyo astu lokānāṃ ye ca saṃmatāḥ ।। cakrahasto yathā yuddhe sarvān asurapuṃgavān ।।
dadṛśur vāhinīṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasānāṃ gatāyuṣām ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ bhūyo rākṣasāś ca viniḥsṛtāḥ ।। durjayaḥ karavīrākṣaḥ paruṣaḥ kālakārmukaḥ ।। dvādaśaite mahāvīryāḥ pratasthur abhitaḥ kharam ।।
catvāra ete senāgryā dūṣaṇaṃ pṛṣṭhato anvayuḥ ।। tau rājaputrau sahasābhyupetā mālā grahāṇām iva candrasūryau ।। tān evautpātikān rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā dadarśa ha ।। prajānām ahitān dṛṣṭvā vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।।
samutthitān mahotpātān saṃhartuṃ sarvarākṣasān ।। vyomni meghā vivartante paruṣā gardabhāruṇāḥ ।। rukmapṛṣṭhāni cāpāni viveṣṭante ca lakṣmaṇa ।। agrato no bhayaṃ prāptaṃ saṃśayo jīvitasya ca ।।
ayam ākhyāti me bāhuḥ sphuramāṇo muhur muhuḥ ।। suprabhaṃ ca prasannaṃ ca tava vaktraṃ hi lakṣyate ।। niṣprabhaṃ vadanaṃ teṣāṃ bhavaty āyuḥparikṣayaḥ ।। āpadaṃ śaṅkamānena puruṣeṇa vipaścitā ।।
guhām āśraya śailasya durgāṃ pādapasaṃkulām ।। śāpito mama pādābhyāṃ gamyatāṃ vatsa māciram ।। śarān ādāya cāpaṃ ca guhāṃ durgāṃ samāśrayat ।। hanta niryuktam ity uktvā rāmaḥ kavacam āviśat ।।
babhūva rāmas timire vidhūmo agnir ivotthitaḥ ।। babhūvāvasthitas tatra jyāsvanaiḥ pūrayan diśaḥ ।। ūcuḥ paramasaṃtrastā guhyakāś ca parasparam ।। ekaś ca rāmo dharmātmā kathaṃ yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
anīkaṃ yātudhānānāṃ samantāt pratyadṛśyata ।। cāpāni visphārayatāṃ jṛmbhatāṃ cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ ।। teṣāṃ sutumulaḥ śabdaḥ pūrayāmāsa tad vanam ।। dudruvur yatra niḥśabdaṃ pṛṣṭhato nāvalokayan ।।
dhṛtanānāpraharaṇaṃ gambhīraṃ sāgaropamam ।। dadarśa kharasainyaṃ tad yuddhābhimukham udyatam ।। krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā tejasāviṣṭaṃ prāvyathan vanadevatāḥ ।।
dakṣasyeva kratuṃ hantum udyatasya pinākinaḥ ।। dadarśāśramam āgamya kharaḥ saha puraḥsaraiḥ ।। rāmasyābhimukhaṃ sūtaṃ codyatām ity acodayat ।। yatra rāmo mahābāhur eko dhunvan dhanuḥ sthitaḥ ।।
nardamānā mahānādaṃ sacivāḥ paryavārayan ।। babhūva madhye tārāṇāṃ lohitāṅga ivoditaḥ ।। rāmaṃ nānāvidhaiḥ śastrair abhyavarṣanta durjayam ।। rākṣasāḥ samare rāmaṃ nijaghnū roṣatatparāḥ ।।
abhyadhāvanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ yuddhe jighāṃsavaḥ ।। śailendram iva dhārābhir varṣamāṇā balāhakāḥ ।। tithiṣv iva mahādevo vṛtaḥ pāriṣadāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। pratijagrāha viśikhair nadyoghān iva sāgaraḥ ।।
rāmaḥ pradīptair bahubhir vajrair iva mahācalaḥ ।। babhūva rāmaḥ saṃdhyābhrair divākara ivāvṛtaḥ ।। ekaṃ sahasrair bahubhis tadā dṛṣṭvā samāvṛtam ।। sasarja niśitān bāṇāñ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
mumoca līlayā rāmaḥ kaṅkapattrān ajihmagān ।। ādadū rakṣasāṃ prāṇān pāśāḥ kālakṛtā iva ।। antarikṣagatā rejur dīptāgnisamatejasaḥ ।। viniṣpetur atīvogrā rakṣaḥprāṇāpahāriṇaḥ ।।
bahūn sahastābharaṇān ūrūn karikaropamān ।। bhīmam ārtasvaraṃ cakrur bhidyamānā niśācarāḥ ।। rāmeṇa na sukhaṃ lebhe śuṣkaṃ vanam ivāgninā ।। cikṣipuḥ paramakruddhā rāmāya rajanīcarāḥ ।।
jahāra samare prāṇāṃś cicheda ca śirodharān ।। kharam evābhyadhāvanta śaraṇārthaṃ śarārditāḥ ।। abhyadhāvata kākutsthaṃ kruddho rudram ivāntakaḥ ।। rāmam evābhyadhāvanta sālatālaśilāyudhāḥ ।।
rāmasyāsya mahāghoraṃ punas teṣāṃ ca rakṣasām ।। pratijagrāha dharmātmā rāghavas tīkṣṇasāyakaiḥ ।। rāmaḥ krodhaṃ paraṃ bheje vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām ।। śarair abhyakirat sainyaṃ sarvataḥ sahadūṣaṇam ।।
jagrāha giriśṛṅgābhaṃ parighaṃ romaharṣaṇam ।। āyasaiḥ śaṅkubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ kīrṇaṃ paravasokṣitam ।। dūṣaṇo abhyapatad rāmaṃ krūrakarmā niśācaraḥ ।। dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ cicheda sahastābharaṇau bhujau ।।
parighaś chinnahastasya śakradhvaja ivāgrataḥ ।। viṣāṇābhyāṃ viśīrṇābhyāṃ manasvīva mahāgajaḥ ।। sādhu sādhv iti kākutsthaṃ sarvabhūtāny apūjayan ।। mahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī ca mahābalaḥ ।।
sthūlākṣaḥ paṭṭiśaṃ gṛhya pramāthī ca paraśvadham ।। tīkṣṇāgraiḥ pratijagrāha samprāptān atithīn iva ।। asaṃkhyeyais tu bāṇaughaiḥ pramamātha pramāthinam ।। sa papāta hato bhūmau viṭapīva mahādrumaḥ ।।
jaghanaśeṣaṃ tejasvī tasya sainyasya sāyakaiḥ ।। nijaghnus tāni rakṣāṃsi vajrā iva mahādrumān ।। sahasraṃ ca sahasreṇa jaghāna raṇamūrdhani ।। nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ rajanīcarāḥ ।।
āstīrṇā vasudhā kṛtsnā mahāvediḥ kuśair iva ।। babhūva nirayaprakhyaṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamam ।। hatāny ekena rāmeṇa mānuṣeṇa padātinā ।। rākṣasas triśirāś caiva rāmaś ca ripusūdanaḥ ।।
rathena rāmaṃ mahatā kharas tataḥ samāsasādendra ivodyatāśaniḥ ।। rākṣasas triśirā nāma saṃnipatyedam abravīt ।। paśya rāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ saṃyuge vinipātitam ।। yathā rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi vadhārhaṃ sarvarakṣasām ।।
vinivartya raṇotsāhaṃ muhūrtaṃ prāśniko bhava ।। mayi vā nihate rāmaṃ saṃyugāyopayāsyasi ।। gaccha yudhyety anujñāto rāghavābhimukho yayau ।। abhyadravad raṇe rāmaṃ triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ ।।
vyasṛjat sadṛśaṃ nādaṃ jalārdrasyeva dundubheḥ ।। dhanuṣā pratijagrāha vidhunvan sāyakāñ śitān ।। babhūvātīva balinoḥ siṃhakuñjarayor iva ।। amarṣī kupito rāmaḥ saṃrabdham idam abravīt ।।
mamāpi pratigṛhṇīṣva śarāṃś cāpaguṇacyutān ।। triśirovakṣasi kruddho nijaghāna caturdaśa ।। nyapātayata tejasvī caturas tasya vājinaḥ ।। rāmaś cicheda bāṇena dhvajaṃ cāsya samucchritam ।।
bibheda rāmas taṃ bāṇair hṛdaye so abhavaj jaḍaḥ ।। śirāṃsy apātayat trīṇi vegavadbhis tribhiḥ śataiḥ ।। nyapatat patitaiḥ pūrvaṃ svaśirobhir niśācaraḥ ।। dravanti sma na tiṣṭhanti vyāghratrastā mṛgā iva ।।
rāmam evābhidudrāva rāhuś candramasaṃ yathā ।। kharasyāpy abhavat trāso dṛṣṭvā rāmasya vikramam ।। hatam ekena rāmeṇa dūṣaṇas triśirā api ।। āsasāda kharo rāmaṃ namucir vāsavaṃ yathā ।।
kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya kruddhān āśīviṣān iva ।। cacāra samare mārgāñ śarai rathagataḥ kharaḥ ।। pūrayāmāsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo api sumahad dhanuḥ ।। nabhaś cakārāvivaraṃ parjanya iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।
paryākāśam anākāśaṃ sarvataḥ śarasaṃkulam ।। anyonyavadhasaṃrambhād ubhayoḥ samprayudhyatoḥ ।। ājaghāna raṇe rāmaṃ totrair iva mahādvipam ।। dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni pāśahastam ivāntakam ।।
dṛṣṭvā nodvijate rāmaḥ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā ।। āsasāda raṇe rāmaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakam ।। kharaś cicheda rāmasya darśayan pāṇilāghavam ।। nijaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ śakrāśanisamaprabhān ।।
papāta kavacaṃ bhūmau rāmasyādityavarcasaḥ ।। rarāja samare rāmo vidhūmo agnir iva jvalan ।। cakārāntāya sa ripoḥ sajyam anyan mahad dhanuḥ ।। varaṃ tad dhanur udyamya kharaṃ samabhidhāvata ।।
cicheda rāmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kharasya samare dhvajam ।। jagāma dharaṇīṃ sūryo devatānām ivājñayā ।। vivyādha hṛdi marmajño mātaṃgam iva tomaraiḥ ।। viddho rudhirasiktāṅgo babhūva ruṣito bhṛśam ।।
mumoca parameṣvāsaḥ ṣaṭ śarān abhilakṣitān ।। tribhiś candrārdhavaktraiś ca vakṣasy abhijaghāna ha ।। jighāṃsū rākṣasaṃ kruddhas trayodaśa śilāśitān ।। ṣaṣṭhena ca śiraḥ saṃkhye cicheda kharasāratheḥ ।।
dvādaśena tu bāṇena kharasya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ ।। trayodaśenendrasamo bibheda samare kharam ।। gadāpāṇir avaplutya tasthau bhūmau kharas tadā ।। apūjayan prāñjalayaḥ prahṛṣṭās tadā vimānāgragatāḥ sametāḥ ।।
mṛdupūrvaṃ mahātejāḥ paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt ।। kṛtaṃ sudāruṇaṃ karma sarvalokajugupsitam ।। trayāṇām api lokānām īśvaro api na tiṣṭhati ।। tīkṣṇaṃ sarvajano hanti sarpaṃ duṣṭam ivāgatam ।।
bhraṣṭaḥ paśyati tasyāntaṃ brāhmaṇī karakād iva ।। kiṃ nu hatvā mahābhāgān phalaṃ prāpsyasi rākṣasa ।। aiśvaryaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti śīrṇamūlā iva drumāḥ ।। ghoraṃ paryāgate kāle drumaḥ puṣpam ivārtavam ।।
saviṣāṇām ivānnānāṃ bhuktānāṃ kṣaṇadācara ।। aham āsādito rājā prāṇān hantuṃ niśācara ।। vidārya nipatiṣyanti valmīkam iva pannagāḥ ।। tān adya nihataḥ saṃkhye sasainyo anugamiṣyasi ।।
nirayasthaṃ vimānasthā ye tvayā hiṃsitāḥ purā ।। adya te pātayiṣyāmi śiras tālaphalaṃ yathā ।। pratyuvāca tato rāmaṃ prahasan krodhamūrchitaḥ ।। ātmanā katham ātmānam apraśasyaṃ praśaṃsasi ।।
kathayanti na te kiṃcit tejasā svena garvitāḥ ।। nirarthakaṃ vikatthante yathā rāma vikatthase ।। mṛtyukāle hi samprāpte svayam aprastave stavam ।। suvarṇapratirūpeṇa tapteneva kuśāgninā ।।
dharādharam ivākampyaṃ parvataṃ dhātubhiś citam ।। trayāṇām api lokānāṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ ।। astaṃ gaccheddhi savitā yuddhavighnas tato bhavet ।। tvadvināśāt karomy adya teṣām aśrupramārjanam ।।
kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya pradīptām aśaniṃ yathā ।। bhasma vṛkṣāṃś ca gulmāṃś ca kṛtvāgāt tatsamīpataḥ ।। antarikṣagatāṃ rāmaś cicheda bahudhā śaraiḥ ।। gadāmantrauṣadhibalair vyālīva vinipātitā ।।
smayamānaḥ kharaṃ vākyaṃ saṃrabdham idam abravīt ।। śaktihīnataro matto vṛthā tvam avagarjasi ।। abhidhānapragalbhasya tava pratyayaghātinī ।। rākṣasānāṃ karomīti mithyā tad api te vacaḥ ।।
prāṇān apahariṣyāmi garutmān amṛtaṃ yathā ।। vidāritasya madbāṇair mahī pāsyati śoṇitam ।। svapsyase gāṃ samāśliṣya durlabhāṃ pramadām iva ।। bhaviṣyanty aśaraṇyānāṃ śaraṇyā daṇḍakā ime ।।
nirbhayā vicariṣyanti sarvato munayo vane ।। bāṣpārdravadanā dīnā bhayād anyabhayāvahāḥ ।। anurūpakulāḥ patnyo yāsāṃ tvaṃ patir īdṛśaḥ ।। tvatkṛte śaṅkitair agnau munibhiḥ pātyate haviḥ ।।
kharo nirbhartsayāmāsa roṣāt kharatarasvanaḥ ।। vācyāvācyaṃ tato hi tvaṃ mṛtyuvaśyo na budhyase ।। kāryākāryaṃ na jānanti te nirastaṣaḍindriyāḥ ।। sa dadarśa mahāsālam avidūre niśācaraḥ ।।
sa tam utpāṭayāmāsa saṃdṛśya daśanacchadam ।। rāmam uddiśya cikṣepa hatas tvam iti cābravīt ।। roṣam āhārayat tīvraṃ nihantuṃ samare kharam ।। nirbibheda sahasreṇa bāṇānāṃ samare kharam ।।
gireḥ prasravaṇasyeva toyadhārāparisravaḥ ।। matto rudhiragandhena tam evābhyadravad drutam ।। apāsarpat pratipadaṃ kiṃcit tvaritavikramaḥ ।। kharasya rāmo jagrāha brahmadaṇḍam ivāparam ।।
saṃdadhe ca sa dharmātmā mumoca ca kharaṃ prati ।। rāmeṇa dhanur udyamya kharasyorasi cāpatat ।। rudreṇaiva vinirdagdhaḥ śvetāraṇye yathāndhakaḥ ।। balo vendrāśanihato nipapāta hataḥ kharaḥ ।।
sabhājya muditā rāmam idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।। śarabhaṅgāśramaṃ puṇyam ājagāma puraṃdaraḥ ।। eṣāṃ vadhārthaṃ krūrāṇāṃ rakṣasāṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।। sukhaṃ dharmaṃ cariṣyanti daṇḍakeṣu maharṣayaḥ ।।
giridurgād viniṣkramya saṃviveśāśramaṃ sukhī ।। praviveśāśramaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇenābhivāditaḥ ।। babhūva hṛṣṭā vaidehī bhartāraṃ pariṣasvaje ।। hatāny ekena rāmeṇa rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām ।।
dṛṣṭvā punar mahānādaṃ nanāda jaladopamā ।। jagāma paramodvignā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇapālitām ।। upopaviṣṭaṃ sacivair marudbhir iva vāsavam ।। rukmavedigataṃ prājyaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam ।।
ajeyaṃ samare śūraṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam ।। airāvataviṣāṇāgrair utkṛṣṭakiṇavakṣasam ।। viśālavakṣasaṃ vīraṃ rājalakṣmaṇalakṣitam ।। subhujaṃ śukladaśanaṃ mahāsyaṃ parvatopamam ।।
āhatāṅgaṃ samastaiś ca devapraharaṇais tathā ।। kṣeptāraṃ parvatāgrāṇāṃ surāṇāṃ ca pramardanam ।। sarvadivyāstrayoktāraṃ yajñavighnakaraṃ sadā ।। takṣakasya priyāṃ bhāryāṃ parājitya jahāra yaḥ ।।
vimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ tasya kāmagaṃ vai jahāra yaḥ ।। vināśayati yaḥ krodhād devodyānāni vīryavān ।। nivārayati bāhubhyāṃ yaḥ śailaśikharopamaḥ ।। purā svayambhuve dhīraḥ śirāṃsy upajahāra yaḥ ।।
abhayaṃ yasya saṃgrāme mṛtyuto mānuṣād ṛte ।। havirdhāneṣu yaḥ somam upahanti mahābalaḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvalokabhayāvaham ।। rākṣasendraṃ mahābhāgaṃ paulastyakulanandanam ।।
sudāruṇaṃ vākyam abhītacāriṇī mahātmanā śūrpaṇakhā virūpitā ।। amātyamadhye saṃkruddhā paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt ।। samutpannaṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ boddhavyaṃ nāvabudhyase ।। lubdhaṃ na bahu manyante śmaśānāgnim iva prajāḥ ।।
sa tu vai saha rājyena taiś ca kāryair vinaśyati ।। varjayanti narā dūrān nadīpaṅkam iva dvipāḥ ।। te na vṛddhyā prakāśante girayaḥ sāgare yathā ।। ayuktacāraś capalaḥ kathaṃ rājā bhaviṣyasi ।।
asvādhīnā narendrāṇāṃ prākṛtais te janaiḥ samāḥ ।। cāreṇa tasmād ucyante rājāno dīrghacakṣuṣaḥ ।। svajanaṃ ca janasthānaṃ hataṃ yo nāvabudhyase ।। hatāny ekena rāmeṇa kharaś ca sahadūṣaṇaḥ ।।
dharṣitaṃ ca janasthānaṃ rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। viṣaye sve samutpannaṃ bhayaṃ yo nāvabudhyase ।। vyasane sarvabhūtāni nābhidhāvanti pārthivam ।। krodhanaṃ vyasane hanti svajano api narādhipam ।।
kṣipraṃ rājyāc cyuto dīnas tṛṇais tulyo bhaviṣyati ।। na tu sthānāt paribhraṣṭaiḥ kāryaṃ syād vasudhādhipaiḥ ।। evaṃ rājyāt paribhraṣṭaḥ samartho api nirarthakaḥ ।। kṛtajño dharmaśīlaś ca sa rājā tiṣṭhate ciram ।।
vyaktakrodhaprasādaś ca sa rājā pūjyate janaiḥ ।। yasya te aviditaś cārai rakṣasāṃ sumahān vadhaḥ ।। ayuktabuddhir guṇadoṣaniścaye vipannarājyo na cirād vipatsyate ।। dhanena darpeṇa balena cānvito vicintayāmāsa ciraṃ sa rāvaṇaḥ ।।
amātyamadhye saṃkruddhaḥ paripapraccha rāvaṇaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ praviṣṭaś ca suduścaram ।। kharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇas triśirās tathā ।। tato rāmaṃ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame ।।
kandarpasamarūpaś ca rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ ।। dīptān kṣipati nārācān sarpān iva mahāviṣān ।। na kārmukaṃ vikarṣantaṃ rāmaṃ paśyāmi saṃyuge ।। indreṇevottamaṃ sasyam āhataṃ tv aśmavṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।
nihatāni śarais tīkṣṇais tenaikena padātinā ।। ṛṣīṇām abhayaṃ dattaṃ kṛtakṣemāś ca daṇḍakāḥ ।। strīvadhaṃ śaṅkamānena rāmeṇa viditātmanā ।। anuraktaś ca bhaktaś ca lakṣmaṇo nāma vīryavān ।।
rāmasya dakṣiṇo bāhur nityaṃ prāṇo bahiścaraḥ ।। sītā nāma varārohā vaidehī tanumadhyamā ।। tathārūpā mayā nārī dṛṣṭapūrvā mahītale ।। atijīvet sa sarveṣu lokeṣv api puraṃdarāt ।।
tavānurūpā bhāryā sā tvaṃ ca tasyās tathā patiḥ ।। bhāryārthe tu tavānetum udyatāhaṃ varānanām ।। manmathasya śarāṇāṃ ca tvaṃ vidheyo bhaviṣyasi ।। śīghram uddhriyatāṃ pādo jayārtham iha dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
vadhāt tasya nṛśaṃsasya rāmasyāśramavāsinaḥ ।। hatanāthāṃ sukhaṃ sītāṃ yathāvad upabhokṣyase ।। kriyatāṃ nirviśaṅkena vacanaṃ mama rāghava ।। kharaṃ ca buddhvā nihataṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ tvam adya kṛtyaṃ pratipattum arhasi ।।
sacivān abhyanujñāya kāryaṃ buddhvā jagāma ha ।। doṣāṇāṃ ca guṇānāṃ ca sampradhārya balābalam ।। sthirabuddhis tato ramyāṃ yānaśālāṃ jagāma ha ।। sūtaṃ saṃcodayāmāsa rathaḥ saṃyujyatām iti ।।
rathaṃ saṃyojayāmāsa tasyābhimatam uttamam ।। piśācavadanair yuktaṃ kharaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। rākṣasādhipatiḥ śrīmān yayau nadanadīpatim ।। snigdhavaiḍūryasaṃkāśas taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
tridaśārir munīndraghno daśaśīrṣa ivādrirāṭ ।। vidyunmaṇḍalavān meghaḥ sabalāka ivāmbare ।। nānāpuṣpaphalair vṛkṣair anukīrṇaṃ sahasraśaḥ ।। viśālair āśramapadair vedimadbhiḥ samāvṛtam ।।
sālais tālais tamālaiś ca tarubhiś ca supuṣpitaiḥ ।। nāgaiḥ suparṇair gandharvaiḥ kiṃnaraiś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। ājair vaikhānasair māṣair vālakhilyair marīcipaiḥ ।। krīḍāratividhijñābhir apsarobhiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
devadānavasaṃghaiś ca caritaṃ tv amṛtāśibhiḥ ।। vaiḍūryaprastaraṃ ramyaṃ snigdhaṃ sāgaratejasā ।। tūryagītābhijuṣṭāni vimānāni samantataḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva dadarśa dhanadānujaḥ ।।
vanāni paśyan saumyāni ghrāṇatṛptikarāṇi ca ।। takkolānāṃ ca jātyānāṃ phalānāṃ ca sugandhinām ।। muktānāṃ ca samūhāni śuṣyamāṇāni tīrataḥ ।। kāñcanāni ca śailāni rājatāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
dhanadhānyopapannāni strīratnair āvṛtāni ca ।। taṃ samaṃ sarvataḥ snigdhaṃ mṛdusaṃsparśamārutam ।। tatrāpaśyat sa meghābhaṃ nyagrodham ṛṣibhir vṛtam ।। bhakṣārthaṃ garuḍaḥ śākhām ājagāma mahābalaḥ ।।
suparṇaḥ parṇabahulāṃ babhañjātha mahābalaḥ ।। ajā babhūvur dhūmrāś ca saṃgatāḥ paramarṣayaḥ ।। jagāmādāya vegena tau cobhau gajakacchapau ।। praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mokṣayitvā mahāmunīn ।।
amṛtānayanārthaṃ vai cakāra matimān matim ।। mahendrabhavanād guptam ājahārāmṛtaṃ tataḥ ।। nāmnā subhadraṃ nyagrodhaṃ dadarśa dhanadānujaḥ ।। dadarśāśramam ekānte puṇye ramye vanāntare ।।
dadarśa niyatāhāraṃ mārīcaṃ nāma rākṣasam ।। tataḥ paścād idaṃ vākyam abravīd vākyakovidaḥ ।। ārto asmi mama cārtasya bhavān hi paramā gatiḥ ।। dūṣaṇaś ca mahābāhuḥ svasā śūrpaṇakhā ca me ।।
anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā labdhalakṣā niśācarāḥ ।। bādhamānā mahāraṇye munīn ye dharmacāriṇaḥ ।। śūrāṇāṃ labdhalakṣāṇāṃ kharacittānuvartinām ।। saṃgatāḥ param āyattā rāmeṇa saha saṃyuge ।।
anuktvā paruṣaṃ kiṃcic charair vyāpāritaṃ dhanuḥ ।। nihatāni śarais tīkṣṇair mānuṣeṇa padātinā ।। hatvā triśirasaṃ cāpi nirbhayā daṇḍakāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। sa hantā tasya sainyasya rāmaḥ kṣatriyapāṃsanaḥ ।।
tyaktadharmas tv adharmātmā bhūtānām ahite rataḥ ।। karṇanāsāpahāreṇa bhaginī me virūpitā ।। ānayiṣyāmi vikramya sahāyas tatra me bhava ।। bhrātṛbhiś ca surān yuddhe samagrān nābhicintaye ।।
vīrye yuddhe ca darpe ca na hy asti sadṛśas tava ।। śṛṇu tat karma sāhāyye yat kāryaṃ vacanān mama ।। āśrame tasya rāmasya sītāyāḥ pramukhe cara ।। gṛhyatām iti bhartāraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ cābhidhāsyati ।।
nirābādho hariṣyāmi rāhuś candraprabhām iva ।। viśrabdhaḥ prahariṣyāmi kṛtārthenāntarātmanā ।। śuṣkaṃ samabhavad vaktraṃ paritrasto babhūva ca ।। kṛtāñjalis tattvam uvāca vākyaṃ hitaṃ ca tasmai hitam ātmanaś ca ।।
pratyuvāca mahāprājño mārīco rākṣaseśvaram ।। apriyasya ca pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ ।। ayuktacāraś capalo mahendravaruṇopamam ।। api rāmo na saṃkruddhaḥ kuryāl lokam arākṣasam ।।
api sītā nimittaṃ ca na bhaved vyasanaṃ mahat ।। na vinaśyet purī laṅkā tvayā saha sarākṣasā ।। ātmānaṃ svajanaṃ rāṣṭraṃ sa rājā hanti durmatiḥ ।। na lubdho na ca duḥśīlo na ca kṣatriyapāṃsanaḥ ।।
na ca tīkṣṇo hi bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca hite rataḥ ।। kariṣyāmīti dharmātmā tataḥ pravrajito vanam ।। hitvā rājyaṃ ca bhogāṃś ca praviṣṭo daṇḍakāvanam ।। anṛtaṃ na śrutaṃ caiva naiva tvaṃ vaktum arhasi ।।
rājā sarvasya lokasya devānām iva vāsavaḥ ।। icchasi prasabhaṃ hartuṃ prabhām iva vivasvataḥ ।। rāmāgniṃ sahasā dīptaṃ na praveṣṭuṃ tvam arhasi ।। cāpabāṇadharaṃ vīraṃ śatrusenāpahāriṇam ।।
nātyāsādayituṃ tāta rāmāntakam ihārhasi ।। na tvaṃ samarthas tāṃ hartuṃ rāmacāpāśrayāṃ vane ।। dīptasyeva hutāśasya śikhā sītā sumadhyamā ।। jīvitaṃ ca sukhaṃ caiva rājyaṃ caiva sudurlabham ।।
mantrayitvā tu dharmiṣṭhaiḥ kṛtvā niścayam ātmanaḥ ।। hitaṃ hi tava niścitya kṣamaṃ tvaṃ kartum arhasi ।। idaṃ hi bhūyaḥ śṛṇu vākyam uttamaṃ kṣamaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca niśācarādhipa ।। balaṃ nāgasahasrasya dhārayan parvatopamaḥ ।।
vyacaraṃ daṇḍakāraṇyam ṛṣimāṃsāni bhakṣayan ।। svayaṃ gatvā daśarathaṃ narendram idam abravīt ।। mārīcān me bhayaṃ ghoraṃ samutpannaṃ nareśvara ।। pratyuvāca mahābhāgaṃ viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim ।।
vadhiṣyāmi muniśreṣṭha śatruṃ tava yathepsitam ।। rāmān nānyad balaṃ loke paryāptaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥ ।। gamiṣye rāmam ādāya svasti te astu paraṃtapa ।। jagāma paramaprīto viśvāmitraḥ svam āśramam ।।
babhūvāvasthito rāmaś citraṃ visphārayan dhanuḥ ।। ekavastradharo dhanvī śikhī kanakamālayā ।। adṛśyata tadā rāmo bālacandra ivoditaḥ ।। balī dattavaro darpād ājagāma tadāśramam ।।
māṃ tu dṛṣṭvā dhanuḥ sajyam asambhrāntaś cakāra ha ।। viśvāmitrasya tāṃ vedim adhyadhāvaṃ kṛtatvaraḥ ।। tenāhaṃ tāḍitaḥ kṣiptaḥ samudre śatayojane ।। prāpya saṃjñāṃ cirāt tāta laṅkāṃ prati gataḥ purīm ।।
akṛtāstreṇa rāmeṇa bālenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। kariṣyasy āpadaṃ ghorāṃ kṣipraṃ prāpya naśiṣyasi ।। rakṣasāṃ caiva saṃtāpam anarthaṃ cāhariṣyasi ।। drakṣyasi tvaṃ purīṃ laṅkāṃ vinaṣṭāṃ maithilīkṛte ।।
parapāpair vinaśyanti matsyā nāgahrade yathā ।। drakṣyasy abhihatān bhūmau tava doṣāt tu rākṣasān ।। hataśeṣān aśaraṇān drakṣyasi tvaṃ niśācarān ।। pradagdhabhavanāṃ laṅkāṃ drakṣyasi tvam asaṃśayam ।।
bhava svadāranirataḥ svakulaṃ rakṣa rākṣasa ।। yadīcchasi ciraṃ bhoktuṃ mā kṛthā rāmavipriyam ।। gamiṣyasi kṣīṇabalaḥ sabāndhavo yamakṣayaṃ rāmaśarāttajīvitaḥ ।। idānīm api yad vṛttaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yad uttaram ।।
sahito mṛgarūpābhyāṃ praviṣṭo daṇḍakāvanam ।। vyacaraṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ māṃsabhakṣo mahāmṛgaḥ ।। atyantaghoro vyacaraṃ tāpasāṃs tān pradharṣayan ।। rudhirāṇi pibaṃs teṣāṃ tathā māṃsāni bhakṣayan ।।
tadā rudhiramatto ahaṃ vyacaraṃ daṇḍakāvanam ।। āsādayaṃ tadā rāmaṃ tāpasaṃ dharmam āśritam ।। tāpasaṃ niyatāhāraṃ sarvabhūtahite ratam ।। tāpaso ayam iti jñātvā pūrvavairam anusmaran ।।
jighāṃsur akṛtaprajñas taṃ prahāram anusmaran ।। vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ suparṇānilatulyagāḥ ।। ājagmuḥ sahitāḥ sarve trayaḥ saṃnataparvaṇaḥ ।। samutkrāntas tato muktas tāv ubhau rākṣasau hatau ।।
iha pravrājito yuktas tāpaso ahaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। gṛhītadhanuṣaṃ rāmaṃ pāśahastam ivāntakam ।। rāmabhūtam idaṃ sarvam araṇyaṃ pratibhāti me ।। dṛṣṭvā svapnagataṃ rāmam udbhramāmi vicetanaḥ ।।
ratnāni ca rathāś caiva trāsaṃ saṃjanayanti me ।। na te rāmakathā kāryā yadi māṃ draṣṭum icchasi ।। sabāndhavas tyakṣyasi jīvitaṃ raṇe hato adya rāmeṇa śarair ajihmagaiḥ ।। ukto na pratijagrāha martukāma ivauṣadham ।।
abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyam ayuktaṃ kālacoditaḥ ।। vākyaṃ niṣphalam atyarthaṃ bījam uptam ivoṣare ।। pāpaśīlasya mūrkhasya mānuṣasya viśeṣataḥ ।। strīvākyaṃ prākṛtaṃ śrutvā vanam ekapade gataḥ ।।
prāṇaiḥ priyatarā sītā hartavyā tava saṃnidhau ।। na vyāvartayituṃ śakyā sendrair api surāsuraiḥ ।। apāyaṃ vāpy upāyaṃ vā kāryasyāsya viniścaye ।। udyatāñjalinā rājño ya icched bhūtim ātmanaḥ ।।
upacāreṇa yuktaṃ ca vaktavyo vasudhādhipaḥ ।। nābhinandati tad rājā mānārho mānavarjitam ।। auṣṇyaṃ tathā vikramaṃ ca saumyaṃ daṇḍaṃ prasannatām ।। tvaṃ tu dharmam avijñāya kevalaṃ moham āsthitaḥ ।।
asmiṃs tu sa bhavān kṛtye sāhāyyaṃ kartum arhasi ।। pralobhayitvā vaidehīṃ yatheṣṭaṃ gantum arhasi ।। ānayainam iti kṣipraṃ rāmaṃ vakṣyati maithilī ।। ānayiṣyāmi vaidehīṃ sahasrākṣaḥ śacīm iva ।।
rājyasyārdhaṃ pradāsyāmi mārīca tava suvrata ।। laṅkāṃ prati gamiṣyāmi kṛtakāryaḥ saha tvayā ।। rājño hi pratikūlastho na jātu sukham edhate ।। etad yathāvat parigṛhya buddhyā yad atra pathyaṃ kuru tat tathā tvam ।।
abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ mārīco rākṣasādhipam ।। saputrasya sarāṣṭrasya sāmātyasya niśācara ।। kenedam upadiṣṭaṃ te mṛtyudvāram upāyataḥ ।। icchanti tvāṃ vinaśyantam uparuddhaṃ balīyasā ।।
yas tvām icchati naśyantaṃ svakṛtena niśācara ।। ye tvām utpatham ārūḍhaṃ na nigṛhṇanti sarvaśaḥ ।। nigrāhyaḥ sarvathā sadbhir na nigrāhyo nigṛhyase ।। svāmiprasādāt sacivāḥ prāpnuvanti niśācara ।।
vyasanaṃ svāmivaiguṇyāt prāpnuvantītare janāḥ ।। tasmāt sarvāsv avasthāsu rakṣitavyo narādhipaḥ ।। na cāpi pratikūlena nāvinītena rākṣasa ।। viṣameṣu rathāḥ śīghraṃ mandasārathayo yathā ।।
pareṣām aparādhena vinaṣṭāḥ saparicchadāḥ ।। rakṣyamāṇā na vardhante meṣā gomāyunā yathā ।। yeṣāṃ tvaṃ karkaśo rājā durbuddhir ajitendriyaḥ ।। atra kiṃ śobhanaṃ yat tvaṃ sasainyo vinaśiṣyasi ।।
anena kṛtakṛtyo asmi mriye yad ariṇā hataḥ ।। ātmānaṃ ca hataṃ viddhi hṛtvā sītāṃ sabāndhavam ।। naiva tvam asi naivāhaṃ naiva laṅkā na rākṣasāḥ ।। paretakalpā hi gatāyuṣo narā hitaṃ na gṛhṇanti suhṛdbhir īritam ।।
gacchāvety abravīd dīno bhayād rātriṃcaraprabhoḥ ।। madvidhodyataśastreṇa vinaṣṭaṃ jīvitaṃ ca me ।। eṣa gacchāmy ahaṃ tāta svasti te astu niśācara ।। pariṣvajya susaṃśliṣṭam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
idānīm asi mārīcaḥ pūrvam anyo niśācaraḥ ।। mayā saha ratho yuktaḥ piśācavadanaiḥ kharaiḥ ।। āruhya yayatuḥ śīghraṃ tasmād āśramamaṇḍalāt ।। girīṃś ca saritaḥ sarvā rāṣṭrāṇi nagarāṇi ca ।।
dadarśa sahamarīco rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ ।। haste gṛhītvā mārīcaṃ rāvaṇo vākyam abravīt ।। kriyatāṃ tat sakhe śīghraṃ yadarthaṃ vayam āgatāḥ ।। mṛgo bhūtvāśramadvāri rāmasya vicacāra ha ।।
raktapadmotpalamukha indranīlotpalaśravāḥ ।। madhūkanibhapārśvaś ca kañjakiñjalkasaṃnibhaḥ ।। indrāyudhasavarṇena pucchenordhvaṃ virājitaḥ ।। kṣaṇena rākṣaso jāto mṛgaḥ paramaśobhanaḥ ।।
manoharaṃ darśanīyaṃ rūpaṃ kṛtvā sa rākṣasaḥ ।। vicaran gacchate samyak śādvalāni samantataḥ ।। viṭapīnāṃ kisalayān bhaṅktvādan vicacāra ha ।। samāśrayan mandagatiḥ sītāsaṃdarśanaṃ tadā ।।
rāmāśramapadābhyāśe vicacāra yathāsukham ।। gatvā muhūrtaṃ tvarayā punaḥ pratinivartate ।। āśramadvāram āgamya mṛgayūthāni gacchati ।। sītādarśanam ākāṅkṣan rākṣaso mṛgatāṃ gataḥ ।।
samudvīkṣya ca sarve taṃ mṛgā ye anye vanecarāḥ ।। rākṣasaḥ so api tān vanyān mṛgān mṛgavadhe rataḥ ।। tasminn eva tataḥ kāle vaidehī śubhalocanā ।। karṇikārān aśokāṃś ca cūtāṃś ca madirekṣaṇā ।।
muktāmaṇivicitrāṅgaṃ dadarśa paramāṅganā ।। vismayotphullanayanā sasnehaṃ samudaikṣata ।। vicacāra tatas tatra dīpayann iva tad vanam ।। vismayaṃ paramaṃ sītā jagāma janakātmajā ।।
hemarājatavarṇābhyāṃ pārśvābhyām upaśobhitam ।। bhartāram api cākrandal lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva sāyudham ।। vīkṣamāṇau tu taṃ deśaṃ tadā dadṛśatur mṛgam ।। tam evainam ahaṃ manye mārīcaṃ rākṣasaṃ mṛgam ।।
anena nihatā rāma rājānaḥ kāmarūpiṇā ।। bhānumatpuruṣavyāghra gandharvapurasaṃnibham ।। jagatyāṃ jagatīnātha māyaiṣā hi na saṃśayaḥ ।। uvāca sītā saṃhṛṣṭā chadmanā hṛtacetanā ।।
ānayainaṃ mahābāho krīḍārthaṃ no bhaviṣyati ।। mṛgāś caranti sahitāś camarāḥ sṛmarās tathā ।। vicaranti mahābāho rūpaśreṣṭhā mahābalāḥ ।। tejasā kṣamayā dīptyā yathāyaṃ mṛgasattamaḥ ।।
dyotayan vanam avyagraṃ śobhate śaśisaṃnibhaḥ ।। mṛgo adbhuto vicitro asau hṛdayaṃ haratīva me ।। āścaryabhūtaṃ bhavati vismayaṃ janayiṣyati ।। antaḥpuravibhūṣārtho mṛga eṣa bhaviṣyati ।।
mṛgarūpam idaṃ divyaṃ vismayaṃ janayiṣyati ।। ajinaṃ naraśārdūla ruciraṃ me bhaviṣyati ।। śaṣpabṛsyāṃ vinītāyām icchāmy aham upāsitum ।। vapuṣā tv asya sattvasya vismayo janito mama ।।
babhūva rāghavasyāpi mano vismayam āgatam ।। uvāca rāghavo hṛṣṭo bhrātaraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ vacaḥ ।। rūpaśreṣṭhatayā hy eṣa mṛgo adya na bhaviṣyati ।। kutaḥ pṛthivyāṃ saumitre yo asya kaścit samo mṛgaḥ ।।
śobhante mṛgam āśritya citrāḥ kanakabindubhiḥ ।। jihvāṃ mukhān niḥsarantīṃ meghād iva śatahradām ।। kasya nāmābhirūpo asau na mano lobhayen mṛgaḥ ।। nānāratnamayaṃ divyaṃ na mano vismayaṃ vrajet ।।
ghnanti lakṣmaṇa rājāno mṛgayāyāṃ mahāvane ।। dhātavo vividhāś cāpi maṇiratnasuvarṇinaḥ ।। manasā cintitaṃ sarvaṃ yathā śukrasya lakṣmaṇa ।। tam artham arthaśāstrajñaḥ prāhur arthyāś ca lakṣmaṇa ।।
upavekṣyati vaidehī mayā saha sumadhyamā ।। bhaved etasya sadṛśī sparśaneneti me matiḥ ।। ubhāv etau mṛgau divyau tārāmṛgamahīmṛgau ।। māyaiṣā rākṣasasyeti kartavyo asya vadho mayā ।।
vane vicaratā pūrvaṃ hiṃsitā munipuṃgavāḥ ।। nihatāḥ parameṣvāsās tasmād vadhyas tv ayaṃ mṛgaḥ ।। udarastho dvijān hanti svagarbho aśvatarīm iva ।। agastyaṃ tejasā yuktaṃ bhakṣyas tasya babhūva ha ।।
utsmayitvā tu bhagavān vātāpim idam abravīt ।। jīvaloke dvijaśreṣṭhās tasmād asi jarāṃ gataḥ ।। madvidhaṃ yo atimanyeta dharmanityaṃ jitendriyam ।। iha tvaṃ bhava saṃnaddho yantrito rakṣa maithilīm ।।
aham enaṃ vadhiṣyāmi grahīṣyāmy athavā mṛgam ।। paśya lakṣmaṇa vaidehīṃ mṛgatvaci gataspṛhām ।। apramattena te bhāvyam āśramasthena sītayā ।। hatvaitac carma ādāya śīghram eṣyāmi lakṣmaṇa ।।
bhavāpramattaḥ pratigṛhya maithilīṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ sarvata eva śaṅkitaḥ ।। babandhāsiṃ mahātejā jāmbūnadamayatsarum ।। ābadhya ca kalāpau dvau jagāmodagravikramaḥ ।। babhūvāntarhitas trāsāt punaḥ saṃdarśane abhavat ।।
taṃ sa paśyati rūpeṇa dyotamānam ivāgrataḥ ।। ativṛttam iṣoḥ pātāl lobhayānaṃ kadācana ।। daśyamānam adṛśyaṃ ca navoddeśeṣu keṣucit ।। muhūrtād eva dadṛśe muhur dūrāt prakāśate ।।
āsīt kruddhas tu kākutstho vivaśas tena mohitaḥ ।। mṛgaiḥ parivṛto vanyair adūrāt pratyadṛśyata ।। saṃdhāya sudṛḍhe cāpe vikṛṣya balavad balī ।। mumoca jvalitaṃ dīptam astrabrahmavinirmitam ।।
mārīcasyaiva hṛdayaṃ vibhedāśanisaṃnibhaḥ ।। mriyamāṇas tu mārīco jahau tāṃ kṛtrimāṃ tanum ।। sadṛśaṃ rāghavasyaiva hā sīte lakṣmaṇeti ca ।। cakre sa sumahākāyo mārīco jīvitaṃ tyajan ।।
hemamālī mahādaṃṣṭro rākṣaso abhūc charāhataḥ ।। jagāma manasā sītāṃ lakṣmaṇasya vacaḥ smaran ।। mamāra rākṣasaḥ so ayaṃ śrutvā sītā kathaṃ bhavet ।। iti saṃcintya dharmātmā rāmo hṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ ।।
rākṣasaṃ mṛgarūpaṃ taṃ hatvā śrutvā ca tatsvaram ।। tvaramāṇo janasthānaṃ sasārābhimukhas tadā ।। uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ sītā gaccha jānīhi rāghavam ।। krośataḥ paramārtasya śrutaḥ śabdo mayā bhṛśam ।।
taṃ kṣipram abhidhāva tvaṃ bhrātaraṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇam ।। na jagāma tathoktas tu bhrātur ājñāya śāsanam ।। saumitre mitrarūpeṇa bhrātus tvam asi śatruvat ।। icchasi tvaṃ vinaśyantaṃ rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇa matkṛte ।।
tena tiṣṭhasi viśrabdhas tam apaśyan mahādyutim ।। kartavyam iha tiṣṭhantyā yat pradhānas tvam āgataḥ ।। abravīl lakṣmaṇas trastāṃ sītāṃ mṛgavadhūm iva ।। rākṣaseṣu piśāceṣu kiṃnareṣu mṛgeṣu ca ।।
yo rāmaṃ pratiyudhyeta samare vāsavopamam ।। na tvām asmin vane hātum utsahe rāghavaṃ vinā ।। tribhir lokaiḥ samudyuktaiḥ seśvaraiḥ sāmarair api ।। āgamiṣyati te bhartā śīghraṃ hatvā mṛgottamam ।।
gandharvanagaraprakhyā māyā sā tasya rakṣasaḥ ।। rāmeṇa tvaṃ varārohe na tvāṃ tyaktum ihotsahe ।। kharasya nidhane devi janasthānavadhaṃ prati ।। hiṃsāvihārā vaidehi na cintayitum arhasi ।।
abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ satyavādinam ।। ahaṃ tava priyaṃ manye tenaitāni prabhāṣase ।। tvadvidheṣu nṛśaṃseṣu nityaṃ pracchannacāriṣu ।। mama hetoḥ praticchannaḥ prayukto bharatena vā ।।
upasaṃśritya bhartāraṃ kāmayeyaṃ pṛthag janam ।। rāmaṃ vinā kṣaṇam api na hi jīvāmi bhūtale ।। abravīl lakṣmaṇaḥ sītāṃ prāñjalir vijitendriyaḥ ।। vākyam apratirūpaṃ tu na citraṃ strīṣu maithili ।।
vimuktadharmāś capalās tīkṣṇā bhedakarāḥ striyaḥ ।। nyāyavādī yathā vākyam ukto ahaṃ paruṣaṃ tvayā ।। strītvād duṣṭasvabhāvena guruvākye vyavasthitam ।। rakṣantu tvāṃ viśālākṣi samagrā vanadevatāḥ ।।
api tvāṃ saha rāmeṇa paśyeyaṃ punar āgataḥ ।। pratyuvāca tato vākyaṃ tīvraṃ bāṣpapariplutā ।। ābandhiṣye athavā tyakṣye viṣame deham ātmanaḥ ।। na tv ahaṃ rāghavād anyaṃ padāpi puruṣaṃ spṛśe ।।
pāṇibhyāṃ rudatī duḥkhād udaraṃ prajaghāna ha ।। āśvāsayāmāsa na caiva bhartus taṃ bhrātaraṃ kiṃcid uvāca sītā ।। avekṣamāṇo bahuśaś ca maithilīṃ jagāma rāmasya samīpam ātmavān ।। sa vikāṅkṣan bhṛśaṃ rāmaṃ pratasthe nacirād iva ।।
abhicakrāma vaidehīṃ parivrājakarūpadhṛk ।। parivrājakarūpeṇa vaidehīṃ samupāgamat ।। rahitāṃ sūryacandrābhyāṃ saṃdhyām iva mahattamaḥ ।। rohiṇīṃ śaśinā hīnāṃ grahavad bhṛśadāruṇaḥ ।।
samīkṣya na prakampante na pravāti ca mārutaḥ ।। stimitaṃ gantum ārebhe bhayād godāvarī nadī ।। upatasthe ca vaidehīṃ bhikṣurūpeṇa rāvaṇaḥ ।। abhyavartata vaidehīṃ citrām iva śanaiścaraḥ ।।
atiṣṭhat prekṣya vaidehīṃ rāmapatnīṃ yaśasvinīm ।। āsīnāṃ parṇaśālāyāṃ bāṣpaśokābhipīḍitām ।। abhyagacchata vaidehīṃ duṣṭacetā niśācaraḥ ।। abravīt praśritaṃ vākyaṃ rahite rākṣasādhipaḥ ।।
vibhrājamānāṃ vapuṣā rāvaṇaḥ praśaśaṃsa ha ।। kamalānāṃ śubhāṃ mālāṃ padminīva ca bibhratī ।। bhūtir vā tvaṃ varārohe ratir vā svairacāriṇī ।। viśāle vimale netre raktānte kṛṣṇatārake ।।
etāv upacitau vṛttau sahitau saṃpragalbhitau ।। maṇipravekābharaṇau rucirau te payodharau ।। mano harasi me rāme nadīkūlam ivāmbhasā ।। naiva devī na gandharvī na yakṣī na ca kiṃnarī ।।
iha vāsaś ca kāntāre cittam unmādayanti me ।। rākṣasānām ayaṃ vāso ghorāṇāṃ kāmarūpiṇām ।। sampannāni sugandhīni yuktāny ācarituṃ tvayā ।। bhartāraṃ ca varaṃ manye tvadyuktam asitekṣaṇe ।।
vasūnāṃ vā varārohe devatā pratibhāsi me ।। rākṣasānām ayaṃ vāsaḥ kathaṃ nu tvam ihāgatā ।। ṛkṣās tarakṣavaḥ kaṅkāḥ kathaṃ tebhyo na bibhyasi ।। katham ekā mahāraṇye na bibheṣi varānane ।।
ekā carasi kalyāṇi ghorān rākṣasasevitān ।। sarvair atithisatkāraiḥ pūjayāmāsa maithilī ।। abravīt siddham ity eva tadā taṃ saumyadarśanam ।। aśakyam udveṣṭum upāyadarśanān nyamantrayad brāhmaṇavad yathāgatam ।।
idaṃ ca siddhaṃ vanajātam uttamaṃ tvadartham avyagram ihopabhujyatām ।। prahasya tasyā haraṇe dhṛtaṃ manaḥ samarpayāmāsa vadhāya rāvaṇaḥ ।। nirīkṣamāṇā haritaṃ dadarśa tan mahad vanaṃ naiva tu rāmalakṣmaṇau ।। parivrājakarūpeṇa śaśaṃsātmānam ātmanā ।।
iti dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ tu sītā vacanam abravīt ।। sītā nāmnāsmi bhadraṃ te rāmabhāryā dvijottama ।। bhuñjānā mānuṣān bhogān sarvakāmasamṛddhinī ।। abhiṣecayituṃ rāmaṃ sameto rājamantribhiḥ ।।
kaikeyī nāma bhartāraṃ mamāryā yācate varam ।। dvāv ayācata bhartāraṃ satyasaṃdhaṃ nṛpottamam ।। eṣa me jīvitasyānto rāmo yady abhiṣicyate ।। ayācatārthair anvarthair na ca yācñāṃ cakāra sā ।।
viśālākṣo mahābāhuḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। kaikeyī mama bhartāram ity uvāca drutaṃ vacaḥ ।। bharatāya pradātavyam idaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam ।। vane pravraja kākutstha pitaraṃ mocayānṛtāt ।।
cakāra tadvacas tasyā mama bhartā dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। etad brāhmaṇa rāmasya vrataṃ dhruvam anuttamam ।। rāmasya puruṣavyāghraḥ sahāyaḥ samare arihā ।। anvagacchad dhanuṣpāṇiḥ pravrajantaṃ mayā saha ।।
vicarāma dvijaśreṣṭha vanaṃ gambhīram ojasā ।। āgamiṣyati me bhartā vanyam ādāya puṣkalam ।। ekaś ca daṇḍakāraṇye kimarthaṃ carasi dvija ।। pratyuvācottaraṃ tīvraṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ ।।
ahaṃ sa rāvaṇo nāma sīte rakṣogaṇeśvaraḥ ।। ratiṃ svakeṣu dāreṣu nādhigacchāmy anindite ।। sarvāsām eva bhadraṃ te mamāgramahiṣī bhava ।। sāgareṇa parikṣiptā niviṣṭā girimūrdhani ।।
na cāsyāraṇyavāsasya spṛhayiṣyasi bhāmini ।। sīte paricariṣyanti bhāryā bhavasi me yadi ।। pratyuvācānavadyāṅgī tam anādṛtya rākṣasam ।। mahodadhim ivākṣobhyam ahaṃ rāmam anuvratā ।।
nṛsiṃhaṃ siṃhasaṃkāśam ahaṃ rāmam anuvratā ।। pṛthukīrtiṃ mahābāhum ahaṃ rāmam anuvratā ।। nāhaṃ śakyā tvayā spraṣṭum ādityasya prabhā yathā ।। rāghavasya priyāṃ bhāryāṃ yas tvam icchasi rāvaṇa ।।
āśīviṣasya vadanād daṃṣṭrām ādātum icchasi ।। kālakūṭaṃ viṣaṃ pītvā svastimān gantum icchasi ।। rāghavasya priyāṃ bhāryām adhigantuṃ tvam icchasi ।। yo rāmasya priyāṃ bhāryāṃ pradharṣayitum icchasi ।।
kalyāṇavṛttāṃ rāmasya yo bhāryāṃ hartum icchasi ।। rāmasya sadṛśīṃ bhāryāṃ yo adhigantuṃ tvam icchasi ।। surāgryasauvīrakayor yad antaraṃ tad antaraṃ dāśarathes tavaiva ca ।। yad antaraṃ hastibiḍālayor vane tad antaraṃ dāśarathes tavaiva ca ।।
yad antaraṃ sārasagṛdhrayor vane tad antaraṃ dāśarathes tavaiva ca ।। hṛtāpi te ahaṃ na jarāṃ gamiṣye vajraṃ yathā makṣikayāvagīrṇam ।। gātraprakampād vyathitā babhūva vātoddhatā sā kadalīva tanvī ।। kulaṃ balaṃ nāma ca karma cātmanaḥ samācacakṣe bhayakāraṇārtham ।।
lalāṭe bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā rāvaṇaḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। rāvaṇo nāma bhadraṃ te daśagrīvaḥ pratāpavān ।। vidravanti bhayād bhītā mṛtyor iva sadā prajāḥ ।। dvaṃdvam āsāditaḥ krodhād raṇe vikramya nirjitaḥ ।।
kailāsaṃ parvataśreṣṭham adhyāste naravāhanaḥ ।। vīryād āvarjitaṃ bhadre yena yāmi vihāyasam ।। vidravanti paritrastāḥ surāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ ।। tīvrāṃśuḥ śiśirāṃśuś ca bhayāt sampadyate raviḥ ।।
bhavanti yatra yatrāhaṃ tiṣṭhāmi ca carāmi ca ।। sampūrṇā rākṣasair ghorair yathendrasyāmarāvatī ।। hemakakṣyā purī ramyā vaiḍūryamayatoraṇā ।। sarvakāmaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ saṃkulodyānaśobhitā ।।
na smariṣyasi nārīṇāṃ mānuṣīṇāṃ manasvini ।। na smariṣyasi rāmasya mānuṣasya gatāyuṣaḥ ।। mandavīryaḥ suto jyeṣṭhas tataḥ prasthāpito vanam ।। kariṣyasi viśālākṣi tāpasena tapasvinā ।।
na manmathaśarāviṣṭaṃ pratyākhyātuṃ tvam arhasi ।। caraṇenābhihatyeva purūravasam urvaśī ।। abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ rahite rākṣasādhipam ।। bhrātaraṃ vyapadiśya tvam aśubhaṃ kartum icchasi ।।
yeṣāṃ tvaṃ karkaśo rājā durbuddhir ajitendriyaḥ ।। na tu rāmasya bhāryāṃ mām apanīyāsti jīvitam ।। na mādṛśīṃ rākṣasa dharṣayitvā pītāmṛtasyāpi tavāsti mokṣaḥ ।। haste hastaṃ samāhatya cakāra sumahad vapuḥ ।।
nonmattayā śrutau manye mama vīryaparākramau ।। āpibeyaṃ samudraṃ ca mṛtyuṃ hanyāṃ raṇe sthitaḥ ।। kāmarūpiṇam unmatte paśya māṃ kāmadaṃ patim ।। kruddhasya hariparyante rakte netre babhūvatuḥ ।।
svaṃ rūpaṃ kālarūpābhaṃ bheje vaiśravaṇānujaḥ ।। daśāsyaḥ kārmukī bāṇī babhūva kṣaṇadācaraḥ ।। pratipede svakaṃ rūpaṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ ।। raktāmbaradharas tasthau strīratnaṃ prekṣya maithilīm ।।
vasanābharaṇopetāṃ maithilīṃ rāvaṇo abravīt ।। mām āśraya varārohe tavāhaṃ sadṛśaḥ patiḥ ।। tyajyatāṃ mānuṣo bhāvo mayi bhāvaḥ praṇīyatām ।। kair guṇair anuraktāsi mūḍhe paṇḍitamānini ।।
asmin vyālānucarite vane vasati durmatiḥ ।। jagrāha rāvaṇaḥ sītāṃ budhaḥ khe rohiṇīm iva ।। ūrvos tu dakṣiṇenaiva parijagrāha pāṇinā ।। prādravan mṛtyusaṃkāśaṃ bhayārtā vanadevatāḥ ।।
pratyadṛśyata hemāṅgo rāvaṇasya mahārathaḥ ।। aṅkenādāya vaidehīṃ ratham āropayat tadā ।। rāmeti sītā duḥkhārtā rāmaṃ dūragataṃ vane ।। viveṣṭamānām ādāya utpapātātha rāvaṇaḥ ।।
bhṛśaṃ cukrośa matteva bhrāntacittā yathāturā ।। hriyamāṇāṃ na jānīṣe rakṣasā kāmarūpiṇā ।। hriyamāṇām adharmeṇa māṃ rāghava na paśyasi ।। katham evaṃvidhaṃ pāpaṃ na tvaṃ śādhi hi rāvaṇam ।।
kālo apy aṅgī bhavaty atra sasyānām iva paktaye ।। jīvitāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ rāmād vyasanam āpnuhi ।। hriyeyaṃ dharmakāmasya dharmapatnī yaśasvinaḥ ।। kṣipraṃ rāmāya śaṃsadhvaṃ sītāṃ harati rāvaṇaḥ ।।
kṣipraṃ rāmāya śaṃsadhvaṃ sītāṃ harati rāvaṇaḥ ।। kṣipraṃ rāmāya śaṃsadhvaṃ sītāṃ harati rāvaṇaḥ ।। namaskaromy ahaṃ tebhyo bhartuḥ śaṃsata māṃ hṛtām ।। sarvāṇi śaraṇaṃ yāmi mṛgapakṣigaṇān api ।।
vivaśāpahṛtā sītā rāvaṇeneti śaṃsata ।। āneṣyati parākramya vaivasvatahṛtām api ।। lakṣmaṇāya ca tat sarvam ākhyātavyam aśeṣataḥ ।। niraikṣad rāvaṇaṃ kṣipraṃ vaidehīṃ ca dadarśa saḥ ।।
vanaspatigataḥ śrīmān vyājahāra śubhāṃ giram ।। jaṭāyur nāma nāmnāhaṃ gṛdhrarājo mahābalaḥ ।। lokānāṃ ca hite yukto rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ ।। sītā nāma varārohā yāṃ tvaṃ hartum ihecchasi ।।
nivartaya matiṃ nīcāṃ paradārābhimarśanam ।। yathātmanas tathānyeṣāṃ dārā rakṣyā vimarśanāt ।। vyavasyanty anu rājānaṃ dharmaṃ paulastyanandana ।। dharmaḥ śubhaṃ vā pāpaṃ vā rājamūlaṃ pravartate ।।
aiśvaryam abhisamprāpto vimānam iva duṣkṛtiḥ ।। na hi duṣṭātmanām āryam āvasaty ālaye ciram ।। nāparādhyati dharmātmā kathaṃ tasyāparādhyasi ।। ativṛtto hataḥ pūrvaṃ rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।।
yasya tvaṃ lokanāthasya hṛtvā bhāryāṃ gamiṣyasi ।। dahed dahanabhūtena vṛtram indrāśanir yathā ।। grīvāyāṃ pratimuktaṃ ca kālapāśaṃ na paśyasi ।। tad annam upabhoktavyaṃ jīryate yad anāmayam ।।
śarīrasya bhavet khedaḥ kas tat karma samācaret ।। pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyaṃ yathāvad anutiṣṭhataḥ ।। tathāpy ādāya vaidehīṃ kuśalī na gamiṣyasi ।। hetubhir nyāyasaṃyuktair dhruvāṃ vedaśrutim iva ।।
śayiṣyase hato bhūmau yathāpūrvaṃ kharas tathā ।। nacirāc cīravāsās tvāṃ rāmo yudhi vadhiṣyati ।। kṣipraṃ tvaṃ naśyase nīca tayor bhīto na saṃśayaḥ ।। sītāṃ kamalapattrākṣīṃ rāmasya mahiṣīṃ priyām ।।
jīvitenāpi rāmasya tathā daśarathasya ca ।। vṛntād iva phalaṃ tvāṃ tu pātayeyaṃ rathottamāt ।। kruddhasyāgninibhāḥ sarvā rejur viṃśatidṛṣṭayaḥ ।। rākṣasendro abhidudrāva patagendram amarṣaṇaḥ ।।
babhūva vātoddhatayor meghayor gagane yathā ।। sapakṣayor mālyavator mahāparvatayor iva ।। abhyavarṣan mahāghorair gṛdhrarājaṃ mahābalaḥ ।। jaṭāyuḥ pratijagrāha rāvaṇāstrāṇi saṃyuge ।।
cakāra bahudhā gātre vraṇān patagasattamaḥ ।। mṛtyudaṇḍanibhān ghorāñ śatrumardanakāṅkṣayā ।। bibheda niśitais tīkṣṇair gṛdhraṃ ghoraiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ ।। acintayitvā bāṇāṃs tān rākṣasaṃ samabhidravat ।।
caraṇābhyāṃ mahātejā babhañja patageśvaraḥ ।। pakṣābhyāṃ ca mahātejā vyadhunot patageśvaraḥ ।। tāṃś cāsya javasampannāñ jaghāna samare balī ।। pūrṇacandrapratīkāśaṃ chattraṃ ca vyajanaiḥ saha ।।
aṅkenādāya vaidehīṃ papāta bhuvi rāvaṇaḥ ।। sādhu sādhv iti bhūtāni gṛdhrarājam apūjayan ।। utpapāta punar hṛṣṭo maithilīṃ gṛhya rāvaṇaḥ ।। gṛdhrarājaḥ samutpatya jaṭāyur idam abravīt ।।
alpabuddhe harasy enāṃ vadhāya khalu rakṣasām ।। viṣapānaṃ pibasy etat pipāsita ivodakam ।। śīghram eva vinaśyanti yathā tvaṃ vinaśiṣyasi ।। vadhāya baḍiśaṃ gṛhya sāmiṣaṃ jalajo yathā ।।
dharṣaṇaṃ cāśramasyāsya kṣamiṣyete tu rāghavau ।। taskarācarito mārgo naiṣa vīraniṣevitaḥ ।। śayiṣyase hato bhūmau yathā bhrātā kharas tathā ।। vināśāyātmano adharmyaṃ pratipanno asi karma tat ।।
kurvīta lokādhipatiḥ svayambhūr bhagavān api ।। nipapāta bhṛśaṃ pṛṣṭhe daśagrīvasya vīryavān ।। adhirūḍho gajāroho yathā syād duṣṭavāraṇam ।। keśāṃś cotpāṭayāmāsa nakhapakṣamukhāyudhaḥ ।।
amarṣasphuritauṣṭhaḥ san prākampata sa rākṣasaḥ ।। talenābhijaghānārto jaṭāyuṃ krodhamūrchitaḥ ।। vāmabāhūn daśa tadā vyapāharad ariṃdamaḥ ।। muṣṭibhyāṃ caraṇābhyāṃ ca gṛdhrarājam apothayat ।।
rākṣasānāṃ ca mukhyasya pakṣiṇāṃ pravarasya ca ।। pakṣau pādau ca pārśvau ca khaḍgam uddhṛtya socchinat ।। nipapāta hato gṛdhro dharaṇyām alpajīvitaḥ ।। abhyadhāvata vaidehī svabandhum iva duḥkhitā ।।
dadarśa laṅkādhipatiḥ pṛthivyāṃ jaṭāyuṣaṃ śāntam ivāgnidāvam ।। punaḥ pariṣvajya śaśiprabhānanā ruroda sītā janakātmajā tadā ।। dadarśa gṛdhraṃ patitaṃ samīpe rāghavāśramāt ।। gṛdhrarājaṃ vinihataṃ vilalāpa suduḥkhitā ।।
avaśyaṃ sukhaduḥkheṣu narāṇāṃ pratidṛśyate ।। dhāvanti nūnaṃ kākutstha madarthaṃ mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।। susaṃtrastā samākrandac chṛṇvatāṃ tu yathāntike ।। abhyadhāvata vaidehīṃ rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ ।।
muñca muñceti bahuśaḥ pravadan rākṣasādhipaḥ ।। jīvitāntāya keśeṣu jagrāhāntakasaṃnibhaḥ ।। jagat sarvam amaryādaṃ tamasāndhena saṃvṛtam ।। kṛtaṃ kāryam iti śrīmān vyājahāra pitāmahaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā sītāṃ parāmṛṣṭāṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।। jagāmākāśam ādāya rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ ।। rarāja rājaputrī tu vidyut saudāmanī yathā ।। adhikaṃ paribabhrāja girir dīpta ivāgninā ।।
padmapattrāṇi vaidehyā abhyakīryanta rāvaṇam ।। babhau cādityarāgeṇa tāmram abhram ivātape ।। na rarāja vinā rāmaṃ vinālam iva paṅkajam ।। śuklaiḥ suvimalair dantaiḥ prabhāvadbhir alaṃkṛtam ।।
sunāsaṃ cārutāmrauṣṭham ākāśe hāṭakaprabham ।। śuśubhe na vinā rāmaṃ divā candra ivoditaḥ ।। śuśubhe kāñcanī kāñcī nīlaṃ maṇim ivāśritā ।। vidyudghanam ivāviśya śuśubhe taptabhūṣaṇā ।।
babhūva vimalo nīlaḥ saghoṣa iva toyadaḥ ।। sītāyā hriyamāṇāyāḥ papāta dharaṇītale ।। samādhūtā daśagrīvaṃ punar evābhyavartata ।। nakṣatramālāvimalā meruṃ nagam ivottamam ।।
vidyunmaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ papāta madhurasvanam ।। prāśobhayata vaidehī gajaṃ kaṣyeva kāñcanī ।। jahārākāśam āviśya sītāṃ vaiśravaṇānujaḥ ।। saghoṣāṇy avakīryanta kṣīṇās tārā ivāmbarāt ।।
vaidehyā nipatan bhāti gaṅgeva gaganāc cyutā ।। mā bhair iti vidhūtāgrā vyājahrur iva pādapāḥ ।। sakhīm iva gatotsāhāṃ śocantīva sma maithilīm ।। anvadhāvaṃs tadā roṣāt sītāchāyānugāminaḥ ।।
sītāyāṃ hriyamāṇāyāṃ vikrośantīva parvatāḥ ।। pravidhvastaprabhaḥ śrīmān āsīt pāṇḍuramaṇḍalaḥ ।। yatra rāmasya vaidehīṃ bhāryāṃ harati rāvaṇaḥ ।। vitrastakā dīnamukhā rurudur mṛgapotakāḥ ।।
supravepitagātrāś ca babhūvur vanadevatāḥ ।। tāṃ tu lakṣmaṇa rāmeti krośantīṃ madhurasvarām ।। jahārātmavināśāya daśagrīvo manasvinīm ।। apaśyatī rāghavalakṣmaṇāv ubhau vivarṇavaktrā bhayabhārapīḍitā ।।
duḥkhitā paramodvignā bhaye mahati vartinī ।। rudatī karuṇaṃ sītā hriyamāṇedam abravīt ।। jñātvā virahitāṃ yo māṃ corayitvā palāyase ।। yo hi mām udyatas trātuṃ so apy ayaṃ vinipātitaḥ ।।
viśrāvya nāmadheyaṃ hi yuddhe nāsti jitā tvayā ।। striyāś ca haraṇaṃ nīca rahite ca parasya ca ।। sunṛśaṃsam adharmiṣṭhaṃ tava śauṇḍīryamāninaḥ ।। kulākrośakaraṃ loke dhik te cāritram īdṛśam ।।
muhūrtam api tiṣṭhasva na jīvan pratiyāsyasi ।। sasainyo api samarthas tvaṃ muhūrtam api jīvitum ।। vane prajvalitasyeva sparśam agner vihaṃgamaḥ ।। vidhāsyati vināśāya tvaṃ māṃ yadi na muñcasi ।।
vyavasāyaḥ sa te nīca bhaviṣyati nirarthakaḥ ।। utsahe śatruvaśagā prāṇān dhārayituṃ ciram ।। mṛtyukāle yathā martyo viparītāni sevate ।। paśyāmīva hi kaṇṭhe tvāṃ kālapāśāvapāśitam ।।
vyaktaṃ hiraṇmayān hi tvaṃ saṃpaśyasi mahīruhān ।। khaḍgapattravanaṃ caiva bhīmaṃ paśyasi rāvaṇa ।। drakṣyase śālmalīṃ tīkṣṇām āyasaiḥ kaṇṭakaiś citām ।। dharituṃ śakṣyasi ciraṃ viṣaṃ pītveva nirghṛṇaḥ ।।
kva gato lapsyase śarma bhartur mama mahātmanaḥ ।। rākṣasā nihatā yena sahasrāṇi caturdaśa ।। na tvāṃ hanyāc charais tīkṣṇair iṣṭabhāryāpahāriṇam ।। bhayaśokasamāviṣṭā karuṇaṃ vilalāpa ha ।।
jahāra pāpas taruṇīṃ viveṣṭatīṃ nṛpātmajām āgatagātravepathum ।। dadarśa giriśṛṅgasthān pañcavānarapuṃgavān ।। mumoca yadi rāmāya śaṃseyur iti maithilī ।। sambhramāt tu daśagrīvas tat karma na ca buddhavān ।।
vikrośantīṃ tadā sītāṃ dadṛśur vānararṣabhāḥ ।। jagāma rudatīṃ gṛhya maithilīṃ rākṣaseśvaraḥ ।। utsaṅgenaiva bhujagīṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṃ mahāviṣām ।। sa kṣipraṃ samatīyāya śaraś cāpād iva cyutaḥ ।।
saritāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā samatīyāya sāgaram ।। vaidehyāṃ hriyamāṇāyāṃ babhūva varuṇālayaḥ ।। etadanto daśagrīva iti siddhās tadābruvan ।। praviveśa purīṃ laṅkāṃ rūpiṇīṃ mṛtyum ātmanaḥ ।।
saṃrūḍhakakṣyābahulaṃ svam antaḥpuram āviśat ।। nidadhe rāvaṇaḥ sītāṃ mayo māyām ivāsurīm ।। yathā naināṃ pumān strī vā sītāṃ paśyaty asaṃmataḥ ।। yad yad icchet tad evāsyā deyaṃ macchandato yathā ।।
ajñānād yadi vā jñānān na tasyā jīvitaṃ priyam ।। dadarśāṣṭau mahāvīryān rākṣasān piśitāśanān ।। uvācaitān idaṃ vākyaṃ praśasya balavīryataḥ ।। janasthānaṃ hatasthānaṃ bhūtapūrvaṃ kharālayam ।।
pauruṣaṃ balam āśritya trāsam utsṛjya dūrataḥ ।। sadūṣaṇakharaṃ yuddhe hataṃ tad rāmasāyakaiḥ ।। vairaṃ ca sumahajjātaṃ rāmaṃ prati sudāruṇam ।। na hi lapsyāmy ahaṃ nidrām ahatvā saṃyuge ripum ।।
rāmaṃ śarmopalapsyāmi dhanaṃ labdhveva nirdhanaḥ ।। pravṛttir upanetavyā kiṃ karotīti tattvataḥ ।। kartavyaś ca sadā yatno rāghavasya vadhaṃ prati ।। ataś cāsmiñ janasthāne mayā yūyaṃ niyojitāḥ ।।
vihāya laṅkāṃ sahitāḥ pratasthire yato janasthānam alakṣyadarśanāḥ ।। prasajya rāmeṇa ca vairam uttamaṃ babhūva mohān muditaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ buddhivaiklavyāt kṛtakṛtyam amanyata ।। praviveśa gṛhaṃ ramyaṃ sītāṃ draṣṭum abhitvaran ।।
apaśyad rākṣasīmadhye sītāṃ śokaparāyaṇām ।। vāyuvegair ivākrāntāṃ majjantīṃ nāvam arṇave ।। adhomukhamukhīṃ dīnām abhyetya ca niśācaraḥ ।। sa balād darśayāmāsa gṛhaṃ devagṛhopamam ।।
nānāpakṣigaṇair juṣṭaṃ nānāratnasamanvitam ।। vajravaiḍūryacitraiś ca stambhair dṛṣṭimanoharaiḥ ।। sopānaṃ kāñcanaṃ citram āruroha tayā saha ।। hemajālāvṛtāś cāsaṃs tatra prāsādapaṅktayaḥ ।।
daśagrīvaḥ svabhavane prādarśayata maithilīm ।। rāvaṇo darśayāmāsa sītāṃ śokaparāyaṇām ।। uvāca vākyaṃ pāpātmā rāvaṇo janakātmajām ।। varjayitvā jarāvṛddhān bālāṃś ca rajanīcarān ।।
sahasram ekam ekasya mama kāryapuraḥsaram ।। jīvitaṃ ca viśālākṣi tvaṃ me prāṇair garīyasī ।। tāsāṃ tvam īśvarī sīte mama bhāryā bhava priye ।। bhajasva mābhitaptasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi ।।
neyaṃ dharṣayituṃ śakyā sendrair api surāsuraiḥ ।। ahaṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu yo me vīryasamo bhavet ।। kiṃ kariṣyasi rāmeṇa mānuṣeṇālpatejasā ।। yauvanaṃ hy adhruvaṃ bhīru ramasveha mayā saha ।।
kāsya śaktir ihāgantum api sīte manorathaiḥ ।। dīpyamānasya vāpy agner grahītuṃ vimalāṃ śikhām ।। vikrameṇa nayed yas tvāṃ madbāhuparipālitām ।। abhiṣekodakaklinnā tuṣṭā ca ramayasva mām ।।
yaś ca te sukṛto dharmas tasyeha phalam āpnuhi ।। bhūṣaṇāni ca mukhyāni tāni seva mayā saha ।। vimānaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ ca tad vimānaṃ manojavam ।। vadanaṃ padmasaṃkāśaṃ vimalaṃ cārudarśanam ।।
alaṃ vrīḍena vaidehi dharmalopakṛtena te ।। etau pādau mayā snigdhau śirobhiḥ paripīḍitau ।। nemāḥ śūnyā mayā vācaḥ śuṣyamāṇena bhāṣitāḥ ।। evam uktvā daśagrīvo maithilīṃ janakātmajām ।।
tṛṇam antarataḥ kṛtvā rāvaṇaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। satyasaṃdhaḥ parijñāto yasya putraḥ sa rāghavaḥ ।। dīrghabāhur viśālākṣo daivataṃ sa patir mama ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā yas te prāṇān hariṣyati ।।
śayitā tvaṃ hataḥ saṃkhye janasthāne yathā kharaḥ ।। rāghave nirviṣāḥ sarve suparṇe pannagā yathā ।। śarīraṃ vidhamiṣyanti gaṅgākūlam ivormayaḥ ।। utpādya sumahad vairaṃ jīvaṃs tasya na mokṣyase ।।
paśor yūpagatasyeva jīvitaṃ tava durlabham ।। rakṣas tvam adya nirdagdho gaccheḥ sadyaḥ parābhavam ।। sāgaraṃ śoṣayed vāpi sa sītāṃ mocayed iha ।। laṅkā vaidhavyasaṃyuktā tvatkṛtena bhaviṣyati ।।
yāhaṃ nītā vinā bhāvaṃ patipārśvāt tvayā vanāt ।। nirbhayo vīryam āśritya śūnye vasati daṇḍake ।। apaneṣyati gātrebhyaḥ śaravarṣeṇa saṃyuge ।। tadā kārye pramādyanti narāḥ kālavaśaṃ gatāḥ ।।
ātmano rākṣasānāṃ ca vadhāyāntaḥpurasya ca ।। dvijātimantrasaṃpūtā caṇḍālenāvamarditum ।। na hi śakṣyāmy upakrośaṃ pṛthivyāṃ dātum ātmanaḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ maithilī tatra punar novāca kiṃcana ।।
pratyuvāca tataḥ sītāṃ bhayasaṃdarśanaṃ vacaḥ ।। tatas tvāṃ prātarāśārthaṃ sūdāś chetsyanti leśaśaḥ ।। rākṣasīś ca tataḥ kruddha idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। darpam asyā vineṣyadhvaṃ māṃsaśoṇitabhojanāḥ ।।
kṛtaprāñjalayo bhūtvā maithilīṃ paryavārayan ।। pracālya caraṇotkarṣair dārayann iva medinīm ।। tatreyaṃ rakṣyatāṃ gūḍham yuṣmābhiḥ parivāritā ।। ānayadhvaṃ vaśaṃ sarvā vanyāṃ gajavadhūm iva ।।
aśokavanikāṃ jagmur maithilīṃ parigṛhya tām ।। sarvakālamadaiś cāpi dvijaiḥ samupasevitām ।। rākṣasīvaśam āpannā vyāghrīṇāṃ hariṇī yathā ।। patiṃ smarantī dayitaṃ ca devaraṃ vicetanābhūd bhayaśokapīḍitā ।।
nihatya rāmo mārīcaṃ tūrṇaṃ pathi nyavartata ।। krūrasvaro atha gomāyur vinanādāsya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। cintayāmāsa gomāyoḥ svareṇa pariśaṅkitaḥ ।। svasti syād api vaidehyā rākṣasair bhakṣaṇaṃ vinā ।।
vikruṣṭaṃ mṛgarūpeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ śṛṇuyād yadi ।। tayaiva prahitaḥ kṣipraṃ matsakāśam ihaiṣyati ।। kāñcanaś ca mṛgo bhūtvā vyapanīyāśramāt tu mām ।। hā lakṣmaṇa hato asmīti yad vākyaṃ vyājahāra ha ।।
nimittāni ca ghorāṇi dṛśyante adya bahūni ca ।। ājagāma janasthānaṃ rāghavaḥ pariśaṅkitaḥ ।। savyaṃ kṛtvā mahātmānaṃ ghorāṃś ca sasṛjuḥ svarān ।। tato lakṣmaṇam āyāntaṃ dadarśa vigataprabham ।।
viṣaṇṇaḥ sa viṣaṇṇena duḥkhito duḥkhabhāginā ।। vihāya sītāṃ vijane vane rākṣasasevite ।। uvāca madhurodarkam idaṃ paruṣam ārtavat ।। sītām ihāgataḥ saumya kaccit svasti bhaved iti ।।
vinaṣṭā bhakṣitā vāpi rākṣasair vanacāribhiḥ ।। api lakṣmaṇa sītāyāḥ sāmagryaṃ prāpnuyāvahe ।। hataṃ kathaṃcin mahatā śrameṇa sa rākṣaso abhūn mriyamāṇa eva ।। asaṃśayaṃ lakṣmaṇa nāsti sītā hṛtā mṛtā vā pathi vartate vā ।।
paryapṛcchata dharmātmā vaidehīm āgataṃ vinā ।। kva sā lakṣmaṇa vaidehī yāṃ hitvā tvam ihāgataḥ ।। kva sā duḥkhasahāyā me vaidehī tanumadhyamā ।। kva sā prāṇasahāyā me sītā surasutopamā ।।
vinā tāṃ tapanīyābhāṃ neccheyaṃ janakātmajām ।। kaccit pravrājanaṃ saumya na me mithyā bhaviṣyati ।। kaccit sakāmā sukhitā kaikeyī sā bhaviṣyati ।। upasthāsyati kausalyā kaccit saumya na kaikayīm ।।
suvṛttā yadi vṛttā sā prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi lakṣmaṇa ।। punaḥ prahasitā sītā vinaśiṣyāmi lakṣmaṇa ।। tvayi pramatte rakṣobhir bhakṣitā vā tapasvinī ।। madviyogena vaidehī vyaktaṃ śocati durmanāḥ ।।
vadatā lakṣmaṇety uccais tavāpi janitaṃ bhayam ।। trastayā preṣitas tvaṃ ca draṣṭuṃ māṃ śīghram āgataḥ ।। pratikartuṃ nṛśaṃsānāṃ rakṣasāṃ dattam antaram ।। taiḥ sītā nihatā ghorair bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
kiṃ tv idānīṃ kariṣyāmi śaṅke prāptavyam īdṛśam ।। ājagāma janasthānaṃ tvarayā sahalakṣmaṇaḥ ।। viniḥśvasañ śuṣkamukho viṣaṇṇaḥ pratiśrayaṃ prāpya samīkṣya śūnyam ।। etat tad ity eva nivāsabhūmau prahṛṣṭaromā vyathito babhūva ।।
paripapraccha saumitriṃ rāmo duḥkhārditaḥ punaḥ ।। yadā sā tava viśvāsād vane virahitā mayā ।। śaṅkamānaṃ mahat pāpaṃ yat satyaṃ vyathitaṃ manaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇa dūre tvāṃ sītāvirahitaṃ pathi ।।
bhūyo duḥkhasamāviṣṭo duḥkhitaṃ rāmam abravīt ।। pracoditas tayaivograis tvatsakāśam ihāgataḥ ।। paritrāhīti yad vākyaṃ maithilyās tac chrutiṃ gatam ।। gaccha gaccheti mām āha rudantī bhayavihvalā ।।
pratyuktā maithilī vākyam idaṃ tvatpratyayānvitam ।। nirvṛtā bhava nāsty etat kenāpy evam udāhṛtam ।। trāhīti vacanaṃ sīte yas trāyet tridaśān api ।। na bhavatyā vyathā kāryā kunārījanasevitā ।।
jāto vā jāyamāno vā saṃyuge yaḥ parājayet ।। uvācāśrūṇi muñcantī dāruṇaṃ mām idaṃ vacaḥ ।। vinaṣṭe bhrātari prāpte na ca tvaṃ mām avāpsyasi ।। krośantaṃ hi yathātyarthaṃ nainam abhyavapadyase ।।
rāghavasyāntaraprepsus tathainaṃ nābhipadyase ।। krodhāt prasphuramāṇauṣṭha āśramād abhinirgataḥ ।। abravīd duṣkṛtaṃ saumya tāṃ vinā yat tvam āgataḥ ।। anena krodhavākyena maithilyā niḥsṛto bhavān ।।
kruddhāyāḥ paruṣaṃ śrutvā striyā yat tvam ihāgataḥ ।। krodhasya vaśam āgamya nākaroḥ śāsanaṃ mama ।। mṛgarūpeṇa yenāham āśramād apavāhitaḥ ।। mārgīṃ tanuṃ tyajya ca viklavasvaro babhūva keyūradharaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ ।।
udāhṛtaṃ tad vacanaṃ sudāruṇaṃ tvam āgato yena vihāya maithilīm ।। prāsphurac cāskhalad rāmo vepathuś cāsya jāyate ।। api kṣemaṃ tu sītāyā iti vai vyājahāra ha ।। śūnyam āvasathaṃ dṛṣṭvā babhūvodvignamānasaḥ ।।
tatra tatroṭajasthānam abhivīkṣya samantataḥ ।। śriyā virahitāṃ dhvastāṃ hemante padminīm iva ।। śriyā vihīnaṃ vidhvastaṃ saṃtyaktavanadaivatam ।। dṛṣṭvā śūnyoṭajasthānaṃ vilalāpa punaḥ punaḥ ।।
nilīnāpy atha vā bhīrur atha vā vanam āśritā ।। atha vā padminīṃ yātā jalārthaṃ vā nadīṃ gatā ।। śokaraktekṣaṇaḥ śokād unmatta iva lakṣyate ।। babhūva vilapan rāmaḥ śokapaṅkārṇavaplutaḥ ।।
kadamba yadi jānīṣe śaṃsa sītāṃ śubhānanām ।। śaṃsasva yadi vā dṛṣṭā bilva bilvopamastanī ।। janakasya sutā bhīrur yadi jīvati vā na vā ।। latāpallavapuṣpāḍhyo bhāti hy eṣa vanaspatiḥ ।।
eṣa vyaktaṃ vijānāti tilakas tilakapriyām ।। tvannāmānaṃ kuru kṣipraṃ priyāsaṃdarśanena mām ।। kathayasva varārohāṃ kāruṇyaṃ yadi te mayi ।। priyāṃ yadi vijānīṣe niḥśaṅkaṃ kathayasva me ।।
mṛgaviprekṣaṇī kāntā mṛgībhiḥ sahitā bhavet ।। tāṃ manye viditāṃ tubhyam ākhyāhi varavāraṇa ।। maithilī mama viśrabdhaḥ kathayasva na te bhayam ।। vṛkṣeṇācchādya cātmānaṃ kiṃ māṃ na pratibhāṣase ।।
nātyarthaṃ hāsyaśīlāsi kimarthaṃ mām upekṣase ।। dhāvanty api mayā dṛṣṭā tiṣṭha yady asti sauhṛdam ।। kṛcchraṃ prāptaṃ hi māṃ nūnaṃ yathopekṣitum arhati ।। vibhajyāṅgāni sarvāṇi mayā virahitā priyā ।।
sā hi campakavarṇābhā grīvā graiveyaśobhitā ।। nūnaṃ vikṣipyamāṇau tau bāhū pallavakomalau ।। mayā virahitā bālā rakṣasāṃ bhakṣaṇāya vai ।। hā lakṣmaṇa mahābāho paśyasi tvaṃ priyāṃ kvacit ।।
ity evaṃ vilapan rāmaḥ paridhāvan vanād vanam ।। kvacin matta ivābhāti kāntānveṣaṇatatparaḥ ।। kānanāni ca vegena bhramaty aparisaṃsthitaḥ ।। aniṣṭhitāśaḥ sa cakāra mārgaṇe punaḥ priyāyāḥ paramaṃ pariśramam ।।
rahitāṃ parṇaśālāṃ ca vidhvastāny āsanāni ca ।। uvāca rāmaḥ prākruśya pragṛhya rucirau bhujau ।। kenāhṛtā vā saumitre bhakṣitā kena vā priyā ।। alaṃ te hasitenādya māṃ bhajasva suduḥkhitam ।।
ete hīnās tvayā saumye dhyāyanty asrāvilekṣaṇāḥ ।। paraloke mahārājo nūnaṃ drakṣyati me pitā ।। apūrayitvā taṃ kālaṃ matsakāśam ihāgataḥ ।। dhik tvām iti pare loke vyaktaṃ vakṣyati me pitā ।।
mām ihotsṛjya karuṇaṃ kīrtir naram ivānṛjum ।। tvayā virahitaś cāhaṃ mokṣye jīvitam ātmanaḥ ।। na dadarśa suduḥkhārto rāghavo janakātmajām ।। lakṣmaṇo rāmam atyartham uvāca hitakāmyayā ।।
idaṃ ca hi vanaṃ śūra bahukandaraśobhitam ।। sā vanaṃ vā praviṣṭā syān nalinīṃ vā supuṣpitām ।। jijñāsamānā vaidehī tvāṃ māṃ ca puruṣarṣabha ।। manyase yadi kākutstha mā sma śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।।
tau vanāni girīṃś caiva saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca ।। tasya śailasya sānūni guhāś ca śikharāṇi ca ।। vicitya sarvataḥ śailaṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।। tato duḥkhābhisaṃtapto lakṣmaṇo vākyam abravīt ।।
prāpsyasi tvaṃ mahāprājña maithilīṃ janakātmajām ।। evam uktas tu vīreṇa lakṣmaṇena sa rāghavaḥ ।। vanaṃ sarvaṃ suvicitaṃ padminyaḥ phullapaṅkajāḥ ।। na hi paśyāmi vaidehīṃ prāṇebhyo api garīyasīm ।।
dīnaḥ śokasamāviṣṭo muhūrtaṃ vihvalo abhavat ।। viṣasādāturo dīno niḥśvasyāśītam āyatam ।। hā priyeti vicukrośa bahuśo bāṣpagadgadaḥ ।। bahuprakāraṃ dharmajñaḥ praśritaḥ praśritāñjaliḥ ।।
apaśyaṃs tāṃ priyāṃ sītāṃ prākrośat sa punaḥ punaḥ ।। api godāvarīṃ sītā padmāny ānayituṃ gatā ।। nadīṃ godāvarīṃ ramyāṃ jagāma laghuvikramaḥ ।। naināṃ paśyāmi tīrtheṣu krośato na śṛṇoti me ।।
na hi taṃ vedmi vai rāma yatra sā tanumadhyamā ।। rāmaḥ samabhicakrāma svayaṃ godāvarīṃ nadīm ।। sa tām upasthito rāmaḥ kva sītety evam abravīt ।। na tāṃ śaśaṃsū rāmāya tathā godāvarī nadī ।।
