na ca sābhyavadat sītāṃ pṛṣṭā rāmeṇa śocitā ।। dhyātvā bhayāt tu vaidehīṃ sā nadī na śaśaṃsa tām ।। uvāca rāmaḥ saumitriṃ sītādarśanakarśitaḥ ।। mātaraṃ caiva vaidehyā vinā tām aham apriyam ।।
sarvaṃ vyapanayacchokam vaidehī kva nu sā gatā ।। manye dīrghā bhaviṣyanti rātrayo mama jāgrataḥ ।। sarvāṇy anucariṣyāmi yadi sītā hi dṛśyate ।। vasuṃdharāyāṃ patitaṃ puṣpamārgam apaśyatām ।।
uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ vīro duḥkhito duḥkhitaṃ vacaḥ ।। apinaddhāni vaidehyā mayā dattāni kānane ।। kruddho abravīd giriṃ tatra siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā ।। yāvat sānūni sarvāṇi na te vidhvaṃsayāmy aham ।।
asevyaḥ satataṃ caiva nistṛṇadrumapallavaḥ ।। yadi nākhyāti me sītām adya candranibhānanām ।। dadarśa bhūmau niṣkrāntaṃ rākṣasasya padaṃ mahat ।। saṃbhrāntahṛdayo rāmaḥ śaśaṃsa bhrātaraṃ priyam ।।
bhūṣaṇānāṃ hi saumitre mālyāni vividhāni ca ।। āvṛtaṃ paśya saumitre sarvato dharaṇītalam ।। bhittvā bhittvā vibhaktā vā bhakṣitā vā bhaviṣyati ।। babhūva yuddhaṃ saumitre ghoraṃ rākṣasayor iha ।।
dharaṇyāṃ patitaṃ saumya kasya bhagnaṃ mahad dhanuḥ ।। viśīrṇaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau kavacaṃ kasya kāñcanam ।। bhagnadaṇḍam idaṃ kasya bhūmau saumya nipātitam ।। bhīmarūpā mahākāyāḥ kasya vā nihatā raṇe ।।
apaviddhaś ca bhagnaś ca kasya sāṃgrāmiko rathaḥ ।। kasyeme abhihatā bāṇāḥ prakīrṇā ghorakarmaṇaḥ ।। sughorahṛdayaiḥ saumya rākṣasaiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ ।। na dharmas trāyate sītāṃ hriyamāṇāṃ mahāvane ।।
ke hi loke priyaṃ kartuṃ śaktāḥ saumya mameśvarāḥ ।। ajñānād avamanyeran sarvabhūtāni lakṣmaṇa ।। nirvīrya iti manyante nūnaṃ māṃ tridaśeśvarāḥ ।। saṃhṛtyaiva śaśijyotsnāṃ mahān sūrya ivoditaḥ ।।
kiṃnarā vā manuṣyā vā sukhaṃ prāpsyanti lakṣmaṇa ।। niḥsampātaṃ kariṣyāmi hy adya trailokyacāriṇām ।। vipranaṣṭānalamarudbhāskaradyutisaṃvṛtam ।। dhvastadrumalatāgulmaṃ vipraṇāśitasāgaram ।।
asmin muhūrte saumitre mama drakṣyanti vikramam ।। mama cāpaguṇān muktair bāṇajālair nirantaram ।। samākulam amaryādaṃ jagat paśyādya lakṣmaṇa ।। kariṣye maithilīhetor apiśācam arākṣasam ।।
drakṣyanty adya vimuktānām amarṣād dūragāminām ।। bhaviṣyanti mama krodhāt trailokye vipraṇāśite ।। nirmaryādān imāṃl lokān kariṣyāmy adya sāyakaiḥ ।। tathāhaṃ krodhasaṃyukto na nivāryo asmy asaṃśayam ।।
sadevagandharvamanuṣyapannagaṃ jagat saśailaṃ parivartayāmy aham ।। lokānām abhave yuktaṃ saṃvartakam ivānalam ।। hantukāmaṃ paśuṃ rudraṃ kruddhaṃ dakṣakratau yathā ।। abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā ।।
na krodhavaśam āpannaḥ prakṛtiṃ hātum arhasi ।। etac ca niyataṃ sarvaṃ tvayi cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ ।। kena vā kasya vā hetoḥ sāyudhaḥ saparicchadaḥ ।। deśo nivṛttasaṃgrāmaḥ sughoraḥ pārthivātmaja ।।
na hi vṛttaṃ hi paśyāmi balasya mahataḥ padam ।। yuktadaṇḍā hi mṛdavaḥ praśāntā vasudhādhipāḥ ।। ko nu dārapraṇāśaṃ te sādhu manyeta rāghava ।। nālaṃ te vipriyaṃ kartuṃ dīkṣitasyeva sādhavaḥ ।।
maddvitīyo dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sahāyaiḥ paramarṣibhiḥ ।। guhāś ca vividhā ghorā nalinīḥ pārvatīś ca ha ।। yāvan nādhigamiṣyāmas tava bhāryāpahāriṇam ।। kosalendra tataḥ paścāt prāptakālaṃ kariṣyasi ।।
tataḥ samutsādaya hemapuṅkhair mahendravajrapratimaiḥ śaraughaiḥ ।। mohena mahatāviṣṭaṃ paridyūnam acetanam ।। rāmaṃ saṃbodhayāmāsa caraṇau cābhipīḍayan ।। rājñā daśarathenāsīl labdho amṛtam ivāmaraiḥ ।।
rājā devatvam āpanno bharatasya yathā śrutam ।। prākṛtaś cālpasattvaś ca itaraḥ kaḥ sahiṣyati ।। ārtāḥ prajā naravyāghra kva nu yāsyanti nirvṛtim ।। gataḥ śakreṇa sālokyam anayas taṃ samaspṛśat ।।
ahnā putraśataṃ jajñe tathaivāsya punar hatam ।। asyāś ca calanaṃ bhūmer dṛśyate satyasaṃśrava ।। ādityacandrau grahaṇam abhyupetau mahābalau ।। na daivasya pramuñcanti sarvabhūtāni dehinaḥ ।।
śrūyete naraśārdūla na tvaṃ vyathitum arhasi ।। śocituṃ nārhase vīra yathānyaḥ prākṛtas tathā ।। sumahatsv api kṛcchreṣu rāmānirviṇṇadarśanāḥ ।। buddhyā yuktā mahāprājñā vijānanti śubhāśubhe ।।
nāntareṇa kriyāṃ teṣāṃ phalam iṣṭaṃ pravartate ।। anuśiṣyāddhi ko nu tvām api sākṣād bṛhaspatiḥ ।। śokenābhiprasuptaṃ te jñānaṃ saṃbodhayāmy aham ।। ikṣvākuvṛṣabhāvekṣya yatasva dviṣatāṃ vadhe ।।
tam eva tu ripuṃ pāpaṃ vijñāyoddhartum arhasi ।। sāragrāhī mahāsāraṃ pratijagrāha rāghavaḥ ।। avaṣṭabhya dhanuś citraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।। kenopāyena paśyeyaṃ sītām iti vicintaya ।।
idam eva janasthānaṃ tvam anveṣitum arhasi ।। santīha giridurgāṇi nirdarāḥ kandarāṇi ca ।। āvāsāḥ kiṃnarāṇāṃ ca gandharvabhavanāni ca ।। tvadvidhā buddhisampannā mahātmāno nararṣabha ।।
ity uktas tad vanaṃ sarvaṃ vicacāra salakṣmaṇaḥ ।। tataḥ parvatakūṭābhaṃ mahābhāgaṃ dvijottamam ।। anena sītā vaidehī bhakṣitā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। enaṃ vadhiṣye dīptāgrair ghorair bāṇair ajihmagaiḥ ।।
kruddho rāmaḥ samudrāntāṃ cālayann iva medinīm ।। abhyabhāṣata pakṣī tu rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam ।। sā devī mama ca prāṇā rāvaṇenobhayaṃ hṛtam ।। hriyamāṇā mayā dṛṣṭā rāvaṇena balīyasā ।।
vidhvaṃsitarathacchattraḥ pātito dharaṇītale ।। ayam asya raṇe rāma bhagnaḥ sāṃgrāmiko rathaḥ ।। rakṣasā nihataṃ pūrvaṃ na māṃ hantuṃ tvam arhasi ।। gṛdhrarājaṃ pariṣvajya ruroda sahalakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
samīkṣya duḥkhito rāmaḥ saumitrim idam abravīt ।। īdṛśīyaṃ mamālakṣmīr nirdahed api pāvakam ।। so api nūnaṃ mamālakṣmyā viśuṣyet saritāṃ patiḥ ।। yeneyaṃ mahatī prāptā mayā vyasanavāgurā ।।
śete vinihato bhūmau mama bhāgyaviparyayāt ।। jaṭāyuṣaṃ ca pasparśa pitṛsnehaṃ nidarśayan ।। kva maithili prāṇasamā mameti vimucya vācaṃ nipapāta bhūmau ।। saumitriṃ mitrasampannam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
rākṣasena hataḥ saṃkhye prāṇāṃs tyajati dustyajān ।। tathā svaravihīno ayaṃ viklavaṃ samudīkṣate ।। sītām ākhyāhi bhadraṃ te vadham ākhyāhi cātmanaḥ ।। aparāddhaṃ tu yaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇena hṛtā priyā ।।
sītayā kāni coktāni tasmin kāle dvijottama ।। kva cāsya bhavanaṃ tāta brūhi me paripṛcchataḥ ।। vācātisannayā rāmaṃ jaṭāyur idam abravīt ।। māyām āsthāya vipulāṃ vātadurdinasaṃkulām ।।
sītām ādāya vaidehīṃ prayāto dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।। paśyāmi vṛkṣān sauvarṇān uśīrakṛtamūrdhajān ।। vipraṇaṣṭaṃ dhanaṃ kṣipraṃ tatsvāmī pratipadyate ।। jhaṣavad baḍiśaṃ gṛhya kṣipram eva vinaśyati ।।
vaidehyā raṃsyase kṣipraṃ hatvā taṃ rākṣasaṃ raṇe ।। āsyāt susrāva rudhiraṃ mriyamāṇasya sāmiṣam ।। ity uktvā durlabhān prāṇān mumoca patageśvaraḥ ।। tyaktvā śarīraṃ gṛdhrasya jagmuḥ prāṇā vihāyasam ।।
vikṣipya ca śarīraṃ svaṃ papāta dharaṇītale ।। rāmaḥ subahubhir duḥkhair dīnaḥ saumitrim abravīt ।। anena daṇḍakāraṇye vicīrṇam iha pakṣiṇā ।। so ayam adya hataḥ śete kālo hi duratikramaḥ ।।
sītām abhyavapan no vai rāvaṇena balīyasā ।। mama hetor ayaṃ prāṇān mumoca patageśvaraḥ ।। śūrāḥ śaraṇyāḥ saumitre tiryagyonigateṣv api ।। yathā vināśo gṛdhrasya matkṛte ca paraṃtapa ।।
pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca tathāyaṃ patageśvaraḥ ।। gṛdhrarājaṃ didhakṣāmi matkṛte nidhanaṃ gatam ।। imaṃ dhakṣyāmi saumitre hataṃ raudreṇa rakṣasā ।। aparāvartināṃ yā ca yā ca bhūmipradāyinām ।।
gṛdhrarāja mahāsattva saṃskṛtaś ca mayā vraja ।। dadāha rāmo dharmātmā svabandhum iva duḥkhitaḥ ।। sthūlān hatvā mahārohīn anu tastāra taṃ dvijam ।। śakunāya dadau rāmo ramye haritaśādvale ।।
tat svargagamanaṃ tasya kṣipraṃ rāmo jajāpa ha ।। udakaṃ cakratus tasmai gṛdhrarājāya tāv ubhau ।। maharṣikalpena ca saṃskṛtas tadā jagāma puṇyāṃ gatim ātmanaḥ śubhām ।। avekṣantau vane sītāṃ paścimāṃ jagmatur diśam ।।
aviprahatam aikṣvākau panthānaṃ pratipedatuḥ ।। āvṛtaṃ sarvato durgaṃ gahanaṃ ghoradarśanam ।। subhīmaṃ tan mahāraṇyaṃ vyatiyātau mahābalau ।। krauñcāraṇyaṃ viviśatur gahanaṃ tau mahaujasau ।।
nānāvarṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ puṣpair mṛgapakṣigaṇair yutam ।। tatra tatrāvatiṣṭhantau sītāharaṇakarśitau ।। abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ bhrātaraṃ dīptatejasam ।। prāyaśaś cāpy aniṣṭāni nimittāny upalakṣaye ।।
mamaiva hi nimittāni sadyaḥ śaṃsanti sambhramam ।। āvayor vijayaṃ yuddhe śaṃsann iva vinardati ।। saṃjajñe vipulaḥ śabdaḥ prabhañjann iva tad vanam ।। vanasya tasya śabdo abhūd divam āpūrayann iva ।।
dadarśa sumahākāyaṃ rākṣasaṃ vipulorasam ।। vivṛddham aśirogrīvaṃ kabandham udare mukham ।। nīlameghanibhaṃ raudraṃ meghastanitaniḥsvanam ।। ekenorasi ghoreṇa nayanenāśudarśinā ।।
bhakṣayantaṃ mahāghorān ṛkṣasiṃhamṛgadvipān ।। karābhyāṃ vividhān gṛhya ṛkṣān pakṣigaṇān mṛgān ।। sthitam āvṛtya panthānaṃ tayor bhrātroḥ prapannayoḥ ।। mahāntaṃ dāruṇaṃ bhīmaṃ kabandhaṃ bhujasaṃvṛtam ।।
jagrāha sahitāv eva rāghavau pīḍayan balāt ।। bhrātarau vivaśaṃ prāptau kṛṣyamāṇau mahābalau ।। kau yuvāṃ vṛṣabhaskandhau mahākhaḍgadhanurdharau ।। vadataṃ kāryam iha vāṃ kimarthaṃ cāgatau yuvām ।।
mamāsyam anusaṃprāptau durlabhaṃ jīvitaṃ punaḥ ।। uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo mukhena pariśuṣyatā ।। vyasanaṃ jīvitāntāya prāptam aprāpya tāṃ priyām ।। nātibhāro asti daivasya sarvabhūteṣu lakṣmaṇa ।।
kālābhipannāḥ sīdanti yathā vālukasetavaḥ ।। avekṣya saumitrim udagravikramaṃ sthirāṃ tadā svāṃ matim ātmanākarot ।। bāhupāśaparikṣiptau kabandho vākyam abravīt ।। āhārārthaṃ tu saṃdiṣṭau daivena gatacetasau ।।
uvācārtisamāpanno vikrame kṛtaniścayaḥ ।। tasmād asibhyām asyāśu bāhū chindāvahai gurū ।। achindatāṃ susaṃhṛṣṭau bāhū tasyāṃsadeśayoḥ ।। cicheda rāmo vegena savyaṃ vīras tu lakṣmaṇaḥ ।।
khaṃ ca gāṃ ca diśaś caiva nādayañ jalado yathā ।। dīnaḥ papraccha tau vīrau kau yuvām iti dānavaḥ ।। śaśaṃsa tasya kākutsthaṃ kabandhasya mahābalaḥ ।। asyaivāvarajaṃ viddhi bhrātaraṃ māṃ ca lakṣmaṇam ।।
rakṣasāpahṛtā bhāryā yām icchantāv ihāgatau ।। āsyenorasi dīptena bhagnajaṅgho viceṣṭase ।। uvāca paramaprītas tad indravacanaṃ smaran ।। diṣṭyā cemau nikṛttau me yuvābhyāṃ bāhubandhanau ।।
tan me śṛṇu naravyāghra tattvataḥ śaṃsatas tava ।। yathā somasya śakrasya sūryasya ca yathā vapuḥ ।। ṛṣīn vanagatān rāma trāsayāmi tatas tataḥ ।। saṃcinvan vividhaṃ vanyaṃ rūpeṇānena dharṣitaḥ ।।
etad eva nṛśaṃsaṃ te rūpam astu vigarhitam ।। abhiśāpakṛtasyeti tenedaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vacaḥ ।। tadā tvaṃ prāpsyase rūpaṃ svam eva vipulaṃ śubham ।। indrakopād idaṃ rūpaṃ prāptam evaṃ raṇājire ।।
dīrgham āyuḥ sa me prādāt tato māṃ vibhramo aspṛśat ।। ity evaṃ buddhim āsthāya raṇe śakram adharṣayam ।। sakthinī ca śiraś caiva śarīre saṃpraveśitam ।। pitāmahavacaḥ satyaṃ tad astv iti mamābravīt ।।
vajreṇābhihataḥ kālaṃ sudīrgham api jīvitum ।। prādād āsyaṃ ca me kukṣau tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭram akalpayat ।। siṃhadvipamṛgavyāghrān bhakṣayāmi samantataḥ ।। chetsyate samare bāhū tadā svargaṃ gamiṣyasi ।।
śakyo hantuṃ yathātattvam evam uktaṃ maharṣiṇā ।। mitraṃ caivopadekṣyāmi yuvābhyāṃ saṃskṛto agninā ।। idaṃ jagāda vacanaṃ lakṣmaṇasyopaśṛṇvataḥ ।। niṣkrāntasya janasthānāt saha bhrātrā yathāsukham ।।
nivāsaṃ vā prabhāvaṃ vā vayaṃ tasya na vidmahe ।। kāruṇyaṃ sadṛśaṃ kartum upakāre ca vartatām ।। bhakṣyāmas tvāṃ vayaṃ vīra śvabhre mahati kalpite ।। kuru kalyāṇam atyarthaṃ yadi jānāsi tattvataḥ ।।
provāca kuśalo vaktuṃ vaktāram api rāghavam ।। yas tāṃ jñāsyati taṃ vakṣye dagdhaḥ svaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ ।। rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahāvīryaṃ sītā yena hṛtā tava ।। svakṛtena mayā prāptaṃ rūpaṃ lokavigarhitam ।।
tāvan mām avaṭe kṣiptvā daha rāma yathāvidhi ।। vakṣyāmi tam ahaṃ vīra yas taṃ jñāsyati rākṣasam ।। kalpayiṣyati te prītaḥ sāhāyyaṃ laghuvikramaḥ ।। sarvān parisṛto lokān purā vai kāraṇāntare ।।
giripradaram āsādya pāvakaṃ visasarjatuḥ ।। citām ādīpayāmāsa sā prajajvāla sarvataḥ ।। medasā pacyamānasya mandaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ ।। araje vāsasī bibhran mālāṃ divyāṃ mahābalaḥ ।।
utpapātāśu saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sarvapratyaṅgabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। prabhayā ca mahātejā diśo daśa virājayan ।। śṛṇu rāghava tattvena yathā sīmām avāpsyasi ।। parimṛṣṭo daśāntena daśābhāgena sevyate ।।
yat kṛte vyasanaṃ prāptaṃ tvayā dārapradharṣaṇam ।। akṛtvā na hi te siddhim ahaṃ paśyāmi cintayan ।। bhrātrā nirastaḥ kruddhena vālinā śakrasūnunā ।। nivasaty ātmavān vīraś caturbhiḥ saha vānaraiḥ ।।
adrohāya samāgamya dīpyamāne vibhāvasau ।। kṛtajñaḥ kāmarūpī ca sahāyārthī ca vīryavān ।। kṛtārtho vākṛtārtho vā kṛtyaṃ tava kariṣyati ।। bhāskarasyaurasaḥ putro vālinā kṛtakilbiṣaḥ ।।
kuru rāghava satyena vayasyaṃ vanacāriṇam ।। naramāṃsāśināṃ loke naipuṇyād adhigacchati ।। yāvat sūryaḥ pratapati sahasrāṃśur ariṃdama ।। anviṣya vānaraiḥ sārdhaṃ patnīṃ te adhigamiṣyati ।।
diśo vicetuṃ tāṃ sītāṃ tvadviyogena śocatīm ।। plavaṃgamānāṃ pravaras tava priyāṃ nihatya rakṣāṃsi punaḥ pradāsyati ।। vākyam anvartham arthajñaḥ kabandhaḥ punar abravīt ।। pratīcīṃ diśam āśritya prakāśante manoramāḥ ।।
aśvatthāḥ karṇikārāś ca cūtāś cānye ca pādapāḥ ।। phalāny amṛtakalpāni bhakṣayantau gamiṣyathaḥ ।। tataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ vīrau pampāṃ nāma gamiṣyathaḥ ।। rāma saṃjātavālūkāṃ kamalotpalaśobhitām ।।
valgusvarā nikūjanti pampāsalilagocarāḥ ।। ghṛtapiṇḍopamān sthūlāṃs tān dvijān bhakṣayiṣyathaḥ ।। pampāyām iṣubhir matsyāṃs tatra rāma varān hatān ।। tava bhaktyā samāyukto lakṣmaṇaḥ sampradāsyati ।।
padmagandhi śivaṃ vāri sukhaśītam anāmayam ।। atha puṣkaraparṇena lakṣmaṇaḥ pāyayiṣyati ।। rūpānvitāṃś ca pampāyāṃ drakṣyasi tvaṃ narottama ।। śītodakaṃ ca pampāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā śokaṃ vihāsyasi ।।
utpalāni ca phullāni paṅkajāni ca rāghava ।। mataṃgaśiṣyās tatrāsann ṛṣayaḥ susamāhitaḥ ।। ye prapetur mahīṃ tūrṇaṃ śarīrāt svedabindavaḥ ।। svedabindusamutthāni na vinaśyanti rāghava ।।
śramaṇī śabarī nāma kākutstha cirajīvinī ।। dṛṣṭvā devopamaṃ rāma svargalokaṃ gamiṣyati ।। āśramasthānam atulaṃ guhyaṃ kākutstha paśyasi ।। ṛṣes tasya mataṃgasya vidhānāt tac ca kānanam ।।
nānāvihagasaṃkīrṇe raṃsyase rāma nirvṛtaḥ ।। udāro brahmaṇā caiva pūrvakāle vinirmitaḥ ।। yat svapne labhate vittaṃ tat prabuddho adhigacchati ।। tatraiva praharanty enaṃ suptam ādāya rākṣasāḥ ।।
krīḍatāṃ rāma pampāyāṃ mataṃgāraṇyavāsinām ।। pracaranti pṛthak kīrṇā meghavarṇās tarasvinaḥ ।। nivṛttāḥ saṃvigāhante vanāni vanagocarāḥ ।। śilāpidhānā kākutstha duḥkhaṃ cāsyāḥ praveśanam ।।
bahumūlaphalo ramyo nānānagasamāvṛtaḥ ।। kadācicchikhare tasya parvatasyāvatiṣṭhate ।। sragvī bhāskaravarṇābhaḥ khe vyarocata vīryavān ।। prasthitau tvaṃ vrajasveti vākyam ūcatur antikāt ।।
suprītau tāv anujñāpya kabandhaḥ prasthitas tadā ।। nidarśayan rāmam avekṣya khasthaḥ sakhyaṃ kuruṣveti tadābhyuvāca ।। ātasthatur diśaṃ gṛhya pratīcīṃ nṛvarātmajau ।। vīkṣantau jagmatur draṣṭuṃ sugrīvaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau ।।
pampāyāḥ paścimaṃ tīraṃ rāghavāv upatasthatuḥ ।। apaśyatāṃ tatas tatra śabaryā ramyam āśramam ।। suramyam abhivīkṣantau śabarīm abhyupeyatuḥ ।। pādau jagrāha rāmasya lakṣmaṇasya ca dhīmataḥ ।।
kaccit te nirjitā vighnāḥ kaccit te vardhate tapaḥ ।। kaccit te guruśuśrūṣā saphalā cārubhāṣiṇi ।। śaśaṃsa śabarī vṛddhā rāmāya pratyupasthitā ।। itas te divam ārūḍhā yān ahaṃ paryacāriṣam ।।
āgamiṣyati te rāmaḥ supuṇyam imam āśramam ।। taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā varāṃl lokān akṣayāṃs tvaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। tavārthe puruṣavyāghra pampāyās tīrasambhavam ।। rāghavaḥ prāha vijāne tāṃ nityam abahiṣkṛtām ।।
śrutaṃ pratyakṣam icchāmi saṃdraṣṭuṃ yadi manyase ।। śabarī darśayāmāsa tāv ubhau tad vanaṃ mahat ।। mataṃgavanam ity eva viśrutaṃ raghunandana ।। juhavāṃścakrire tīrthaṃ mantravan mantrapūjitam ।।
puṣpopahāraṃ kurvanti śramād udvepibhiḥ karaiḥ ।। dyotayanti diśaḥ sarvāḥ śriyā vedyo atulaprabhāḥ ।। cintite abhyāgatān paśya sametān sapta sāgarān ।। adyāpi na viśuṣyanti pradeśe raghunandana ।।
tad icchāmy abhyanujñātā tyaktum etat kalevaram ।। munīnām āśramo yeṣām ahaṃ ca paricāriṇī ।। anujānāmi gaccheti prahṛṣṭavadano abravīt ।। jvalatpāvakasaṃkāśā svargam eva jagāma sā ।।
tat puṇyaṃ śabarī sthānaṃ jagāmātmasamādhinā ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā cintayāmāsa rāghavaḥ ।। hitakāriṇam ekāgraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāghavo abravīt ।। viśvastamṛgaśārdūlo nānāvihagasevitaḥ ।।
upaspṛṣṭaṃ ca vidhivat pitaraś cāpi tarpitāḥ ।। tena tv etat prahṛṣṭaṃ me mano lakṣmaṇa samprati ।। tad āgaccha gamiṣyāvaḥ pampāṃ tāṃ priyadarśanām ।। nityaṃ vālibhayāt trastaś caturbhiḥ saha vānaraiḥ ।।
।। tadadhīnaṃ hi me saumya sītāyāḥ parimārgaṇam ।। gacchāvas tvaritaṃ tatra mamāpi tvarate manaḥ ।। ājagāma tataḥ pampāṃ lakṣmaṇena sahābhibhūḥ ।।
etaiś cānyaiś ca vividhair nāditaṃ tad vanaṃ mahat ।। paśyan kāmābhisaṃtapto jagāma paramaṃ hradam ।। mataṃgasarasaṃ nāma hradaṃ samavagāhata ।। viveśa nalinīṃ pampāṃ paṅkajaiś ca samāvṛtām ।।
ramyopavanasambādhāṃ padmasaṃpīḍitodakām ।। matsyakacchapasambādhāṃ tīrasthadrumaśobhitām ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇāṃ śītavārinidhiṃ śubhām ।। nīlāṃ kuvalayoddhātair bahuvarṇāṃ kuthām iva ।।
puṣpitāmravaṇopetāṃ barhiṇodghuṣṭanāditām ।। vilalāpa ca tejasvī kāmād daśarathātmajaḥ ।। puṣpitaiḥ karavīraiś ca puṃnāgaiś ca supuṣpitaiḥ ।। anyaiś ca vividhair vṛkṣaiḥ pramadevopaśobhitām ।।
ṛśyamūka iti khyātaś citrapuṣpitakānanaḥ ।। adhyāste taṃ mahāvīryaḥ sugrīva iti viśrutaḥ ।। ity uvāca punar vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ satyavikramam ।। dadarśa pampāṃ śubhadarśakānanām anekanānāvidhapakṣisaṃkulām ।।
